
 
 
 saduktikarṇāmṛtam [śrīdharadāsa-saṅkalitam] 
 maṅgalam 
 
 prajñāṃ kām api sampadaṃ ca kurute yatpādasaṃvāhanaṃ 
 nityaṃ śāmyati viṣvagandhatamasaṃ yaccakṣur unmīlanāt | 
 yatpādārghyapayo vidhūya duritaṃ niḥśreyasaṃ yacchati 
 svānte naḥ sa vasatv anāratam anākhyeyasvarūpo hariḥ  ||1|| 
 
 
 prastāvaḥ 
 
 śauryāṇīva tapāṃsi bibhrati bhayaṃ yasmin na yasyāvadhir 
 jñāne dāna iva dviṣām iva jayo yenendriyāṇāṃ kṛtaḥ | 
 samrājām iva yoginām api gurur yaś ca kṣamāmaṇḍale 
 sa śrīlalakṣmaṇasena ekanṛpatir muktaś ca jīvann abhūt  ||1|| 
 
 
 tasyāsīt pratirājatadvṛtamahāsāmantacūḍāmaṇir 
 nāmnā śrībaṭudāsa ity anupamapremaikapātraṃ sakhā | 
 tāpaṃ santamasaṃ harann aharahaḥ kīrtiṃ dadhat kaumudīṃ 
 sākṣād akṣayasūnṛtāmṛtamayaḥ pūrṇaḥ kalānāṃ nidhiḥ  ||2|| 
 
 
 śrīmān śrīdharadāsa ity adhiguṇādhāraḥ sa tasmād abhūd 
 ākaumārapārapauruṣaparādhīnasya yasyāniśam | 
 lakṣmīr vedavidāṃ gṛheṣu guṇitā goṣṭhīṣu vidyāvatāṃ 
 bhaktiḥ śrīpatipādaopallavanakhajyotsnāsu viśrāmyati  ||3|| 
 
 
 pratyekaṃ viṣayeṣu pañcakamitaiḥ ślokaiḥ kavīnām idaṃ 
 tenākāraṇabāndhavena vidadhe śrīsūktikarṇāmṛtam | 
 prītiṃ pallavayantu karṇakalasīmāpūrayantaś ciraṃ 
 majjantaḥ pariśīlayantu rasikāḥ pañca pravāhān iha  ||4|| 
 
 
 amarāḥ śṛṅgāracaṭū apadeśoccāvace kramaśaḥ | 
 iti pañcabhiḥ pravāhaiḥ saduktikarṇāmṛtaṃ kriyate  ||5|| 
 
 
 
 
 amarapravāhavīcayaḥ 
 
 
 atha dhātā ravir īśapraṇatimahādevaśivaharakrīḍāḥ | 
 praśnottarāṭṭahāsāv amuṣya mūrdhīttamāṅgagaṅgā ca  ||1|| 
 mauliśaśī koṭīro muṇḍāvalir akṣi purabhidārambhaḥ | 
 bāṇānaloṣṭamūrtir bhairavaharatāṇḍavārambhau  ||2|| 
 nṛtyaṃ haraprasādanam atha gaurī pariṇayasthagaurī ca | 
 śṛṅgāro giriduhitur durgā kālī tathārdhanārīśaḥ  ||3|| 
 śṛṅgārī ca gajānanaśarasambhavabhṛṅgiṇaḥ pramathāḥ | 
 atha hariharau sakāntau surasindhur jahnkanyakāśaṃsā  ||4|| 
 matsyakamaṭhasūkarakeśarinṛsiṃhapāṇijanmānaḥ | 
 śṛṅgārī ca nṛsiṃho vāmanamūrtis trivikramo bhṛgujaḥ  ||5|| 
 dāśarathir eṣa virahī haladharajinakalkino’tha kṛṣṇasya | 
 śiśutākumārabhāvau svapnāyitayauvanakrīḍāḥ  ||6|| 
 praśnottaraṃ ca veṇudhvananaṃ gītaṃ bhujaś ca giridharaṇam | 
 utkaṇṭhā gopavadhūsandeśo harir amuṣya bhaktiś ca  ||7|| 
 udadhimathanaharir ambudhimathanotthaśrīḥ svayaṃvaro lakṣmyāḥ | 
 śrī śṛṅgāraḥ kamalākamalopālabhavāk praśastenduḥ  ||8|| 
 candrakalā śaśibimbaṃ prauḍhavidhuḥ sarucicandramā raśmiḥ | 
 jyotsnā kalaṅkatamauḍukairavasahitendubhāvaś ca  ||9|| 
 miśrabahurūpakāstaṅgatabahuviṣayendavo’tha gandhavahaḥ | 
 dakṣiṇanadīsamudraprabhātabhinnaś ca puṣpadhanvā ca  ||10|| 
 smaraśauryam athoccāvacam iti pañcopetanavativīcibhiḥ | 
 śrīdharadāsena kṛtaḥ kṛtinā devapravāho’yam  ||11|| 
 
 
 devapravāhaḥ 
 1. atha brahmavīciḥ 
 
 
 śambhoḥ sākṣāt sakhaikaḥ surapatiparo dharmarājas tathānyaḥ 
 prāṇā viśvasya kasya prathamataramataḥ ko’nu sambhāṣaṇīyaḥ | 
 kāryāyātān viditvā muhur iti caturo lokapālāṃś caturbhir 
 vaktrair ābhāṣamāṇaḥ samam uditaravaḥ pātu padmodbhavo vaḥ  ||1|| 
 
 
 pālitasya | 
 
 
 āgaskāriṇi kālanemidalane tattāḍanārthaṃ ruṣā 
 nābhīpaṅkajam astratāṃ gamayituṃ jāne prayatne śriyaḥ | 
 āvāsonmathanopapāditabhayabhrāntātmanaḥ sambhramād 
 abrahmaṇyaparāḥ purātanamuner vācaḥ prasīdantu vaḥ  ||2|| 
 
 
 bhaṭṭaśrīnivāsasya | (sū.mu. 2.108) 
 
 
 pāyād vo madhukaiṭabhāsuravadhe viṣṇuprabodhoddhuro 
 dhātā vaktracatuṣṭayaṃ tu yugapad yasyābhavatsārthakam | 
 ekaṃ stauti mukhaṃ śivām itarad apy ārtaṃ varān yācate  
 daityau praty aparaṃ vitarjati haraty anyac chriyaḥ sambhramam  ||3|| 
 
 
 vasantadevasya | 
 
 
 yan na kṣuṇṇaṃ kadācit tuhinakaṇacayasyandibhiś candrapādair 
 nāpi vyālīnamusrair navanalinasarobandhubhir bhānavīyaiḥ | 
 tatkalpāntānuṣaṅgi drutam atanutamaḥ pāṭayantyaḥ samantād 
 ādyādhītau vidhātur mukhaśaśivisṛtāḥ pāntu vo dantabhāsaḥ  ||4|| 
 
 
 bījakasya | 
 
 
 jātas te’dharakhaṇḍanāt paribhavaḥ kāpālikādyo’bhavat 
 sa brahmādiṣu kathyatām iti muhur bālyād guhe jalpati | 
 gaurīṃ hastayugena ṣaṇmukhavaco roddhuṃ nirīkṣyākṣamāṃ 
 vailakṣyāc caturāsyaniṣphalaparāvṛttiś ciraṃ pātu vaḥ  ||5|| 
 
 
 (su.ra. 101, sū.mu. 2.105) 
 2. sūryaḥ 
 
 
 tuṅgodayādribhujagendraphaṇopalāya 
 vyomendranīlatarukāñcanapallavāya | 
 saṃsārasāgarasamutkramiyogisārtha 
 prasthānapūrṇakalasāya namaḥ savitre  ||6|| 
 
 
 varāhamihirasya | (su.ra. 150) 
 
 
 viṣvagvisāritimiraprakarāvaruddha 
 trailokyanetrapuṭasiddharasāyanāya | 
 tubhyaṃ namaḥ kamalaṣaṇḍaviṣādanidrā 
 vidrāvaṇodyatakarāya divākarāya  ||7|| 
 
 
 śrīkaṇṭhasya | 
 
 
 śukatuṇḍacchavi savituś caṇḍarucaḥ puṇḍarīkavanabandhoḥ | 
 maṇḍalam uditaṃ vande kuṇḍalam ākhaṇḍalāśāyāḥ  ||8|| 
 
 
 vidyāyāḥ | (su.ra. 149, śā.pa. 86) 
 
 
 jīyād ekaphalaṃ nabhastalataror abhraṃśi sindūriṇī 
 mudrā kairavakānanasya timirasteyāya sandhir divaḥ | 
 mandārastavakontarīkṣakavarībhārasya gaurīpateḥ 
 kampillacchadapāṭalacchavi kulacchatraṃ raghūṇāṃ raviḥ  ||9|| 
 
 
 hareḥ |  
 
 
 ādyūnas tamasāṃ cakoraramaṇīrāgābdhimanthācalo 
 jīvātur jalajasya vāsavadiśāśailendracūḍāmaṇiḥ | 
 ādeṣṭā śrutikarmaṇāṃ kumudinīśokāgnipūrṇāhutir 
 devaḥ somarasāyanaṃ vijayate viśvasya bījaṃ raviḥ  ||10|| 
 
 
 vibhākarasya | 
 
 
 3. īśapraṇatiḥ 
 
 
 maulau vegād udañcaty api caraṇabharanyañcadurvītalatvād 
 akṣuṇṇasvargalokasthitimuditasuraśreṣṭhagoṣṭhīstutāya | 
 saṃtrāsān niḥsaranaty avirataviṣajaddakṣiṇārdhāṅga 
 bandhād atyaktāyādriputryā tirpuraharajagatkleśahantre namas te  ||11|| 
 
 
 bāṇasya | (su.ra. 56) 
 
 
 namas tuṅgaśiraś cumbicandracāmaracārave | 
 trailokyanagarārambhamūlastambhāya śambhave  ||12|| 
 
 
 (su.ra. 48) 
 
 
 tādṛksaptasamudramudritamahībhūbhṛdbhir abhraṃkaṣais 
 tāvadbhiḥ parivāritā pṛthudvīpaiḥ samantād iyam | 
 yasya sphāraphaṇāmaṇau nilayanāt tiryakkalaṅkākṛtiḥ 
 śeṣaḥ so’py agamad yadaṅgadapadaṃ tasmai namaḥ śambhave  ||13|| 
 
 
 ballaṇasya | (su.ra. 38) 
 
 
 namas tasmai kasmaicana vacanavittendriyayamī 
 yam īśānaṃ jyotirmayam ayam upāste munijanaḥ | 
 gurūpajñaprajñāmukuranikurambapratiphalan 
 nijānandajyotsnābhyudayabhidurājñānatimiraḥ  ||14|| 
 
 
 hareḥ | 
 
 
 vṛṣadhana dhanadapriya priyārdha 
 grathanavidagdha vidagdhacittayone | 
 purahara hariṇāṅkacūḍa cūḍā 
 bhujagabhayaṅkara dhūrjaṭe namas te  ||15|| 
 
 
 bhojadevasya | 
 
 
 4. mahādevaḥ 
 
 
 śilpaṃ trīṇi jaganti yasya kavitā yasya trivedī guror 
 yaś cakre tripuravyayaṃ tripathagā yanmūrdhni mālyāyate | 
 trīn kālān iva vīkṣituṃ vahati yo visphūrjadakṣṇāṃ trayaṃ  
 sa traiguṇyaparicchedo vijayate devas triśūlāyudhaḥ  ||16|| 
 
 
 vasukalpadattasya | (su.ra. 30) 
 
 
 arvāñcatpañcaśākhaḥ sphuraduparijaṭāmaṇḍalaḥ saṃśritānāṃ 
 nityāparṇo’pi tāpatritayam apanayan sthāṇur avyād apūrvaḥ | 
 yaḥ pronmīlatkapardaiḥ śirasi viracitābālabandhe dyusindhoḥ 
 pāthobhir labdhasekaḥ phalati phalaśataṃ vāñchitaṃ bhaktibhājām  ||17|| 
 
 
 jahnoḥ | 
 
 
 kāmaṃ mā kāmayadhvaṃ vṛṣam api ca bhṛśaṃ mādriyadhvaṃ na vitte 
 cittaṃ datta śrayadhvaṃ param amṛtaphalā yā kalā tām ihaikām | 
 itthaṃ devaḥ smarārir vṛṣam adharacarīkṛtya mūrtyaiva ditsan 
 niḥsvo viśvopadeśānamṛtakarakalāśekharas trāyatāṃ vaḥ  ||18|| 
 
 
 kavipaṇḍitaśrīharṣasya | 
 
 
 bhūtivyājena bhūmīm amarapurasaritkaitavād ambu bibhral 
 lālāṭākṣicchalena jvalanam ahipatiśvāsalakṣyaṃ samīram | 
 vistīrṇāghoravaktrodarakuharanibhenāmbaraṃ pañcabhūtair 
 viśvaṃ śaśvad vitanvan vitaratu bhavataḥ sampadaṃ candramauliḥ  ||19|| 
 
 
 jayadevasya | 
 
 
 pīyūṣeṇa viṣeṇa tulyam aśanaṃ svarge śmaśāne sthitir 
 nirbhedāḥ payaso’nalasya vahane yasyāviśeṣagrahaḥ | 
 aiśvaryeṇa ca bhikṣayā ca gamayan kālaṃ samaḥ sarvato 
 devaḥ svātmani kautukī haratu vaḥ saṃsārapāśaṃ haraḥ  ||20|| 
 
 
 vaidyagadādharasya | 
 5. śivaḥ 
 
 
 vedānteṣu yam āhur ekapuruṣaṃ vyāpya sthitaṃ rodasī 
 yasminn īśvara ity ananyaviṣayaḥ śabdo yathārthākṣaraḥ | 
 antaryaś ca mumukṣubhir niyamitaprāṇādibhir mṛgyate  
 sa sthāṇuḥ sthirabhaktiyogasulabho niḥśreyasāyāstu vaḥ  ||21|| 
 
 
 kālidāsasya | (Vik. 1.1) 
 
 
 kaṇṭhacchāyamiṣeṇa kalparajanīm uttaṃsamandākinī 
 rūpeṇa pralayābdhim ūrdhvanayanavyājena kalpājalam | 
 bhūṣāpannagakelipānakapaṭād ekonapañcāśataṃ 
 vātān apy upasaṃharann avatu vaḥ kalpāntaśāntau śivaḥ  ||22|| 
 
 
 cittapasya | 
 
 
 kvāpy agniḥ kvacid adribhūr naraśiraḥkīrṇā kvacin nimnagā 
 rūkṣā kvāpi jaṭā kvacid viṣadharā raudraṃ viṣaṃ kutracit | 
 tādṛg bhūtagaṇair vṛto mama citābhasmormikirmīritaḥ 
 saṃsāraṃ pratimucya yātur apunaryogāya panthāḥ śivaḥ  ||23|| 
 
 
 bilhaṇasya | 
 
 
 nirmātā jagadartham eva vacasāṃ vācaṃ yamo yaḥ svayaṃ 
 bhogān viśvakṛte tanoti viṣayavyāvartitātmendriyaḥ | 
 dhatte’strāṇi jaganti rakṣitum udāsīnaḥ svadehagrahe  
 yogīndro’stu sadāśivaḥ sa bhavatāṃ bhūtyai parārthavratī  ||24|| 
 
 
 vaidyagadādharasya | 
 
 
 dūronmuktakhageśvare murabhidi vyākṣiptabāhau graha 
 vyūhe vāritamātariśvani namaty āśāpatīnāṃ gaṇe | 
 niṣkamporagahāravallir acalaccūḍendur avyākula 
 svaḥsindhuḥ sthirayoganirvṛtamanāḥ pāyāt trilokīṃ śivaḥ  ||25|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 6. haraśṛṅgāraḥ 
 
 
 evaṃ sthāpaya subhru bāhulatikām evaṃ kuru sthānakaṃ 
 nātyuccair nama kuñcitāgracaraṇaṃ māṃ paśya tāvat kṣaṇam | 
 gaurīṃ nartayataḥ svavaktramurajenāmbhodharadhvāninā 
 śambhor vaḥ sukhayantu lambhitalayacchedāhatās tālikāḥ  ||26|| 
 
 
 yogeśvarasya | (su.ra. 60) 
 
 
 tasyā nāma mayā kathaṃ katham api bhrāntyā samuccāritaṃ 
 jānāsy eva mamāśayaṃ tava kṛte gauri prasannā bhava | 
 kṣāntiḥ svīkriyatāṃ dayāvati mayi krodhaḥ parityajyatā 
 mityevaṃ bahu jalpataḥ smararipoḥ premāñjaliḥ pātu vaḥ  ||27|| 
 
 
 cakrapāṇeḥ | 
 
 
 bālaḥ sundari candramāḥ srutasudhādhārābhirāpyāyito 
 nidrām eti phaṇīśvaraḥ suradhunī ruddhā jaṭāvallibhiḥ | 
 itthaṃ manmathakelikautukavidhau vrīḍāvatīṃ pārvatīṃ 
 pāyād vaḥ pratibodhayan navavadhūṃ candrārdhacūḍāmaṇiḥ  ||28|| 
 
 
 kakkolasya |  
 
 
 śrutiḥ saktā mugdhe vacasi vadanendau nipatitā 
 dṛśaḥ svādau bimbādharamadhuni magnaiva rasanā | 
 niṣaṇṇābhūn nāsā nijaparimale śailaduhitu 
 rghanāśleṣānande vapur api vilīnaṃ purabhidaḥ  ||29|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 dūre dāruvanābhisāraka mṛṣā cāṭūni muñcādhunā 
 bhūyas tvaṃ punar apy ahaṃ yadi tadā candraḥ kṣitiṃ yāsyati | 
 ity uktaḥ śaśimaulir adrisutayā cūḍendubhūlambhana 
 vyājavyañjitapādapadmapatanaprītapriyaḥ pātu vaḥ  ||30|| 
 
 
 kavipaṇḍitaśrīharṣasya | (sū.mu. 2.8) 
 
 
 7. śivayoḥ praśnottaram 
 
 
 kasmāt pārvati niṣṭhurāsi sahaja śailīdbhavānām idaṃ 
 niḥsnehāsi kuto na bhasmaparuṣaḥ snehaṃ kvacin nindati | 
 kopas te mayi niṣphalaḥ priyatame sthāṇau phalaṃ kiṃ bhaved 
 itthaṃ nirvacanīkṛto dayitayā śambhuḥ śivāyās tu vaḥ  ||31|| 
 
 
 bhojadevasya | (su.ra. 35) 
 
 
 kiṃ gauri māṃ prati ruṣā nanu gauḥ kim asmi 
 kupyāmi kaṃ prati mayīty anumānato’ham | 
 jānāmi satyam aunāmanata eva sa tvam 
 itthaṃ giro giribhuvaḥ kuṭilā jayanti  ||32|| 
 
 
 rudraṭasya | (Kāvyālaṅkāra 2.15, sū.mu. 99.6) 
 
 
 keyaṃ mūrdhny andhakāre timiram iha kutaḥ subhru kāntenduyukte 
 kāntāpy atraiva kāmin nanu jalam umayā pṛṣṭam etāvad eva | 
 nāhaṃ dvandvaṃ karomi vyapanaya śirasas tūrṇam enām idānīm 
 evaṃ proktaṃ bhavān yā prativacanajaḍaḥ pātu vo manmathāriḥ  ||33|| 
 
 
 kasyacit || 
 
 
 eṣā te hara kā sugātri katamā mūrdhni sthitā kiṃ jaṭā 
 haṃsaḥ kiṃ bhajate jaṭāṃ na hi śaśī candro jalaṃ sevate | 
 mugdhe bhūtir iyaṃ kuto’tra salilaṃ bhūtis taraṅgāyate 
 itthaṃ yo vinigūhate tripathagāṃ pāyān sa vaḥ śṛṅgāraḥ  ||34|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (Sv 67) 
 
 
 dhanyā keyaṃ sthitā te śirasi śaśikalā kiṃ nu nāmaitad asyā 
 nāmaivāsyās tad etat paricitam api te vismṛtaṃ kasya hetoḥ | 
 nārīṃ pṛcchāmi nenduṃ kathayatu vijayā na pramāṇaṃ yadīndur 
 devyā nihnotum icchor iti surasaritaṃ śāṭhyam avyād vibhor vaḥ  ||35|| 
 
 
 viśākhadattasya | (Mudrārākṣas 1.1, sū.mu. 99.1) 
 
 
 8. harahāsyam 
 
 
 pāṇau kaṅkaṇam utphaṇaḥ phaṇipatir netraṃ jvalatpāvakaṃ 
 kaṇṭhaḥ kuṇṭhitakālakūṭakuṭilo vastraṃ gajendrājinam | 
 gaurīlocanalobhanāya subhago veṣo varasyeti me 
 gaṇḍollāsavibhāvitaḥ paśupater hāsodgamaḥ pātu vaḥ  ||36|| 
 
 
 rudraṭasya | (śṛ.ti. 3.2a) 
 
 
 uddāmadantarucipallavitārdhacandra 
 jyotsnānipītatimiraprakarāvarodhaḥ | 
 śreyāṃsi vo diśatu tāṇḍavitasya śambhor 
 ambhodharāvalighanadhvanir aṭṭahāsaḥ  ||37|| 
 
 
 saṅghamitrasya | (su.ra. 41) 
 
 
 mātar brūhi kim etad añjalipuṭe tātena gopāyitaṃ 
 vatsa svāduphalaṃ prayacchati na me gatvā gṛhāṇa svayam | 
 mātraivaṃ prahite guhe vighaṭayaty ākṛṣya sandhyāñjaliṃ 
 śambhor bhagnasamādhiruddhamanaso hāsyodgamaḥ pātu vaḥ  ||38|| 
 
 
 yogeśvarasya | (su.ra. 59) 
 
 
 nirvighnaṃ ghanasārasāraviśadasvarlokakallolinī 
 kallolapratimallabāhucalanair vyāptāntarālaśriyaḥ | 
 śambhoḥ sambhavadaṅgahārataralottaṃsāmṛtāṃśudrava 
 prāṇāt prāṇikapālacāpaladṛśo hāsormayaḥ pāntu vaḥ  ||39|| 
 
 
 vācaspateḥ || 
 
 
 bhṛṅgī kas tava carcike guha na ko’py ākāra ekas tu nau 
 satyaṃ bhṛṅgariṭe susatyam anṛtaṃ lokaṃ tu moṭir vadet | 
 nagnaṃ pṛcchatam astu vāṃ pariṇayaikātmatvam ity udbhaṭa 
 stāv utsṛjya saparṣadaḥ paśupater hāsyodgamaḥ pātu vaḥ  ||40|| 
 9. haraśiraḥ 
 
 
 tvaṅgadgaṅgam udañcadinduśakalaṃ bhraśyatkapālāvali 
 kroḍabhrāmyadamandamārutacayasphārībhavadbhāṅkṛti | 
 pāyād vo ghanatāṇḍavavyatikaraprāgbhārakhedaskhala 
 dbhogīndraślathapiṅgalotkaṭajaṭājūṭaṃ śiro dhūrjaṭeḥ  ||41|| 
 
 
 vīryamitrasya | (su.ra. 42) 
 
 
 sandhyātāṇḍavitasya khaṇḍaparaśor avyāj jaganti jvalal 
 lālāṭākṣipuṭodbhavānalaśikhālīḍhendulekhaṃ śiraḥ | 
 bhraśyatkṛtti calanmahāhivigaladvyomāpagāmbuskhalat 
 khaṇḍendūcchalabhūticaṭulabhrāmyajjaṭāsantati  ||42|| 
 
 
 yogeśvarasya | 
 
 
  dhūmodbhedānabhijñasphuradana,am anāghrātapaṅkādhikāra 
 preṅkhatkallolavārivyatikaram anaghasparśajāgratkapālam | 
 ajñātāstatriyāmādayitam aviditaprāṇihiṃsoragasrag 
 bhūteśasya prabhūtādbhutam avatu śiraḥ śreyasāṃ santatiṃ vaḥ  ||43|| 
 
 
 vaidyagadādharasya | 
 
 
 nāṭyāvegaviniḥsṛtatripathagāvāripravāhākulaḥ 
 śīghrabhrāntivaśāl lalāṭanayanajvālātaḍidbhīṣaṇaḥ | 
 muṇḍālīkuharaprasarpadanilāsphālaprayuktadhvaniḥ 
 prāvṛṭkāla ivoditaḥ śivaśiromeghaḥ śivāyās tu vaḥ  ||44|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 antaḥsvīkṛtajāhnavījalam atisvacchandaratnāṅkura 
 śreṇīśoṇabhujaṅganāyakaphaṇācakrīl lasatpallavam | 
 bhūyād abhuyadāya mokṣanagaraprasthānabhājam itaḥ 
 pratyūhapraśamaikapūrṇakalaśaprāyaṃ śiro dhūrjaṭeḥ  ||45|| 
 
 
 jalacandrasya | 
 10. haraśirogaṅgā  
 
 
 kapāle gambhīraḥ kuhariṇi jaṭāsandhiṣu kṛśaḥ 
 samuttānaś cūḍābhujagamaṇibandhavyatikare | 
 mṛdur lekhākoṇe rayavaśavilolasya śaśinaḥ  
 punītād dīrghaṃ vo haraśirasi gaṅgākalakalaḥ  ||46|| 
 
 
 yogeśvarasya | (su.ra. 53) 
 
 
 sa jayati gāṅgajalaughaḥ śambhor uttuṅgamauliviniviṣṭaḥ | 
 majjati punar unmajjati candrakalā yatra śapharīva  ||47|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 45) 
 
 
 yaccandrakoṭikarakorakabhāvabhāji  
 babhrāma babhruṇi jaṭāpaṭale harasya | 
 tad vaḥ punātu himaśailaśilānikuñja 
 sātkāraḍambaravirāvi surāpagāmbhaḥ  ||48|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (sa.ka.ā. 1.77) 
 
 
 gaurīvibhajyamānārdhasaṅkīrṇe haramūrdhani | 
 amba dviguṇagambhīre bhāgīrathi namo’stu te  ||49|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 78, sū.mu. 1.24) 
 
 
 muktābhā nṛkapālaśuktiṣu jaṭāvallīṣu mallīnibhā 
 bahvau lājanibhā dṛśor maṇinibhā bhogotkare bhoginaḥ | 
 nṛtyāvartaparampareritapayaḥ mūrcchanocchālitāḥ 
 khelanto haramūrdhni pāntu bhavato gaṅgāpayobindavaḥ  ||50|| 
 
 
 naḍagāṅgokasya || śā.pa. 106, sū.mu. 2.53) 
 11. haraśiraścandraḥ 
 
 
 sa vaḥ pāyād indur navavisalatākoṭikuṭilaḥ 
 smarārer yo mūrdhni jvalanakapiśe bhāti nihitaḥ | 
 sravanmandākinyāḥ pratidivasasiktena payasā  
 kapālenonmuktaḥ sphaṭikadhavalenāṅkura iva  ||51|| 
 
 
 rājaśekharasya | (su.ra. 46) 
 
 
 vyalīke pārvatyāḥ parilaghulavair añjanajuṣaḥ  
 patadbhir bāṣpasya kramalikhitalakṣmyā vijayate | 
 lasallīlācandraś caraṇagatamauleḥ smarajitaḥ 
 kiradbhiḥ svajyotsnānakhamaṇibhir āpūritakaṇaḥ  ||52|| 
 
 
 vāmanasya | 
 
 
 śambhor indukalā śivaṃ viśatu vo yasyāḥ praticchāyikāṃ 
 trisrotaḥpatitām anekakuṭilībhāvaṃ gatāṃ vīcibhiḥ | 
 senānīr avalokate dhvajapaṭākūtena kātyāyanī  
 mallīdāmasmīhayā nijavadhūbodhena nāgādhipaḥ  ||53|| 
 
 
 umāpateḥ | 
 
 
 amudrakumudatviṣaḥ sphuritaphenalakṣīspṛśo 
 marālakulavibhramāḥ śapharaphālalīlābhṛtaḥ | 
 jayanti girijāpates taralamaulimandākinī 
 taraṅgacayacumbinas tuhinadīdhiter aṃśavaḥ  ||54|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya |  
 
 
 cyutām indor lekhāṃ ratikalahabhagnaṃ ca valayaṃ 
 dvayaṃ cakrīkṛtya prahasitamukhī śailatanayā | 
 avocad yaṃ paśyedty avatu sa śivaḥ sā ca girijā 
 sa ca krīḍācandro daśanakiraṇāpūritakalaḥ  ||55|| 
 
 
 vararuceḥ | (su.ra. 47, Sv 66, śā.pa. 96) 
 
 
 12. harajaṭā 
 
 
 jvālevordhvavisarpiṇī pariṇatasyāntas tapas tejaso 
 gaṅgātoyataraṅgasarpavasatir valmīkalakṣmīr iva | 
 sandyevārdramṛṇālakomalatanor indoḥ sahasthāyinī 
 pāyād vas taruṇāṃśukapilā śambhor jaṭāsaṃhatiḥ  ||56|| 
 
 
 ravināgasya | (su.ra. 55) 
 
 
 cūḍāpīḍanibaddhavāsukiphaṇāphūtkāraniryadviṣa 
 jvālājṛmbhitamatsyakaccapavadhūlīḍhendulekhāmṛtam | 
 avyād vaḥ smarasūdanasya madanakrīḍākacākarṣaṇaś 
 cyotannākasaritsaroṣagirijādṛṣṭaṃ jaṭāmaṇḍalam  ||57|| 
 
 
 bhavabhūteḥ | 
 
 
 kvacid amarasarit kvacit kapālaṃ 
 kvacid uragāḥ kvacid aindavī ca lekhā | 
 iti viṣamavibhūṣaṇair upetā  
 pramathapater avatāj jaṭāṭavī  ||58|| 
 
 
 daṇḍinaḥ | 
 
 
 utpatreva dṛśorciṣā kusumitevendoḥ karair bhogibhiḥ  
 sāroheva jaṭāṭavī phalatu vaḥ śreyo bhavānīpateḥ | 
 yatparyantavivartinaḥ surasaritpūrasya bhūrisphurat 
 pheneṇḍūkavilāsam añcati vidher jīrṇā kapālāvalī  ||59|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 mūlāvanaddhabhujagendrakṛtālavāla 
 bandhāḥ skhalattridaśasindhujalaughasiktāḥ | 
 unmuktacandrakusumā jagatāṃ hitāya 
 śambhor jaṭāḥ kanakakalpalatāḥ phalantu  ||60|| 
 
 
 daṅkasya | 
 
 
 13. harakapālaḥ 
 
 
 śāntyai vo’stu kapāladāma jagatāṃ patur yadīyāṃ lipiṃ 
 kvāpi kvāpi gaṇāḥ paṭhanti padaśo nātiprasiddhākṣaram | 
 viśvaṃ srakṣyati vakṣyati kṣitim apām īśiṣyate śiṣyate 
 nāgān rāgiṣu raṃsyate syati jagan nirvekṣyati dyām iti  ||61|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 54) 
 
 
 gāḍhagranthipraphulladgalavikalaphaṇāpīṭhaniryadviṣāgni 
 jvālāniṣṭaptacandradravadamṛtarasaproṣitapretabhāvāḥ | 
 ujjṛmbhā babhrunetradyuitm asakṛdasṛktṛṣṇayālokayantyaḥ 
 pāntu tvāṃ nāganālagrathitaśavaśiraḥśreṇayo bhairavasya  ||62|| 
 
 
 bhavabhūteḥ | (su.ra. 39) 
 
 
 jayati bhujagarajjugranthiniṣpīḍitendu 
 sravadamṛtanivṛttapretabhāvaiḥ kapālaiḥ | 
 viracitanutibandho mūrdhni sadyaḥ purāreḥ 
 pariṇatabahukalpabrahmaṇāṃ brahmaghoṣaḥ  ||63|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (sa.ka.ā. 1.84) 
 
 
 liptā lālāṭanetrasphuradurudahanajvālajālapratāpot 
 tāmyatkoṭīr abhārasthiraśaśiśakalaprasrutābhiḥ sudhābhiḥ | 
 antarnṛtyapramodapracalitaśiraś candramauleḥ kapālāḥ 
 kalyāṇaṃ vaḥ kriyāsuḥ stutim abhidhatas tāṇḍavāḍambareṣu  ||64|| 
 
 
 narasiṃhasya | 
 
 
 pāyād vaḥ sa śirāṃsi tāṇḍavavidhau yan mūrdhni khinnoraga 
 śvāsāgnidrutacūḍacandrasudhayā prāṇanty akasmād vidheḥ | 
 ṛksāme katicit paṭhanti katicin majjanti gaṅgājale 
 svātmānaṃ katicin mananti katicin netrānale juhvati  ||65|| 
 
 
 vāmadevasya | 
 
 
 14. haranayanam 
 
 
 dhūmaśyāmakakumbhi bhūdharataṭatruydyaddṛṣanti sphuṭā 
 ṭopolluṇṭhitasāgarāmpi vikalavyālokabhāsvanti ca | 
 dṛpyattūrṇamarunti kātaratarabhraśyajjaganti prabhor 
 udyanti tripurāntakṛnti nayanād arcīṃṣi puṣyantu vaḥ  ||66|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 yajjyotir dvādaśārkaṃ himagiriduhitur yan niśākelidīpo 
 yat kandarpāsthibhasmīkaraṇataruṇitābhyantarajvālalekham | 
 kalpānte juhvato yat tribhuvanasamidhaṃ vedhasaḥ puṇyavahnir 
 bibhrāṇaṃ babhrukāntiṃ trinayananayanajyotir astu śriye vaḥ  ||67|| 
 
 
 aṃśudharasya | 
 
 
 ānandastimitāḥ samādhiṣu mukhe gaur yā vilāsālasāḥ 
 sambhrāntāḥ kṣaṇam adbhutāḥ kṣaṇam atha smerā nije vaikṛte | 
 krūrāḥ kṛṣṭaśarāsane manasije dagdhe ghṛṇākūṇitās 
 tatkāntāruditeśrupūrataralāḥ śambhor dṛśaḥ pāntu vaḥ  ||68|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 pakṣmālīpiṅgalimnaḥ kaṇa iva taḍitāṃ yasya kṛtsnaḥ samūho 
 yasmin brahmāṇḍamīṣadvighaṭitamukule kālayajvā juhāva | 
 arcir niṣṭaptacūḍāśaśigalitasudhāghorajhāṅkārikoṇaṃ 
 tārtīyokaṃ purārer tad avatu madanaplīṣaṇaṃ locanaṃ vaḥ  ||69|| 
 
 
 bhavabhūteḥ | (Mm 1, after 5.2; śā.pa. 99) 
 
 
 ekaṃ yoganiyojanān mukulitaṃ cakṣur dvitīyaṃ punaḥ 
 pārvatyā jaghanasthale stanataṭe śṛṅgārabhāvālasam | 
 anyad dūravikṛṣṭacāpamadanakrodhānaloddīpitaṃ 
 śambhor bhinnarasaṃ samādhisamaye netratrayaṃ pātu vaḥ  ||70|| 
 
 
 śrīharṣadevasya | 
 15. tripuradāhārambhaḥ 
 
 
 saṃrabdhāṅghriniveśanād anibhṛtaṃ sarvaṃsahāvigrahe 
 vītālambanam ārasātalam adhovistraṃsini syandane | 
 yāte dṛkpathadūratāṃ mayapure devasya bhūtaprabhor 
 drāgviśvambharabāṇamokṣaviṣayo yatnaḥ śivāyāstu vaḥ  ||71|| 
 
 
 vaidyagadādharasya | 
 
 
 cāpotkṣepāpasarpadvalayaphaṇiguṇottaṃsitāpāṅgabhitti 
 pratyālīḍhānubandhocchalitajalanidhivyāptavelopakaṇṭham | 
 unmīladbhālavahni kramaśithilajaṭālambigaṅgendulekhaṃ 
 bhūyād vaś candramauler mayanagarabhidaḥ sauṣṭhavaṃ maṅgalāya  ||72|| 
 
 
 jalacandrasya | 
 
 
 saṅvyānāṃśukapallaveṣu taralaṃ veṇīguṇeṣu sthitaṃ 
 mandaṃ kañcukasandhiṣu stanataṭotsaṅgeṣu dīptārciṣam | 
 ālokya tripurāvarodhanavadhūvargasya dhūmadhvajaṃ 
 hastasrastaśarāsano vijayate devo dayārdrekṣaṇaḥ  ||73|| 
 
 
 mayūrasya | (su.ra. 61) 
 
 
 vāṇībhūtapurāṇapūruṣadhṛtipratyāśayā dhāvite 
 nidrātīkṣaṇajāśuśukṣaṇikaṇaklānte śakunteśvare | 
 namronnamrabhujaṅgapuṅgavaguṇavyākṛṣṭabāṇāsana 
 kṣiptāstrasya puradruho vijayate sandhānasīmāśramaḥ  ||74|| 
 
 
 murāreḥ | (Ar 7.114, su.ra. 31) 
 
 
 dṛṣṭaḥ saprema devyā kim idam iti bhayāt sambhramāc cāsurībhiḥ 
 śāntāntastattvasāraiḥ sakaruṇam ṛṣibhir viṣṇunā sasmitena | 
 ākṛṣyāstraṃ sagarvair upaśamitabandhusaṃbhramair daityavīraiḥ 
 sānandaṃ devatābhir mayapuradahane dhūrjaṭiḥ pātu yuṣmān  ||75|| 
 
 
 bhaṭṭanārāyaṇasya | (Vs 1.3) 
 16. harabāṇaḥ 
 
 
 kṣipto hastāvalagnaḥ prasabham abhihato’py ādadāno’ṃśukāntaṃ 
 gṛhṇan keśeṣv apāstaś caraṇanipatito nekṣitaḥ sambhrameṇa | 
 āliṅgan yo’vadhūtas tripurayuvatibhiḥ sāśrunetrotpalābhiḥ 
 kāmīvārdrāparādhaḥ sa dahatu duritaṃ śāmbhavo vaḥ śarāgniḥ  ||76|| 
 
 
 
 amaroḥ | (amaru 2; su.ra. 49) 
 
 
 sindūraśrīr lalāṭe kanakarasamayaḥ karṇapāśāvataṃso 
 vaktre tāmbūlarāgaḥ pṛthukucakalase kuṅkumasyānulepaḥ | 
 daityādhīśāṅganānāṃ jaghanaparisare lākṣikakṣaumalakṣmī 
 raśreyāṃsi kṣiṇotu tripuraharaśarodgārajanmānalo vaḥ  ||77|| 
 
 
 maṅgalasya | (su.ra. 67) 
 
 
 viṣvag vyādhūya dhūmapracayayavanikāṃ sphāyamānasphuliṅga 
 vyājād avakīrya puṣpāñjalim upari padaṃ nyasyato mandirāṇām | 
 svacchandābhogasīmā mahati mayapure dattaraudrāṅgarāga 
 vyāptāśeṣasya viśveśvaraśaraśikhinas tāṇḍavaṃ naḥ punātu  ||78|| 
 
 
 vaidyagadādharasya | 
 
 
 bāṣpair vītāṅgarāgacchaviṣu viracayann acchadhūmacchaṭābhiḥ  
 kastūrīpatramāyāṃ mayanagaravadhūvargavakṣoruheṣu | 
 āsāmlānapuṣpastavakanavakalām aṃśubhiḥ kuntaleṣu  
 vyākurvann andhakāraṃ haratu haraśarodgārajanmānalo vaḥ  ||79|| 
 
 
 jalacandrasya | 
 
 
 cāpaṃ muṣṭir bhavānyāḥ sarasijamukulaśrīḥ kathaṃ vā vidhatte 
 pratyālīḍhaṃ kathaṃ vā racayatu maṇiman nūpuro vāmapādaḥ | 
 itthaṃ yāvad vitarkaṃ vidadhati vibudhās tāvad agre ya āsīd 
 vāṇāgniḥ pluṣṭadaityo mayapuramathane dhūrjaṭeḥ so’vatād naḥ  ||80|| 
 17. aṣṭamūrtiḥ 
 
 
 payodānāṃ panthāḥ kavalaviṣayo vā parimalaṃ 
 vahan bibhrāṇo vā suhṛdapasuhṛd vā jalaruhām | 
 dadad gṛhṇāno vā havir iti muhur yasya vibudhāḥ  
 stuvanty aṣṭau mūrtīḥ sa jagad avatād andhakaripuḥ  ||81|| 
 
 
 śrīhanūmataḥ | 
 
 
 dikkālātmasamaiva yasya vibhutā yas tatra vidyotate 
 yatrāmuṣya sudhībhavanti kiraṇā rāśeḥ sa yāsām abhūt | 
 yas tatpittam uṣaḥsu yo’sya vidhaye yas tasya jīvātave 
 voḍhā yad gaṇam eṣa manmatharipos tāḥ pāntu vo mūrtayaḥ  ||82|| 
 
 
 cittapasya | (Kuval. 1056) 
 
 
 mauliṃ nenokti bhālaṃ tilakayati tanor aṅgarāgaṃ vidhatte 
 dhammillaṃ sandadhāti prathayati śirasi vyaktam uttaṃsalakṣmīm | 
 samprīṇīte bhujaṅgān apanayati rasaṃ vetti saṃmodamudrāṃ 
 yābhiḥ śṛṅgārabandhas tanubhir iva śivas tābhir astu śriye vaḥ  ||83|| 
 
 
 jalacandrasya | 
 
 
 yāṃ dhammillapade’bhiṣiñcati yayā sandhyāsu baddhāñjalir 
 yām āyamya yadātmakāni nayanāny āmīlya yāṃ dhyāyati | 
 yāṃ ca syandanatāṃ nināya sahitas tābhiḥ svayaṃ mūrtibhir 
 devo viśvatanuḥ punātu sa jagaccandrārdhacūḍāmaṇiḥ  ||84|| 
 
 
 sudhākarasya | 
 
 
 yā sṛṣṭiḥ sraṣṭur ādyā vahati vidhihutaṃ yā havir yā ca hotrī 
 ye dve kālaṃ vidhattaḥ śrutiviṣyaguṇā yā sthitā vyāpya viśvam | 
 yām āhuḥ sarvabījaprakṛtir iti yayā prāṇinaḥ prāṇavantaḥ 
 pratyakṣābhiḥ prapannas tanubhir avatu vas tābhir aṣṭābhir īśaḥ  ||85|| 
 
 
 kālidāsasya | (Çak 1.1) 
 18. bhairavaḥ 
 
 
 khaṭvāṅgīkṛtadhūmaketudhaṭitapretādhirāṭpañjara 
 protabrahmaśiraḥ kapālavalayaṃ bibhrajjaṭāmaṇḍalam | 
 kaṇṭhe saptamaharṣivaktraracitām ekāvalīm udvahan 
 pāyād vaḥ sulabhavratopakaraṇaḥ kalpāntakāpālikaḥ  ||86|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 sadyaḥ pradhvastadevāsurasarasaśiraḥśreṇiśoṇāravinda 
 sragdāmānaddhamūrter ghanarudhirakaṇaklinnacarmāṃśukasya | 
 niṣparyāyatrilokībhavakavalarasavyāttavaktrasya jīyād 
 ānandaḥ kālarātrīkucakalasaparīrambhiṇo bhairavasya  ||87|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 vaikuṇṭhasya karaṅkam aṅkanihitaṃ sraṣṭuḥ kapālaṃ kare 
 pratyaṅgaṃ ca vibhūṣaṇaṃ viracitaṃ nākaukasāṃ kīkasaiḥ | 
 bhasma sthāvarajaṅgamasya jagataḥ śubhraṃ tanau bibhrataḥ  
 kalpānteṣu kapālino vijayate raudraṃ kapālavratam  ||88|| 
 
 
 bhavabhūteḥ | 
 
 
 ekāmbhodhīkṛtāyāṃ bhuvi jagad akhilaṃ nirjanīkṛtya khelan  
 devaḥ kālīsahāyaḥ prasabhaviharaṇonmuktalīlāṭṭahāsaḥ | 
 sadyo daṃṣṭrāṃśubhinne tamasi nijavapurbimbam ālokya kas tvaṃ 
 kas tvaṃ brūhīti kopād abhidadhad abhayaṃ bhairavaś ceṣṭatāṃ vaḥ  ||89|| 
 
 
 vaidyagadādharasya | 
 
 
 kalpānte śayitatrivikramamahākaṅkāladantī sphurac 
 cheṣasyūtanṛsiṃhapāṇinakharaprotādikolāmiṣaḥ | 
 viśvaikārṇavatānitāntam uditau tau matsyakūrmāv ubhau 
 karṣan dhīvaratāṃ gato’sya tu mahāmohaṃ mahābhairavaḥ  ||90|| 
 
 
 cittapasya | (sū.mu. 2.24) 
 19. haranṛtyārambhaḥ  
 
 
 ārdrāṃ kaṇṭhe mukhābjasrajam avanamayaty ambikā jānulambāṃ 
 sthāne kṭvendulekhāṃ niviḍayati jaṭāpannagendreṇa nandī | 
 kālaḥ kṛttiṃ nibadhnāty upanayati kare kālarātriḥ kapālaṃ 
 śambhor nṛtyāvatāre pariṣad iti pṛthag vyāpṛtā vaḥ punātu  ||91|| 
 
 
 śatānandasya | (su.ra. 76, sū.mu. 2.29) 
 
 
 nandin khañjanamañjunādam urajaṃ saṃgṛhya sajjībhava 
 kuṣmāṇḍānaya bhasmabhājanam ito lambodarāgamyatām | 
 skandaṃ nandaya mandirodaragataṃ devīti raṅgāṅgaṇe 
 śambhos tāṇḍavamaṇḍanairkamanasaḥ saṃjalpitaṃ pātu vaḥ  ||92|| 
 
 
 yogeśvarasya | 
 
 
 bho bho dikpatayaḥ prayāta parataḥ khaṃ muñcatāmbhomucaḥ 
 pātālaṃ vraja medini praviśata kṣoṇītalaṃ kṣmābhṛtaḥ | 
 brahmann unnaya dūram ātmasadanaṃ devasya no nṛtyataḥ  
 śambhoḥ saṃkaṭam etad ity avatu vaḥ protsāraṇā nandinaḥ  ||93|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (su.ra. 74, sū.mu. 2.30) 
 
 
 asthīny asthīny ajinam ajinaṃ bhasma bhasmendur indur 
 gaṅgā gaṅgoraga uraga ity ākulāḥ sambhrameṇa | 
 bhūṣād ānopakaraṇagaṇaprāpaṇavyāpṛtānāṃ 
 nṛtyārambhapraṇayini śive pāntu vāco gaṇānām  ||94|| 
 
 
 dhanapālasya | (sa.ka.ā. 2.235, sū.mu. 2.27) 
 
 
 kṣoṇi kṣobhaṃ kṣamasva tvam api kuru mahākūrma karma svakīyaṃ 
 bho bhoḥ kailāsameruprabhṛtikuladharādhāriṇo gacchatādhaḥ | 
 brahmann udgaccha dūraṃ kuruta jaladhayaḥ sthairyam ity aṣṭamūrter 
 bhartur nṛtyāvatāre sarabhasagaditāḥ pāntu vo nandivācaḥ  ||95|| 
 
 
 dvaipāyanasya | 
 
 
 20. haranṛtyam  
 
 
 bhrāmyadviśvaṃbharāṇi bhramicalananamatkūrmakumbhīnasāni 
 truṣṭyattārāṇi riṅgaddhariṇadharaśiraḥśreṇīśīryaddṛṣanti | 
 dikkīreodañcad ampi dravadamaracamūcakracañcadviyanti  
 vyasyantu vyāpadaṃ vas tripuravijayinas tāṇḍavārambhaṇāni  ||96|| 
 
 
 rājaśekharasya | 
 
 
 helāpādrapratāpān namadavanibharākrāntakūrmeśaśeṣa 
 prodbhūtaśvāsavātocchaladudadhipayodhautasūryendutāram | 
 bhrāmyaddoḥsaṅghavegāpatadacalakuladhvānasaṃtrastaviśvaṃ 
 trailokyaiśvaryakāri dyatu tava duritaṃ tāṇḍavaṃ candramauleḥ  ||97|| 
 
 
 vācchokasya | 
 
 
 uttānāḥ kati vellitāḥ kati rayād ābhugnamadhyāḥ kati  
 kṣiptotkṣiptavikuñcitāḥ kati bhujās tauryatrikānukramāt | 
 kalpānteṣu mahānaṭasya jhaṭiti prakrāntacakrabhrami  
 bhrāntau kevalam agnihāsagaralair lekhātrayaṃ pātu vaḥ  ||98|| 
 
 
 sāgaradharasya | 
 
 
 pāyād vaḥ suradīrghikājalarayabhrāmyajjaṭāmaṇḍalī 
 vegavyākulanāganāyakaphaṇāphūtkāravātocchalam | 
 saptāmbhonidhijanmacaṇḍalaharīmajjannabhomaṇḍala 
 grāsatrastasurāṅganākalakalakrīḍāvilakṣo haraḥ  ||99|| 
 
 
 brahmahareḥ | (su.ra. 68, karkarājasya) 
 
 
 sandhyātāṇḍavaḍambaravyasanino bhīmasya caṇḍabhrami 
 vyānṛtyadbhujadaṇḍamaṇḍalabhuvo jhañjhānilāḥ pāntu vaḥ | 
 yeṣām ucchalatāṃ javena jhagiti vyūheṣu bhūmībhṛtām 
 uḍḍīneṣu viḍaujasā punar asau dambholir ālokitaḥ  ||100|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 50, sū.mu. 2.31) 
 
 
 21. haraprasādanam 
 
 
 niḥśaṅkaṃ śaṅkara karagrathitāhibhoga 
 bhogaprada pradalitāmaravairivṛnda | 
 vṛndārakārcita citābhasitāṅgarāga 
 rāgātidūra duritāpahara prasīda  ||101|| 
 
 
 bāṇasya | 
 
 
 karakalitapināka nākanātha 
 dviṣadurumānasaśūla śūlapāṇe | 
 bhava vṛṣabhavimāna mānaśauṇḍa 
 trijagadakāraṇatāraka prasīda  ||102|| 
 
 
 sañcādharasya | 
 
 
 kaṭuviśikhaśikhiprapañca pañcā 
 nana dhanadapriyamitra mitranetra | 
 dhṛtasakalavikalpa kalpaśeṣa 
 prakaṭamahānaṭa nāṭaya prasādam  ||103|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 bhava śiva śavabhasmagaura gaurī 
 grathitaśarīra sarīsṛpottarīya | 
 smarahara hara bhīma bhīmabhūta 
 prakarabhayaṅkara śaṅkara prasīda  ||104|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 dhṛtanidhanadhanuḥ pracaṇḍa caṇḍī 
 mukhakamalabhramarāmarādhinātha | 
 hara raṇaraṇakānta kāntamūrte 
 gaganadukūla vikūlayāpadaṃ naḥ  ||105|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 22. gaurī 
 
 
 yān uddhūlayatīśvaraḥ sikatilā yair maulimandākinī 
 yair bālendukaṇārdraketakadalotsaṅge parāgāyitam | 
 yaiḥ kailāsavilāsakānanataṭīkaṅkellipuṣpodgama 
 krīḍākārmaṇam adrijācaraṇayos te reṇavaḥ pāntu vaḥ  ||106|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 lākṣārāgaṃ harati śikharāj jāhnavīvāri yeṣāṃ 
 ye tatvanti srajam adhijaṭāmaṇḍalaṃ mālatīnām | 
 pratyutsarpadvimalakiraṇair yais tirodhānam indor 
 devyāḥ sthāṇau caraṇapatite te nakhāḥ pāntu viśvam  ||107|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 81, dakṣasya) 
 
 
 bhavajaladhijalāvalambayaṣṭir  
 mahiṣamahāsuraśailavajradhārā | 
 harahṛdayataḍāgarājahaṃsī  
 diśatu śivaṃ bhavataś ciram  ||108|| 
 
 
 bhagīrathadattasya | (su.ra. 86) 
 
 
 kāṃ tapasvī gato’vasthām iti smerāv iva stanau | 
 vande gaurīghanāśleṣabhavabhūtisitānanau  ||109|| 
 
 
 bhavabhūteḥ | 
 
 
 abhimataphalasiddhisiddhamantrā 
 vali balijitparameṣṭinor upāsye | 
 bhagavati madanārināri vande 
 nikhilanagādhipabhartṛdārike tvām  ||110|| 
 
 
 vāmadevasya | 
 
 
 23. vivāhasamayagaurī 
 
 
 gonāsāya viyojitāgadarajāḥ sarpāya baddhauṣadhiḥ 
 kaṇṭhasthāya viṣāya vīryamahataḥ pāṇau maṇīn bibhratī | 
 bhartur bhūtagaṇāya gotrajaratīnirdiṣṭamantrākṣarā 
 rakṣatv adrisutā vivāhasamaye prītā ca bhītā ca vaḥ  ||111|| 
 
 
 rājaśekharasya | (vi.śā.bha. 1.3, su.ra. 102, sū.mu. 2.36) 
 
 
 pratyāsannavivāhamaṅgalavidhau devārcanavyastayā 
 dṛṣṭvāgre pariṇetur eva likhitāṃ gaṅgādharasyākṛtim | 
 unmādasmitaroṣalajjitarasair gauryā kathaṃcic cirād 
 vṛddhastrīvacanāt priye vinihitaḥ puṣpāñjaliḥ pātu vaḥ  ||112|| 
 
 
 bhāsasya | (su.ra. 88, śā.pa. 102, sū.mu. 2.37) 
 
 
 brahmāyaṃ viṣṇur eṣa tridaśapatir asau lokapālās tathaite 
 jāmātā ko’tra yo’sau bhujagaparivṛto bhasmarūkṣaḥ kapālī | 
 hā vatse vañcitāsīty anabhimatavaraprārthanāvrīḍitābhir 
 devībhiḥ śocyamānāpy upacitapulakā śreyase vo’stu gaurī  ||113|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 dhūmavyākuladṛṣṭir indukiraṇair āhlāditākṣī punaḥ 
 paśyantī varam utsukā natamukhī bhūyo hriyā brahmaṇaḥ | 
 serṣyā pādanakhācchadarpaṇagatāṃ gaṅgāṃ dadhāne hare 
 sparśād utpulakā karagrahavidhau gaurī śivāyāstu vaḥ  ||114|| 
 
 
 śrīharṣadevasya | (Priyadarśikā 1.1) 
 
 
 pādāgre sthitayā muhuḥ stanabhareṇānītayā namratāṃ 
 śambhoḥ sasprṛhalocanatrayapathaṃ yāntyā tadārādhane | 
 hrīmatyā śirasīhitaḥ sapulakasvedodgamotkampayā  
 viśliṣyan kusumāñjalir girijayā kṣipto’ntare pātu vaḥ  ||115|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (Ratnāvali 1, sū.mu. 2.38) 
 
 
 24. gaurīśṛṅgāraḥ 
 
 
 svedas te katham īdṛśaḥ priyatame tvannetravahner vibho 
 kasmāt kampitam etad induvadane bhogīndrabhīter bhava | 
 romāñcaḥ katham eṣa devi bhagavan gaṅgāmbhasāṃ śīkara 
 itthaṃ bhartari bhāvagopanaparā gaurī ciraṃ pātu vaḥ  ||116|| 
 
 
 
 lakṣmīdharasya | (su.ra. 75, śā.pa. 104) 
 
 
 śambho satyam idaṃ payodhimathane lakṣmyā vṛte keśave 
 vailakṣyāt kila kākakūṭam aśitaṃ pītaṃ viṣaṃ yat tvayā | 
 satyaṃ pārvati nāsti naḥ subhagatā sākṣī tathā ca smaro 
 deveneti kṛtasmṛtiḥ smitamukhī gaurī ciraṃ pātu vaḥ  ||117|| 
 
 
 śrīharṣadevasya | 
 
 
 carmālambidukūlavallaricitābhasmāvadhūtastano 
 nmīlaccandanam uttarīyabhujagavyāsaktamuktāvali | 
 mugdhāyā api śailarājaduhitur gaṅgādhārāliṅganaṃ 
 gāḍhapremarasānubandhanikaṣagrāvā śivāyās tu vaḥ  ||118|| 
 
 
 jalacandrasya | 
 
 
 śirasi kuṭilā sindhur doṣākaras tava bhūṣaṇaṃ 
 saha viṣadharaiḥ pratyāsannā piśācaparamparā | 
 harasi na hara prāṇān eva na veda kathaṃ nv iti 
 praṇayakupitakṣmābhṛtputrīvacāṃsi punantu vaḥ  ||119|| 
 
 
 bhagavadgovindasya | 
 
 
 nādatte phaṇikaṅkaṇapraṇayinaṃ nīīvīniveśe karaṃ 
 no cūṇair upahanti bhālanayanajyotirmayīṃ dīpikām | 
 dhatte carma hareṇa muktam api na dvaipaṃ bhayād ity asau 
 pāyād vo navamohanavyatikaravrīḍāvatī pārvatī  ||120|| 
 
 
 ācāryagopīkasya | 
 
 
 25. durgā 
 
 
 ekaṃ mahiṣaśiraḥsthitam 
 aparaṃ sānandasuragaṇapraṇatam | 
 giriduhituḥ padayugalaṃ 
 śoṇitamaṇirāgarañjitaṃ jayati  ||121|| 
 
 
 jalacandrasya | 
 
 
 tribhuvanaśubhapañjikāñjikeva 
 sphurati bhavāni tavāṅkuśaḥ karāgre | 
 ḍamarur api bibharti devi tat tad 
 vipadavasānavisarjanīyalakṣmīm  ||122|| 
 
 
 hareḥ | 
 
 
 jyākṛṣṭibaddhakhaṭakāmukhapāṇipṛṣṭha 
 preṅkhannakhāṃśucayasaṃvalito’mbikāyāḥ | 
 tvāṃ pātu mañjaritapallavakarṇapūra 
 lobhabhramadbhramaravibhramabhṛtkaṭākṣaḥ  ||123|| 
 
 
 
 amaroḥ | (amaru 1; su.ra. 100) 
 
 
 pādāvaṣṭambhanamrīkṛtamahiṣatanor ullasadbāhumūlaṃ 
 śūlaṃ prollāsayantyāḥ saralitavapuṣo madhyabhāgasya devyāḥ | 
 viśliṣṭaspaṣṭadṛṣṭonnataviralabahuvyaktagaurāntarālās 
 tisro vaḥ pāntu rekhāḥ kramavaśavikasatkañcukaprāntamuktāḥ  ||124|| 
 
 
 bāṇasya | 
 
 
 vidrāṇe rudravṛnde savitari tarale vajriṇi dhvastavajre 
 jātāśaṅke śaśāṅke viramati maruti tyaktavaire kubere | 
 vaikuṇṭhe kuṇṭhitās te mahiṣam atiruṣaṃ pauruṣopaghnivighnaṃ 
 nirvighnaṃ nighnatī vaḥ śamayatu duritaṃ bhūribhāvā bhavānī  ||125|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 26. kālī 
 
 
 yadvaktrākāśaśeṣo nabhasi na sulabho yadbhujānāṃ sahasraiḥ 
 preṅkhadbhiḥ kīryamāṇāsvanur api vidito nāvakāśo diśāsu | 
 pañca grāsā na yasyās tribhuvanam abhavat pūraṇārthaṃa samastaṃ 
 kṣṇḍtkṣāmākāṇḍacaṇḍī ciram avatutarāṃ bhairavī kālarātriḥ  ||126|| 
 
 
 bhāsokasya | 
 
 
 śikhaṇḍe khaṇḍenduḥ śaśidinakarau karṇayugale 
 gale tārāhārastaralam uḍucakraṃ ca kucayoḥ | 
 taḍitkāñcī sandhyāsicayaracitā kāli tad ayaṃ 
 tavākalpaḥ kalpavyuparamavidheyo vijayate  ||127|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 nirmāṃsaprakaṭāsthijālavikaṭāṃ pātālanimnodarīṃ 
 kūpakroḍagabhīranetrakuharām unnaddhajūṭāṭavīm | 
 dantāntargatadaityakīkasakaṇavyākarṣaṇavyāpṛta 
 krūraikāgranakhām akhaṇḍitarucaṃ tvāṃ caṇḍi vandāmahe  ||128|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 tārāntarjvaladagnilakṣanayanaśvabhrāntakṛpāntarāṃ 
 kruddāgastyanirastavāridhipayaḥpātālanimnodarīm | 
 vande tvām ajitāvṛtotkaṭasirāpṛṣṭhāsthisārākṛtiṃ 
 daṃṣṭrākoṭitaṭotpatiṣṇuditijāsṛkcarcitāṃ carcikām  ||129|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 jayati tava kūṇitekṣaṇam aśnatyā daśanapeṣam asurāsthi | 
 kalpaśikhisphuṭadadrikvāṇakarālaḥ kaḍatkāraḥ  ||130|| 
 
 
 śatānandasya | 
 
 
 27. ardhanārīśaḥ  
 
 
 sa jayati girikanyāmiśritāścarymūrtis 
 tripurayuvatilīlāvibhramabhraṃśahetuḥ | 
 upacayavati yasya pronnataikastanatvād 
 upari bhujagahāraḥ sthānavaiṣamyam eti  ||131|| 
 
 
 māghasya | 
 
 
 āśleṣādharabimbacumbanasukhālāpasmitānyāsatāṃ 
 dūre tāvad idaṃ mitho na sulabhaṃ jātaṃ mukhālokanam | 
 itthaṃ vyarthakṛtaikadehaghaṭanāvinyāsayor āvayoḥ  
 keyaṃ prītividambanety avatu vaḥ smero’rdhanārīśvaraḥ  ||132|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (Sv 68) 
 
 
 candrālokaya paśya pannagapate vīkṣadhvam etadgaṇāḥ 
 kāmāreḥ stanabhāramantharam uro lākṣāruṇāṅghriśriyaḥ | 
 ākarṇya tridaśāpagāgiram imāṃ sollāsam ābhāṣitāṃ 
 vrīḍāsmeranatānano vijayate kāntārdhanārīśvaraḥ  ||133|| 
 
 
 yogeśvarasya | 
 
 
 svacchandaikastanaśrīrubhayagatamilanmaulicandraḥ phaṇīndra 
 prācīnāvītavāhī sukhayatu bhagavān ardhanārīśvaro vaḥ | 
 yasyārdhe viśvadāhavyasanavisṛmarajyotir ardhaṃ kṛpodyad 
 bāṣpaṃ cānyonyavegaprahatisimasimākāri cakṣṇḍsmṛtīyam  ||134|| 
 
 
 murāreḥ | (Ar 7.38, sū.mu. 2.21) 
 
 
 dhammillaṃ ca jaṭāṃ ca mauktikasaraṃ cāhiṃ ca ratnāni ca 
 brahmāsthīni ca kuṅkumaṃ ca nṛśiraś cūrṇottaraṃ bhasma ca | 
 kṣaumaṃ ca dvipacarma caikavapuṣā bibhraddiśann ekatāṃ 
 bhāvānām iva yogināṃ diśatu vaḥ śreyo’rdhanārīśvaraḥ  ||135|| 
 
 
 śaṅkaradevasya | 
 
 
 28. śṛṅgārātmakārdhanārīśvaraḥ 
 
 
 ardhaṃ dantacchadasya sphurati japavaśād ardham apy utprakopād  
 ekaḥ pāṇiḥ praṇantuṃ śirasi kṛtapadaḥ kṣeptum anyas tam eva | 
 ekaṃ dhyānān nimīlaty aparam avikasad vīkṣate netram itthaṃ  
 tulyān icchāvidhitsā tanur avatu sa vo yasya saṃdhyāvidhāne  ||136|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 acchinnamekhalam alabdhadṛḍhopagūḍham  
 aprāptacumbanam avīkṣitavaktrakānti | 
 kāntāvimiśravapuṣaḥ kṛtavipralambha 
 sambhogasakhyam iva pātu vapuḥ smarāreḥ  ||137|| 
 
 
 chittipasya | 
 
 
 prauḍhapremarasād abhedaghaṭitām aṅge dadhānaḥ priyāṃ 
 devaḥ pātu jaganti kelikalahe tasyāḥ prasādāya yaḥ | 
 vyāhartuṃ praṇayocitaṃ namayituṃ mūrdhānam apy akṣamo 
 dhatte kevalam eva vāmacaraṇāmbhoje karaṃ dakṣiṇam  ||138|| 
 
 
 gadādharasya | 
 
 
 miśrībhūtāṃ tava tanulatāṃ bibhrato gauri kāmaṃ 
 devasya syād aviralaparīrambhajanmā pramodaḥ | 
 kintu premastimitamadhurasnigdhamugdhā na dṛṣṭir 
 dṛṣṭety antaḥkaraṇam asakṛt tāmyati tryambakasya  ||139|| 
 
 
 bhagīrathasya | (su.ra. 82) 
 
 
 anyasyai saṃpratīyaṃ kuru madanaripo svāṅgadānaprasādaṃ  
 nāhaṃ soḍhuṃ samarthā śirasi suranadīṃ nāpi saṃdhyāṃ praṇantum | 
 ity uktvā kopabiddhāṃ vighaṭayitum umām ātmadehaṃ pravṛttāṃ  
 rundhānaḥ pātu śambhoḥ kucakalasahaṭhasparśakṛṣṭo bhujo vaḥ  ||140|| 
 
 
 mayūrasya |  
 
 
 29. gaṇeśaḥ  
 
 
 ekaḥ sa eva paripālayatāj jaganti 
 gaurīgirīśacaritānukṛtiṃ dadhānaḥ | 
 ābhāti yo daśanaśūnyamukhaikadeśa 
 dehārdhahāritavadhūka ivakadantaḥ  ||141|| 
 
 
 vasukalpasya | (su.ra. 94) 
 
 
 kapolād uḍḍīnair bhayavaśavilolair madhukarair  
 madāmbhaḥsaṃlobhād upari patituṃ baddhapaṭalaiḥ | 
 caladbarhacchatraśriyam iva dadhāno’tirucirām 
 avighnaṃ herambo jagadaghavighâtaṃ ghaṭayatu  ||142|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (su.ra. 93) 
 
 
 sandhyāsindūrarāgāruṇagaganatalāsaṅgigaṅgottamāṅga 
 tvaṅgannakṣatramālākṛtaruciraruciḥ karṇaśaṃkhīkṛtenduḥ | 
 nistoyaāmbhodavṛndaiḥ śrutiyugalacalaccāmarāḍambaraśrīr 
 avyājālaṅkṛtir vaḥ pravitaratu gaṇagrāmaṇīr maṅgalāni  ||143|| 
 
 
 daṅkasya | 
 
 
 garjadgabhīraghanaghargharaghoraghoṣa 
 digdantibhītijananodgatakaṇṭhanādaḥ | 
 dhunvan mukhaṃ tava nirasyatu sarvavighnaṃ 
 lambodaraḥ sahajanāṭhyarasapravṛttaḥ  ||144|| 
 
 
 pāpākasya | 
 
 
 devendramaulimandāramakarandakaṇāruṇāḥ | 
 vighnaṃ harantu herambacaraṇāmbujareṇavaḥ  ||145|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya || 
 30. kārttikeyaḥ 
 
 
 svecchāramyaṃ luṭhitvā pitur urasi ciraṃ bhasmadhūlīcitāṅgo 
 gaṅgāvāriṇy agādhe jhaṭiti harajaṭājūṭato dattajhampaḥ | 
 sadyaḥ sītkārakārī jalajaḍimaraṇahantapaṅktir guho vaḥ 
 kampī pāyād apāyāj jvalitaśikhiśikhe cakṣuṣi nyastahastaḥ  ||146|| 
 
 
 bāṇasya | (su.ra. 91, sū.mu. 2.43) 
 
 
 arciṣmanti vidārya vaktrakuharāṇy āsṛkkato vāsukes 
 tarjanyā viṣakarburān gaṇayataḥ saṃspṛśya dantāṅkurān | 
 ekaṃ trīṇi navāṣṭa sapta ṣaḍativyastāstasaṅkhyākramā 
 vācaḥ śaktidharasya śaiśavakalāḥ kurvantu vo maṅgalam  ||147|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 95, śā.pa. 105) 
 
 
 suptaṃ pakṣapuṭe nilīnaśirasaṃ sṛṣṭvā mayūraṃ puraḥ 
 kṛttaṃ kena śiro’sya tāta katham ity ākrandataḥ śaiśavāt | 
 antarhāsapinākipāṇiyugalasphālollasaccetasas 
 tanmūrdhekṣaṇaharṣitasya hasitaṃ pāyāt kumārasya vaḥ  ||148|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 96) 
 
 
 haṃsaśreṇikutūhalena kalayan bhūṣākapālāvalīṃ 
 bālām indukalāṃ mṛṇālarabhasād āndolayan pāṇinā | 
 raktāmbhojadhiyā ca locanapuṭaṃ lālāṭam udghāṭayan 
 pāyād vaḥ pitur aṅkabhāk śiśujanakrīḍonmukhaḥ ṣaṇmukhaḥ  ||149|| 
 
 
 balabhadrasya | (su.ra. 92) 
 
 
 nālair nīlotpalānāṃ racitagurujaṭājūṭavinyāsaśobhaḥ 
 kṛtvā saṃbhugnakoṭidvayam atha visinīkandam indoḥ pradeśe | 
 mātuś citrāṃśukena tvacam ucitapade pauṇḍarīkīṃ vidhāya 
 krīḍārudrāyamāṇo jagad avatu guho vīkṣyamāṇaḥ pitṛbhyām  ||150|| 
 
 
 halāyudhasya | 
 
 
 31. bhṛṅgī 
 
 
 digvāsā yadi tat kim asya dhanuṣā sāstrasya kiṃ bhasmanā 
 bhasmāthāsya kim aṅganā yadi ca sā kāmaṃ paridveṣṭi kim | 
 ity anyonyaviruddhaceṣṭitam idaṃ paśyan nijasvāmino 
 bhṛṅgī sāndraśirāvanaddhaparuṣaṃ dhatte’sthiśeṣaṃ vapuḥ  ||151|| 
 
 
 
 yogeśvarasya (su.ra. 103, Sv 2399) 
 
 
 kasmāt tvaṃ tāta gehād aparam abhinavā brūhi kā tatra vārtā  
 devyā devo jitaḥ kiṃ vṛṣaḍamarucitābhasmabhogīndracandrān | 
 ity evaṃ barhināthe kathayati sahasā bhartṛbhikṣā vibhūṣā 
 vaiguṇyodvegajanmā jagad avatu ciraṃ hāravo bhṛṅgirīṭeḥ  ||152|| 
 
 
 tuṅgokasya | (su.ra. 98) 
 
 
 carceyaṃ kṣudhitā sadaiva gṛhiṇī putro’py ayaṃ ṣaṇmukho 
 duṣpūrodarabhāramantharavapurlambodaro’pi svayam | 
 ity evaṃ svakuṭumbam ekavṛṣabho devaḥ kathaṃ pokṣatīty 
 ālokyeva viśuṣkapañjaratanur bhṛṅgī ciraṃ pātu vaḥ  ||153|| 
 
 
 nīlāṅgasya | 
 
 
 bhikṣābhojini kṛttivāsasi vasuprāptiḥ kutaḥ syād iti  
 prāg ardhaṃ vapuṣaḥ svayaṃ vyasanino yasyāharat pārvatī | 
 tasyārdhaṃ kupitā haṭhād yadi haren mūrdhni sthitā jāhnavī 
 hā nātha kva tadeti duḥsthahṛdayo bhṛṅgī bhṛśaṃ śuṣyati  ||154|| 
 
 
 bhavānandasya | 
 
 
 sevāṃ no kurute karoti na kṛṣiṃ vāṇijyam asyāsti no 
 paitryaṃ nāsti dhanaṃ na bāndhavabalaṃ naivāsti kaścid gaṇaḥ | 
 dyūtastrīvyasanaṃ na muñcati tathāpīśas tad asmāt phalaṃ 
 kiṃ me syād iti cintayann iva kṛśo bhṅgī ciraṃ pātu vaḥ  ||155|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 32. gaṇoccāvacam 
 
 
 sthūlo dūramayaṃ na yāsyati kṛśo naiṣa prayāṇakṣamas 
 tenaikasya mamaiva tatra kaśipuprāptiḥ paraṃ dṛśyate | 
 ity ādau paricintitaṃ pratimuhus tadbhṛṅgikūṣmāṇḍayor 
 anyonyapratikūlam īśaśivayoḥ pāṇigrahe pātu vaḥ  ||156|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 99) 
 
 
 carcāyāḥ katham eva rakṣati sadā sadyo nṛmuṇḍasrajaṃ 
 caṇḍīkeśariṇo vṛṣaṃ ca bhujagān sūnor mayūrād api | 
 ity antaḥparibhāvayan bhagavato dīrghaṃ dhiyaḥ kauśalaṃ 
 kūṣmāṇḍo dhṛtisambhṛtām anudinaṃ puṣṇāti tundaśriyam  ||157|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 97) 
 
 
 devī sūnum asūta nṛtyata gaṇāḥ kiṃ tiṣṭhatety udbhuje 
 harṣād bhṛṅgariṭāvayācitagirā cāmuṇḍayāliṅgite | 
 avyād vo hatadundubhisvanaghanadhvānātiriktas tayor 
 anyonyapracalāsthitpañjararaṇatkaṅkālajanmā ravaḥ  ||158|| 
 
 
 yogeśvarasya | (su.ra. 71, sū.mu. 2.55) 
 
 
 śṛṅgaṃ bhṛṅgin vimuñca tyaja gajavadana tvaṃ ca lāṅgūlamūlaṃ 
 mandānando’si nandinn alam abala mahākāla kaṇṭhagraheṇa | 
 ity uktvā nīyamānaḥ sukhayatu vṛṣabhaḥ pārvatīpādamūle 
 paśyann akṣair vilakṣaṃ valitagalacalatkambalaṃ tryambakaṃ vaḥ  ||159|| 
 
 
 abhinandasya | (su.ra. 77) 
 
 
 digvāsā vṛṣavāhano naraśirodhārī dadhāno’jinaṃ 
 bhikṣur bhasmabhujaṅgabhūṣitatanur bhūtair bhraman kānanam | 
 smartṬṇāṃ śivakṛt tathāpi jagati jyeṣṭho’smadīyaḥ prabhur 
 dhanyo’smīty atitoṣapuṣṭajaṭharaḥ kūṣmāṇḍako’vyāj jagat  ||160|| 
 
 
 mahānidheḥ | 
 
 
 33. hariharau  
 
 
 yad baddhārdhajaṭaṃ yadardhamukuṭaṃ yaccandramandārayor 
 dhatte dhāma ca dāma ca smitalasatkundendranīlaśriyoḥ | 
 tat khaṭvāṅgarathāṅgasaṅgavikaṭaṃ śrīkaṇṭhavaikuṇṭhayor 
 vande nandimahokṣatārkṣyapariṣannāmāṅkam ekaṃ vapuḥ  ||161|| 
 
 
 rājaśekharasya | (su.ra. 1639) 
 
 
 niyamitajaṭāvallīlīlāprasuptamahoragaṃ 
 caraṇakamalaprānte muktasvavikramagovṛṣam | 
 vitataphaṇibhukpatracchatraṃ gadālaguḍaśriyaṃ 
 hariharavapurbrahmopāsyaṃ punātu jagat trayam  ||162|| 
 
 
 bhavānandasya | 
 
 
 yena dhvastamanobhavena balijitkāyaḥ purāstrīkṛto 
 yo gaṅgāṃ ca dadhe’ndhakakṣayakaro yo barhipatrapriyaḥ | 
 yasyāhuḥ śaśimacchiro hara iti stutyaṃ ca nāmāmarāḥ  
 so’vyād iṣṭabhujaṅgahāravalayas tāṃ sarvado mādhavaḥ  ||163|| 
 
 
 bhāraveḥ | (Sv 44, sū.mu. 2.104, Sāh.D. 10.12) 
 
 
 ekāvasthitir astu vaḥ puramurapradveṣiṇor devayoḥ  
 prāleyāñjanaśailaśṛṅgasubhagacchāyāṅgayoḥ śreyase | 
 tārkṣyatrāsavihastapannagaphaṭā yasyāṃ jaṭāpālayo  
 bālendudyutikośasuptajalajo yasyāṃ ca nābhīhradaḥ  ||164|| 
 
 
 tuṅgokasya | 
 
 
 yajjambūkamburociḥ phaṇadharapariṣadbhojibhogīndrakāntaṃ 
 nandaccandrāravindadyuticaraṇaśiraḥsyandimandākinīkam | 
 rakṣāsaṃhāradakṣaṃ madanasamudayoddīpanaṃ śaśvad avyād 
 avyāghātaṃ vibodhe’py udadhigirisutākāntayor deham ekam  ||165|| 
 
 
 jalacandrasya | 
 
 
 34. kāntāsahitahariharau 
 
 
 sambhogaspṛhayālumanmathapunarjanmāspadaṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ 
 svaḥ pāyāt puruṣottamakratubhidor ardhārdhapūrṇaṃ vapuḥ | 
 yallakṣmīgirijākaṭākṣakuṭilakrīḍāhaṭhākṛṣṭibhiḥ 
 syād eva truṭitaṃ parasparaguṇasyūtaṃ na ced antarā  ||166|| 
 
 
 tripurāripālasya | 
 
 
 vapur avatu jaṭākirīṭamiśraṃ 
 puramurasūdanayor vimiśritaṃ vaḥ | 
 girijalaghisutāsvabhartṛkaṇṭha 
 grahacalitāhṛtabāhuvallarīkam  ||167|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 sphaṭikamarakataśrīhāriṇoḥ prītiyogāt 
 tad avatu vapur ekaṃ kāmakaṃsadviṣor vaḥ | 
 na viramati bhavānyāḥ sārdham abdher duhitrā 
 sadṛśamahasi kaṇṭhe yatra sīmāvivādaḥ  ||168|| 
 
 
 yogeśvarasya | (śā.pa. 110, sū.mu. 2.103) 
 
 
 devasyaikatamālapatramukuṭasyārdhaṃ puradveṣiṇo 
 dehārdhena samasyamānam asamaṃ śvaḥśreyasāyās tu vaḥ | 
 yasmin bhūdharakanyakābdhisutayor aprāptasambhogayor 
 anyonyapratikarmanarmabhiduro bhūyān anaṅgajvaraḥ  ||169|| 
 
 
 hareḥ | 
 
 
 dhātrā sauhṛdasīmavismitamukhaṃ bhedabhramāpāsanāt 
 sānandaṃ munibhiḥ sanirvṛti surair ekatra sevāsukhāt | 
 pārvatyā svapadāvakṛṣṭikuṭilabhrūbhaṅgam ālokitaḥ  
 pāyād vo bhagavāṃś carācaragurur dehārdhahārī haraḥ  ||170|| 
 
 
 āryāvilāsasya | 
 
 
 35. gaṅgā 
 
 
 brāhmaṃ tejo dvijānāṃ jvalayati jaḍimaprakramaṃ hanti buddher 
 vṛddhiṃ sekena sadyaḥ śamayati valino duṣkṛtānokahasya | 
 ūrdhvaṃ caivātra lokād api nayatitarāṃ janmino magnamūrtīṃs 
 tvaddhārāvāri kāśīpraṇayini paritaḥ prakriyā kīdṛśīyam  ||171|| 
 
 
 kolāhalasya | 
 
 
 durvāradoṣatimirāgamavāsaraśrīḥ  
 kaivalyakairavavikāsasitāṃśulekhā | 
 jīyāt triviṣṭapadhunī kalikālabhagna 
 gīrvāṇarājanagarākaravaijayantī  ||172|| 
 
 
 graheśvarasya | 
 
 
 tīrthāṭanaiḥ kim adhikaṃ kṣaṇam īkṣitā cet 
 pītaṃ tvadambu yadi devi mudhā sudhāpi | 
 snātaṃ yadi tvayi viriñcipadaṃ na dūre 
 muktiḥ kare yadi ca sā samupāsitāsi  ||173|| 
 
 
 viriñceḥ | 
 
 
 tīraṃ tavāvataratīha yathā yathaiva 
 dehena devi jaratā munajo mumūrṣuḥ | 
 amba svayaṃvaravaśaṃvadanākanārī  
 dorvallipallavi nabho’pi tathā tathaiva  ||174|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 taptaṃ yan na tapo hutaṃ ca na havir yaj jātavedo mukhe 
 dattaṃ yac ca na kiṃcid eva na kṛto yat tīrthayātrādaraḥ | 
 kākeneva śuneva kevalam ayaṃ yat pūritaḥ pudgalo 
 mātas tvāṃ parirabhya jāhnavi sa me śānto’yam antarjvaraḥ  ||175|| 
 
 
 sentutasya | 
 
 
 36. gaṅgāpraśaṃsā  
 
 
 dharmasyotsavavaijayantimukuṭasragveṇigaurīpates 
 tvāṃ ratnākarapatni jahnutanaye bhāgīrathi prārthaye | 
 tvattoyāntaśilāniṣaṇṇavapuṣas tvadvīcibhiḥ preṅkhatas 
 tvannāma smaratas tadarpitadṛśaḥ prāṇāḥ prayāsyanti me  ||176|| 
 
 
 lakṣmīdharasya | (su.ra. 1613, sa.ka.ā. 4.183) 
 
 
 śatrau me suhṛdīva kāpy upakṛtir bhūyād asūyā na tu 
 svācchyaṃ satsu matir janeṣu karuṇā hīnā na dīnātmasu | 
 prakṣīṇā kalikalmaṣakṣayakarī tṛṣṇā na kṛṣṇārcane 
 devi śraddadhatāṃ gatis tvayi mudā mandā na mandākini  ||177|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 prasīda śrīgaṅge mṛḍamukuṭacūḍāgrasubhage 
 tavollolonmūlaḥ skhalatu mama saṃsāraviṭapī | 
 athotpatsye bhūyas trijagad adhirājo’pi na tadā 
 śvapākaḥ kāko vā bhagavati bhaveyaṃ tava taṭe  ||178|| 
 
 
 pādukasya | 
 
 
 kadā te sānandaṃ vitatanavadūrvāñcitataṭī 
 kuṭīre tīre vā savanam anu manvādikathitaiḥ | 
 kathābandhair andhaṅkaraṇakaraṇagrāmaniyamād 
 yamād ujjhan bhītiṃ bhagavati bhaveyaṃ pramuditaḥ  ||179|| 
 
 
 gopīcandrasya | 
 
 
 baddhāñjalir naumi kuru prasādam 
 apūrvamātā bhava devi gaṅge | 
 ante vayasy aṅgagatāya mahyam 
 adehabandhāya payaḥ prayaccha  ||180|| 
 
 
 kevaṭṭapapīpasya | 
 37. harer matsyāvatāraḥ 
 
 
 matsyaḥ punātu jagadoṅkṛtikuñcitāsyo 
 brahmādvayapraṇayapīvaramadhyabhāgaḥ | 
 krīḍann asau jaladhivīcibhir eva neti 
 nety ādarād iva vibhāvitapucchakampaḥ  ||181|| 
 
 
 āvantyakṛṣṇasya | 
 
 
 devyāḥ śruter danujadurṇayadūṣitāyā 
 bhūyaḥsamudgamavidhāvavalambabhūmiḥ | 
 ekārṇavībhavadaśeṣapayodhimadhya 
 dvīpaṃ vapur jayati mīnatanor murāreḥ  ||182|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 brahmāṇḍodaradarpaṇe bhramirayotkṣiptāmbudhikṣālite 
 saṃkrāntām animeṣalocanayugenotpaśyataḥ svāṃ tanum | 
 śaurer mīnatanoḥ kṛśānukapiśaṃ pārśvadvayaṃ prollasac 
 candrārkāṅkitakāñcanādriśikharākāraṃ śiraḥ pātu vaḥ  ||183|| 
 
 
 vasantadevasya | 
 
 
 pātu trīṇi jaganti pārśvakaṣaṇaprakṣuṇṇadiṅmaṇḍalo 
 naikābdhistimitodaraḥ sa bhagavān krīḍājhaṣaḥ keśavaḥ | 
 tvaṅganniṣṭhurapṛṣṭharomakhacitabrahmāṇḍabhāṇḍāvadher 
 yasyotphālakutūhalena katham apy aṅgeṣu jīrṇāyitam  ||184|| 
 
 
 raghunandasya | (su.ra. 135) 
 
 
 matsyaḥ pucchābhighātena tucchīkṛtamahodadhiḥ | 
 aparyāptajalakrīḍāraso diśatu vaḥ śivam  ||185|| 
 
 
 kasyacit |  
 
 
 38. kūrmaḥ 
 
 
 pṛṣṭhabhrāmyad amandamandaragirigrāvāgrakaṇḍūyanān 
 nidrāloḥ kamaṭhākṛter bhagavataḥ śvāsānilāḥ pāntu vaḥ | 
 yatsaṃskārakalānuvartanavaśād velāchalenāmbhasāṃ 
 yātāyātam ayantritaṃ jalanidher nādyāpi viśrāmyati  ||186|| 
 
 
 keśaṭācāryasya | (BhP 12.13.2; su.ra. 105, vākpatirājasya; Sv 36) 
 
 
 kṣīrābdhau mathyamāne tridaśadanusutonmuktakolāhalaughe 
 brahmāṇḍakāṇḍacaṇḍasphuṭanagururavabhrāntibhājitrilokyām | 
 sadyo nirdāvabodhād upari rayavaśakṣiptadīrghakṣitidhā 
 lagnagrīvāprakāṇḍo jayati kamaṭharāṭ caṇḍaviṣkambhatulyaḥ  ||187|| 
 
 
 vasusenasya | 
 
 
 pāyād vo mandarādribhramaṇanikaṣaṇākṛṣṭapṛṣṭhāgrakaṇḍū 
 līnānidrālur abdheḥ kṣubhitam agaṇayann adbhutaḥ kūrmarājaḥ | 
 yasyāṅgamardahelāvaśacalitamahāśailakīlā dharitrī 
 tvaṅgatkallolaratnākaravalayacalanmekhalā nṛtyatīva  ||188|| 
 
 
 sūreḥ | 
 
 
 pārśvāsphālātivegāj jhagiti ca virahād ucchaladbhiḥ patadbhir 
 bhūyo bhūyaḥ samudrair mihiramatirayād āpibadbhir vamadbhiḥ | 
 koṭīras toyadānāṃ kṣaṇam iva gagane darśayan vaḥ punītād 
 pṣad gātrāvahelācalitavasumatīmaṇḍalaḥ kūrmarājaḥ  ||189|| 
 
 
 dharaṇīdharasya | 
 
 
 kurmaḥ kūrmākṛtaye haraye muktāvalambanāya namaḥ | 
 pṛṣṭhe yasya niṣaṇṇaṃ śaivalavallīsamaṃ viśvam  ||190|| 
 
 
 bhavānandasya | 
 39. varāhaḥ 
 
 
 daṃṣṭrāpiṣṭeṣu sadyaḥ śikhariṣu na kṛtaḥ skandhakaṇḍūvinodaḥ 
 sindhuṣv aṅgāvagāhaḥ khurakuharaviśattoyatuccheṣu nāptaḥ | 
 prāptāḥ pātālapaṅke na luṭhanaratayaḥ potramātropayukte 
 yenoddhāre dharitryāḥ sa jayati vibhutābṛṃhiteccho varāhaḥ  ||191|| 
 
 
 varāhamihirasya | (su.ra. 134) 
 
 
 asti śrīstanapatrabhaṅgam akarīmudrāṅkitoraḥsthalī 
 devaḥ sarvajagatpatir madhuvadhūvaktrābjacandrodayaḥ | 
 krīḍākroḍatanor navenduviśade daṃṣṭrāṅkure yasya bhūr 
 bhāti sma pralayābdhipalvalatalotkhātaikamustākṛtiḥ  ||192|| 
 
 
 nagnasya | (su.ra. 104) 
 
 
 seyaṃ candrakaleti nāgavantiānetrotpalair arcitā 
 madbhārāpagamakṣameti phaṇinā sānandam ālokitā | 
 diṅnāgaiḥ saralīkṛtāyatakaraiḥ spṛṣṭā mṛṇālāśayā 
 bhittvorvīm abhiniḥsṛtā madhuripor daṃṣṭrā ciraṃ pātu vaḥ  ||193|| 
 
 
 keśavasya | 
 
 
 ghoṇāghorābhidhātocchaladudadhijalāsārasiktāgraromā 
 romāgraprotatārānikara iti surair dhīram ālokito vaḥ | 
 śvāsākṛṣṭāvakṛṣṭapraviśad apasarad budhnabimbānubandhād 
 āvir naktaṃ dinaśrīḥ sa diśatu duritadhvaṃsam ādyo varāhaḥ  ||194|| 
 
 
 narasiṃhasya | 
 
 
 yenādhomukhapadminīdaladhiyā kūrmaś ciraṃ vīkṣito 
 ghrāto yena mṛṇālamugdhalatikābuddhyā phaṇigrāmaṇīḥ | 
 yaḥ śālūkam ivoddadhāra dharaṇībimbaṃ punītād asau 
 tvām ekārṇavapalvalaikarasikaḥ krīḍāvarāho hariḥ  ||195|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 40. narasiṃhaḥ 
 
 
 somārdhāyitaniṣpidhānadaśanaḥ sandhyāyitāntarmukho 
 bālārkāyitalocanaḥ suradhanur lekhāyitabhrūlataḥ | 
 antarnādagabhīrapalvalagalatvagrūpaniryattaḍit 
 tārasphārasaṭāvaruddhagaganaḥ pāyān nṛsiṃho jagat  ||196|| 
 
 
 murāreḥ | 
 
 
 caṭaccaṭini carmaṇi ccham iti cocchalacchoṇite 
 dhagaddhag iti medasi sphuṭataro’sthiṣu ṣṭhād iti | 
 punātu bhavato harer amaravairināthorasi 
 kvaṇatkarajapañjarakrakacakāṣajanmā ravaḥ  ||197|| 
 
 
 vākpatirājasya | (su.ra. 116, śā.pa. 126, sū.mu. 2.77) 
 
 
 preṅkhadbhāsvarakeśaraugharacitatrailokyasandhyātapo 
 brahmāṇḍodararodhighargharasaghūtkārapracaṇḍadhvaniḥ | 
 sphūrjadvajrakaṭhoranakharakṣuṇṇāsuroraḥsthalī 
 raktāsvādavidīrṇadīrgharasanaḥ pāyān nṛsiṃho jagat  ||198|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 cakra brūhi vibho gade jaya hare kambo samājñāpaya 
 bho bho nandaka jīva pannagaripo kiṃ nātha bhinno mayā | 
 ko daityaḥ katamo hiraṇyakaśipuḥ satyaṃ bhavadbhyaḥ śape 
 kenāstreṇa nakhair iti pravadataḥ śaurer giraḥ pāntu vaḥ  ||199|| 
 
 
 keśaṭasya | 
 
 
 kiṃ kiṃ siṃhas tataḥ kiṃ narasadṛśavapur deva citraṃ gṛhīto 
 naivaṃ dhik ko’tra jīva drutam upanaya taṃ so’pi samprāpta eva | 
 cāpaṃ cāpaṃ na khaḍgaṃ jhaṭiti hahahahā karkaśatvaṃ nakhānām 
 ity evaṃ daityarājaṃ nijanakhakuliśair jaghnivān so’vatād vaḥ  ||200|| 
 
 
 śrīvyāsapādānām | (su.ra. 128, sū.mu. 2.76) 
 
 
 41. narasiṃhanakhāḥ 
 
 
 daṃṣṭrāsaṅkaṭavaktraghargharalalajjihvābhṛto havyabhug 
 jvālābhāsvarabhūrikeśarasaṭābhārasya daityadruhaḥ | 
 vyāvalgad balavad dhiraṇyakaśipukroḍasthalīpāṭana 
 spaṣṭaprasphuṭadasthipañjararavakrūrā nakhāḥ pāntu vaḥ  ||201|| 
 
 
 dakṣasya | (su.ra. 141) 
 
 
 ye bālendukalārdhavibhramabhṛto māyānṛsiṃhākṛter 
 niryātā iva ye sirāsaraṇibhir nābhyabjakandāṅkurāḥ | 
 te vakṣaḥsthaladāritāsurasaritkīlāladhārāruṇāḥ 
 pāyāsur navakiṃśukāmramukulaśrīsākṣiṇaḥ pāṇijāḥ  ||202|| 
 
 
 varāhasya | 
 
 
 asrasrotas taraṅgabhramiṣu taralitā māṃsapaṅkte luṭhantaḥ 
 sthūlāsthibhaṅgair dhavalavisalatāgrāsam ākalpayantaḥ | 
 māyāsiṃhasya śaureḥ sphuradaruṇahṛdambhojasaṃśleṣabhājaḥ 
 pāyāsur daityavakṣaḥsthalakuharasarorājahaṃsā nakhā vaḥ  ||203|| 
 
 
 mayūrasya | 
 
 
 punantu bhuvanatrayaṃ dalitadaityavakṣaḥsthala 
 prasarpirudhiracchaṭācchuraṇabālasūryatviṣaḥ | 
 dṛḍhāsthicayacūrṇanāghaṭitaśabdasārā harer 
 nṛsiṃhavapuṣaś ciraṃ piśitapiṇḍagarbhā nakhāḥ  ||204|| 
 
 
 dhūrjaṭirājasya | 
 
 
 jayanti nirdāritadaityavakṣaso 
 nṛsiṃharūpasya harer nakhāṅkurāḥ | 
 vicintya yeṣāṃ caritaṃ surārayaḥ  
 priyānakhebhyo’pi rateṣu bibhyati  ||205|| 
 
 
 
 kasyacit (su.ra. 130) 
 
 
 42. śṛṅgārinarasiṃhaḥ 
 
 
 lakṣmīm uraḥparisare vahataḥ salīlaṃ 
 yogāsanaṃ ca carato nṛharer jayanti | 
 ekakṣaṇopanatamānmathabhāvamugdha 
 svātmāvabodham asṛṇāni vilokitāni  ||206|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 nyañcatkesaram uttaraṅgapulakasraṅnaddhamardhaskhalad 
 dvandvālāpam apāstagarjanam aṭadbhrūbhaṅgam ārdrekṣaṇam | 
 svidyatpāṇi vinītadṛptikarajaṃ pāyān nṛsiṃhākṛter 
 devasya śriyam aṅkasīmni dadhato viśrāntaraudraṃ vapuḥ  ||207|| 
 
 
 vaidyagadādharasya | 
 
 
 svacchandaṃ vairivakṣaḥsthalakuliśabhido vīkṣya kandarpacāpa 
 krīḍābhājo nakhāgrān samasamayabhayānandalolāyatākṣyāḥ | 
 lakṣmyā vakṣojakumbhaṃ karikalabhaśiraḥśaṅkayā vīkṣyamāṇaḥ 
 svairaṃ śāntākṣirāgo jayati naraharir jātacittānurāgaḥ  ||208|| 
 
 
 jalacandrasya | 
 
 
 avyād vo vajrasārasphuradurunakharakrūracakrakramāgra 
 prodbhinnendrārivakṣaḥsthalagaladasṛgāsārakāśmīragauraḥ | 
 prasphūrjatkeśarāgragrathitajaladharaśreṇinīlābjamālyaḥ  
 sūryācandrāvataṃso naraharir asamābaddhaśṛṅgāralīlaḥ  ||209|| 
 
 
 prajāpateḥ | 
 
 
 ānandamugdhanayanāṃ śriyam aṅkabhittau  
 bibhrat punātu bhavato bhagavān nṛsiṃhaḥ | 
 yasyāvalokanavilāsavaśād ivāsīd  
 utsannalāñchanamṛgaḥ kamalāmukhenduḥ  ||210|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 43. vāmanaḥ 
 
 
 idaṃ prāyo loke na paricitapūrvaṃ nayanayor 
 na yācñā yat puṃsaḥ suguṇaparimāṇaṃ laghayati | 
 viśadbhir viśvātmā svavapuṣi baliprārthanakṛte 
 trapālīnair aṅgair yad ayam abhavad vāmanatanuḥ  ||211|| 
 
 
 vaṅkasya | 
 
 
 apasara pṛthivi samudrāḥ saṃvṛṇutāmbūni bhūbhṛto namata | 
 vāmanaharilaghutunde jagatīkalahaḥ sa vaḥ pātu  ||212|| 
 
 
 bhavānandasya | 
 
 
 kutas tvam aṇukaḥ svataḥ svam iti kiṃ na yat kasyacit 
 kim icchasi padatrayaṃ nanu bhuvā kim ity alpayā | 
 dvijasya śamino mama tribhuvanaṃ tad ity āśayo 
 harer jayati nihnutaḥ prakaṭitaś ca vakroktibhiḥ  ||213|| 
 
 
 vākpateḥ | (su.ra. 114) 
 
 
 pūjyo brahmavidāṃ tvam eva vimalajñānaikapātraṃ bhavān 
 madbhāgyena gato’tithitvam adhunā kiṃ te tribhir bhūpadaiḥ | 
 trailokyaṃ bhavataṃ svam ity upagato daityeśvareṇādarāj 
 jñāto’smīti salajjanamravadanaḥ pāyāj jagad vāmanaḥ  ||214|| 
 
 
 vasusenasya | 
 
 
 lakṣmīpayodharotsaṅgakuṅkumāruṇito hareḥ | 
 balir eṣa sa yenāsya bhikṣāpātrīkṛtaḥ karaḥ  ||215|| 
 
 
 gaṇādhyakṣasya | (śā.pa. 278) 
 
 
 44. trivikramaḥ 
 
 
 kiṃ chatraṃ kiṃ nu ratnaṃ tilakam atha tathā kuṇḍalaṃ kaustubho vā 
 cakraṃ vā vārijaṃ vety amarayuvatibhir yad balidhvaṃsi dehe | 
 ūrdhvaṃ maulau lalāṭe śravasi hṛdi kare nābhideśe ca dṛṣṭaṃ 
 pāyāt tad vo’rkabimbaṃ sa ca danujaripur vardhamānaḥ krameṇa  ||216|| 
 
 
 śrīhanūmataḥ | 
 
 
 jyotiś cakrākṣadaṇḍaḥ kṣaradamarasaritpaṭṭikā ketudaṇḍaḥ 
 kṣoṇīnaukūpadaṇḍaḥ śatadhṛtibhavanāmbhoruho nāladaṇḍaḥ | 
 brahmāṇḍacchatra daṇḍas tribhuvanastambhadaṇḍoṅghridaṇḍaḥ 
 śreyas trivikramas te vitaratu vibudhadveṣiṇāṃ kāladaṇḍaḥ  ||217|| 
 
 
 daṇḍinaḥ | 
 
 
 cañcatpādanakhāgramaṇḍalaruciprasyanigaṅgājalo 
 visphūrjadbalirājyanāśapiśunotpātāmbuvāhadyutiḥ | 
 pātu tvāṃ caraṇo hareḥ kramavidhau yasyādhikaṃ dyotate 
 dūrād aṅgulimudrikāmaṇir iva sphārāṅkuśajālo raviḥ  ||218|| 
 
 
 vikramādityasya | 
 
 
 yat kāṇḍaṃ gaganadrumasya yad api kṣoṇītaḍāgodare 
 devasyaiva yaśo’mbuśobhini mahāyaṣṭiḥ pratiṣṭhākarī | 
 tad viṣṇoḥ padam antarālajaladher ādhārato bhūtalāt 
 pāraṃ dyāmupagantum udyamavatāṃ setūbhavat pātu vaḥ  ||219|| 
 
 
 cakrapāṇeḥ | 
 
 
 kharvagranthivimuktasandhivikasadvakṣaḥsphuratkaustubhaṃ 
 niryan nābhisarojakuḍmalakuṭīgambhīrasāmaedhvani | 
 pātrāvāptisamutsukena balinā sānandam ālokitaṃ 
 pāyād vaḥ kramavardhamānamahimāścaryaṃ murārer vapuḥ  ||220|| 
 
 
 vākpatirājasya | (su.ra. 124) 
 
 
 45. paraśurāmaḥ  
 
 
 diṅmātaṅgaghaṭāvibhaktacaturāghāṭā mahī sādhyate 
 siddhā sāpi vadanta eva hi vayaṃ romāñcitāḥ paśyata | 
 viprāya pratipādyate kim aparaṃ rāmāya tasmai namo 
 yatraivāvirabhūt kathādbhutam idaṃ yatraiva cāstaṃgatam  ||221|| 
 
 
 keśaṭasya | 
 
 
 hā tāteti na jalpitaṃ na ruditaṃ na svīkṛtaṃ tad dhanaṃ 
 na snātaṃ na ca vīkṣitaḥ parijanaḥ pitre na dattaṃ jalam | 
 yāvan na krakacābhighātavigaladdāmnām arīṇām asṛg 
 gaṇḍūṣair ghanaghoragharghararavāḥ santarpitāḥ pheravaḥ  ||222|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 śauryaṃ śatrukulakṣayāvadhi yaśo brahmāṇḍakhaṇḍāvadhi 
 tyāgaḥ saptasamudramudritamahīnirvājadānāvadhiḥ | 
 vryaṃ yantu girāṃ na tat pathi nanu vyaktaṃ hi tatkarmabhiḥ  
 satyaṃ brahmataponidher bhagavataḥ kiṃ kiṃ na lokottaram  ||223|| 
 
 
 bhavabhūteḥ | 
 
 
 gotrācāraviśeṣapāragatayā vṛddhābhir ādiṣṭayā 
 mātrā vastuṣu teṣu teṣu viśadanyasteṣu dṛṣṭeḥ puraḥ | 
 annaprāśanavāsare sarabhasaṃ vakṣobharotsarpiṇā  
 yenāttaṃ dhanur īkṣitāś ca jhaṭiti kṣatrāvataṃsā diśaḥ  ||224|| 
 
 
 keśaṭasya | 
 
 
 triḥsaptāvadhi vādhitā kṣitibhujām ājanma vaikhānasaḥ  
 kartā mātṛvadhainasaḥ sa sakalaśrutyarthavīthīguruḥ | 
 viśvasyāś ca bhuvaḥ kratau vitaritā śyāmakamuṣṭiṃpaco 
 rāmaḥ so’yam udagrageyamahimā kāsāṃ girāṃ gocaraḥ  ||225|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 46. śrīrāmaḥ 
 
 
 śauryotkarṣatṛṇīkṛtatribhuvano laṅkāpatiḥ so’bhavat 
 kārāyām upavāsayan vijayate taṃ helayā haihayaḥ | 
 līlālūnaviśālatadbhujavano’bhūj jāmadagnyas tatas 
 tajjetā janakātmajāparivṛḍho rāmaḥ kathaṃ varṇyatām  ||226|| 
 
 
 surabheḥ | 
 
 
 rāmaḥ kasya na vismayāya manaso niḥśaṅkalaṅkeśvara 
 truṭyanmaulisirāsamucchaladasṛgdhārānubandhena yaḥ | 
 taddorvikramavidrutā daśadiśo bhogāya bhūmaṇḍale 
 samyag vāsayituṃ pravālaghaṭitā yaṣṭīr udastambhayan  ||227|| 
 
 
 daṅkasya | 
 
 
 mārtaṇḍaikakulaprakāṇḍatilakas trailokyarakṣāmaṇir 
 viśvāmitramahāmuner nirupadhiḥ śiṣyo raghugrāmaṇīḥ | 
 rāmas tāḍitatāḍakaḥ kim aparaṃ pratyakṣanārāyaṇaḥ  
 kauśayānayanotsavo vijayate bhūkaśyapasyātmajaḥ  ||228|| 
 
 
 rājaśekharasya | 
 
 
 rāmo nūnam ayaṃ niśācaracamūkālāgnirudropamo 
 niḥsandeham ayaṃ ca vikramanidhiḥ saumitrir asyānujaḥ | 
 vāraṃ vāram apāṅgabhāgacalitair yad dṛṣṭipātair iyaṃ 
 laṅkābhartur anīkinī pitṛpateḥ pāśair ivāvadhyate  ||229|| 
 
 
 śrīmitrasya | 
 
 
 rāmo’sau bhuvaneṣu vikramaguṇair yātaḥ prasiddhiṃ parām 
 asmadbhāgyaviparyayād yadi punaḥ devo na jānāti tam | 
 vandīvaiṣa yaśāṃsi gāyati marud yasyaikabāṇāhati 
 śrīeṇībhūtaviśālasālavivarodgīrṇaiḥ śaraiḥ saptabhiḥ  ||230|| 
 
 
 viśākhadattasya | 
 
 
 47. virahiśrīrāmaḥ 
 
 
 sarasi virasaḥ prasthe duḥstho latāsu gatādaraḥ 
 prati parisaraṃ bhrāntodbhrāntaḥ saritsu nirutsukaḥ | 
 dadad api dṛśau kubje kubje rudann upanirjharaṃ 
 suciravirahakṣāmo rāmo na kari anurudyate  ||231|| 
 
 
 vāsudevajyotiṣaḥ | 
 
 
 niṣpandaṃ girikandareṣu vipinacchāyāsu mūrcchālasaṃ 
 sāsraṃ pañcavaṭītaṭīṣu taṭinītīreṣu tīvravyatham | 
 kākutsthaṃ tadavastham ādhividhuraṃ dṛṣṭvā taḍidvyājato 
 manye manyubharair abhedi hṛdayaṃ gāḍhaṃ ghanānām api  ||232|| 
 
 
 vasurathasya | 
 
 
 anuvanam anuśailaṃ tām anālokya sītāṃ 
 pratidinam atidīnaṃ vīkṣya rāmaṃ virāmam | 
 girir aśanimayo’yaṃ yas tadā na dvidhābhūt 
 kṣitir api na vidīrṇā sāpi sarvaṃsahaiva  ||233|| 
 
 
 śobhākasya | 
 
 
 ko’haṃ vatsa sa ārya eva bhagavān āryaḥ sa ko rāghavaḥ  
 ke yūyaṃ bata nātha nātha kim idaṃ bhṛtyo’smi te lakṣmaṇaḥ | 
 kāntāre kim ihāsmahe bata vṛthā devyā gatir mṛgyate 
 kā devī janakādhirājatanayā hā jānaki kvāsi me  ||234|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 kūjan kuñje kim api karuṇaṃ kandare kāndiśīkaḥ 
 sānau śūnyapraṇihitamanāḥ kānane dhyānanetraḥ | 
 gacchan mūrcchāṃ kusumaśayane vītarāgas taḍāge 
 jīyāj jāyāvirahaviduṣāṃ grāmaṇīḥ rāmabhadraḥ  ||235|| 
   
 ācāryagopīkasya | 
 48. haladharaḥ  
 
 
 surāpīto gotraskhalanaparivṛddhādhikaruṣaḥ 
 prasādaṃ revatyā janayitum anīśaḥ katham api | 
 vicumban saṃśliṣyan stanavasanam asyann avirataṃ 
 madhūn mādāviṣṭaḥ sa kila balabhadro vijayate  ||236|| 
 
 
 lakṣmīdharasya | 
 
 
 āghūrṇadvapuṣaḥ skhalanmṛdugiraḥ kiñcillasadvāsaso 
 revatyaṃ saniṣaṇṇaniḥsahabhujasyātāmranetradyuteḥ | 
 śvāsāmodamadāndhaṣaṭpadakulavyādaṣṭakaṇṭhasrajaḥ 
 pāyāsuḥ parimantharāṇi halino mattasya yātāni vaḥ  ||237|| 
 
 
 kokasya | 
 
 
 bhabhabhramati medinī lalalandate candramāḥ 
 kṛkṛṣṇa vavada drutaṃ hahahasanti kiṃ vṛṣṇayaḥ | 
 sisīdhu mumumuñca me papapapānapātre sthitaḥ 
 madaskhalitam ālapan haladharaḥ śriyaḥ vaḥ kriyāt  ||238|| 
 
 
 puruṣottamadevasya | (su.ra. 127; bā.rā.s 2.4.37) 
 
 
 revatīdaśanocchiṣṭaparipūtapuṭe dṛśau | 
 vahan halī madakṣīvaḥ pānagoṣṭhyāṃ punātu vaḥ  ||239|| 
 
 
 māghabhojadevayoḥ | (sa.ka.ā. 2.61) 
 
 
 bhramati dharaṇīcakraṃ cakre nabhastalayantraṇāt 
 prabhavati na me gātraṃ kiñcit kriyāsu vidhūrṇate | 
 jaladhisalile magnaṃ viśvaṃ vilokya revati 
 trijagad avatāj jalpann evaṃ halī madavihvalaḥ  ||240|| 
 
 
 mādhavasya | 
 
 
 49. buddhaḥ 
 
 
 kāmakrodhau dvayam api yadi pratyanīkaṃ prasiddhaṃ 
 hatvānaṅgaṃ kim iva hi ruṣā sādhitaṃ tryambakena | 
 yas tu kṣāntyā śamayati śataṃ manmathādīnarātīn 
 kalyāṇaṃ vo diśatu sa munigrāmaṇīr arkabandhuḥ  ||241|| 
 
 
 saṅghaśriyaḥ | (su.ra. 4)  
 
 
 pādāmbhojasamīpasannipatitasvarṇāthadehasphuran 
 netrastomatayā parisphuṭamilannīlābjapūjāvidhiḥ | 
 vandārutridaśaudharatramukuṭotsarpatprabhāpallava 
 pratyunmīladapūrvacīvarapaṭaḥ śākyo muniḥ pātu vaḥ  ||242|| 
 
 
 vasukalpasya | (su.ra. 15) 
 
 
 kāruṇyāmṛtakandalīsumanasaḥ prajñāvadhūmauktika 
 grīvālaṅkaraṇaśriyaḥ śamasaritpūrocchalacchīkarāḥ | 
 te maulau bhavatāṃ milantu jagatīrājyābhiṣekocita 
 sragbhedā abhayapradānacaraṇapreṅkhannakhāgrāṃśavaḥ  ||243|| 
 
 
 śrīdharanandinaḥ | (su.ra. 7) 
 
 
 śīlāmbhaḥpariṣekaśītaladṛḍhadhyānālavālasphurad 
 dānaskandhamahonnatiḥ pṛthutaraprajñollasatpallavaḥ | 
 deyāt tubhyaṃ avārthavīryaviṭapaḥ kṣāntiprasūnodgamaḥ 
 succhāyaḥ ṣaḍabhijñakalpaviṭapīsambodhabījaṃ phalam  ||244|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (su.ra. 8) 
 
 
 yadākhyānāsaṅgād uṣasi punate vācam ṛṣayo 
 yadīyaḥ saṅkalpo hṛdi sukṛtināmeva ramate | 
 sa sārvaḥ sarvajñaḥ pathi nirapavāde kṛtapado 
 jino jantūn uccair damayatu bhavāvartapatitān  ||245|| 
 
 
 maṅgalasya | 
 
 
 50. kalkī 
 
 
 bhrāntvā mahīṃ tata itas turagādhirūḍho 
 vedadviṣo vidalayan dalitākhilāśaḥ | 
 devo nivartitakaliḥ kṛtamārgadarśī 
 kalkaṃ sa te haratu kalkikule bhaviṣyan  ||246|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 vāmanād aṇutamād anu jīyās 
 tvaṃ trivikrama tanūbhṛtadikkaḥ | 
 vītahiṃsanapathād atha buddhāt 
 kalkitāhatasamasta namaste  ||247|| 
 
 
 śrīharṣasya | (Nc 21.96) 
 
 
 kalkī kalkaṃ haratu jagataḥ sphūrjadūrjasvitejā 
 vedocchedasphuritaduritadhvaṃsane dhūmaketuḥ | 
 yenotkṣipya kṣaṇam asilatāṃ dhūmavat kalmaṣecchān 
 mlecchān hatvā dalitakalinākāri satyāvatāraḥ  ||248|| 
 
 
 jayadevasya |  
 
 
 āghrāṇaśravaṇāvalokanarasāsvādādayaś cumbana 
 śraddhā vāg viṣavarṣaṇaṃ ca śiraso doṣā ime yair janaḥ | 
 mūḍho laṅghitasatpatho’yam iti saṃkruddhaḥ śaṭhānāṃ haṭhād yaḥ 
 śīrṣāṇi kṛpāṇapāṇir alunāt tasmai namaḥ kalkine  ||249|| 
 
 
 kuladevasya |  
 
 
 tīrthānāṃ śatam asti kintu phalati śraddhābharādity aser 
 dhārātīrhtam apūrvam eva kalayan kalkī śivāyāstu vaḥ | 
 yat prāpyākhilavedabhedakadhiyaḥ śraddhātiraskāriṇaḥ 
 śakrasyātithayo bhavanti bhavaenṣv enasvino jantavaḥ  ||250|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 51. kṛṣṇaśaiśavam 
 
 
 kṛṣṇenādya gatena rantumanasā mṛdbhakṣitā svecchayā 
 satyaṃ kṛṣṇa ka evam āha musalī mithyāmba paśyānanam | 
 vyādehīti vidārite śiśumukhe dṛṣṭvā samastaṃ jagan 
 mātā yasya jagāma vismayapadaṃ pāyāt sa vaḥ keśava  ||251|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (sa.ka.ā.v 23, śā.pa. 4016) 
 
 
 līlottānaśayo’pi gopanivahair udgīyamāneṣv ati 
 prauḍhaprauḍhamurārivikramakathāgīteṣu dattaśravāḥ | 
 kasmiṃścit kṣubhitaḥ kuto’pi calitaḥ kutrāpi romāñcitaḥ 
 kvāpi prasphuritaḥ kuto’pi hasitaḥ prāpto hariḥ pātu vaḥ  ||252|| 
 
 
 mahīdharasya | 
 
 
 nyañcann udañcan bahuśaḥ kathaṃcid 
 udañcito vephathumān harir vaḥ | 
 devo’si devo’si sapāṇitālaṃ 
 yaśodayoktaḥ prahasan punātu  ||253|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 adharamadhure kaṇṭhaṃ kaṇṭhe sacāṭu dṛśau dṛśor  
 alikam alike kṛtvā gopījanena sasambhramam | 
 śiśur iti rudan kṛṣṇo vakṣaḥsthale nihitaś cirān 
 nibhṛtapulakaḥ smeraḥ pāyāt smarālasavigrahaḥ  ||254|| 
 
 
 
 divākaradattsya | (padyā. 135; bā.rā.k 5.1751) 
 
 
 brūmas tvaccaritaṃ tavādhijanani cchadmātibālyākṛte 
 tvaṃ yādṛg girikandareṣu nayanānandaḥ kuraṅgīdṛśām | 
 ity uktaḥ parilehanacchalatayā nyastāṅguliḥ svānane 
 gopībhiḥ purataḥ punātu jagatīm uttānasupto hariḥ  ||255|| 
 
 
 
 vanamālinaḥ | (padyā. 135) 
 
 
 52. kṛṣṇakaumāram 
 
 
 vatsa sthavarakandareṣu vicaran dūrapracāre gavāṃ 
 hiṃsrān vīkṣya puraḥ purāṇapuruṣaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ dhyāsyasi | 
 ity uktasya yaśodayā murāripor avyāj jaganti sphurad 
 bimboṣṭhadvayagāḍhapīḍanavaśād avyaktabhāvaṃ smitam  ||256|| 
 
 
 
 abhinandasya | (su.ra. 144, padyā. 149) 
 
 
 śyāmoccandrā svapiti na śiśo naiti mām amba nidrā 
 nidrāhetoḥ śṛṇu kathāṃ kām apūrvāṃ kuruṣva | 
 vyaktaḥ stambhān naraharir abhūd dānavaṃ dārayiṣyann 
 ity uktasya smitam udayate devakīnandanasya  ||257|| 
 
 
 
 śatānandasya | (su.ra. 123; Pk 151 sarvānandasya; bā.rā.k 5.1761) 
 
 
 mā dūraṃ vraja vatsa tiṣṭhati puras te lūnakarṇo vṛkaḥ 
 potān atti iti prapañcacaturodārā yaśodāgiraḥ | 
 ākarṇyocchaladacchahāsavikasadbimbābhadantacchada 
 dvandvodīritadantamauktikamaṇiḥ kṛṣṇaḥ sa puṣṇātu vaḥ  ||258|| 
 
 
 kasyacit |  
 
 
 kālindīpuline mayā na na mayā śīlopaśalye na na 
 nyagrodhasya tale mayā na na mayā rādhāpituḥ prāṅgane | 
 dṛṣṭaḥ kṛṣṇa itīrite saniyamaṃ gopair yaśodāpater 
 vismerasya puro hasan nijagṛhān niryan hariḥ pātu vaḥ  ||259|| 
 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | (padyā. 148) 
 
 
 manthānam ujjha mathituṃ dadhi na kṣamas tvaṃ 
 bālo’si vatsa virameti yaśodayoktaḥ | 
 kṣīrābdhimanthanavidhismṛtijātahāso 
 vāñchāspadaṃ diśatu vo vāsudevasūnuḥ  ||260|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 53. kṛṣṇasvapnāyitam 
 
 
 śambho svāgatam āsyatām ita ito vāmena padmodbhava 
 krauñcāre kuśalaṃ sukhaṃ surapate vitteśa no dṛśyate | 
 itthaṃ svapnagatasya kaiṭabharipoḥ śrutvā jananyā giraḥ  
 kiṃ kiṃ bālaka jalpasīty anucitaṃ thūthūtkṛtaṃ pātu vaḥ  ||261|| 
 
 
 
 mayūrasya (KKA 2.59, padyā. 146; bā.rā.k 5.1758) 
 
 
 dhīrā dharitri bhāva bhāram avehi śāntaṃ 
 nanv eṣa kaṃsahatakaṃ vinipātayāmi | 
 ity adbhutastimitagopavadhūśrutāni 
 svapnāyitāni vasudevaśiśor jayanti  ||262|| 
 
 
 
 abhinandasya | (padyā. 147) 
 
 
 ete lakṣmaṇa jānakīvirahiṇaṃ māṃ khedayanty ambudā 
 marmāṇīva ca ghaṭṭayanty alam amī krūrāḥ kadambānilāḥ | 
 itthaṃ vyāhṛtapūrvajanmaviraho yo rādhayā vīkṣitaḥ  
 serṣyaṃ śaṅkitayā sa vaḥ sukhayatu svapnāyamāno hariḥ  ||263|| 
 
 
 
 śubhāṅkasya | (KK 2.69(70); su.ra. 131, padyā. 252) 
 
 
 kālindīpulināntavañjulalatā kuñja kutaścit kramāt 
 suptasyaiva mithaḥ kathājuṣi śanaiḥ saṃvāhikāmaṇḍale | 
 vaidehīṃ daśakandharo’paharatīty ākarṇya kaṃsadviṣo 
 huṃ huṃ vatsa dhanur dhanur iti vyagrā giraḥ pāntu vaḥ  ||264|| 
 
 
 viriñceḥ | 
 
 
 nirmagnena mayāmbhasi smarabhayād ālī samāliṅgitā 
 kenālīkam idaṃ tavādya kathitaṃ rādhe mudhā tāmyasi | 
 itthaṃ svapnaparamparāsu śayane śrutvā giraṃ śārṅgiṇaḥ  
 savyājaṃ śithilīkṛtaḥ kamalayā kaṇṭhagrahaḥ pātu vaḥ  ||265|| 
 
 
 
 kasyacit | (da.rū. under 4.60, padyā. 372) 
 
 
 54. kṛṣṇayauvanam 
 
 
 sottāpaṃ jaratītbhir aphuṭarasaṃ bālābhir unmīlita 
 śvāsaṃ veśma suvāsinībhir adhikākṛtaṃ bhujiṣyājanaiḥ | 
 pratyagraprakaṭīkṛtārti kulaṭāsārthena dṛṣṭaṃ harer 
 avyād vo navayauvanotsavadaśānirvyājamugdhaṃ vapuḥ  ||266|| 
 
 
 bhaṭṭaśālīyapītāmbarasya | 
 
 
 rādhāyām anubaddhanarmanibhṛtākāraṃ yaśodābhayād 
 abhyarṇeṣv atinirjaneṣu yamunārodholatāveśmasu | 
 mandākṣaślathavallavānukaraṇakrīḍasya kaṃsadviṣo 
 labdhaṃ yauvanamātrayā vijayate gambhīraśobhaṃ vapuḥ  ||267|| 
 
 
 abhinandasya | 
 
 
 vatsa tvaṃ navayauvano’si capalāḥ prāyeṇa gopastriyaḥ 
 kaṃso bhūpatir abjanālabhiduragrīvā vayaṃ goduhaḥ | 
 saiṣānarthaparampareti bhagavaty āśaṅktātikrame 
 kṛṣṇe tadvinayāya nandagṛhiṇīśikṣoktayaḥ pāntu vaḥ  ||268|| 
 
 
 vardhamānasya | 
 
 
 ārūḍhāntarayauvanasya parito goṣṭhīr anubhrāmyatas 
 tat tat tāsu manogataṃ sunibhṛtaṃ saṃvyācikīrṣor hareḥ | 
 vegād ucchalitāsphuṭākṣaradaśā garbhāstrapāgauravāt 
 pratyañco valitā bhavantu bhavatāṃ kṛtyāya vāgūrmayaḥ  ||269|| 
 
 
 cakrapāṇeḥ | 
 
 
 āhūtādya mayotsave niśi gṛhaṃ śūnyaṃ vimucyāgatā 
 kṣīvaḥ preṣyajanaḥ kathaṃ kulavadhūr ekākinī yāsyati | 
 vatsa tvaṃ tad imāṃ nayālayam iti śrutvā yaśodāgiro 
 rādhāmādhavayor jayanti madhurasmerālasā dṛṣṭayaḥ  ||270|| 
 
 
 
 śrīmatkeśavasenadevasya | (padyā. 206) 
 
 
 55. harikrīḍā 
 
 
 iha niculanikuñje madhyamadhyāsya rantur 
 vijanam ajani śayyā kasya bālapravālaiḥ | 
 iti nigadati vṛnde yoṣitāṃ pāntu yuṣmān 
 smitaśavalitarādhāmādhavālokitāni  ||271|| 
 
 
 (padyā. 201) 
 
 
 kṛṣṇa tvadvanamālayā saha kṛtaṃ kenāpi kuñjāntare 
 gopīkuntalabarhadāma tad idaṃ prāptaṃ mayā gṛhyatām | 
 itthaṃ dugdhamukhena gopaśiśunākhyāne trapānamrayo 
 rādhāmādhavayor jayanti balitasmerālasā dṛṣṭayaḥ  ||272|| 
 
 
 
 lakṣmaṇasenadevasya | (padyā. 202) 
 
 
 bhrūvallīcalanaiḥ kayāpi nayanonmeṣaiḥ kayāpi smita 
 jyotsnāvicchuritaiḥ kayāpi nibhṛtaṃ sambhāvitasyādhvani | 
 garvād bhedakṛtāvahelavinayaśrībhāji rādhānane 
 sātaṅkānunayaṃ jayanti patitāḥ kaṃsadviṣaḥ dṛṣṭayaḥ  ||273|| 
 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | (padyā. 259, RKAD 129) 
 
 
 vyālāḥ santi tamālavalliṣu vṛtaṃ vṛndāvanaṃ vānarair 
 unnakraṃ yamunāmbu ghoravadanavyāghrā gireḥ sandhayaḥ | 
 itthaṃ gopakumārakeṣu vadataḥ kṛṣṇasya tṛṣṇottara 
 smerābhīravadhūniḍedhinayanasyākuñcanaṃ pātu vaḥ  ||274|| 
 
 
 ācāryagopīkasya | 
 
 
 saṅketīkṛtakokilādininadaṃ kaṃsadviṣaḥ kurvato 
 dvāronmocanalolaśaṅkhavalayakvāṇaṃ muhuḥ śṛṇvataḥ | 
 keyaṃ keyam iti pragalbhajaratīvākyena dūnātmano 
 rādhāprāṅgaṇakoṇakoliviṭapikroḍe gatā śarvarī  ||275|| 
 
 
 
 ācārya gopīkasya (padyā. 205; bā.rā.k 5.1159) 
 
 
 56. praśnottaram 
 
 
 rādhe tvaṃ kupitā tvam eva kupitā ruṣṭāsi bhūmer yato 
 mātā tvaṃ jagatāṃ tvam eva jagatāṃ mātā na vijño’paraḥ | 
 devi tvaṃ parihāsakelikalahe’nantā tvam evety asau 
 smero vallavasundarīm avanamac chauriḥ śriyaḥ vaḥ kriyāt  ||276|| 
 
 
 
 vākpateḥ | (su.ra. 108; padyā. 284) 
 
 
 ko’yaṃ dvāri hariḥ prayāhy upavanaṃ śākhāmṛgeṇātra kiṃ 
 kṛṣṇo’haṃ dayite bibhemi sutarāṃ kṛṣṇaḥ kathaṃ vānaraḥ | 
 mugdhe’haṃ madhusūdano vraja latāṃ tām eva puṣpānvitām 
 itthaṃ nirvacanīkṛto dayitayā hrīṇo hariḥ pātu vaḥ  ||277|| 
 
 
 śubhaṅkarasya | (su.ra. 109, Sv. 104, śā.pa. 122) 
 
 
 kas tvaṃ bho niśi keśavaḥ śirasijai :y kiṃ nāma garvāyase 
 bhadre śaurir ahaṃ guṇaiḥ pitṛgataiḥ putrasya kiṃ syād iha | 
 cakrī candramukhi prayacchasi na me kuṇḍīṃ ghaṭīṃ dohanīm 
 itthaṃ gopavadhūjitottaratayā hrīṇo hariḥ pātu vaḥ  ||278|| 
 
 
 
 kasyacit | (padyā. 282) 
 
 
 vāsaḥ samprati keśava kva bhavato mugdhekṣaṇe nanv idaṃ 
 vāsaṃ brūhi śaṭha prakāmasubhage tvadgātrasaṃsargataḥ | 
 yāminyām uṣitaḥ kva dhūrta vitanur muṣṇāti kiṃ yāminī 
 śaurir gopavadhūṃ chalaiḥ parihasann evaṃvidhaiḥ pātu vaḥ  ||279|| 
 
 
 
 kasyacit | (padyā. 283; bha.ra.si. 2.1.83) 
 
 
 kuśalaṃ rādhe sukhito’si kaṃsa kaṃ sa kva nu sā rādhā | 
 iti pālīprativacanair vilakṣahāso harir jayati  ||280|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (sa.ka.ā. 2.351) 
 57. veṇunādaḥ 
 
 
 kṛṣṇaḥ pātu sa yasya saṃsadi gavāṃ veṇupraṇādor mayo 
 gopīnām anuvāsaraṃ navanavā ghūrṇanti karṇodare | 
 tadvaktrāsavavāsitā iva tadākūtiprapañcā iva  
 bhrāmyattatkarapallavāṅguligalallāvaṇyaliptā iva  ||281|| 
 
 
 lakṣmīdharasya | 
 
 
 tiryakkandharam aṃsadeśamilitaśrotrāvataṃsaṃ sphurad 
 barhottambhitakeśapāśam anṛjubhrūvallarīvibhramam | 
 guñjadveṇuniveśitādharapuṭaṃ sākūtarādhānana 
 nyastāmīlitadṛṣṭi gopavapuṣo viṣṇor mukhaṃ pātu vaḥ  ||282|| 
 
 
 
 lakṣmaṇasenadevasya | (padyā. 260) 
 
 
 sāyaṃ vyāvartamānakhilasurabhikulāhvānasaṃketanāmāny 
 abhīrīvṛndaceto haṭhaharaṇakalāsiddhamantrākṣarāṇi | 
 saubhāgyaṃ vaḥ samantād dadhatu madhubhidaḥ keligopālamūrteḥ 
 sānandakṛṣṭavṛndāvanarasikamṛgaśreṇayo veṇunādāḥ  ||283|| 
 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | (padyā. 5) 
 
 
 mandrakvāṇitaveṇur ahni śithile vyāvartayan gokulaṃ 
 barhāpīḍakam uttamāṅgaracitaṃ godhūlidhumraṃ dadhat | 
 mlāyantyā vanamālayā parigataḥ śrānto’pi ramyākṛtir 
 gopastrīnayanotsavo vitaratu śreyāṃsi vaḥ keśavaḥ  ||284|| 
 
 
 
 kasyacit | (Kvs 22, SKM 1.57.4, su.ra. 110, padyā. 256) 
 
 
 aṃsāsaktakapolavaṃśavadanavyāsaktabimbādhara 
 dvandvodīritamandamandapavanaprārabdhamugdhadhvaniḥ | 
 īṣadvakrimalolahāranikaraḥ pratyekarokānana 
 nyañcaccañcadudañcadaṅgulicayas tvāṃ pātu rādhādhavaḥ  ||285|| 
 
 
 
 keśarakīlīyanāthokasya | (padyā. 261, nāthokasya) 
 
 
 58. gītam 
 
 
 sañjāte virahe kayāpi hṛdaye sandānite cintayā 
 kālindītaṭavetasīvanaghanacchāyāniṣaṇṇātmanaḥ | 
 pāyāsuḥ kalakaṇṭhakūjitakalā gopasya kaṃsadviṣo 
 jihvāvarjitatālumūrcchitamarudvisphāritā gītayaḥ  ||286|| 
 
 
 
 kasyacit | (padyā. 240) 
   
 kālindījalakuñjavañjulavanacchāyāniṣaṇṇātmano 
 rādhābaddhanavānurāgarasikasyotkaṇṭhitaṃ gāyataḥ | 
 tat pāyād apariskhalajjalaruhāpīḍaṃ kalaspṛṅnata 
 grīvottānitakarṇatarṇakakulair ākarṇyamānaṃ hareḥ  ||287|| 
 
 
 udbhaṭasya |  
 
 
 devas tvām ekajaṅghāvalayitaguḍīmūrdhni vinyastabāhur 
 gāyan goyuddhagītir uparacitaśiraḥśekharaḥ pragraheṇa | 
 darpasphūrjan mahokṣadvayasamarakalābaddhadīrghānubandhaḥ 
 krīḍāgopālamūrtir muraripur avatād āttagorakṣalīlaḥ  ||288|| 
 
 
 
 yogeśvarasya | (su.ra. 129, sonnokasya; padyā. 152)  
 
 
 yāte dvāravatīpuraṃ muraripau tadvastrasaṃvyānayā 
 kālindītaṭakuñjavañjulalatām ālāmbya sotkaṇṭhayā | 
 udgītaṃ gurubāṣpagadgadagalattārasvaraṃ rādhayā 
 yenāntarjalacāribhir jalacarair apy utkam utkūjitam  ||289|| 
 
 
 
 kasyacit | (Dhv, Vak 2.59; etc.; padyā. 373 aparājitasya, u.nī.
                            14.188) 
 
 
 yāni taccaritāmṛtāni rasanālehyāni dhanyātmanāṃ 
 ye vā śaiśavacāpalyavyatikarā rādhāvarodhonmukhāḥ | 
 yā vā bhāvitaveṇugītagatayo līlāmukhāmbhoruhe 
 dhārāvāhikayā vahantu hṛdaye tāny eva tāny eva me  ||290|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (KKA 1.106) 
 
 
 59. kṛṣṇabhujaḥ 
 
 
 bhrāmyadbhāsvaramandarādriśikharavyāghaṭṭanād visphurat 
 keyūrāḥ puruhūtakuñjarakaraprāgbhārasaṃvardhinaḥ | 
 daityendrapramadākapolavilasatpatrāṅkuracchedino 
 dordaṇḍāḥ kalilkālakalmaṣamuṣaḥ kaṃsadviṣo pātu vaḥ  ||291|| 
 
 
 
 kasyacit | (padyā. 386) 
 
 
 lakṣmyāḥ keśaprasavarajasāṃ bindubhiḥ sāndrapātair 
 udvarṇaśrīr ghananidhuvanaklāntinidrāntareṣu | 
 dordaṇḍo’sau jayati jayinaḥ śārṅgiṇo mandarādri 
 grāvaśreṇikaṣamasṛṇakṣuṇṇukeyūrapatraḥ  ||292|| 
 
 
 bhagīrathasya | (su.ra. 142) 
 
 
 ye govardhanamūlakardamarasavyādaṣṭabarhacchadā 
 ye vṛndāvanakukṣiṣu vrajavadhūlīlopadhānāni ca | 
 ye cābhyaṅgasugandhayaḥ kuvalayāpīḍasya dānāmbhasā 
 te vo maṅgalam ādiśantu satataṃ kaṃsadviṣo bāhavaḥ  ||293|| 
 
 
 
 śubhāṅkasya | (padyā. 4) 
 
 
 jayaśrīvinyastair mahita iva mandārakusumaiḥ  
 svayaṃ sindūreṇa dviparaṇamudā mudrita iva |  
 bhujāpīḍakrīḍāhatakuvalayāpīḍakariṇaḥ 
 prakīrṇāsṛgbindur jayati bhujadaṇḍo murajitaḥ  ||294|| 
 
 
 jayadevasya | (Gg 11.35) 
 
 
 pāntu vo jaladaśyāmāḥ 
 śārṅgajyāghātakarkaśāḥ | 
 trailokyanagarastambhāś 
 catvāro haribāhavaḥ  ||295|| 
 
 
 śrīvyāsapādānām | (śā.pa. 113) 
 60. govardhanoddhāraḥ  
 
 
 satrāsarti yaśodayā priyaguṇaprītekṣaṇaṃ rādhayā 
 lagnair vallavasūnubhiḥ sarabhasaṃ sambhāvitātmorjitaiḥ | 
 bhītānanditavismitena viṣamaṃ nandena cālokitaḥ  
 pāyād vaḥ karapadmasusthitamahāśailaḥ salīlo hariḥ  ||296|| 
 
 
 
 sollokasya | (su.ra. 140 sonnokasya; padyā. 264 sohnokasya) 
 
 
 ekenaiva cirāya kṛṣṇa bhavatā govardhano’yaṃ dhṛtaḥ  
 śrānto’si kṣaṇam āssva sāmpratam amī sarve vayaṃ dadhmahe | 
 ity ullāsitadoṣṇi gopanivahe kiñcid bhujākuñcana 
 nyañcacchailabharārdite viruvati smero hariḥ pātu vaḥ  ||297|| 
 
 
 
 śaraṇasya | (padyā. 265) 
 
 
 snehād aṃsataṭe’valambya caraṇāv āropya tatpādayor 
 dūrād astamahīdharasya tanutām āśaṅkya doṣṇo hareḥ | 
 śailoddhārasahāyatāṃ jigamiṣor aprāptagovardhanā 
 rādhāyāḥ suciraṃ jayanti gagane bandhyāḥ karabhrāntayaḥ  ||298|| 
 
 
 śatānandasya || 
 
 
 dūraṃ dṛṣṭipathāt tirobhava harer govardhanaṃ vibhratas 
 tvayy āsaktadṛśaḥ kṛśodari karasrasto’sya mā bhūd ayam | 
 gopīnām iti jalpitaṃ kalayato rādhānirodhāśrayaṃ 
 śvāsāḥ śailabharaśramabhramakarāḥ kaṃsadviṣaḥ pāntu vaḥ  ||299|| 
 
 
 
 śubhāṅkasya | (padyā. 267) 
 
 
 mugdhe nātha kim āttha tanvi śikhariprāgbhārabhugno bhujaḥ 
 sāhāyyaṃ priya kiṃ bhajāmi subhage dorvallim āyāsaya | 
 ity ullāsitabāhumūlavicalaccelāñcalavyaktayo 
 rādhāyāḥ kucayor jayanti calitāḥ kaṃsadviṣo dṛṣṭayaḥ  ||300|| 
 
 
 śaṅkarasya |  
 61. utkaṇṭhā 
 
 
 ratnacchāyācchuritajaladhau mandire dvārakāyā 
 rukmiṇyāpi prabalapulakodbhedam āliṅgitasya | 
 viśvaṃ pāyān masṛṇayamunātīravānīrakuñje 
 rādhākelīparimalabharadhyānamūrcchā murāreḥ  ||301|| 
 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | (padyā. 371, u.nī. 14.184; Jīva and VCT to bha.ra.si.
                            2.4.178) 
 
 
 kalindīm anukūlakomalarayām indīvaraśyāmalāḥ  
 śailopāntabhuvaḥ kadambakusumair āmodinaḥ kandarāt | 
 rādhāṃ ca prathamābhisāramadhurāṃ jātānutāpaḥ smarann 
 astu dvāravatīpatis tribhuvanāmodāya dāmodaraḥ  ||302|| 
 
 
 
 śaraṇasya | (padyā. 369) 
 
 
 kāmaṃ kāmayate na kelinalinīṃ nāmodate kaumudī 
 nisyandair na samīhate mṛgadṛśām ālāpalīlām api | 
 sīdann eṣa niśāsu niḥsahatanur bhogābhilāṣālasair 
 aṅgais tāmyati cetasi vrajavadhūm ādhāya mugdho hariḥ  ||303|| 
 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (padyā. 370) 
 
 
 pratyagrojjhitagokulasya śayanād utsvapnamūḍhasya māṃ 
 mā gotraskhalitād upaitu ca divā rādheti bhīror ati | 
 rātrāv asvapato divā ca vijane lakṣmīti cābhyasyato 
 rādhāṃ saṃsmarataḥ śriyaṃ ramayataḥ khedo hareḥ pātu vaḥ  ||304|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (sa.ka.ā.v 448) 
 
 
 talpīkṛtasya bhujagādhipateḥ phaṇāyāṃ 
 ratneṣu saṃvalitabimbatasyācalāyāḥ | 
 kṛṣṇāvatārakṛtagopavadhūsahasra 
 saṅgasmṛtir jayati sotkalikasya viṣṇoḥ  ||305|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 62. gopīsandeśaḥ 
 
 
 te govardhanakandarāḥ sa yamunākacchaḥ sa ceṣṭāraso 
 bhāṇḍīraḥ sa vamaspatiḥ sahacarās te tac ca goṣṭhāṅganam | 
 kiṃ dvāravatībhujaṅga hṛdayaṃ nāyāti doṣair apīty 
 avyād vo hṛdi duḥsahaṃ vrajavadhūsandeśaśalyaṃ hareḥ  ||306|| 
 
 
 
 nīlasya | (padyā. 375) 
 
 
 pāntha dvāravatīṃ prayāsi yadi he tad devakīnandano 
 vaktavyaḥ smaramohamantravivaśo gopyo’pi nāmojjhitāḥ | 
 etāḥ kelikadambadhūlipaṭalair ālokaśūnyā diśaḥ  
 kālindītaṭabhūmayo bhavato nāyānti cittāspadam  ||307|| 
 
 
 
 govardhanācāryasya | (padyā. 374; Çṛṅgāraprakāśa, check su.ra.) 
 
 
 upanaya masiṃ patraṃ cedaṃ likhāmi kim atra vā 
 tvam iti vinayabhraṃśo yūyaṃ tviti praṇayakṣatiḥ | 
 suhṛd iti mṛṣā nāthety ūnaṃ nṛpeti taṭasthatā  
 katham iti tataḥ sandeṣṭavyo mayā yadunandanaḥ  ||308|| 
 
 
 puṃsokasya || 
 
 
 kālindyāḥ pulinaṃ pradoṣamaruto ramyāḥ śaśaṅkāṃśavaḥ  
 santāpaṃ na harantu nāma nitarāṃ kurvanti kasmāt punaḥ | 
 sandiṣṭaṃ vrajayoṣitām iti hareḥ saṃśṛṇvato’ntaḥpure  
 niḥśvāsāḥ prasṛtā jayanti ramaṇīsaubhāgyagarvacchidaḥ  ||309||
