 hastāvāpitadātrarajjulaguḍair vṛddhair avṛddhaiḥ saha 
 tyaktvā śālicikartiṣām ita ito dhāvanty amī pāmarāḥ  ||1340|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 300) 
 
 
 174. hemantapathikaḥ | 
 
 
 mātar dharmapare dayāṃ kuru mayi śrānte ca vaideśike 
 dvārālindakakoṇakeṣu nibhṛtaṃ sthitvā kṣipāmi kṣapām | 
 ity evaṃ gṛhiṇīpracaṇḍavadanāvākyena nirbhartsito 
 hastanyastapalālamuṣṭivibhavaḥ pānthaḥ śanair gacchati  ||1341|| 
 
 
 śatānandasya | (Sv 2416, śā.pa. 580, sū.mu. 96.3, su.ra. 1316) 
 
 
 svairaṃ saṃcarati pradoṣamaruti tv aṅgattuṣāre jarat 
 tantucchedaviśīrṇasandhiśakalavyākṛṣṭakanthāñcalaḥ | 
 śītārtaḥ karuṇārdrahālikavinirdiṣṭe kṣipāmi kṣapām  
 ity uccārya palālakūṭakuhare śrāntaḥ prasuptodhvagaḥ  ||1342|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 rundhānaḥ karṇasandhī śiśirabharabhayāt pāṇiyugmena gāḍhaṃ 
 bāḍhaṃ vinyasya bāhudvayam urasi raṇaddantapaṅktiḥ samantāt | 
 aṣṭīvadbhyāṃ vicumbannipatitacibukaṃ pṛṣṭhamātraṃ himartau 
 śete saṃchādya sadyas truṭitacirajaratkanthayā pāntharaṅkaḥ  ||1343|| 
 
 
 suvratadattasya | 
 
 
 puṇyānau pūrṇavāñchaḥ prathamam agaṇitaploṣadoṣaḥ pradoṣe 
 pānthas taptvā prasuptaḥ pratatatanutṛṇe dhāmani grāmadevyāḥ | 
 utkampī karpaṭārghe jarati padahaticchidrite cchinnanidro 
 vāte vāti prakamaṃ himakaṇini kaṇan koṇataḥ koṇam eti  ||1344|| 
 
 
 bāṇasya | (Sv 1857, śā.pa. 3946, sū.mu. 64.12, su.ra. 1305) 
 
 
 saṃviṣṭo grāmadevyās tṛṇaghaṭitakuṭīkuḍyakoṇaikadeśe 
 śīte saṃvāti vāyau himakaṇini kaṇahantapaṅktidvayāgraḥ | 
 pānthaḥ kanthāṃ niśīthe parikalitajarattantusantānagurvīṃ 
 grīvāpādāgrajānudvayaghaṭanaraṭatkarpaṭāṃ prāvṛṇoti  ||1345|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (śā.pa. 3947, sū.mu. 64.13) 
 
 
 175. śiśiraḥ 
 
 
 dhanyānāṃ varapūritamukhaśyāmāṅganāliṅgana 
 prāptānekasukhapramodavapuṣāṃ ramyas tuṣārodgamaḥ | 
 asmākaṃ tu vidīrṇakhaṇḍitapaṭapracchāditodghāṭita 
 kroḍasvīkṛtajānuvepathumatāṃ cetaḥ paraṃ sīdati  ||1346|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 312) 
 
 
 virahivanitāvaktraupamyaṃ bibharti niśāpatir 
 galitavibhavasyājhevādya dyutir masṛṇā raveḥ | 
 abhinavavadhūroṣasvāduḥ karīṣatanūnapād 
 asaralajanāśelṣakrūras tuṣārasamīraṇaḥ  ||1347|| 
 
 
 bhāsasya | (su.ra. 317, abhinandasya) 
 
 
 ete vāmavilocanākucasakhaiḥ soḍhavyaśītārtayaḥ 
 prāptāḥ paścimasaindhavasya marutaḥ premacchido vāsarāḥ | 
 yatrāpāsya purāṇapaṅkajamayaṃ devaḥ saśṛṅgārabhūr 
 ādatte navakundakuḍmalaśikhānirmāṇam anyad dhanuḥ  ||1348|| 
 
 
 prabhākarasya  
 
 
 kampante kapayo bhṛśaṃ jaḍakṛśaṃ gojāvikaṃ glāyati 
 śvā cullīkuharodaraṃ kṣaṇam api kṣipto’pi naivojjhati | 
 śītārtivyasanāturaḥ punar ayaṃ dīno janaḥ kūrvavat 
 svāny aṅgāni śarīra eva hi nije nihnotum ākāṅkṣati  ||1349|| 
 
 
 śatānandasya | (sa.ka.ā. 3.10, su.ra. 313 lakṣmīdharasya, sū.mu.
                            63.17) 
 
 
 pākakṣāmatilāḥ samutsukayituṃ śaktāḥ kapotān bhuvaḥ 
 śyāmatvaṃ phalapīḍyamānakusumān āpadyate sarṣapān | 
 vāyur vyastaśaṇas tuṣārakaṇavān abhyeti kampapradaḥ 
 pānthaiḥ śuṣkavivādabaddhakalahaiḥ puṇyāgnir āsevyate  ||1350|| 
 
 
 yogeśvarasya | (su.ra. 315) 
 
 
 176. śiśiragrāmaḥ 
 
 
 ābhoginaḥ kim api samprati vāsarānte

 dhūmāvalīvalayamekhalino haranti  ||1351|| 
 
 
 abhinandasya | (su.ra. 303) 
 
 
 udvegaṃ janayanti saṃcitavṛṣavyāptājiropāntakāḥ

 grāmā gomayadhūmasaṃtatiparikliṣṭāruṇaśmaśrubhir

 viriñceḥ |

 177. śiśiraśasyāni 
 
 
 māṣīṇaṃ muṣitaṃ yaveṣu yavasaśyāmacchaviḥ śīryate 
 grāmāntāś ca madhūkadhūsarabhuvaḥ smeraṃ yavānīvanam | 
 puṣpāḍhyāḥ śatapuṣpikāḥ phalabhṛtaḥ siddhyanti siddhārthakāḥ 
 snigdhāḥ vāstukavāstavaḥ stavakitastambā ca kustumbarī  ||1356|| 
 
 
 śubhāṅkasya | (su.ra. 321, śubhāṅgasya) 
 
 
 siddhārthāḥ phalasūcibandhagurubhir lolanty amī pallavair 
 ucchindanty adha eva bandhuratayā kolīphalāny arbhakāḥ | 
 pākapraślathapatrakoṣadalanavyaktāṅkuragranthayo 
 niṣṭhīvanty api hastayantrakalitāḥ puṇḍrekṣayaṣṭyo rasam  ||1357|| 
 
 
 vācaspateḥ (su.ra. 316) 
 
 
 īṣallomaśabhāvabhāñji kapiśaśyāmānubandhacchavī

 spardhāvanti phalāni bibhrati parīṇāmābhirāmaśriyaḥ  ||1358||

 siddhārthayaṣṭiṣu yathodayahīyamāna 
 santānabaddhaphalasūcitaparamparāsu |

 lakṣmīdharasya | (su.ra. 1184, kasyacit)

 vilīnāśābandhāḥ śukaśiśukatuṇḍacchavimuṣaḥ  ||1360||

 178. śiśirasukham 
 
 
 dvāraṃ gṛhasya pihitaṃ śayanasya pārśve

 sadyo dhūpitam utpradīpam abhitaḥ saṃruddhavātāyanaṃ

 viriñceḥ | 
 
 
 cūḍāgarbhaniveśidāmavikalaṃ muktāphalair bhūṣaṇaiḥ

 179. uccāvacaṃ 
 
 
 paśyāmo mayi kiṃ prapadyata iti sthairyaṃ mayālambitaṃ 
 kiṃ mām ālapatīty ayaṃ khala śaṭhaḥ kopas tayāpy āśritaḥ | 
 ity anyonyavilakṣadṛṣṭicature tasminn avasthāntare 
 savyājaṃ hasitaṃ mayā dhṛtiharo bāṣpas tu muktas tayā  ||1366|| 
 
 
 amaroḥ (amaru 20, Kuval., 185) 
 
 
 parimlāne māne mukhaśaśini tasyāḥ karadhṛte 
 mayi kṣīṇopāye praṇipatanamātraikaśaraṇe | 
 tayā pakṣmaprāntavrajapuṭaniruddhena sahasā 
 prasādo bāṣpena stanataṭaviśīrṇena kathitaḥ  ||1367|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva (amaru 21, Sbh 1608, sū.mu. 58.1) 
 
 
 gate premābandhe praṇayabahumāne vigalite 
 nivṛtte sadbhāve jana iva jane gacchati puraḥ | 
 tad utprekṣyotprekṣya priyasakhi gatāṃs tāṃś ca divasān 
 na jāne ko hetur dalati śatadhā yan na hṛdayam  ||1368|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (amaru 38, su.ra. 697, Sbh 1141, śā.pa. 3545, sū.mu. 84.1,
                            Rask 2.263c) 
 
 
 śliṣṭaḥ kaṇṭhe kim iti na mayā mūḍhayā prāṇanāthaś 
 cumbaty asmin vadanavidhutiḥ kiṃ kṛtā kiṃ na dṛṣṭaḥ | 
 noktaḥ kasmād iti navavadhūceṣṭitaṃ cintayantī 
 paścāt tāpaṃ vahati taruṇī premṇi jāte rasajñā  ||1369|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (amaru 56, Sv 2143) 
 
 
 yāvat tvaccaritaṃ prasaṅgata iva prastaumi tāvat tvayā 
 vande tān aham ity udīrya śirasā nyastaḥ praṇāmāñjaliḥ | 
 tad yāvac ca ruṣeva doṣam api te pṛcchāmi nābhāṣya māṃ 
 niḥśvāsaiḥ kiyad aṃśubhiś ca kiyad ākhyātaṃ tavāgastayā  ||1370|| 
 
 
 gotithīyadivākarasya | 
 
 
 iti śrīdharadāsakṛte saduktikarṇāmṛte dviītye’smin  
 madayatu suhṛdaya hāsaṃ śṛṅgārākhyaḥ pravāho’yam | 
 
 iti śrīmahāmāṇḍalikaśrīdharadāsakṛte saduktikarṇāmṛte  
 śṛṅgārapravāho nāma dvitīyaḥ |  
 vīcayaḥ 179 | ślokāḥ 895 |

 (3) 
 cāṭupravāhavīcayaḥ 
 
 
 cāṭuḥ saṃmukhacāṭur vidyāguṇadharmarūpam atha dṛṣṭiḥ | 
 bhujakaracaraṇaṃ preyo’bhidhānam atyukticitroktī  ||1|| 
 api kāryagatī deśāśrayau ca dānaṃ daridrabharaṇaṃ ca | 
 atidānam api ca vikramapauruṣaśauryapratāpatejāṃsi  ||2|| 
 gajavājināvanīkaṃ khaḍgodbhutakhaḍgakupitakṛpāṇau | 
 cāpaṃ prayāṇabhogāvalitūryasvānasainikarajāṃsi  ||3|| 
 aśvarajoraṇadhūlir yuddhaṃ yuddhasthalī ca digvijayaḥ | 
 ripuripunagarīsambhramavairivadhūvairiyoṣidaśrūṇi  ||4|| 
 arinagaravairibhavane yaśasā vīryaṃ yaśaḥ praśastayaśaḥ | 
 kīrtiḥ savīryakīrtiḥ praśastakīrtiś ca kīrtigītiś ca  ||5|| 
 uccāvacaṃ caturbhir yutayā pañcāśatātha vīcīnām | 
 śrīdharadāsena kṛtaḥ kṛtinā cāṭupravāho’yam  ||6||

 1. sāmānyacāṭuḥ 
 
 
 svāminn ambujanātha dhūrjaṭiśiraścūḍāmaṇe candramaḥ  
 pādau vāṃ praṇato’smi sādhu vadataṃ kṣatraprasūtī yuvām | 
 rājā yady upasevitāṅghrir akhilakṣmāpālacūḍāśatair 
 āsīd asti bhaviṣyati kṣititale śrībhojadevopamaḥ  ||1371|| 
 
 
 chittipasya |  
 
 
 kālindi brūhi kubhodbhavajaladhir ahaṃ nāma gṛhṇāsi kasmāc 
 chatror me narmadāhaṃ tvam api vadasi me nāma kasmāt sapatnyāḥ | 
 mālinyaṃ tarhi kasmād anuharasi milatkajjalair mālavīnāṃ 
 bāṣpāmbhobhiḥ kim āsāṃ samajani kupitaḥ kuntalakṣoṇipālaḥ  ||1372|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 dṛptoddāmakarīndravṛndaśitimacchāyeṣu nārārthiṣu 
 pāthodeṣu taṭābhidhātadiksādārabhya nas tāmyati | 
 nūnaṃ mālavarājadigjayavidhau taiḥ pītam ambhonidher 
 mādyadgandhagajasravanmadanadīgandhānubiddhaṃ payaḥ  ||1373|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 āvācāṃ vyaktatāyāḥ kavipadaviṣayeṣv ācacaṣṭe samanyo 
 muktāsmābhir na ko’pi smarapadam avanau saṃstutaḥ satyam etat | 
 mithayitad bhoḥ kathaṃ re nanu śatam akṛthāḥ kuntalendrasya tat tat 
 kāvyastotrāṇi dhik tvāṃ jaḍamaya na manor eva mūrtiprabhedaḥ  ||1374|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 krūre kadru kim āttha dāsi vinate muktāsmi dattvāmṛtaṃ 
 tenānāyi sudhā mudhā tṛṇaliho nāgās tvayā vañcitāḥ | 
 tvatpāpair musitāḥ sutāḥ śṛṇu tṛṇaṃ dattvādya yāvan mukhe 
 baṅgakṣmāpatisaṅgare’pi yad amī jīvanti bhūmībhujaḥ  ||1375|| 
 
 
 ācāryagopīkasya | 
 
 
 2. saṃmukhacāṭuḥ 
 
 
 pūrvaḥ kṛtātmanām asi bhagnānāṃ samiti paścimo dviṣatām | 
 tvaṃ dakṣiṇaḥ praṇamatāṃ tathāpi sarvottaras tvam asi  ||1376|| 
 
 
 yogeśvarasya | 
 
 
 yasya dvīpaṃ dharitrī sa ca jaladhir abhūd yasya gaṇḍūṣatoyaṃ 
 tasyāścaryaikamūrter api nabhasi vapur yatra durlakṣyam āsīt | 
 tatpītaṃ tvadyaśobhis tribhuvanam abhajaṃs tāni viśrāmahetos 
 tac cāntaḥ kaiṭabhāreḥ sa ca tava hṛdaye vandanīyas tvam eva  ||1377|| 
 
 
 tathāgatadāsasya | (su.ra. 1389) 
 
 
 na lopo varṇānāṃ na khalu parataḥ pratyayavidhir 
 vikāro nāsty eva kvacid api na bhagnāḥ prakṛtayaḥ | 
 guṇo vā vṛddhir vā satatam upakārāya jagatāṃ 
 muner dākṣīputrād api tava samarthaḥ padavidhiḥ  ||1378|| 
 
 
 śabdārṇavasya | (su.ra. 1387) 
 
 
 tvaṃ ṣāḍguṇyajuṣāṃ śiromaṇir asi traiguṇyamūrter asāv 
 indus tatra ca ṣoḍaśa tvayi catuḥṣaṣṭhir valante kalāḥ | 
 tasyaikaṃ nanu maṇḍalaṃ tava nava kṣmāmaṇḍalīsiddhayas 
 tejaś candramaso nṛcandra bhavataś caivaṃ davīyo’ntaram  ||1379|| 
 
 
 laṅgadattasya | 
 
 
 pīyūṣaṃ viṣam apy asūta jaladhiḥ kānteḥ kalaṅkasya ca 
 sthānaṃ śītaruciḥ svabhāvakaṭhino dātā ca kalpadrumaḥ | 
 akṣīṇapraṇayāmṛtasya kaluṣair apṛṣṭamūrter asaṃ 
 kṣiptatyāgarasodayasya bhavataḥ sāmyaṃ samabhyetu kaḥ  ||1380|| 
 
 
 śaraṇadevasya | 
 
 
 3. vidyā 
 
 
 vācaṃ niṣprathayanti meyam akhilaṃ puṣṇanti muṣṇanti ca 
 prajñālāñchanam advayaṃ prasuvate sārasvataḥ brāhmaṇaḥ | 
 saubhāgyaṃ duhate śriyaṃ vidadhati śvaḥ śreyase tanvate 
 bhindanti bhramamuktayas tava satām aṣṭau mahāsiddhayaḥ  ||1381|| 
 
 
 bhaṭṭavāmadevasya | 
 
 
 jātāḥ smaḥ prativeśinaḥ padavidāṃ jānanti naḥ śrotriyāḥ 
 ṣaṭkarmādhvani gacchatāṃ ca viduṣāṃ sārthe prapannā vayam | 
 dṛṣṭāḥ smaḥ kavividyayā mukulitair natratribhāgaiś ciraṃ 
 kiṃ vidmaḥ kiyad anyathāstu nikaṣagrāvā bhavādṛgjanaḥ  ||1382|| 
 
 
 vidyāpateḥ | 
 
 
 agrāhyaṃ śravaṇasya bhūṣaṇam alaṅkāro na bhāvocitaḥ 
 kaṇṭhasyāñjanam ujjvalaṃ nayanayoḥ sūkṣmatvam āvekṣitum | 
 vaktrasya kṣaṇiko’dhivāsanavidhiḥ kānte priye nābhava 
 saubhāgyapratikarmanirmitamahāvidyaiva yenātmanaḥ  ||1383|| 
 
 
 śukṣokasya | 
 
 
 kaścid vāco racayitum alaṃ voḍhum evāparas tāḥ 
 sā kalyāṇī matir ubhayathā vismaye nas tanoti | 
 nanv ekasminn atiśayavatāṃ sanniveśo guṇānām 
 ekaḥ sūte kanakam analas tatparīkṣākṣamo’nyaḥ  ||1384|| 
 
 
 kālidāsasya | (su.ra. 1723) 
 
 
 devaḥ sarvavivecanaikanipuṇo devaḥ kavitve gurur 
 devas tarkaniśātanirmalamatiḥ śrīrājacūḍāmaṇiḥ | 
 ity ākarṇya vijṛmbhamāṇapulakasphītā viriśer mukhāḥ 
 saṅgeṣv adya sarasvatī … kṛcchreṇa saṃmāsyati  ||1385|| 
 
 
 vasukalpasya | 
 4. guṇaḥ 
 
 
 ābālyādhigamān mayaiva gamitaḥ koṭiṃ parām unnater 
 asmatsaṅkathanena pārthivasutaḥ sampraty asau lajjate | 
 itthaṃ khinna ivātyayena yaśasā datto’valambo’mbudher 
 yātas tīratapovanāni bhavato vṛddho guṇānāṃ gaṇaḥ  ||1386|| 
 
 
 śrīhanūmataḥ | (su.ra. 1433, sū.mu. 97.14) 
 
 
 sūryo dhāmavatāṃ na kiṃ na kim ayaṃ prahlādakaś candramā 
 gambhīro na kim ambudhiḥ kṣitibhṛtāṃ rāmaḥ sa jetā na kim | 
 kiṃ tv ekaikaguṇastutau na hi vayaṃ śaktās tad etadgaṇa 
 śrotṬṇāṃ sumahotsavāya nṛpate tvām ekam eva stumaḥ  ||1387|| 
 
 
 cchittipasya | 
 
 
 ete śāradakaumudīkulabhuvaḥ kṣīrodadheḥ sodarāḥ 
 śeṣāheḥ suhṛdo vinidrakumudaśreṇīmahaḥsrāviṇaḥ | 
 śītāṃśoḥ sahapāṃśukhelanasakhāḥ svaḥsindhusaṃbandhinaḥ 
 prāleyācalabandhavas tava guṇāḥ kair neha karṇārpitāḥ  ||1388|| 
 
 
 hareḥ | 
 
 
 devasya tripurārihāsamahasi prastūyamāne guṇe 
 prītyā ca śrutikautukena ca balād ākṛṣyamāṇaḥ svayam | 
 ekaṃ saṃnatapakṣma pannagapatir dhatte sahasraṃ dṛśām 
 anyanmantharatārakāviluṭhanād atyantavisphāritam ||1389|| 
 
 
 kasyāpi | 
 
 
 merur daṇḍo yadi ca paṭalaṃ medinīmaṇḍalaṃ syāc 
 cheṣaḥ sūtraṃ samadharaṇam apy eṣa vindhyo mahīdhraḥ | 
 tan mātā ca tripuravijayī keśavo vā yadā syād 
 unmīyeta kṣitipatanaya tvadguṇānāṃ samūhaḥ  ||1390|| 
 
 
 pravarasenasya | 
 
 
 5. dharmaḥ 
 
 
 bhrāntaṃ yena caturbhir eva caraṇaiḥ satyābhidhāne yuge 
 tretāyāṃ tribhir aṅghribhiḥ katham api dvābhyāṃ tato dvāpare | 
 na syās tvaṃ yadi deva paṅgulaguṅdaḥ kāle kalāv utkale 
 so’yaṃ paṅgur avasthitaikacaraṇo dharmaḥ kathaṃ bhrāmyati  ||1391|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 1455, cittūkasya) 
 
 
 ucchann eva kalau vṛṣasya caraṇaśreṇī navīnāṃ punas  
 tāṃ nirmāya kṛtas tvayā punar api nyastaḥ padasyandanaḥ | 
 bhindānais taraṇiṃ tvadastraniyatair etat kilodīritaṃ 
 śrutvānūrurasau vihāya mihiraṃ tvāṃ deva seviṣyate  ||1392|| 
 
 
 ācāryagopīkasya | 
 
 
 padaiś caturbhiḥ sukṛte sthirīkṛte 
 kṛte’munā kena tapaḥ prapedire | 
 bhuvaṃ yad ekāṅghrikaniṣṭhayā spṛśan 
 dadhāvadharmo’pi kṛśas tapasvitām  ||1393|| 
 
 
 śrīharṣasya | (Nc 1.7) 
 
 
 yūpair utkaṭakaṇṭakair iva makhaprodbhūtadhūmodgamair 
 apy andhaṃkaraṇauṣadhair iva pade netre ca jātavyathaiḥ | 
 yasmin dharmapare praśāsati tapaḥsaṃbhedinīṃ medinīm 
 āstām ākramituṃ vilokitum api vyaktaṃ na śaktaḥ kaliḥ  ||1394|| 
 
 
 jayadevasya | 
 
 
 aśrāntaviśrāṇitayajñayūpa 
 stambhāvalīr drāgavalambamānaḥ | 
 yasya svabhāvād bhuvi saṃcacāra  
 kālakramād ekapado’pi dharmaḥ  ||1395|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 6. rūpam  
 
 
 śrīmadrūpaviṭaṅkadeva sakalakṣmāpālacuḍāmaṇe 
 yuktaṃ saṃcaraṇaṃ yad atra bhavataś candreṇa rātrāv api | 
 mā bhūt tvadvadanāvalokanavaśād vrīḍāvilakṣaḥ śaśī 
 mā bhūc ceyam arundhatī bhagavatī duḥśīlatābhājanam  ||1396|| 
 
 
 tribhuvanasarasvatyāḥ | 
 
 
 āvaktrendu tadaṅgam eva sṛjataḥ sraṣṭuḥ samagras tviṣāṃ 
 koṣaḥ śoṣam agād agādhajagatīśilpe’pi nālpāyitaḥ | 
 niḥśeṣadyutimaṇḍalavyayavaśādīṣallabhais tat tanū 
 śeṣaḥ keśamayaḥ kim andhatamasastomair abhūn nirmitaḥ  ||1397|| 
 
 
 śrīharṣasya | 
 
 
 etat te mukham akṣatendulaḍahacchāyaṃ bhavallocanaṃ 
 nīlendīvaranirviśeṣam adharas te bandhujīvāruṇaḥ | 
 bhrūvallis tava kāmakārmukalatā līlāsahādhyāyinī 
 na dhyāyantu kathaṃ nu deva kathaya tvām ekam eṇīdṛśaḥ  ||1398|| 
 
 
 hareḥ | 
 
 
 kiṃ vātena vilaṅghitā na na mahābhūtārditā kiṃ na na 
 śrāntā kiṃ na na saṃnnipātalaharīpraccharditā kiṃ na na | 
 tat kiṃ muhyati roditi śvasiti ca smeraṃ ca dhatte mukhaṃ 
 dṛṣṭaḥ kiṃ katham apy akāraṇaripuḥ śrībhojadevo’nayā  ||1399|| 
 
 
 chittapasya | (su.ra. 749) 
 
 
 rūpāsavaṃ tava nṛpendra yad eṇanetrā 
 mātrāṃ vyatītya nayanāñjalibhiḥ pibanti | 
 svedacchalād atha vamanti kadambakalpaiḥ 
 raṅgair anaṅgaśarajarjaritair bhramanti  ||1400|| 
 
 
 śaṅkaradevasya | 
 
 
 7. dṛṣṭiḥ 
 
 
 janayati jananātha dṛṣṭir eṣā 
 tava navanīlasaroruhābhirāmā | 
 praṇayiṣu susamāśriteṣu lakṣmīm 
 ariṣu hi bhaṅgam anaṅgam aṅganāsu  ||1401|| 
 
 
 vidyāyāḥ | 
 
 
 pratyañcatkhalarohaṇādriṣu haṭhād āmūlam unmūlayan 
 ####### kalpaśākhiṣu sudhāsāndrāḥ suhṛnmaṇḍale | 
 prauḍhārāticamūvaneṣu dahanajvālāvalībhāsvarāḥ 
 śṛṅgāraikarasāyanāni subhaga tvaddṛṣṭipātāḥ punaḥ  ||1402|| 
 
 
 mādhavasya | 
 
 
 yato yato nṛpavara padmapāṭalaṃ 
 vilocanaṃ calati tava prasīdataḥ | 
 tatas tato nalinavanādhivāsinī 
 tadīpsayā kila kamalānudhāvati  ||1403|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 1450) 
 
 
 te kaupīnadhanās ta eva hi paraṃ dhātrīphalaṃ bhuñjate 
 teṣāṃ dvāri nadanti vājinivahās tair eva labdhā kṣitiḥ | 
 tair etat samalaṅkṛtaṃ nijakulaṃ kiṃ vā bahu brūmahe  
 ye dṛṣṭāḥ parameśvareṇa bhavatā tuṣṭena ruṣṭena vā  ||1404|| 
 
 
 jayādityasya | (su.ra. 1410, śā.pa. 1224) 
 
 
 teṣāṃ dvāri dviradapatayas tadvaśā viśvadhātrī 
 tadgehinyas taralitatulākoṭisaudhā naṭanti | 
 hemacchatracchuritaharito bhūtayas tān bhajante 
 yeṣu prītyā bhavati bhavato dṛṣṭipātaprasādaḥ  ||1405|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 8. bhujaḥ 
 
 
 vālmīkeḥ katamo’si kas tvam athavā vyāsasya yenaiṣa bhoḥ 
 ślāghyaḥ syāt tava bhojabhūpatibhujastambhastutāv udyamaḥ | 
 paṅguḥ parvatam ārurukṣasi vidhusparśaṃ kareṇehase 
 dorbhyāṃ sāgaram uttitīrṣasi yadi brūmaḥ kim atrottaram  ||1406|| 
 
 
 chittapasya | 
 
 
 atyuccāḥ paritaḥ sphuranti girayaḥ sphārās tathāmbhodhayas 
 tān etān api bibhratī kim api na klāntāsi tubhyaṃ namaḥ | 
 āścaryeṇa punaḥ punaḥ stutim imāṃ prastaumi yāvad bhuvas 
 tāvad vibhrad imāṃ smṛtas tava bhujo vācas tato mudritāḥ  ||1407|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (Kp 118, Kuval, 183, sū.mu. 97.10) 
 
 
 mithyā deva bhujena te’lpavibhavaḥ kalpadrumaḥ spardhate 
 nahy enaṃ bhuvanatrayābhayamahāsatrī kṛpāṇo’rcati | 
 cintyas tatra bhavān sakalpaviṭapī yasyaitad ekārṇave 
 kalpānte viniveśya viśvam akhilaṃ chāyāsu śete hariḥ  ||1408|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (sa.ka.ā. 3.101) 
 
 
 śailendro daśakandhareṇa tulitas taṃ cārjuno hehayaḥ  
 kārādhāmni babandha tasya ca bhujāraṇyaṃ muniś chinnavān | 
 itthaṃ granthinibaddhavikramakathāsandehaśalyākula 
 trailokyapratipatticumbakaśilāstambhas tadīyo bhujaḥ  ||1409|| 
 
 
 bhikṣoḥ | 
 
 
 pretāntroṣṇīṣavadhbhir vikaṭakariśiraḥkarparākrāntahastaiḥ 
 pārśvasthābhiḥ priyābhir madavikalapadaṃ yat tad apy ucyamānaiḥ | 
 helānirvāritāre yamamusalapṛthuḥ ślāghyate dakṣiṇas te 
 vetālaiḥ prastutāsu pratisamaram asṛkpānagoṣṭhīṣu bāhuḥ  ||1410|| 
 
 
 9. karaḥ 
 
 
 uddaṇḍakokanadakomalakośakāntiḥ 
 kāntākacagrahaṇakaṇṭakitaprakoṣṭhaḥ | 
 mitradvijātiripuvargavilāsinīnāṃ 
 saṃmānadānabhayabhogakaraḥ karas te  ||1411|| 
 
 
 vidyāyāḥ | (sū.mu. 97.50) 
 
 
 nistriṃśatruṭitārivāraṇaghaṭākumbhāsthikūṭāvaṭa 
 sthānasthāyukamauktikotkarakiraḥ kair asya nāyaṃ karaḥ | 
 unnītaś caturaṅgasainyasamaratvaṅgatturaṅgakṣura 
 kṣuṇṇāsu kṣitiṣu kṣipann iva yaśaḥ kṣauṇījabījavrajam  ||1412|| 
 
 
 śrīharṣasya | (Nc 12.66) 
 
 
 asmābhiḥ smayalolamauliphalakair muktāvisārādhipaṃ  
 vedoddhāraparaḥ karas tava paraṃ dānāmbupūtaḥ stutaḥ | 
 kintu kṣmātilaka kṣamasva kavibhiḥ kiṃ nāma nālokyate  
 dṛṣṭaḥ spaṣṭataraṃ tavāpi nibhṛtaḥ pāṇau sa vaisāriṇaḥ  ||1413|| 
 
 
 ācāryagopīkasya | 
 
 
 teṣām alpataraḥ sa kalpaviṭapī teṣāṃ na cintāmaṇiś 
 cintām apy upayāti kāmasurabhis teṣāṃ na kāmāspadam | 
 dīnoddhāradhurīṇapuṇyacarito yeṣāṃ prasanno manāk 
 pāṇis te dharaṇīndra sundarayaśaḥsaṃrakṣiṇo dakṣiṇaḥ  ||1414|| 
 
 
 jayadevasya | 
 
 
 deva tvatkarapallavo vijayatām aśrāntaviśrāṇana 
 krīḍāskanditakalpavṛkṣavibhavaḥ kīrtiprasūnojjvalaḥ | 
 yasyotsargajalacchalena galitāḥ syandānadānodaka 
 srotobhir viduṣāṃ lalāṭalikhitā dainyākṣaraśreṇayaḥ  ||1415|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 10. caraṇam 
 
 
 lakṣmīvaśīkaraṇacūrṇasahodarāṇi 
 tvatpādapaṅkajarajāṃsi ciraṃ jayanti | 
 yāni praṇāmamilitāni nṛṇāṃ lalāṭe  
 lumpanti daivalikhitāni durakṣarāṇi  ||1416|| 
 
 
 abhinandasya | (sa.ka.ā. 5.467, su.ra. 1391) 
 
 
 lakṣmīsadmasarojareṇusuhṛdaḥ sevāvanamrībhavad 
 bhūmīpālakirīṭaratnakiraṇajyotsnānadībālukāḥ | 
 jīyāsuḥ kalikālakarṇanṛpate dāridryadārūdara 
 vyāghūrṇaddhūṇavṛndalaṅghanamuṣas tvatpādayoḥ pāṃśavaḥ  ||1417|| 
 
 
 vallaṇasya | (su.ra. 1416) 
 
 
 devasyāṅghrinakhaprabhāsu nijayā maulīndranīlatviṣā 
 nirmāya tridaśāpagāyamunayoḥ saṃbhedam atyadbhutam | 
 vandya tvatpadavandanāny aghamiladduṣkarmanirmajjana 
 prāyaścittam ivācaran narapatiḥ ko nāma no pupluve  ||1418|| 
 
 
 praśastasya | 
 
 
 lakṣmīvibhramasadmasubhagaṃ ke nāma nor bībhujo 
 deva tvaccaraṇaṃ vrajanti śaraṇe śrīrakṣaṇakāṅkṣiṇaḥ | 
 chāyāyām anugamya samyag abhayās tvadvīryasūryātapa 
 vyāptām apy avanīm aṭanti ripavas tyaktātapatrāḥ  ||1419|| 
 
 
 jayadevasya | 
 
 
 ā pūrvasmād viḍaujaḥkarivamathupayaḥsiktasānor girīndrād  
 ā ca pratyakpayodher varuṇavaravadhūnābhiniṣpītavāraḥ | 
 ā merorā ca setor avanitalamilanmaulivisraṃsamāna 
 sragdāmāno yad īyaṃ caraṇam aśaraṇāḥ paryupāsan narendrāḥ  ||1420|| 
 
 
 vasukalpasya | 
 
 
 11. priyākhyānam  
 
 
 saujanyāmbunidhe budhapriya guṇaprākāradharmadruma 
 prārohapratipannavatsala mahātyāgin vivekāśraya | 
 lakṣmyāvāsamanasvinī manasijavyāpāradīkṣāguro 
 svāmin muñja kim ity amuṃ janam upaspraṣṭum  ||1421|| 
 
 
 bhojadevasya | (sa.ka.ā. 1.86) 
 
 
 saujanyāṅkurakandasundarakathāsarvasva sīmantinī 
 cittākarṣaṇamantramanmathasuhṛtkallolavāgvallabha | 
 saubhāgyaikaniveśa peśalagirām ādhāra dhairyāmbudhe 
 dharmādridruma rājaśekharakave dṛṣṭo’si yāmo vayam  ||1422|| 
 
 
 abhinandasya | (su.ra. 1714) 
 
 
 saṅkalpe’ṅkuritaṃ dvipatritam atha prasthānavelāgame 
 mārge pallavitaṃ puraṃ praviśataḥ śākhāśatair udgatam | 
 bhrātar bhāvini darśane mukulitaṃ dṛṣṭe tu deve tvayi 
 protphullaṃ phalitaṃ ca samprati manorājyadrumeṇādya me  ||1423|| 
 
 
 chittapasya | (su.ra. 1435) 
 
 
 dvīndraṃ bhāti jagattridhāma gaganaṃ viśvaṃ caturdaivataṃ 
 pañcāmnāyam idaṃ ca vāṅmayamayaṃ ṣaṭsāyako manmathaḥ | 
 saptāṃśaḥ parivatsaroṣṭajaladhisphāraṃ dharāmaṇḍalaṃ 
 dikcakraṃ navanāyakaṃ kṣitipatiśreṣṭha tvayi bhrājati  ||1424|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 lakṣmīkelibhujaṅga jaṅgamahare saṃkalpakalpadruma 
 śreyaḥsādhakasaṅga saṅgarakalāgāṅgeya baṅgapriya | 
 gauḍendrapratirājarājakasabhālaṅkārakarṇārpita 
 pratyarthikṣitipāla pālaka satāṃ dṛṣṭo’si tuṣṭā vayam  ||1425|| 
 
 
 jayadevasya | 
 
 
 12. atyuktiḥ 
 
 
 maulau dhāraya puṇḍarīkam amitaṃ tanvātmano vikramaṃ 
 cakrāṅkaṃ vaha pādapadmam avaniṃ doṣṇā samabhyuddhara | 
 lakṣmīṃ bhrūnikaṭe niveśaya bhava jyāyāndivaukaspater  
 viśvāntaḥkaraṇaikacaura tad api jñāto hariḥ khalv asi  ||1426|| 
 
 
 chittapasya | (sa.ka.ā. 1.90, sū.mu. 97.6) 
 
 
 dṛṃsajyotsnākumudaviśade saikate’smin sarayvā 
 vādadyūtaṃ cirataram abhūt siddhayūnoḥ kayościt | 
 eko brūte prathamanihataṃ kaiṭabhaṃ kaṃsam anyaḥ 
 sa tvaṃ tattvaṃ kathaya bhavatā ko hatas tatra pūrvam  ||1427|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 haste kalpataruṃ mukhe himakaraṃ bāhvor anantāhvayaṃ 
 roṣe tat kila kālakūṭagaralaṃ toṣe haripreyasīm | 
 ojasyāvṛṇu nāma vāḍavam imām udghāṭya maryāditāṃ 
 ghoṣo’yaṃ tava nīradhe vanapate chadmāvatāre śramaḥ  ||1428|| 
 
 
 madimnasya | 
 
 
 unnidreṇa mayādya cintitam abhūd yatrāvatārā harer  
 ākhyātā daśa kīrtito’si na kathaṃ tatra tvam ekādaśaḥ | 
 tvaccāritram agocaraṃ kavigirāṃ jānann api kṣmāpate 
 na prastaumi bhayena bhāratakaveḥ kas tādṛśaṃ vakṣyati  ||1429|| 
 
 
 ācāryagopīkasya | 
 
 
 bhūtyā rajjaya viśvam udvaha nakhacchadmārdhacandraṃ padaṃ 
 dṛṣṭiṃ dhehi hṛdi sphuṭaṃ bhava vṛṣādhāro dvijihvaṃ tyaja | 
 saṃkruddho daha vidviṣāṃ puraśataṃ durgānurāgojjhitaḥ  
 kṣoṇīnātha tathāpy udāracaritair jñāto bhavānīśvaraḥ  ||1430|| 
 
 
 vasantadevasya | 
 
 
 13. citroktiḥ 
 
 
 santaḥ kaṇṭakitāḥ kathaṃ yadi kṛtā niṣkaṇṭakā medinī 
 prakhyātā yadi te guṇāḥ katham atha prastauti doṣaṃ janaḥ | 
 nītāvādyadhurandharo yadi bhavān kasmād anītiḥ prajā 
 vṛttaṃ deva na citram eva hi na cec citraṃ vidhatte katham  ||1431|| 
 
 
 samantabhadrasya | 
 
 
 kṣauṇīndra tyajati kṣamāṃ tvayi raṇe doḥśālino’py akṣamāḥ 
 pratarthiṣv atha kampamānatanuṣu tvaṃ cāpi kampākulaḥ | 
 tvaṃ gṛhṇāsi bhuvaḥ karaṃ mṛgadṛśām ete’pi ca svarbhuvāṃ 
 tebhyas tebhyo’dhikaṃ nu kiṃ guṇibhir apy udgīyate yad bhavān  ||1432|| 
 
 
 dhoyīkasya | 
 
 
 ekas tridhā hṛdi sadā vasasīti citraṃ 
 yo vidviṣāṃ ca viduṣāṃ ca mṛgīdṛśāṃ ca | 
 tāpaṃ ca saṃmadarasaṃ ca ratiṃ ca tanvan 
 śauryoṣmaṇā ca vinayena ca līlayā ca  ||1433|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 1438, śrīhanūmataḥ) 
 
 
 tvaṃ dvitrāṇi padāni gacchasi mahīm ullaṅghya yānti dviṣas 
 tvaṃ bāṇān daśa pañca muñcasi bahūny astrāṇi muñcanti te | 
 te devīpatayas tavāsi nihatās tvaṃ mānuṣīṇāṃ patis  
 te nindyās tava varṇanaṃ katham iti śrīkarṇaṃ nirṇīyatām  ||1434|| 
 
 
 vidyāpateḥ | (Sv 2516) 
 
 
 karṇaḥ sarvaśirogatas tribhuvane karṇena kiṃ na śrūtaṃ 
 viśrāmyanti mṛgīdṛśām api dṛśaḥ karṇe na citraṃ kvacit | 
 āścaryaṃ punar etad eva yad ayaṃ niśchidrasanmaṇḍalaḥ 
 saptāmbhonidhimekhalāṃ vasumatīṃ dhatte jaganmaṇḍalaḥ  ||1435|| 
 
 
 kasyāpi | 
 
 
 14. kāryagarvaḥ 
 
 
 pṛthur asi guṇaiḥ kīrtyā rāmo nalo bharato bhavān 
 mahati samare śatrughnas tvaṃ sadaiva yudhiṣṭhiraḥ | 
 iti sucaritair bibhrad rūpaṃ cirantanabhūbhṛtāṃ 
 katham asi na māndhātā deva trilokavidhāyy api  ||1436|| 
 
 
 vīryamitrasya | (Sv 2502, su.ra. 1417) 
 
 
 tvaṃ cen nātha kalānidhiḥ śaśadharas tat toyanāthā vayaṃ 
 maryādānidhir ambhasāṃ patir atha tvaṃ ced vayaṃ vāridāḥ | 
 sarvāśāparipūrako jaladharas tvaṃ ced vayaṃ bhūruhaḥ  
 sanmārgasthitiviśrutas tvam iti cec chākhī vayaṃ cādhvagāḥ  ||1437|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 1392) 
 
 
 labhyante yadi vāñchitāni yamunābhāgīrathīsaṅgame 
 deva preyajanas tavaiva bhavato bhartavyatāṃ vāñchati | 
 nanv etanmaraṇān na kiṃ nu maraṇaṃ kāyān manovicyuti 
 dīrghaṃ jīva manas tvadaṅghrikamale kāyo’tra naḥ kevalam  ||1438|| 
 
 
 chittapasya | (sa.ka.ā. 2.356) 
 
 
 sevyaś cintāmaṇir vā suratarur athavā rohaṇo vā girīṇāṃ 
 bhartā vā jātakope tvayi nikhilamahādānanirvājavīre | 
 ekaś caitanyaśūnyas tyajati kaṭhinatāṃ nāparaś chedakhedaṃ 
 dhatte’nyaḥ kiṃnarāṇām adhipatir aparaḥ kas tvayābhyarthanīyaḥ  ||1439|| 
 
 
 śaraṇasya |  
 
 
 prītas tvaṃ vedavādair mama tu niravadhir nātha nirvedavādaḥ 
 sākūtas tvaṃ kalāsu pratidinavikalā vṛttir ekā mamaiva | 
 sādhyas tvaṃ bhāvaśuddhyā mama tu vijayate ko’py abhāvas tad itthaṃ 
 līlārāmo guṇānāṃ mama viguṇanidheḥ kaur upāyair upāsyaḥ  ||1440|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 15. deśāśrayaḥ  
 
 
 bhūpālāḥ śaśibhāskarānvayabhuvaḥ ke nāma nāsāditā 
 bhartāraṃ punar ekam eva hi bhuvas tvām eva manyāmahe | 
 yenāṅgaṃ parimṛdya kuntalam apākṛṣya vyudasyāyataṃ 
 colaṃ prāpya ca madhyadeśam acirāt kāñcyāṃ karaḥ pātitaḥ  ||1441|| 
 
 
 vidyāyāḥ | 
 
 
 helānirjitakāmarūpa sahasā kṛtvākulān kuntalāṃś 
 coladhvaṃsanam aṅgamardanam api drāg eva sampādyate | 
 nirjityaiva ca madhyadeśam acirāt kāñcyāṃ karaḥ pātito 
 nitvaivaṃ vaśatāṃ priyeṇa bhavatābhīkena bhūr bhujyate  ||1442|| 
 
 
 śabdārṇavasya | 
 
 
 deva tvaṃ kila kuntalagraharuciḥ kāñcīm apāsārayan 
 kṣiptaḥ kṣiptakaragrahaḥ prahaṇanaṃ prārabdham aṅgeṣv api | 
 ity ākūtajuṣas tava stavakṛtā vaitālikenodite 
 lajjante pramadāḥ parasparam abhiprekṣyārayo bibhyati  ||1443|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 1430) 
 
 
 bhrūkṣepād gauḍalakṣmīṃ jayati vijayate kelimātrāt kaliṅgāṃś 
 cetaś cedikṣitīndos tapati vitapate sūryavad durjaneṣa | 
 svecchān mlecchān vināśaṃ nayati vinayate kāmarūpābhimānaṃ 
 kāśībhartuḥ prakāśaṃ harati viharate mūrdhni yo māgadhasya  ||1444|| 
 
 
 śaraṇadevasya | 
 
 
 tvaṃ colollolalīlāṃ kalayasi kuruṣe karṣaṇaṃ kuntalānāṃ 
 tvaṃ kāñcinyañcanāya prabhavati rabhasād aṅgasaṅgaṃ karoṣi | 
 itthaṃ rājendra vandistutibhir upahitotkampam evādya dīrghaṃ 
 nārīṇām apy arīṇāṃ hṛdayam udayate tvatpadārādhanāya  ||1445|| 
 
 
 jayadevasya | 
 
 
 16. dānam  
 
 
 katiṣu na kṛtā sevā ke vā na vāgvibhavaiḥ stutās  
 tṛṇam api guṇaprītaḥ prādān na ko’pi vipaścitām | 
 ayam iha paraṃ duḥkhajvālākalāpam akhaṇḍayat 
 kanakapayasāṃ dhārādaṇḍair akāṇḍaghanāghanaḥ  ||1446|| 
 
 
 silhanasya | 
 
 
 pūrṇo’gre kalaso vilāsavanitā smerānanā kanyakā 
 dānaklinnakapolapaddhatir ibho gauradyutir gaur vṛṣaḥ | 
 kṣīrikṣmāruhi vāyaso madhuravāgvāmā śiveti dhruvaṃ 
 tvāṃ pratyuccalatāṃ narendratilaka prādurbhavanty arthinām  ||1447|| 
 
 
 parameśvarasya | (su.ra. 1449) 
 
 
 vistīrṇaḥ paripanthikaṇṭakaśatāstīrṇo duradhvāntaraḥ 
 krūraśvāpadakoṭisaṅkaṭaśilā śailāṭavī laṅghitā | 
 prāptā tvatkaṭakopakaṇṭataṭinī datto nivāpāñjalir 
 dāridryāya nakāramūkanṛpate duṣṭo’si tuṣṭā vayam  ||1448|| 
 
 
 rājokasya | 
 
 
 vāsaḥ svarṇagṛheṣu sakhyam amaraiḥ kalpadrumāṇāṃ vane 
 krīḍā svargavadhūgaṇaiḥ saha sudhākaṇṭhaṃ mudā pīyate | 
 ruṣṭenedam akāri deva bhavatā hatvā raṇe vairiṇāṃ 
 tuṣṭaḥ preṣyajanāya vedmi na paraṃ gauḍendra kiṃ dāsyasi  ||1449|| 
 
 
 dharmayogeśvarasya | 
 
 
 tvannetre’pi tavānane’pi bhavataḥ pāṇāv api tvatpade’py 
 asti smerasarojasauhṛdasamākṛṣṭaiva padmālayā | 
 yannītā nijabhāvam arthibhir asau tvaddṛṣṭipātais tvadā 
 deśāt tvatkaravibhramair api bhavatpādaprasādād api  ||1450|| 
 
 
 śaraṇasya | 
 
 
 17. daridrabharaṇam 
 
 
 yeṣāṃ veśamasu kambukarparacalattarkudhvanir duḥśravaḥ 
 prāg āsīn naranātha saṃprati punas teṣāṃ tavānugrahāt | 
 ṣaḍjādikramaraṅgadaṅgulicalatpāṇiskhalatkaṅkaṇa 
 śreṇīnisvanamāṃsalaḥ kalagirāṃ vīṇāravaḥ śrūyate  ||1451|| 
 
 
 bhāsokasya | (su.ra. 1394, kasyacit) 
 
 
 karpāsāsthipracayanicitā nirdhanaśrotriyāṇāṃ 
 yeṣāṃ vātyāpravitatakuṭīprāṅgaṇāntā babhūvuḥ | 
 tatsaudhānāṃ parisarabhuvi tvatprasādād idānīṃ 
 krīḍāyuddhacchidurayuvatīhāramuktāḥ patanti  ||1452|| 
 
 
 śubhāṅkasya | (su.ra. 1390) 
 
 
 bālās tālamahīruho ghanadalasnigdhā gṛhaprāṅgaṇe 
 sūkṣmebhyas tava sandiśanti suciraṃ jīva prasanne tvayi | 
 karṇālaṅkṛtakena komaladalaṃ muñcanti no nirdayā  
 niḥsvaśrotriyavallabhāḥ śrutiyuge haimasphuratkuṇḍalāḥ  ||1453|| 
 
 
 umāpateḥ | 
 
 
 ucchidrāṇi digambarasya vasanāny ardhāṅgināsvāmino 
 ratnālaṃkṛtibhir viśoṣitavapuḥśobhāśataṃ subhruvaḥ | 
 paurāḍhyāś ca purīḥ śmaśānavasater bhikṣābhujo’py akṣamā 
 lakṣmīṃ na vyatanod daridrabharaṇeṣv ajño hi senānvayaḥ  ||1454|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 muktāḥ kārpāsabījair marakataśakalaṃ śākapatrair alāvū 
 puṣpai rūpyāṇi ratnaṃ pariṇatibhiduraiḥ kukṣibhir dāḍimīnām | 
 kuṣmāṇḍīvallarīṇāṃ vikasitakusumaiḥ kāñcanaṃ nāgarībhiḥ  
 śikṣyante tvatprasādād bahuvibhavajuṣāṃ yoṣitaḥ śrotriyāṇām  ||1455|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 18. atidānam 
 
 
 kūjatkokilakākalīśrutisukhī nidrāti kalpadrumas 
 tṛptā bālatṛṇena kāmasurabhī romantham abhyasyati | 
 dātuṃ nātha sadā samīhitaphalaṃ lagno’si netre’rthināṃ 
 baddhas tarhi cirāya rohaṇagireṣ ṭaṅkavraṇer aṅkuraḥ  ||1456|| 
 
 
 kāmadevasya | 
 
 
 arthibhraṃśabahūbhavatphalabharavyājena kubjāyitaḥ  
 satyasminn atidānabhāji katham apy āstāṃ sa kalpadrumaḥ | 
 āste nirvyayaratnasaṃpadudayodagraḥ kathaṃ yācaka 
 śreṇīvarjanaduryaśoniviḍitavrīḍas tu ratnācalaḥ  ||1457|| 
 
 
 śrīharṣasya | (Nc 12.67, Sv 2517) 
 
 
 jāne vikramavardhana tvayi dhanaṃ viśrāṇayaty arthināṃ 
 bhāvī śoṇa ivopalair upacito ratnair agādho’mbudhiḥ | 
 utpaśyāmi ca rohaṇair maṇibharair bāṣpāyamāṇodaraḥ 
 pākotpīḍitadāḍimīphaladṛśāṃ kaiścid dinair yāsyati  ||1458|| 
 
 
 ḍimbokasya | (su.ra. 1437) 
 
 
 bhrātaś cakra vyapanaya śucaṃ preyasīviprayogād 
 ādhivyādhir na khalu rajanīṃ prāpya bhāvī punas te | 
 dānair nānyaḥ kalaya kurute kāṃcanādreḥ samāptir 
 bhāviny asmaddinakatipayair vāsarādvaitasiddhiḥ  ||1459|| 
 
 
 sāgarasya | 
 
 
 anviṣyadbhir ayaṃ cirāt katham api prārthyeta yady arthibhir 
 nātha tvaṃ punar arthinaḥ pratidinaṃ yatnāt samanviṣyasi | 
 prāptau cintitamātrakaṃ dadad asau cintātiriktapradaṃ  
 tvām ālokya vidīryate yadi na tadgrāvaiva cintāmaṇiḥ  ||1460|| 
 
 
 chittipasya | 
 
 
 19. vikramaḥ 
 
 
 deve nirbharasāhasaikarasike niḥśaṅkavīre’dhunā 
 niḥsīmaprasare niraṅkuśamatau jñāne manāṅ nirdaye | 
 niḥsaṃpatti nirāyudhaṃ niraśanaṃ nirbhūmi niḥsainikaṃ 
 nistejaś ca nirāśrayaṃ ca nikhilaṃ tadrājakaṃ vartate  ||1461|| 
 
 
 vasukalpasya | 
 
 
 matparyantavasundharāvijayine muktādiratnaṃ mayā 
 ttavyaṃ ḍhaukitam eva so’ham adhunā jāto’smi niṣkiñcanaḥ | 
 ity ullāsitabāhuvīcir udayān mārtaṇḍabimbacchalāt 
 prātas taptakuṭhāram eṣa vahate deva tvadagre’mbudhiḥ  ||1462|| 
 
 
 kasyāpi | (su.ra. 1397) 
 
 
 śāstraiḥ śatruśirodhitakṣaṇakalātīkṣṇojjvalaiḥ kiṃtarām 
 adyāpi kṣitipālalakṣaṇadharau kliśnāsi kāntau karau | 
 tādṛkkrūrakaṭākṣavīkṣaṇamilanmaurvīkam urvītale 
 soḍhā kas tava deva kopakuṭilaṃ bhrūkārmukaṃ bhūpatiḥ  ||1463|| 
 
 
 karañjayogeśvarasya | 
 
 
 yady aṅkeṣu karāḥ śataṃ pratikaraṃ yady aṅgulīnāṃ śataṃ 
 pratyekaṃ yadi parvasandhiṣu bhavanty etāsu rekhāḥ śatam | 
 śakyante nipuṇais tadā gaṇayituṃ yena svadorvikramair 
 utkhātāḥ kati ropitāḥ kati kati vyāpāditāḥ kṣmābhujaḥ  ||1464|| 
 
 
 vāmadevasya | 
 
 
 śikṣante cāṭuvādān vidadhati yavasān ānane kānaneṣu 
 bhrāmyanti jyākiṇāṅkaṃ vidadhati śibiraṃ kurvate parvateṣu  
 abhyasyanti praṇāmaṃ tvayi calati camūcakravikrāntibhāji 
 prāṇatrāṇāya deva tvadarinṛpatayaś cakrire kārmaṇāni  ||1465|| 
 
 
 jayadevasya | 
 
 
 20. pauruṣam 
 
 
 samāje samrājāṃ sadasi viduṣāṃ dhāmni dhanināṃ 
 nikāye nīcānām api ca ramaṇīnāṃ pariṣadi | 
 kathaṃcid yatra smaḥ kṣaṇam itathayas tatra śṛṇumaḥ  
 sphuradromodbhedāḥ subhaga bhavataḥ pauruṣakathāḥ  ||1466|| 
 
 
 chittapasya | 
 
 
 daivena tvadares tavāpi sadṛśī prāyaḥ parājeṣyate  
 nānyeneti kila dvayor api lipir nyastāḥ lalāṭe dhruvam | 
 bhūyān arthakṛtas tu samprati tayor bhedo’yam unmīlati 
 sthāne pauruṣam āśrayanti kṛtino daive nirasyādaram  ||1467|| 
 
 
 laṅgadattasya | 
 
 
 vāhū dvāv idam ekam eva bhuvanaṃ kas tatra vīro rasaḥ 
 sāmrājyasya ca pūrvapūruṣabhujakṣuṇṇasya kiṃ na priyam | 
 ity ūrjasvalapauruṣasya puruṣaprāyaṃ jagat paśyato 
 yasyātmāpi na mānino bahumataḥ kutretare kṣatriyāḥ  ||1468|| 
 
 
 śuṅgokasya | 
 
 
 gandhebhaskandhakaṇḍūmadagurumarudullolalauhityakhelad 
 vīcīvācālakālācalaripuśaśinā kelitalpe niṣaṇṇāḥ | 
 kāminyaḥ sainikānāṃ vidhutavidhuratābhītayo gītabandhair 
 yasya prāgjyotiṣendrapraṇatiparigataṃ pauruṣaṃ prastuvanti  ||1469|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 bhīṣmaḥ klībakatāṃ dadhāra samiti droṇena muktaṃ dhanur 
 mithyā dharmasutena jalpitam abhūd duryodhano durmadaḥ | 
 chidreṣv eva dhanañjayasya vijayaḥ karṇaḥ pramādī tataḥ  
 śrīmann asti na bhārate’pi bhavato yaḥ pauruṣair vardhate  ||1470|| 
 
 
 jayadevasya |  
 
 
 21. śauryam 
 
 
 vyāyāmocitabāhusāhasavaśād eko’pi kopotkaṭaṃ 
 vakṣasy utkaṭasoḍhasāyakabharo bhindan bahūn vidviṣaḥ | 
 tvaṃ yasmād ayaśas ta eva samiti trasto na śastrakṣatais 
 tenaivāyaśasaḥ parigraham amī muktāyudhāḥ kurvate  ||1471|| 
 
 
 kamalaguptasya | 
 
 
 ayaṃ senottaṃsaḥ karakṛtakṛpāṇo raṇabhuvi  
 dviṣadbhūmīpālāḥ kim apasarata prāṇakṛpaṇāḥ | 
 kim abhyarthyaḥ pṛthvīdharakuharavāso’dya bhavatāṃ  
 na kiṃ hṛdyā vidyādharanagaranīlotpaladṛśaḥ  ||1472|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 kaḥ śailān gilati kṣamāṃ calayati kṣārāmbudhau dhāvati 
 ko vā cumbati sūryabimbam analajvālāṃ samāliṅgati | 
 līlollāsitakṛttamastakam iva vyālolajihvālataṃ 
 kas tvāṃ kāñcanabhṛṅgasaṅgarajayaśrīghoṣaṇāghoṣaṇāḥ  ||1473|| 
 
 
 karañjadhanañjayasya | 
 
 
 deva tvattatpratāpajvalanakavalitāḥ sarvato dahyamānair 
 aṅgair yuktaṃ yad ete himagiriśikharotsaṅgam īyur narendrāḥ | 
 kiṃ tu tvacchauryalīlām anuharati puraḥ siṃhayūnāṃ nikāye 
 tatrāpy ātaṅkabhājaḥ kva nanu vidhihatāḥ sthairyam āsādayanti  ||1474|| 
 
 
 yuvarājadivākarasya | 
 
 
 no ko’pi ślokaḥ  ||1475|| 
 
 
 
 22. pratāpaḥ 
 
 
 kūrmaḥ pādo’sya yaṣṭir bhujagapatir asau bhājanaṃ bhūtadhātrī 
 tailotpūrāḥ samudrāḥ kanakagirir ayaṃ vṛttavartiprarohaḥ | 
 arciś caṇḍāṃśurocir gaganamalinimā kajjalaṃ dahyamānā 
 śatruśreṇī pataṅgā jvalati raghupate tvatpratāpapradīpaḥ  ||1476|| 
 
 
 śrīhanūmataḥ | (śā.pa. 1248, sū.mu. 97.47, su.ra. 1457) 
 
 
 tādṛgdīrghaviriñcivāsaravidhau jānāmi yatkartṛtāṃ 
 śaṅke yatpratibimbam ambudhipayaḥ pūrodare bāḍavaḥ | 
 tattādṛkpratipakṣarājakayaśas tārāḥ parābhāvukaḥ 
 kāsām asya na sa pratāpatapanaḥ pāraṃ girāṃ gāhate  ||1477|| 
 
 
 kavipaṇḍitaśrīharṣasya | (Nc 12.11, Sv 2527, sū.mu. 97.48) 
 
 
 niṣpiṣṭapratirāja rājati sajātīyatrayaṃ tejasām 
 aurvaś cāgniriraṃmadaś ca bhavataś caiṣa pratāpānalaḥ | 
 ādyo mādyati vāribhir jalanidher ambhomucāṃ madhyamaḥ 
 pratyarthikṣitipālayauvanadṛśām udgatvarair antimaḥ  ||1478|| 
 
 
 hareḥ | 
 
 
 vaṃśottaṃsam aśokasaṅkulam atiproddāmabāṇāsanaṃ 
 dṛpyaddvīpi camaccamūru ninadahanti bhramatkhaḍgi ca | 
 yasyojjāgaranāgaraṅgam abhitaḥ puṃnāgapuṇyāśrayaṃ 
 jagrāha pratirājakaṃ vanam abhi kruddhaḥ pratāpānalaḥ  ||1479|| 
 
 
 śuṅgokasya | 
 
 
 ekadvitrikalākrameṇa śaśinaṃ gṛhṇan vimuñcann ayaṃ 
 yaccaṇḍadyutir ātanoti bhagavān adyāpi cāndrāyaṇam | 
 devaitad bhavadīyabhāsvarabhujastambhapratāpānala 
 spardhāyai kramabhuktalāñchanapaśor naitat punaḥ setsyati  ||1480|| 
 
 
 ācāryagopīkasya | 
 
 
 23. tejaḥ 
 
 
 śuṣyanty eva payodhayo na maṇayaḥ kuryuḥ padaṃ ced adhaḥ 
 śuṣyaty aṇḍam apīdam ambujabhuvo mantrā bhaveyur na cet | 
 kiṃ caite kaṇaśaḥ sphuṭanti girayo dadhyur na ced auṣadhīs 
 tejobhis tava deva bhūr api bhujacchāyāsu viśrāmyati  ||1481|| 
 
 
 hareḥ | 
 
 
 tvattejaḥsavitā pitāmahapurīm adhyāsta yallīlayā 
 yac cakre bhujendrasadmasu tamaś chedaṃ na tatrādbhutam | 
 citraṃ yat paripanthipārthivamukhāmbhojāny anujjāgarī 
 kurvāṇas trijagadvilaṅghanaparo nāstācalaṃ cumbati  ||1482|| 
 
 
 śrīkarasya | 
 
 
 pītvā sāndratamaṃ tamas timirahā devaḥ prasūte yamaṃ 
 kālindīṃ ca śanaiścaraṃ ca timirāhārānusārād iva | 
 tejas tv asya punar virodhivasudhāpālāṅganākajjalāny 
 ācāmadgurugarbhahūṇataruṇīgaṇḍāvadātaṃ yaśaḥ  ||1483|| 
 
 
 ācāryagopīkasya | 
 
 
 ekaṃ dhāma śamīṣu līnam aparaṃ sūryopalajyotiṣāṃ 
 vyājādadriṣu gūḍham anyad udadhau saṃguptamaurvāyate | 
 tvattejastapanāṃśumāṃsalasamuttāpena durgaṃ bhayād 
 vārkṣaṃ pārvatam audakaṃ yadi yayus tejāṃsi kiṃ pārthivāḥ  ||1484|| 
 
 
 jayadevasya | 
 
 
 vyomany ulkety araṇye dava iti baḍavāvahnir ity amburāśau 
 pakṣeṣu kṣmādharāṇāṃ pavir iti taḍid ity ambuvāhāvalīṣu | 
 bhālotsaṅge purārer nayanam iti punar bhāvikalpāntakāle 
 kālāgniś ceti deva trijagati bhavanas tejasaḥ sphūrjitāni  ||1485|| 
 
 
 śubhāṅkasya | 
 24. hastī 
 
 
 bhūrbhūdāraradāṅkureṇa jaladher antaḥ puravoddhṛtā 
 prāg evābhram u vallabhasya daśanair bhinno himānīgiriḥ | 
 itthaṃ deva nijoṣmaṇā tava gajaḥ kṣuṇṇaṃ vapur vījayan 
 karṇābhyāṃ karayantramuktamathusyandair ayaṃ siñcati  ||1486|| 
 
 
 bhaṭṭaśālīyapītāmbarasya | 
 
 
 etad deva yaśaskaraṃ narapater yat taskare nigraho 
 dīrghaṃ jīva yathāparādhamadhuraṃ daṇḍaṃ jagaty āvahan | 
 yenāyaṃ paripanthipārthivavadhūsindūracauras tvayā 
 baddhaś ca pratidaṇḍabhairavakarī kṣiptaś ca kārāgṛhe  ||1487|| 
 
 
 śuṅgokasya | 
 
 
 ugrāvagrāhamagnā kuśadhuvanadhutādhoraṇāsphālitāṅgaiḥ 
 pratyagroddaṇḍaśuṇḍoḍḍamaraṇasamaratrastadiṅnāgacakraiḥ | 
 ālokyālokya śailān urucaraṇaraṇacchṛṅkhalāghaṭṭayadbhir  
 yasyāśābhittijetur madakalakaribhiḥ kvāpi na prāpi raṅgaḥ  ||1488|| 
 
 
 mahānidhikumārasya | 
 
 
 ayam ayam asāv ākarṇyārāt pratidvipaḍiṇḍimaṃ  
 madakaluṣite netre mārjann udastakarārgalaḥ | 
 agaṇitasṛṇiḥ krodhastabdhāyataśrutipallavaḥ  
 praviśati nṛpasyāntaḥkakṣāṃ javād arim udgaraḥ  ||1489|| 
 
 
 viriñceḥ | 
 
 
 sindūradyutimugdhamūrdhani dhṛtaskandhāvadhiśyāmike 
 vyomāntaḥspṛśi sindhure’sya samarārambhoddhure dhāvati | 
 jānīmo’nupadapradoṣatimiravyāmiśrasandhyādhiye 
 vāstaṃ vānti samastabāhujabhujātejaḥ sahasrāṃśavaḥ  ||1490|| 
 
 
 kavipaṇḍitaśrīharṣasya | (Nc 12.36, sū.mu. 101.8) 
 
 
 25. aśvaḥ 
 
 
 ākarṣann iva gāṃ vamann iva khurān paścārdham ujjhann iva  
 svīkurvann iva khaṃ pibann iva diśaś chāyām amarṣann iva | 
 sāṅgāraprakarāṃ spṛśann iva dharāṃ vātaṃ sam aśnann iva  
 śrīmannātha sa vājirāṭ tava kathaṃ mādṛggirāṃ gocaraḥ  ||1491|| 
 
 
 chittapasya | (Sv 2419, śā.pa. 583) 
 
 
 kiyat padaṃ viṣṇupadaṃ mama krame 
 dharā varākī ca payodhirodhitā | 
 itīva helāvinatorukandharaḥ  
 karoty ayaṃ maṇḍalikārayaṃ hayaḥ  ||1492|| 
 
 
 haridattasya | (sū.mu. 102.1) 
 
 
 prayātum asmākam iyaṃ kiyat padaṃ 
 dharā tadambhodhir api sthalāyatām | 
 itīva vāhair nijavegadarpitaiḥ 
 payodhirodhakṣamam adbhutaṃ rajaḥ  ||1493|| 
 
 
 śrīharṣasya | (Nc 1.69, sū.mu. 102.8) 
 
 
 dhūlībhir divam andhayanvadhirayann āśāḥ khurāṇāṃ ravair 
 vātaṃ saṃyati khañjayan javajayaiḥ stotṬn guṇair mūkayan | 
 dharmārādhanasaṃniyuktajagatā rājñām unādhiṣṭhitaḥ 
 sāndrotphālamiṣād vigāyati padā spraṣṭuṃ turaṅgo’pi gām  ||1494|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (Nc 12.99, Sv 2601, sū.mu. 102.10) 
 
 
 kṣauṇī naḥ kṣitipālamaulimahiṣī dyaur devakīnandana 
 syāṅghriḥ kvāṅghrir ihāsyatām iti manaś cintānamatkandharaḥ | 
 aṅgāny aṅgalatāsu bhaṅgurakhuranyāsaiḥ samāveśayann 
 utkrośann iva vāridhīn adhicalaty uccais tavāyaṃ hayaḥ  ||1495|| 
 
 
 ākāśapālīyaśālūkasya | 
 
 
 26. naukā 
 
 
 bhṛṅgair nāvikasaṃnibhaiḥ parigataṃ śuddhāntavāmabhruvāṃ 
 karṇabhraṣṭam avekṣya ketakadalaṃ vāpījale santarat | 
 śrīmatsāhasamallavīra bhavato nausārtham antaḥ smarann 
 uttrasto’dya punaḥ karoti salilakrīḍāṃ na gauḍādhipaḥ  ||1496|| 
 
 
 vasukalpasya | 
 
 
 jitapavanajavābhir naubhir āskandya sadyas 
 tridivam api vijetuṃ nākṣamaḥ kṣatriyo’yam | 
 yadi na śirasi bhargaḥ svargiṇāṃ bhāgadheyair 
 dadhadamaradhunīṃ syād antarāle’ntarāyaḥ  ||1497|| 
 
 
 śuṅgokasya | 
 
 
 naukābhinītajalakeliṣu kenipāta 
 pātocchalatsalilaśīkarasaṃcayena | 
 deva tvayā viracito nabhasi pragalbha 
 vācālavīcivalitaḥ pracalaḥ payodhiḥ  ||1498|| 
 
 
 harivaṃśasya | 
 
 
 nakhāṅkaṃ nārīṇām anilalulitaṃ ketakadalaṃ 
 kalām indoḥ patraṃ pariṇativiśīrṇajalaruhām | 
 nirīkṣante yasya drutamilitanaukāṭakaghaṭā 
 haṭhākṛṣṭibhraṣṭāś cakitam iva kāśījanapadāḥ  ||1499|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 naukānirgamakenipātapatanodañcatpayobindubhir 
 dhārālāpair viparītavṛṣṭiṣu kathāvṛddho na vṛddhaśravāḥ | 
 kiṃ ca dveṣipure purandarapurīvastrāñcalīkuṅkuma 
 kṣodakṣālanavāripātarudhirabhrānto janas tāmyati  ||1500|| 
 
 
 narasiṃhasya | 
 
 
 27. senā 
 
 
 bhūrbhūpālacamūpadeu gaganaṃ senārajorājiuṃ 
 śrāntadveikalevareu maruto naukātalev abdhayaḥ | 
 tejas tejasi līnam astu bhavataḥ kiṃtv anyad ācakṣmahe 
 sṛṣṭiḥ sraṣṭur ihāstam eṣyati mahābhūtair vinā pañcabhiḥ  ||1501|| 
 
 
 śrīkaṇṭhasya | 
 
 
 nityaṃ nistṛṇapallave pathi nirālambe vrajan vājibhiḥ  
 khinnakhinnaturaṅgakaruṇākṛṣṭo vivasvānayan | 
 yāyād apy avatīrya nirjarapathād eṣā samantān na ced 
 adya tvadgajatāgalan madajalair jambālinī medinī  ||1502|| 
 
 
 karañjayogeśvarasya | 
 
 
 tvatsainyaglapitasya pannagapater acchinnadhārākramaṃ 
 visphārāyataśālini pratiphaṇaṃ phenāmbhasi bhraśyati | 
 deva kṣmāvalayaprabho phaṇikulaiḥ pratyagram ekottara 
 sthūlastambhasahasradhāritam iva kṣmācakram ālokyate  ||1503|| 
 
 
 vasukalpasya | (su.ra. 1425) 
 
 
 śeṣaṃ kleśayituṃ diśaḥ sthagayituṃ peṣṭuṃ dharitrībhṛtaḥ  
 sindhūn dhūlibhareṇa kardamayituṃ tair eva roddhuṃ nabhaḥ | 
 nāsīre ca muhur muhuś calacalety ālāpakolāhalān 
 kartuṃ nātha varuthinīyam avanīṃ jetuṃ punas tvadbhujau  ||1504|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (su.ra. 1426) 
 
 
 aho sthairyaṃ teṣāṃ prakṛtiniyamebhyaḥ sukṛtināṃ  
 pratijñātatyāgo nahi bhavati kṛcchre’pi mahati | 
 tathā hi tvatsenābharanamitadhātrībharadalat 
 kaṭāho’pi svāṅgaṃ kim u kamaṭhanāthaś calayati  ||1505|| 
 
 
 28. khaḍgaḥ 
 
 
 deva tvaṃ malayācalo’si bhavataḥ śrīkhaṇḍaśākhī bhusas 
 tasmin kālabhujaṅgamo nivasati sphūrjatkṛpāṇacchalāt | 
 eṣa svāṅgam anargalaṃ riputaruskandheṣu saṃghaṭṭayan 
 dīrghaṃ vyomavisārinirmalayaśo nirmokam unmuñcati  ||1506|| 
 
 
 chittapasya | (sū.mu. 97.33) 
 
 
 tulyā bāṇakṛpāṇayor anugatiḥ kṣīṇānanao na kvacit 
 koṣaṃ me harati prayacchati sadā lakṣaṃ raṇe patriṇe | 
 itthaṃ deva kunāyakatvam asakṛd buddhvaiva yuddheṣv asiḥ 
 kṛtvā sandhim upoḍhavepathur atikrodhād viveśa dviṣaḥ  ||1507|| 
 
 
 laṅgadattasya | (sū.mu. 97.51) 
 
 
 dvābhyām eva jitaṃ dvayoḥ param amūny aṅgāni bhūmibhara 
 ślāghyaśrīṇi gṛṇanti samprati bhavatsv aṅgasya kūrmasya ca | 
 yat kampe kṣitipālaśatruvasudhācakraṃ samutkampate  
 nirvyājaṃ nipatanti ca kṣitibhṛtāṃ viṣvakśiraḥśreṇayaḥ  ||1508|| 
 
 
 cūḍāmaṇeḥ | 
 
 
 yaśaḥ putraṃ deva tvadasilatikāsūta samare 
 samīras taddhūlīpaṭalapaṭavāsaṃ vikirati | 
 śivā yāyanty uccair aṭati ca kabandhāvalir abhūd 
 arātīnāṃ mokṣaḥ sapadi bhavabandhavyatikarāt  ||1509|| 
 
 
 vidyāyāḥ | 
 
 
 No verse  ||1510|| 
 
 
 29. āścaryakhaḍgaḥ 
 
 
 devaḥ svastutir astu nāma hṛdi naḥ sarve ca santvāgamās 
 tīrthaṃ na kvacid īdṛg atra bhavati tvatkhaḍgadhārā yathā | 
 yām ekaḥ svaśarīraśuddhirasiko mūrdhnā pratīcchann arir 
 dvaividhyād anu pañcatāṃ tad anu ca traidaśyam āpa kṣaṇāt  ||1511|| 
 
 
 rathāṅgasya | (sū.mu. 97.68, su.ra. 1396) 
 
 
 śākhāḥ pañca tavodgatā bhujataros tābhis tathaikaṃ dhṛtaṃ 
 sambhūyaiva kilāsipatram abhavat tatrāpi citrāntaram | 
 viśvavyāpiyaśaḥprasūnam akhilavyāpacchide śrīphalaṃ 
 chāyāṃ kiṃ kathayāmi yatra nikhilaṃ viśrāmyati kṣmātalam  ||1512|| 
 
 
 laṅgadattasya | 
 
 
 apanaya mahāmohaṃ rājann anena tavāsinā  
 kathaya kuhakāścaryaṃ kvedaṃ kathaṃ kva ca śikṣitam | 
 yad arirudhiraṃ pāyaṃ pāyaṃ kusumbharasāruṇaṃ  
 jhaṭiti vamati kṣīrāmbhodhipravāhasitaṃ yaśaḥ  ||1513|| 
 
 
 dakṣasya | (su.ra. 1015) 
 
 
 udyāty eva suhṛtkulaṃ pratibalaṃ yāty eva nīcaistarām 
 āyānty eva yaśaḥśriyaḥ pratidiśaṃ yānty eva satkīrtayaḥ | 
 yenaikena mukhāgrapāṭitatanūbhūtārdrakoṭiśriyā 
 sarvāścaryamayaḥ sa eva jayati tvatkhaḍgadhārāpathaḥ  ||1514|| 
 
 
 śuṅgokasya | 
 
 
 śrīkhaṇḍamūrtiḥ saralāṅgayaṣṭir 
 mākandam āmūlam aho vahantī | 
 śrīman bhavatkhaḍgatamālavallī 
 citraṃ raṇe śrīphalam ātanoti  ||1515|| 
 
 
 jayadevasya | 
 
 
 30. kupitakhaḍgaḥ 
 
 
 paryaṅko rājalakṣmyā haritamaṇimayaḥ paurṣābdhes taraṅgo 
 bhagnapratyarthivaṃśolbaṇavijayakaris tyānadānāmbupaṭṭaḥ | 
 saṃgrāmatrāsatāmyannarapatisuyaśorājahaṃsāmbuvāhaḥ 
 khaḍgaḥ kṣmāsau vidallaḥ samiti vijayate mālavākhaṇḍalasya  ||1516|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 vīraśrīveṇibandho bhujabhujagaphaṇā śatruṣu bhrūpatākā  
 devasya pretabhartuḥ sphuradurupṛtanādvipinī vīcidaṇḍaḥ | 
 krodhāgner dhūmavartiḥ surayuvatidṛśāṃ śṛṅkhalādāma dīrghaṃ 
 lakṣmīlīlākaṭākṣaḥ partisamaram abhūd yasya jaitraḥ kṛpāṇaḥ  ||1517|| 
 
 
 rājaśekharasya | (bā.rā. 3.48) 
 
 
 dṛpyatpratyarthipṛthvīpativitatayaśaḥkaumudīkṛṣṇapakṣo 
 lakṣmīsaṃcāradūtaḥ suranaranagarārambhanirvighnayaṣṭiḥ | 
 saṃgrāmāmbhodhimādyadbhujagaphaṇā talpakalpāntakṛṣṭa 
 khaḍgas te devajīyād ayam uditamahīmaṇḍalākhaṇḍalasya  ||1518|| 
 
 
 śāntyākarasya | 
 
 
 asyāsir bhujagaḥ svakośasuṣirākṛṣṭaḥ sphuratkṛṣṇimā  
 kamponmīladarālanīlarasanaḥ keṣāṃ bhiye na dviṣām | 
 saṃgrāmeṣu nijāṅgulīmayamahāsiddhauṣadhīvīrudhaḥ  
 parvāsye viniveśya jāṅgulikatā yair nāma nālambitā  ||1519|| 
 
 
 kavipaṇḍitaśrīharṣasya | (Nc 12.96, sū.mu. 97.49) 
 
 
 līlottaṃsatamālavallir avaner etatpratāpānala 
 sphūrjaddhūmaśikhā krudhākulatanoḥ kālasya jihvāñcalaḥ | 
 vairistraiṇavilocanāñjanalipistenas tamomandiraṃ 
 nidrāṇasya kaleḥ sa tasya nṛpateḥ khaḍgo na vāggocaraḥ  ||1520|| 
 
 
 yuvarājadivākarasya | 
 
 
 31. cāpaḥ 
 
 
 jyāṃ bibhradbhujago bhujaṅgamayuvā cāpas tavāsmin punaḥ 
 śete kuṇḍalite vipakṣakaṣaṇo nārācanārāyaṇaḥ | 
 bibhrāṇā hṛdayena yaṃ kṣaṇam api kṣoṇībhujo bhejire 
 bhittvāmbhoruhabandhubimbam acirād ānandasāndraṃ mahaḥ  ||1521|| 
 
 
 ācāryagopīkasya | 
 
 
 yaḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ yudhi darśayaty aribhaṭaśreṇīṣu yo vakratām 
 asminn eva bibharti yaś ca kirati krūradhvaniṃ niṣṭhuraḥ | 
 doṣaṃ tasya tathāvidhasya bhajataś cāpasya gṛhṇan guṇaṃ 
 vikhyātaḥ sphuṭam eka eṣa nṛpatiḥ sīmā guṇagrāhiṇām  ||1522|| 
 
 
 kavipaṇḍitaśrīharṣasya | (Nc 12.97, Sv 2508) 
 
 
 bhuje’pasarpaty api dakṣiṇe guṇaṃ 
 saheṣuṇādāya puraḥ prasarpiṇe | 
 dhanuḥparīrambham ivāsya saṃmadān 
 mahāhave yacchati vāmabāhave  ||1523|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (Nc 12.64, Sv 2525) 
 
 
 bhrūcāpaprahitena dṛṣṭiviśikhenaivāsya vidveṣiṇo 
 dhvastāḥ pūrvam atas tadīyadalane saṃbhāvi me duryaśaḥ | 
 ity ālocya karāmbujārcitam api nyastaṃ purastād api 
 drāg jātaṃ samareṣu yasya niviḍavrīḍāvinamraṃ dhanuḥ  ||1524|| 
 
 
 gotithīyadivākarasya | 
 
 
 prāgaṣṭādaśaparva bhāratam idaṃ nirmāya karmādbhutaṃ 
 bhūpānām anapāyapauruṣam iha vyāsena yat kīrtitam | 
 saṃgrāmāṅgaṇasīmni samyag adhunā deva tvadīyo bhujas 
 tatparvatrayabandhureṇa dhanuṣā vyākartum eṣa kṣamaḥ  ||1525|| 
 
 
 jalacandrasya | 
 
 
 32. prayāṇam 
 
 
 nṛpatimukuṭaratnaṃ tvatprayāṇapraśastiṃ 
 prabalabharanimajjadbhūdharākrāntabhogaḥ | 
 likhati daśanaṭaṅkair utpatadbhiḥ patadbhir 
 jaraṭhakamaṭhabhartuḥ karpare sarparājaḥ  ||1526|| 
 
 
 tripurāripālasya | 
 
 
 digyātrāsu tadīyasainikabharakṣubdhābdhikolāhala 
 trastaśrīparirambhamīlitadṛśo devasya kaṃsadviṣaḥ | 
 sasvedālasapāṇipallavagalatkaumodakīm ādarād 
 udgamyānamatphaṇaḥ phaṇabhṛtāṃ bhartā bibharti kṣitim  ||1527|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 rājan duḥsahadoḥpratāpadalitāśeṣakṣitīśasya te 
 velālokanakautukena bhavataḥ ko’yaṃ prayāṇe rasaḥ | 
 yaddantīndracamūmahābharanamannemiḥ kramād ekato 
 bhūr anyatra samunnatā phaṇipater maulau na vartiṣyate  ||1528|| 
 
 
 gadādharanāthasya | 
 
 
 te dikpālavilāsinīkucataṭe kastūrikākāntayo 
 vairistrīvadaneṣu sāñjanagalannetrāmbumaitrīdharāḥ | 
 svargaṅgākamaleṣu bhṛṅgarucayo yasya prayāṇe babhur 
 nirdhūtāḥ pavanena mattakariṇāṃ dānāmbhasāṃ bindavaḥ  ||1529|| 
 
 
 viśveśvarasya | 
 
 
 ambhaḥ kardamatām upaiti sahasā paṅkadravaḥ pāṃśutāṃ  
 pāṃśur vāraṇakarṇatālapavanair dikprāntanīhāratām | 
 nimnatvaṃ girayaḥ samaṃ viṣamatāṃ śūnyaṃ janasthānatāṃ  
 niryāte tvayi rājyapāla bhavati tyaktasvabhāvaṃ jagat  ||1530|| 
 
 
 mahodadheḥ | (su.ra. 1428) 
 
 
 33. bhogāvalī 
 
 
 rājann uddāmanidrābharavivaśabhujāvallarīṇām idānīṃ 
 viśrāmyantu tvadantaḥpurahariṇadṛśāṃ cāmarabhrāmaṇāni | 
 sevante devam ete tuhinakaṇabhṛtaḥ saudhajālāntarāla 
 prāptāḥ pratyagrajāgrannalinavanarajogrāhiṇo gandhavāhāḥ  ||1531|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 bhindānaḥ sundarīṇāṃ patiṣu ruṣamayaṃ harmyapārāvatānāṃ 
 vācālatvaṃ dadhānaḥ kavitṛṣu ca guṇaṃ prātibhaṃ sandadhānaḥ | 
 prātas tyas tūryaghoṣaḥ sthagayati gaganaṃ māṃsalaḥ pāṃśutalpād 
 asvalpād utthitānāṃ naravara kariṇāṃ śṛṅkhalaśiñjitena  ||1532|| 
 
 
 rājaśekharasya | (vi.śā.bha. 1.12, Sv 2223, śā.pa. 3722) 
 
 
 nidrājihmadṛśaḥ sakhīṣv api savailakṣyā nakhāṅkavraṇa 
 vyādaṣṭāṃśukhalekhayā pratipadaṃ sītkārivaktrendavaḥ | 
 tvatsevāsamupāgatakṣitibhujāṃ niryānti līlāgṛhād 
 etāḥ prauḍharatiśramapraśithilair aṅgaiḥ kuraṅgīdṛśaḥ  ||1533|| 
 
 
 dhoyīkasya | 
 
 
 amlānastavakanti kuntalabhare sīmantasīmāsvimāḥ  
 sindūranti kapolabhittiṣu milanmaireyarāganti ca | 
 prauḍherṣyādyutiviśramanti nayanopānte kuraṅgīdṛśaḥ  
 bimboṣṭhe kṣitipāla bālataraṇer lākṣārasanti tviṣaḥ  ||1534|| 
 
 
 sāñcādharasya |  
 
 
 utkarṇaṃ kariṇāṃ gaṇena vikasan modaṃ cirād barhibhiḥ 
 krīḍākeśaribhiś ca pañjaragataiḥ kopasphurallocanam | 
 kuñjotsaṅgabhuvi prakampataralaṃ sīmantinībhiḥ kṣaṇāt 
 pītaḥ śrotrapuṭena deva paritaḥ prātar mṛdaṅgadhvaniḥ  ||1535|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva |  
 
 
 34. tūryadhvaniḥ 
 
 
 herambadhvaniḍambarapratinidhiḥ krīḍannṛpañcānana 
 kṣveḍotpīḍasuhṛnnadīpatinadadvelomigarjāsakhaḥ | 
 saṃvartāmbudavṛndamandarasitaspardhī tavāyaṃ mṛdhe 
 śatruśrotradarīṣu mūrcchati camūbherīravo bhairavaḥ  ||1536|| 
 
 
 hareḥ | 
 
 
 deva tvadvijayaprayāṇasamaye ḍhakkā hatāḥ sainikair 
 mandraṃ dadhvanuradrikukṣiṣu jaratpārīndranidrādruhaḥ | 
 tanvānā malayādriṣu pratiravaṃ dhyānakṣatiṃ yogiṣu 
 krodhaṃ dikkariṣu prakampam ariṣu trāsaṃ raver vājiṣu  ||1537|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 guñjatkrauñcanikuñjakuñjaraghaṭāvistīrṇakarṇajvarāḥ 
 prākpratyagdharaṇīndrakandarajaratpārīndranidrādruhaḥ | 
 laṅkāṅka trikakutpratidhvanighanāḥ paryantayātrājaye 
 yasya bhremuramandamandararavair āśārudho ghoṣaṇāḥ  ||1538|| 
 
 
 jayadevasya | (su.ra. 1567) 
 
 
 yasyāvirbhūtabhītipratibhaṭapṛtanāgarbhiṇībhrūṇabhāra 
 bhraṃśabhreśābhibhūtyai plavanam iva bhajann ambhasāmbhonidhīnām | 
 saṃbhāraṃ sambhramasya tribhuvanam abhito bhūbhṛtāṃ bibhrad uccaiḥ 
 saṃrambhojjṛmbhaṇāya pratiraṇam abhavad bhūribherīninādaḥ  ||1539|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 vighaṭṭayann eṣa haṭhād akuṇṭha 
 vaikuṇṭhakaṇṭhīravakaṇṭhagarjām | 
 bhayaṅkaro dikkariṇāṃ raṇāgre 
 bherīravo bhairavaduḥśravas te  ||1540|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 35. dhūliḥ  
 
 
 yasyodyoge balānāṃ diśi diśi valatām ujjihānai rajobhir 
 jambāliny ambarasya sravadamaradhunīvāripūreṇa mārge | 
 saṃsīdaccakraśalyākulataraṇikarot pīḍitāśvīyadatta 
 dvitrāvaskandamandaḥ katham api calati syandano bhānavīyaḥ  ||1541|| 
 
 
 bāṇasya | (su.ra. 1565) 
 
 
 saptadvīpakuṭumbabhūtalabhuvo niṣpītasaptābdhayas 
 tanmārgeṇa ca saptapannagaphaṇāratnāvalokacchidaḥ | 
 krīḍā digvijaye ca saptajagatībhājo yad akṣauhiṇī 
 janmāḥ prasaranti saptapavanaskandhaspṛśo dhūlayaḥ  ||1542|| 
 
 
 murāreḥ | 
 
 
 yasyāśāvijayapravṛttapṛtanācakre parikrāmati 
 kṣuṇṇakṣmātaladhūlisaṃkulam abhūn martyasthalābhaṃ | 
 etasyām adasīyasamplavaparikṣīṇāmbhasi prāvṛṣi  
 prāyaḥ sambhavati sma bhūparisare bhūyān ivāvagrahaḥ  ||1543|| 
 
 
 tilacandrasya | 
 
 
 abdhau majjanti mīnā iva phaṇina iva kṣauṇirandhraṃ viśanti  
 krāmanty adrīn vihaṅgā iva kapaya iva kvāpy araṇye caranti | 
 deva kṣmāpālaśakra prasaradanupamatvaccamūcakravāha 
 vyūhavyādhūtadhūlīpaṭalahatadṛśaḥ kāndiśīkāḥ kṣitīśāḥ  ||1544|| 
 
 
 viśveśvarasya | 
 
 
 bhūtisnānapramodaṃ tanubhir alabhata spaṣṭam aṣṭābhir īśo 
 bhūyas tuṅgatvam āpuḥ pihitagiriguhāgahvaraāḥ kṣmādharendrāḥ | 
 yātrāyāṃ yasya khelatturagakhurakhurotkhātadhūlībhareṇa 
 prāpur varṣābhralakṣmīm atimalinatayā śāradās toyavāhāḥ  ||1545|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 36. aśvadhūliḥ  
 
 
 yātrā nehasi yasya digvijayinaḥ kāmbojavāhāvalī 
 viṅkhollelkhavisarpiṇi kṣitirajaḥpūre viyac cumbati |  
 bhānor vājibhir aṅgakarṣaṇarasānandaḥ samāsādito 
 labdhaḥ kiṃ ca nabhastalāmaradhunīpaṅkeruhair anvayaḥ  ||1546|| 
 
 
 vasukalpasya | (su.ra. 1381) 
 
 
 deva tvadvijaye turaṅgam akhuravrātakṣatakṣmātala 
 prodbhūte paritaḥ parāgapaṭale dikcakram ākramati | 
 akṣṇāṃ paṃktiśatāni nindati nijaṃ hastadvayaṃ nindati 
 svāṃ nindaty animeṣatāṃ paripatadbāspāmbudhāro hariḥ  ||1547|| 
 
 
 jayokasya | 
 
 
 vāhavyūhakhurāgraṭaṅkavihatikṣuṇṇakṣamājanmābhir 
 dhūlibhiḥ pihite vihāyasi bhavatprasthānakālotsave | 
 diṅmohākulasūrasūtavipathabhrāmyatturaṅgāvalī 
 dīrghāyuḥ prativāsaraṃ pratidiśaṃ vyasto ravir bhrāmyati  ||1548|| 
 
 
 mahodadheḥ | (su.ra. 1447) 
 
 
 tvadbhāvāvaliṭāpaṭaṅkavigaladbhūgoladhūlībharair 
 utpatyāpatayālubhiḥ sthalamaye jāte’dya nīrāmbudhau | 
 śaṅke setukathaikakarmaṭhabhujāśauṭīraśākhāmṛgā 
 haṅkārastutibhir bhaviṣyati kathaṃ na vrīḍito mārutiḥ  ||1549|| 
 
 
 hīrokasya | 
 
 
 saptāmbhodhīn pibadbhir diśi diśi saritaḥ svādayadbhis taḍāga 
 vyūhaṃ gaṇḍūṣayadbhir gaganatalagatāṃ jāhnvaīm ullihadbhiḥ | 
 yātrāyāṃ yasya helācalaturagacamūśaśvaduddhūtadhūlī 
 pūrair aikābdhimātravyayajanitamado lajjitaḥ kumbhajanmā  ||1550|| 
 
 
 chittapasya | 
 
 
 37. saṃgrāmadhūliḥ 
 
 
 yasyāhave hayacamūkhurakhaṇḍitorvī 
 pāṃśuprasāraparipūrtibhiyā vahanti | 
 netrāṇi nityavikacāni maruttaruṇyo 
 nīrandhrapāṇipuṭayugmapidhānavanti  ||1551|| 
 
 
 rājaśekharasya | 
 
 
 tvaṅgatturaṅgamukharocchalitai rajobhir 
 lagnair ajasragaladasrasahasranetraḥ | 
 pāṇigrahe samarabhūmijayaśriyas te 
 svārāḍyaṃ nṛpatinātha sahasradhāraḥ  ||1552|| 
 
 
 pajokasya | 
 
 
 tvaṅgadvairikarīndrakumbhanipatan nistriṃśalekhollasad 
 vahnijvālataḍitkarambitatanur vradhnatviṣo rundhatī | 
 rājaṃs tarpitabarhiṇā sarabhasair ālokitā cātakair 
 balāt tvadbaladhūlijālajaladaśreṇī samutsarpati  ||1553|| 
 
 
 surabheḥ | 
 
 
 etatkṛttottamāṅgapratisubhaṭanaṭārabdhanāṭyādbhutānāṃ 
 kaṣṭaṃ draṣṭaiva nābhūd bhuvi samarasamālokilokāspade’pi | 
 aśvair asvairavegaiḥ kṛtakhurakhuralīmaṅkṣuvikṣudyamāna 
 kṣmāpṛṣṭhottiṣṭhadandhaṃkaraṇaraṇadhurādhūlidhārāndhakārāt  ||1554|| 
 
 
 kavipaṇḍitaśrīharṣasya | (Nc 12.100) 
 
 
 mātaṅgābhodavīthīvikasitamahasi prauḍhasenāparāga 
 dhvāntodgāre garīyasy upanayati muhur viśvadiṅmohamudrām | 
 kīritr velāvaneṣu bhramati bhujam athālambate vīralakṣmīr 
 deva tvatkhaḍgadhārāsaraṇiparisare vairiṇo niṣpatanti  ||1555|| 
 
 
 jalacandrasya | 
 
 
 38. yuddham  
 
 
 rājan vājipadātikuñjaraśiraśchinnaṃ raṇe yat tvayā 
 nṛtyadyodhakabandhakaṇṭhamilitaṃ tenārivīravrajaḥ | 
 herambīyati kiṃnarīyati śirorāhūyatīti kṣaṇaṃ 
 nirmāṇaṃ tava baṅganāyaka kathāpāṇḍityam unmīlati  ||1556|| 
 
 
 udayādityasya | 
 
 
 saṅgrāmāṅgaṇasaṅgatena bhavatā cāpe samāropite 
 devākarṇaya yena yena sahasā yadyatsamāsāditam | 
 kodaṇḍena śarāḥ śarair aśiras tenāpi bhūmaṇḍalaṃ 
 tena tvaṃ bhavatā ca kīrtir anaghā kīrtyā ca lokatrayam  ||1557|| 
 
 
 karkarājasya | (sa.ka.ā. 1.115, su.ra. 1407) 
 
 
 śatrūṇāṃ kālarātrau samiti samudite bāṇavarṣāndhakāre 
 prāgbhāre khaḍgadhārāṃ saritam iva samuttīrya magnārivaṃśām | 
 anyonyāghātamattadviradaghanaghaṭādantavidyucchaṭābhiḥ 
 paśyantīyaṃ samantād abhisarati mudā sāṃyugīnaṃ jayaśrīḥ  ||1558|| 
 
 
 jayadevasya | 
 
 
 yadastravyāpārād abhimukhahataiḥ kṣatriyabhaṭaiḥ  
 svasattvena krītaṃ bhuvanam abhisarpadbhir abhitaḥ | 
 kṛtacchidraśreṇīvidhuraparibhogaṃ bhagavato 
 gabhastīnāṃ patyus titautulanāṃ maṇḍalam agāt  ||1559|| 
 
 
 murāreḥ | 
 
 
 yan nistriṃśahatodgatair ariśiraś cakrair babhūva kṣaṇaṃ 
 loke cāndramase vidhuṃtudaghaṭāvaskandakolāhalaḥ | 
 kiṃ cāmībhir api sphuranmukhatayā śītāṃśukoṭibhramaṃ 
 bibhrāṇair udapādi rāhubhuvane bhūyān subhikṣotsavaḥ  ||1560|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (su.ra. 1570) 
 
 
 39. yuddhasthalī 
 
 
 deva tvadbhujayor balaṃ na gadituṃ vācā vayaṃ śaknumaḥ 
 kurvāṇā hṛdaye’pi tatpulakitāḥ pratyaṅgam ete vayam | 
 śaktā saiva punas tavāsipatanacchinnadviṣatkandharā 
 randhrodvāntasamīrabhairavaravā yuddhasthalī jalpitum  ||1561|| 
 
 
 chittapasya | 
 
 
 raktasrotovahāyās tvaritam avataran snānatṛṣṇālur eko 
 vīra tvadvairsenāghanapiśitavasāpaṅkamagnaikajaṅghaḥ | 
 sākrandakvāṇam āsīt prasaradapasaratpāṇibhiḥ kṛṣṭamuktas 
 tīrasthair uttitīrṣuḥ parihasitaparais tṛptibhiḥ pretavṛddhaḥ  ||1562|| 
 
 
 nīlasya | 
 
 
 ślāghante nahi tāni yasya bhujayor adyāpi yuddhasthalī 
 sīmānte ripukīkasotthitakuśavyājena romāñcitāḥ | 
 pūrvābhyāsagatābhir aṅkapalabhugdaṃṣṭrāvalīcarvaṇān 
 nirmāṃsāsthitayoccaratkaṭakaṭaspaṣṭākṣaraśreṇayaḥ  ||1563|| 
 
 
 gotithīyadivākarasya | 
 
 
 niryannārācadhārācayakhacitapatanmattamātaṅgajātaṃ 
 jātaṃ yasyārisenārudhirajalanidhāvantarīpabhramāya | 
 suptā yasmin ratānte saha ca sahacarair nālavannāganāsā 
 randhradvandvaikapātre rudhiramadhurasaṃ pretakāntāḥ  ||1564|| 
 
 
 jayadevasya | 
 
 
 kṛṣṭe ghoṭakaṭāpasaṃpuṭaghaṭāphālāgrasaṃghaṭṭanaiś 
 chinnārātikabandharandhravigaladraktena sikte raṇe | 
 mūlena tvadasiprahārapatitā vairībhadantavrajā 
 rājante jagadagrapallaviyaśobījaprarohā iva  ||1565|| 
 
 
 vīradattasya | 
 
 
 40. digvijayaḥ 
 
 
 kṣiptaḥ kṣīragṛhe na dugdhajaladhiḥ koṣe na hemācalo 
 dikpālāḥ api pālipālanavidhāva ānīya nāropitāḥ | 
 no vā dikkariṇaḥ kvaṇan madhulihaḥ paryāyaparyāṇana 
 krīḍāyāṃ viniyojitā vada kṛtaṃ kiṃ kiṃ tvayā digjaye  ||1566|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 1446, dakṣasya) 
 
 
 deve digvijayodyate dhṛtadhanuvidveṣisīmantinī 
 vaidhavyavratadāyinī pratidiśaṃ roṣād upakrāmati | 
 kiṃ brūmo’nyad ito’dhikaṃ ratir atitrāsān na pauṣpaṃ kare 
 bhartur bhartur madān madāndhamadhupīnīlīnicolaṃ dhanuḥ  ||1567|| 
 
 
 nārāyaṇadattasya | 
 
 
 tattadvikramadohadena vilasaddordaṇḍadambholinā 
 vidveṣivyayakarmaṭhena diśatā nirvīram urvītalam | 
 kiṃ brūmaś caturabdhisīmabhuvanaṃ rājan vadātanvatā 
 yenābhūr vijigīṣuṇā vidadhire dikpālaśeṣā diśaḥ  ||1568|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 ākaumāraṃ samarajayinā kurvator vīmavīrām  
 etenāmī katham iva diśām īśitāro vimuktāḥ | 
 antarjñātaṃ vapuṣi kalayā tasya te’ṣṭau praviṣṭāḥ  
 prahvībhūte prabhavati nahi kṣatriyāṇāṃ kṛpāṇaḥ  ||1569|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 ekaḥ saṃgrāmariṅgatturagakhurarajorājibhir naṣṭadṛṣṭir  
 digyātrājaitramattadviradabharanamadbhūmibhagnas tathānyaḥ | 
 vīrāḥ ke nāma tasmāt trijagati na yayuḥ kṣīṇatāṃ kāṇakubja 
 nyāyād etena muktāv abhayam abhajatāṃ vāsavo vāsukiś ca  ||1570|| 
 
 
 jayadevasya | 
 
 
 41. ripuḥ 
 
 
 yānty eke parapuṣṭatāṃ balibhujo bhrāmyanti kecin mahīṃ 
 kecid bibhrati lāvakatvam apare jātā vane vartakāḥ | 
 kecit khañjanakībhavanti satatonmāthapramāthair aho 
 tiryaktām api lambhitais tvadaribhir labdhā na pakṣonnatiḥ  ||1571|| 
 
 
 
 kasyacit | (Sv 2582) 
 
 
 nirbhīkabhrāntabhoginy analasamaśake māṃsaladhvāntarāśāv 
 āsāraklinnakuḍye vṛṣabhanikaṣaṇāv arjitadvāradārau | 
 pratyagrodīrṇagarbhe galati vanagirigrāmadevīgṛhānte 
 saṃtrastāḥ śatravas te katham api rajanīṃ prāvṛṣi prerayanti  ||1572|| 
 
 
 yogeśvarasya | 
 
 
 padbyām ūruyugaṃ vibhajya bhujayor madhyaṃ nipīḍyorasā 
 pārśveṣu prasabhaṃ prahṛtya nakharair dantair vilupyādharam | 
 saṃsuptān avabodhya yuṣmadahitān bhūyo’pi bhuṅkte vane 
 kiṃ kāntā surataiṣiṇī nahi nahi vyāghrī karālānanā  ||1573|| 
 
 
 
 chittapasya | (sa.ka.ā. 5.500) 
 
 
 maukharyaṃ varam astu deva tad api prasūyate vismayād 
 aiśvaryāṇi parityajanti bhavato nādyāpi te vairiṇaḥ | 
 manyūnāṃ śatam ācaranti kaṭakaṃ krāmanti bhūmībhṛtāṃ 
 patrālīṃ valayanti ca stanayugābhoge kuraṅgīdṛśām  ||1574|| 
 
 
 jalacandrasya | 
 
 
 padahīnān bilavasatīn  
 bhujagān iva jātabhogasaṅkocān | 
 vyathayati mantrākṣaram iva  
 nāma tavārīn vanecarair gītam  ||1575|| 
 
 
 daṅkasya | (su.ra. 1393) 
 
 
 42. ripusambhramaḥ 
 
 
 koṣān geheṣu muñcan pathi karituragaṃ bāndhavān arghamārge 
 durgeṣv antaḥpurāṇi prativalacakritāḥ parvatebhyo nivṛttāḥ | 
 yasyodyoge bhramantaḥ samasamayasmārambhagambhīrabherī 
 bhāṅgārākīrṇakarṇajvarabharataralaprekṣitāśāḥ kṣitīśāḥ  ||1576|| 
 
 
 viśveśvarasya | 
 
 
 śrutvā yaṃ sahasāgataṃ nijapurāt trāsena nirgacchatāṃ 
 śatrūṇām avarodhanair jalalavaprasyandatimyatpuṭāḥ | 
 śubhre sadmani pallaviny upavane vāpyāṃ navāmbhoruhi  
 krīḍādrau ca saśādvale vivalitagrīvair vimuktā dṛśaḥ  ||1577|| 
 
 
 dhanapateḥ | (sa.ka.ā. 1.83) 
 
 
 mugdhe kiṃ śukapañjareṇa rasike kiṃ sārakānveṣaṇaiḥ 
 susthe muñcasi kiṃ na citraphalakaṃ kiṃ vīṇayā rāgiṇi | 
 nāyaṃ bhūṣaṇasaṃgrahasya samayo līlāvati tvaryatām 
 ity āsan puravidrave bhavadaristrīṇāṃ vayasyāgiraḥ  ||1578|| 
 
 
 rājaśekharasya | 
 
 
 vatse mālati mālikā na racitā puṣpais tvadīyair mayā 
 raktāśokataro tavāpy abhinavo nottaṃsitaḥ pallavaḥ | 
 vyāloālikulāvalīḍhamukulas tvaṃ cūta nālokito 
 hā dhik kaṣṭam iti bruvanti nagaratyāge tavāristriyaḥ  ||1579|| 
 
 
 gadādharasya | 
 
 
 mātar mātar janaka janaka preyasi preyasīti  
 bhrātar bhrātas tanaya tanaya jyāyasi jyāyasīti | 
 yan nāsīrapracuragadhyūhavitrastavairi 
 strīpuṃsānāṃ vidalati daladdikkalāpo vilāpaḥ  ||1580|| 
 
 
 dākṣiṇātyasya | 
 
 
 43. arivadhūḥ 
 
 
 kāntāreṣu karāvalambiśiśavaḥ pādaiḥ sravallohitair  
 arcantyaḥ padavīṃ vilocanajalair āvedayantyaḥ śucam | 
 dṛṣṭāḥ pānthajanair vivṛtya sakṛpaṃ hāśabdagarbhair mukhair  
 yanty ahnā sakalena yojanaturīyāṃśaṃ tavāristriyaḥ  ||1581|| 
 
 
 puruṣottamasya | 
 
 
 pārekandaram iṅgudīvanam ito nīvārakedārikā 
 svacchandaṃ sarasas taṭe kamalinīvṛndāḍhyamandānilaḥ | 
 svacchaṃ nirjharavārivāraṇaradotkhātās tato bhūruhā 
 itthaṃ vyādhavadhūr vibodhya nayati tvadvairivīrāṅganāḥ  ||1582|| 
 
 
 vibhākarasya | 
 
 
 ghrātaṃ tālaphalāśayā stanayugaṃ bimbabhrameṇādharo 
 daṣṭaṃ pākavidīrṇadāḍimadhiyā līḍhāḥ sphuranto radāḥ | 
 bhrāmyantī śramaniḥsahānuvipinaṃ yadvairisīmantinī 
 nidrāṇā muhur āhatā mhur adhikṣiptā ca śākhāmṛgaiḥ  ||1583|| 
 
 
 dhanañjayasya | 
 
 
 kuru taruṣu gṛhāsthāṃ talpabuddhiṃ tṛṇeṣu 
 tvaci nivasanavāñchām annatṛṣṇāṃ phaleṣu | 
 iti vinayati deva preyasīṃ tvadripūṇām 
 abhinavavanavāsodvegamugdhāṃ kirātī  ||1584|| 
 
 
 vīrabhadrasya | 
 
 
 nyañcannīvīnibaddhānyakalitatilakānyakvaṇatkaṅkaṇāni  
 bhraśyanmañjīraśiñjāny acalitavalayasrañji dhautāñjanāni | 
 apreṅkhattārahārāṇyavasitahasitaśrīṇi śīrṇālakāni 
 truṭyatsindūrabindūrabindūny asakṛd akṛta yaḥ śātravāntaḥpurāṇi  ||1585|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 44. arivadhūbāṣpaḥ 
 
 
 hā citrāṅgi kuraṅgi # # # # # hā rājahaṃsapriye 
 hā cūtadruma hā priyaṅgulatike tyaktāḥ stha hā dhik katham | 
 itthaṃ tvatparipanthipārthivapurandhrīṇāṃ vanaprasthitau 
 dhārādhautikapolayor nayanayor asraṃ na viśrāmyati  ||1586|| 
 
 
 gadādharanāthasya |  
 
 
 saṃdiṣṭaṃ marubhūmibhūruhacayair bhūyād bhavān bhūpatir 
 nirjetā navakhaṇḍamaṇḍalabhuvo yat tvatprasādād vayam | 
 pratyāsannavipannahūṇataruṇīnetrapraṇālīgalad 
 bāṣpāmbhaḥplavapūrapicchilatalāḥ śrīmuñja modāmahe  ||1587|| 
 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 1398) 
 
 
 etad bhītārinārī giribilavigaladvāsarā niḥsarantī 
 svakrīḍāhaṃsamohagrahilaśiśubhṛśaprārthi tonnidracandrā | 
 ākrandad bhūri yat tan nayanajalamilaccandrahaṃsānubimba 
 pratyāsattiprahṛṣyattanayavihasitair āśvasīn nyaśvasīc ca  ||1588|| 
 
 
 kavipaṇḍitaśrīharṣasya | (Nc 12.28) 
 
 
 gambhīranīrasarasīr api puruṣāḥ 
 kurvanti ye dinakarasya karās ta eva | 
 tvadvairivīravanitānayanāmbuleśa 
 śoṣe kathaṃ pratihatā iti me vitarkaḥ  ||1589|| 
 
 
 kalpadattasya | (su.ra. 1424) 
 
 
 ke y¨¨uyaṃ munayaḥ kim atra tapase sthānaṃ samīhāmahe 
 nīvārāṅkuradanturā niyamitavyādhāsti vindhyāṭavī | 
 sā sampraty avanīmahendra bhavato vidveṣivāmabhruvām 
 aśrāntacyutalolalocanapayovanyābhir anyādṛśī  ||1590|| 
 
 
 kavirājasomasya | 
 
 
 45. aripuram 
 
 
 adhākṣīn no laṅkām ayam ayam udanvantam atarad  
 viśalyāṃ saumitrair ayam upanināyauṣadhivarām | 
 iti smāraṃ smāraṃ tvadarinagarībhittilikhitaṃ  
 hanūmantaṃ dantair daśati kupito rākṣasagaṇaḥ  ||1591|| 
 
 
 parimalasya | (śā.pa. 1267) 
 
 
 lūtātantupaṭāvanaddhaśiraso vellallatāsaṃtater 
 anyonyaṃ milanāc ciraspṛham iva vyāsaktakaṇṭhagrahāḥ | 
 krīḍānirvṛtaghūtkṛtiravaiḥ sākrandabaddhāravaṃ 
 krandanti tvadarātirājanagarīrathyābhuvo vīrudhaḥ  ||1592|| 
 
 
 yuvarājasya | 
 
 
 varṣāsambhṛtapītimānamanavaṃ stabdhāṅghrihastadvayaṃ 
 bhekaṃ mūrdhni nigṛhya kajjalarajaḥśyāmaṃ bhujaṅgaṃ sthitam | 
 mugdhāvyādhavadhūs tavārinagare śūnye cirāt samprati  
 svarṇopaskṛtamuṣṭisāyakadhiyā sākūtam ākarṣati  ||1593|| 
 
 
 chittapasya | (su.ra. 1401) 
 
 
 līlācūtatamālakeśarataruskandhe pravṛddhālaya 
 svecchonmadakarkareṭuraṭitair bhīmaṃ bahiḥ kānanam | 
 antarveśmavilolacarmacaṭakāpakṣmāñcalodvījana 
 krīḍāsuptapiśācadampatipuraṃ rājan bhavadvidviṣām  ||1594|| 
 
 
 viśveśvarasya | 
 
 
 krūrotkūjatkareṭupratiravavirasajjarjaragranthibandhāḥ 
 sthāārthipretamalladvayakalahasamāvarjitasthūlaśākhāḥ | 
 golomīcchann amātṛpratikṛtiviratapratyabhijñā divāpi 
 tvacchatrugrāmadevīnilayanataravas trāsam utpādayanti  ||1595|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 46. arigṛham 
 
 
 dvāraṃ khaḍgibhir āvṛtaṃ bahir api prasivnnagaṇḍair gajair 
 antaḥ kañcukibhiḥ sphūran maṇidharair adhyāsitā bhūmayaḥ | 
 ākrāntaṃ mahiṣībhir eva śayanaṃ tvadvidviṣāṃ mandire 
 rājan saiva cirantanapraṇayinīśūnye’pi rājyasthitiḥ  ||1596|| 
 
 
 yogeśvarasya | (su.ra. 1403, Sv 2569, sū.mu. 97.78, Kuval, p. 161) 
 
 
 vanyo hastī sphaṭikaghaṭite bhittabhogeṣu bimbaṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā ruṣṭaḥ pratigaja iti tvaddviṣāṃ mandireṣu | 
 dantāghātākulitadaśanas tat punar vīkṣamāṇo 
 mandaṃ mandaṃ spṛśati kariṇīśaṅkayā sāhasāṅkaḥ  ||1597|| 
 
 
 vetālasya | 
 
 
 randhre saṃnyastadṛṣṭiḥ kṣitinihitatanuḥ krīḍasaṃlīnapucchaḥ 
 pratyāśāyojitātmā grahaṇapariṇataḥ stabdhakarṇo viśaṅkaḥ | 
 saṃkocābaddhadeho niyamitacaraṇaḥ prasphuracchmaśrujālaḥ  
 śūnye rājan viḍālas tava ripubhavane mūṣikān ucchinatti  ||1598|| 
 
 
 yogeśvarasya | 
 
 
 vatse mādhavi tāta campaka śiśo mākanda kaundi priye 
 hā mātar madayanti hā kuravaka bhrātaḥ khasar mālati | 
 ity evaṃ ripumandireṣu bhavataḥ śṛṇvanti naktaṃcarā 
 golāṅgūlavimardasaṃbhramavaśād udyānadevīgiraḥ  ||1599|| 
 
 
 śubhāṅkasya | (su.ra. 1412) 
 
 
 snātaḥ samprati vārivāhasalilaiḥ saṃrūḍhaśappāṅkura 
 vyājenāttakuśāḥ praṇālasalilair dattvā nivāpāñjalim | 
 prāsādās tava vidviṣāṃ paripatkuḍyasya piṇḍacchalāt 
 kurvanti prativāsaraṃ nijapatipretāya piṇḍakriyām  ||1600|| 
 
 
 mahādevasya | 
 
 
 47. yaśaḥ  
 
 
 mūlaṃ phaṇāḥ phaṇipater gaganaṃ ca madhyaḥ 
 śākhā diśo jaladhimaṇḍalam ālavālam |  
 trailokyanātha tava deva yaśodrumasya 
 tārāgaṇāḥ sumanasaḥ phalam indubimbam  ||1601|| 
 
 
 śrīhanūmataḥ | 
 
 
 mātuḥ svedamayaṃ tatāna pṛthukaḥ kroḍena dhātryām asau 
 rāgāḍhyas taruṇaḥ purandarapurastrīnyastakaṇṭhagrahaḥ | 
 jyāyān apy abhinatpitāmahapadaṃ nityāvinītas tanū 
 janmā te yaśasāṃ gaṇas taducitavrīḍo’si tatkīrtane  ||1602|| 
 
 
 chittapasya | (sū.mu. 97.39) 
 
 
 baddho naiṣa na laṅghito na mathitaḥ pīto na vā bāḍava 
 vyagro nāpi yaśomayo yadupater amlāyamāno’mbudhiḥ | 
 abdhīṃl labdhaparābhavānadharayann arvāg atho’rvībhṛtaḥ  
 kurvan garvavilaṅghitāvadhir adhi brahmāṇḍam ārohati  ||1603|| 
 
 
 vācaspateḥ | 
 
 
 airāvaṇanti kariṇaḥ phaṇino’py aśeṣāḥ 
 śeṣanti hanta vihagā api haṃsitāraḥ | 
 nīlotpalāni kumudanti ca sarvaśailāḥ 
 kailāsituṃ vyavasitā bhavato yaśobhiḥ  ||1604|| 
 
 
 mahāśakteḥ | (su.ra. 1011) 
 
 
 deva svasti vayaṃ dvijās tata itas tīrtheṣu niṣkalmaṣāḥ 
 kālindīsurasindhusaṅgapayasi snātuṃ samīhāmahe | 
 tad yācemahi saptaviṣṭapaśucībhāvaikatānavrataṃ 
 saṃyaccha svayaśaḥ sitāsitapayobhedād viveko’stu naḥ  ||1605|| 
 
 
 rathāṅgasya | (su.ra. 995) 
 
 
 48. savīryayaśaḥ 
 
 
 na tac citraṃ citte vitatakaravālograrasano 
 mahībhāraṃ soḍhuṃ bhujabhujagarājaḥ prabhavati | 
 yad udbhūtenedaṃ navavisalatātantuśucinā 
 yaśonrimokeṇa sthagitam avanīmaṇḍalam abhūt  ||1606|| 
 
 
 saṅghaśriyaḥ | (su.ra. 1013) 
 
 
 śrīmanpātālakukṣimbharibharitasurasthānam ambhodhirodho 
 rodhi kṣmāśodhi śuddhaṃ prasarati yad idaṃ tvadyaśas tat kim āhuḥ | 
 tad brūmas tvatpratāpānalamilanakṛtakvāthasambhāradūra 
 sphārottālo’yam abhraṃlihalaharibharo vardhate dugdhasindhuḥ  ||1607|| 
 
 
 śrīkaṇṭhasya | 
 
 
 candrābhair bhavato yaśobhir amalair vistāritāyāṃ diśi 
 jyotsnāyāṃ tava vairivargavadane viśrāntam andhaṃ tamaḥ | 
 kiṃ ca bhrūtilakāntapātamilitaśrībhārasaṃvardhita 
 premāṇi prahasanti bandhukumudāny āmodavanti sphuṭam  ||1608|| 
 
 
 gosokasya | 
 
 
 dṛṣṭaṃ saṅgarasākṣibhir nigaditaṃ vaitālikaśreṇibhir 
 nyastaṃ cetasi khañjanaiḥ sukavibhiḥ kāvyeṣu saṃcāritam | 
 utkīrṇaṃ kuśalaiḥ praśastiṣu sadā gītaṃ ca nākeṣadāṃ 
 dānair nirjitavairivīra bhavataś candrāvadātaṃ yaśaḥ  ||1609|| 
 
 
 rājaśekharasya | (su.ra. 1000) 
 
 
 muktāśīkaranirjharāsu sadasi kṣuṇṇāsu kumbhasthalīṣv 
 ādantaḥ sphuṭakarṇacāmaradṛśāsvāvarjināṃ dantinām | 
 kṣetrīkṛtya varūthinīṃ yudhi jayaśrīkarṣakeṇa dviṣāṃ 
 yenoptā iva muṣṭibhir nijayaśobījacchaṭā rejire  ||1610|| 
 
 
 bhikṣoḥ | 
 
 
 49. praśastayaśaḥ 
 
 
 ākṣiptā cāmaraśrīḥ prasabham apahṛtaḥ pauṇḍarīko vilāsaḥ  
 pracchanno vīrakambuḥ samajani vihitaḥ kaṇṭhabhārāya hāraḥ | 
 lupto hāsaprakāśaḥ kam api paribhavaṃ prāpitaḥ puṣparāśiś 
 candrābhair yadyaśobhiḥ pratidharaṇibhujāṃ nihnutā kiṃ ca kīrtiḥ  ||1611|| 
 
 
 śrīmatkeśavasenadevasya |  
 
 
 ambhodhikṣiptamuktāruciharicaraṇodgīrṇagaṅgāmbutulyaṃ  
 kālindīphenakāntisphuritaphaṇadharonmuktanirmokarociḥ | 
 karṇāṭīkuntalāntarvigalitasumanodāmaramyaṃ samantāc  
 chrīkhaṇḍālepalakṣmīm upanayati yaśo yasya khaḍgaprasūtam  ||1612|| 
 
 
 jalacandrasya | 
 
 
 bhūcakraṃ kiyad etad āvṛtam abhūd yad vāmanasyāṅghriṇā 
 nāgānāṃ kiyad āspadaṃ yadurasā laṅghanti gūḍhāṅghrayaḥ | 
 ekāhād yad anūrur añcati kiyan mātraṃ tad apy ambaraṃ 
 yasyetīva yaśo hriyā tribhuvanaṃ vyāpyāpi no tṛpyati  ||1613|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 gṛhād gṛham upāgataṃ vrajati pattanaṃ pattanād 
 vanād dhanam anudrutaṃ bhramati pādapaṃ pādapāt | 
 girer girim adhiśritaṃ tarati vāridhiṃ vāridher 
 yadīyam arisundarīnikarapṛṣṭhalagnaṃ yaśaḥ  ||1614|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 āste dāmodarīyām iyam udaradarīṃ yāv alambya trilokī 
 saṃmātuṃ śaknuvanti prathimabharavaśād atra naitad yaśāṃsi | 
 tām etāṃ pūrayitvā niragur iva madhudhvaṃsinaḥ pāṇḍupadma 
 cchadmāpannāni tāni dvipadaśanasanābhīni nābhīpathena  ||1615|| 
 
 
 kavipaṇḍitaśrīharṣasya | (Nc 12.95, Sv 2520, sū.mu. 97.23) 
 
 
 50. kīrtiḥ  
 
 
 kā tvaṃ, kuntalamallakīrtir, ahaha kvāsi sthitā, na kvacit 
 sakhyas tās tava kutra kutra vada vāg lakṣmīs rucaḥ samprati | 
 vāg yātā caturānanasya vadanaṃ lakṣmīr murārer uraḥ 
 kāntir maṇḍalam aindavaṃ mama punar nādyāpi viśrāmabhūḥ  ||1616|| 
 
 
 chittapasya | (su.ra. 1005) 
 
 
 rāmaḥ sainyasamanvitaḥ kṛtaśilāsetur yad ambhonidheḥ 
 pāraṃ laṅghitavān purā tad adhunā nāścaryam utpādayet | 
 ekākiny api setubandharahitān saptāpi vārāṃ nidhīn 
 helābhis tava deva kīrtivanitā yasmāt samullaṅghati  ||1617|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (su.ra. 1012) 
 
 
 kiṃ vṛttāntaiḥ paragṛhagataiḥ kiṃtu nāhaṃ samarathas 
 tūṣṇīṃ sthātuṃ prakṛtimukharo dākṣiṇātyasvabhāvaḥ | 
 deśe deśe vipaṇiṣu tathā catvare pānagoṣṭhyām 
 unmatteva bhramati bhavato vallabhā hanta kīrtiḥ  ||1618|| 
 
 
 tutātitasya | (Sv 2544, su.ra. 996, śā.pa. 1227) 
 
 
 anantāsau kīrtiḥ kavikumudabandhoḥ kṣitipates  
 trilokīyaṃ kṣudrā tad iha katham asyāḥ sthitir iti | 
 mudheyaṃ vaḥ śaṅkā kalayata kiyaddarpaṇatalaṃ  
 viśālā kiṃ tatra sphurati na kavīndrapratikṛtiḥ  ||1619|| 
 
 
 pañcākṣarasya | 
 
 
 dhyāyantī nirapāyanāyakaguṇaṃ tvatkīrtir ambhonidher 
 bhrāmyanit vipināntareṣu virahavyagreva pāṇḍucchaviḥ | 
 candraṃ nindati candanaṃ na sahate dveṣṭi śriyaṃ śāradīṃ 
 dūrād eva nirākaroti karakākarpūrahārasrajaḥ  ||1620|| 
 
 
 śaraṇasya | 
 
 
 51. savīryakīrtiḥ  
 
 
 vīrakṣīrasamudrasāndralaharīlāvaṇyalakṣmīmusas 
 tvatkīrtes tulanāṃ kalaṅkamalino dhatte kathaṃ candramāḥ | 
 syād evaṃ tvadarātisaudhaśikharaprodbhūtaśaṣpāṅkura 
 grāsavyagramanāḥ pated yadi punas tasyāṅkaśāyī mṛgaḥ  ||1621|| 
 
 
 śākyarakṣitasya | (sū.mu. 97.30) 
 
 
 niḥsṛtyāhavasāgarād atha punaḥ saṃsṛtya pṛthvītalaṃ 
 kṛtvādho himaśailam īśvaraśiraḥśītāṃśulekhām api | 
 gaṅgeva smṛtajanmabhūmir amaraiḥ sāścaryam ālokitā 
 kīrtis te pratilomalaṅghitaviyadbrahmāṇḍam ārohati  ||1622|| 
 
 
 vākpateḥ | (sū.mu. 97.44) 
 
 
 āsīd uptaṃ yad etad raṇabhuvi bhavatā vairimātaṅgakumbhān 
 muktābījaṃ vimuktaṃ trijagati janayāmāsa kīrtidrumaṃ te | 
 śeṣo mūlaṃ prakāṇḍaṃ himagirir udadhir dugdhapūrālavālaṃ 
 jyotsnā śākhāpratānaḥ kusumam uḍucayā yasya candraḥ phalaṃ ca  ||1623|| 
 
 
 hareḥ | (su.ra. 1006) 
 
 
 ekā gaṅgā prayāge malayaparisare candanaṃ mauktikālī 
 kāntākaṇṭhe himāṃśur viyati sarasi śvetam abjaṃ tathāsyāḥ | 
 kālindī kālasarpā marakatataralo lāñchanaṃ bhṛṅgamālety  
 evaṃ te yatra kīrtiḥ pariṇamati yutā yatra śatror akīrtyā  ||1624|| 
 
 
 rāmasya | 
 
 
 sā candrād api candanād api daravyākoṣakundād api 
 kṣīrābdher api śeṣato’pi phaṇinaś caṇḍīśahāsād api | 
 karṇātīsitadantapatramahaso’py atyantam uddyotinī 
 kīrtis te bhujavīryanirjitaripor lokatrayaṃ bhrāmyati  ||1625|| 
 
 
 rājaśekharasya | (su.ra. 997) 
 
 
 52. praśastakīrtiḥ  
 
 
 antaḥsantoṣabāṣpaiḥ sthagayati nayanaṃ na śrutibhraṃśabhīrur 
 nāṅgenānastiromā racayati pulakaśreṇim ānandakandām | 
 na kṣoṇībhaṅgabhīruḥ kalayati ca śiraḥkampanaṃ tan na vidmaḥ  
 śṛṇvann etasya kīrtīḥ katham uragapatiḥ prītim āviṣkaroti  ||1626|| 
 
 
 kavipaṇḍitaśrīharṣasya | (Nc 12.39, sū.mu. 97.24) 
 
 
 kṣīrodanvān alīkaḥ kapaṭamayatanus tryambakasyāṭṭahāso 
 mithyānīhārasampattribhuvanavivare kṛtrimā paurṇamāsī | 
 saṃvṛttāmbhodavṛndasphuradūrukarakāsārasaṃdehadāyī 
 dāyādaḥ kundabhāsāṃ diśi vidiśi babhau yasya kīrtipratānaḥ  ||1627|| 
 
 
 vasukalpasya | 
 
 
 kailāse nihnutaśrīḥ pariphitavapuḥ pārvaṇaḥ śvetabhānuḥ  
 śeṣaḥ pracchannaveśaḥ kalayati na ruciṃ jāhnavīvāriveṇiḥ | 
 pītaḥ kṣīrāmburāśiḥ prasabham apahṛtaḥ kuñjaro devabhartur 
 yatkīrtīnāṃ vivartair ajani sa bhagavān ekadanto’py adantaḥ  ||1628|| 
 
 
 śrīmatkeśavasenadevasya | 
 
 
 yadvartmodyāti roddhuṃ tripuraharagirigrāmaṇīs tan niyantuṃ 
 kauverīṃ kumbhajanmā vrajati yadi tadā durdharā vindhyavṛddhiḥ | 
 itthaṃ yatkīrtirāśau tirdaśapatipurākrāntidattaprayāṇe 
 cintāgniḥ krūrakarmā vyathayati hṛdayaṃ tejasām īśvarasya  ||1629|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 malinayati vairivadanaṃ svajanaṃ rañjayati dhavalayati dhātrīm | 
 api kusumaviśadamūrtir yatkīrtiś citram ācarati  ||1630|| 
 
 
 jayadevasya | 
 
 
 53. kīrtigītiḥ 
 
 
 līlālolakarāṅgulīhatiraṇadvīṇāguṇaproccarad 
 gāndhāradhvanisaṃvadanmṛdukalāsnigdhasvarodgāribhiḥ | 
 lolanmaulikbhir ardhamīlitalasannetrair baladbhūlatair 
 gīyante gaganecaraiḥ surapater agre bhavatkīrtayaḥ  ||1631|| 
 
 
 surabheḥ | 
 
 
 bhogīndraḥ pramadottaraṅgamuragīsaṅgītagoṣṭhīṣu te 
 kīrtiṃ deva śṛṇotu viṃśatiśatī yac cakṣuṣāṃ vartate | 
 raktābhiḥ surasundarībhir abhito gītāṃ tu karṇadvayī 
 duḥsthaḥ śroṣyati nāma kiṃ sa hi sahasrākṣo na cakṣuḥśravāḥ  ||1632|| 
 
 
 murāreḥ | (Ar 7.79; Sv 2638) 
 
 
 gīyante yadi pannagībhir aniśaṃ tvatkīrtayas tad vayaṃ 
 tuṣṭā eva paraṃ tu cetasi camatkāro’yam ārohati | 
 tāsāṃ tādṛśabhāvabhaṅgivalanā saṃsthānasaṃdarśini 
 vyālendre rasadhūtamūrdhani mahīcakraṃ punar bhraṃkṣyate  ||1633|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 adya svargavadhūgaṇe guṇamaya tvatkīrtim indūjjvalām  
 uccair gāyati niṣkalaṅkimadaśām ādāsyate candramāḥ | 
 gītākarṇanamodamuktayavasagrāsābhilāṣo vada  
 svāminn aṅkamṛgaḥ kiyanti hi dināny etasya vartiṣyate  ||1634|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (su.ra. 1007) 
 
 
 asya kṣoṇipateḥ parārdhaparayā lakṣīkṛtāḥ saṃkhyayā  
 prajñācakṣur avekṣyamāṇatimiraprakhyāḥ kilākīrttayaḥ | 
 gīyante svaram aṣṭamaṃ kalayatā jātena vandhyodarān  
 mūkānāṃ prakareṇa kūrmaramaṇīdugdhodadheḥ rodhasi  ||1635|| 
 
 
 kavipaṇḍitaśrīharṣasya | (Kuval, p. 146, Nc 12.106) 
 
 
 54. uccāvacacāṭuḥ 
 
 
 abhyuddhṛtā vasumatī dalitaṃ ripūraḥ  
 krīḍīkṛtā balavatā balirājalakṣmīḥ | 
 ekatra janmani kṛtaṃ tadanena yūnā  
 janmatraye yad akarot puruṣaḥ purāṇaḥ  ||1636|| 
 
 
 śrīhanūmataḥ | (sa.ka.ā. 1.98, V 471, sū.mu. 97.5) 
 
 
 karṇaṃ cakṣur ajīgaṇat tava pitus tātaḥ pitā te punaḥ 
 śaktyādhārakumāram apy ajagaṇat taṃ kātaratvena saḥ | 
 devo’gān mahiṣīti paśyati jagat tv evaṃ vivektuṃ punaḥ 
 prāgalbhyaṃ prathayanti vas tad api ca prajñādhanāḥ sādhavaḥ  ||1637|| 
 
 
 vidyāpateḥ | 
 
 
 prabhur asi vayaṃ mālākāravratavyavasāyino 
 vacanakusumaṃ tenāsmābhis tavādaraḍhaukitam | 
 yadi tadguṇaṃ kaṇṭhe mā dhās tathorasi mā kṛthā 
 navam iti kiyat karṇau dhehi kṣaṇaṃ phalatu śramaḥ  ||1638|| 
 
 
 vīryamitrasya | (su.ra. 1418) 
 
 
 vaktraṃ sākṣāt sarasvaty adhivasati sadā śoṇa evādharas te 
 bāhuḥ kākutsthavīryasmṛtikaraṇapaṭur dakṣiṇas te samudraḥ | 
 vāhinyaḥ pārśvam etāḥ kṣaṇam api bhavato naiva muñcanti rājan 
 svacche’to mānase’sminn avatarati kathaṃ toyaleśābhilāṣaḥ  ||1639|| 
 
 
 hariścandrasya | 
 
 
 devaḥ kupyatu vā vicintya vinayaṃ prīto’stu vā mādṛśair 
 vāñchadbhiḥ prabhukīrtim apratihatāṃ vaktavyam evocitam | 
 sevābhir yadi senavaṃśatilakād āsādanīyāḥ śriyaḥ 
 saṃkalpānuvidhāyinaḥ surataros tat kena hāryo madaḥ  ||1640|| 
 
 
 śaraṇadevasya | 
 
 
 śrīdharadāsakṛte’smin saduktikarṇāmṛte tṛtīyo’yam | 
 cāṭupravāha īpsitaphalaprado bhavatu saṃtataṃ kṛtinām || 
 
 iti śrīmahāmāṇḍalikaśrīdharadāsakṛtau saduktikarṇāmṛte | 
 
 cāṭupravāho nāma tṛtīyaḥ | vīcayaḥ 54 | ślokāḥ 270 || 
 
  o)0(o 
  saduktikarṇāmṛtam 
 
 
 
 
 (4) 
 apadeśapravāhavīcayaḥ 
 
 
 1. vāsudevaḥ 
 
 
 bhūtā eva timiṅgilaprabhṛtayo ye yādasām agrimās 
 te vaisāriṇaveśakeśavaśiśor jātā na rātrau punaḥ | 
 pṛṣṭhaproñchitatoyatucchajaladher āpūrya yenāntaraṃ 
 tāḥ kallolaparamparā iva paraṃ dehatvaco darśitāḥ  ||1641|| 
 
 
 kṣiyākasya | 
 
 
 bhramati girirāṭ pṛṣṭhe garjaty upaśruti sāgaro 
 dahati vitatajvālājālo jaganti viṣānalaḥ | 
 sa tu vinihitagrīvākāṇḍaḥ kaṭāhapuṭāntare 
 svapiti bhagavān kūrmo nidrābharālasalocanaḥ  ||1642|| 
 
 
 cirantanaśaraṇasya | (su.ra. 118, sū.mu. 108.2) 
 
 
 jāyante bahavo’tra kacchapakule kiṃ tu kvacit kacchapī 
 naikāpy ekam asūta sūnum aparaṃ sūtena vā soṣyate | 
 ākalpaṃ dharaṇīdharodvahanataḥ santāpakhinnātmano 
 yaḥ kūrmasya dināni nāma katicid viśrāmadānakṣamaḥ  ||1643|| 
 
 
 śatānandasya | (su.ra. 1105) 
 
 
 niṣkandāmaravindinīṃ sthapuṭitoddeśāṃ sthalīṃ palvale 
 jambālāvilam ambu kartum aparā sūte varāhī sutān | 
 daṃṣṭrāyāṃ caturarṇavormitpaṭalair āplāvitāyām iyaṃ 
 yasyā eva śiśoḥ sthitā vipadi bhūḥ sā putriṇī potriṇī  ||1644|| 
 
 
 abhinandasya | (sa.ka.ā. 4.94, śā.pa. 1214, sū.mu. 36.6) 
 
 
 apatyāni prāyo daśa daśa varāhī janayati 
 kṣamābhāre dhuryaḥ sa punar iha nāsīn na bhavitā | 
 padaṃ kṛtvā yaḥ svaṃ phaṇipatiphaṇācakravalaye 
 nimajjantīm antarjaladhi vasudhām udvalayati  ||1645|| 
 
 
 varāhasya | (su.ra. 1206) 
 
 
 2. mahādevaḥ 
 
 
 devair dugdhapayodhirodhasi urā kair nāma manthācala 
 kṣobhaprodgatacandramaḥprabhṛtaye na preṣitāḥ pāṇayaḥ | 
 svīcakre param eka eva bhagavān udvignalokatrayī 
 rakṣāyai kaṭukālakūṭagaralagrāsaṃ sa gaurīśvaraḥ  ||1646|| 
 
 
 vāsudevasenasya | 
 
 
 chinne brahmaśiro yadi prathayati preteṣu sakhyaṃ yadi 
 kṣīvaḥ krīḍati mātṛbhir yadi ratiṃ dhatte śmaśāne yadi | 
 sṛṣṭvā saṃharati prajā yadi tadāpy ādhāya bhaktyā manas 
 taṃ seve karavāṇi kiṃ trijagatī śūnyā sa eveśvaraḥ  ||1647|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 svaṃ cet saṃcarase vṛṣeṇa laghutā kā nāma digdantināṃ 
 vyālaiḥ kaṅkaṇakuṇḍalāni kuruṣe hānir na hemnām api | 
 mūrdhanyaṃ tanuṣe jaḍāṃśum ayaśaḥ kiṃ nāma lokatrayī 
 dīpasyāmbujabāndhavasya jagatām īśo’si kiṃ brūmahe  ||1648|| 
 
 
 śailasarvasya | 
 
 
 āhāro garalaṃ tṛtīyam alike cakṣuḥ kapālaṃ kare 
 vāsaḥ kuñjaracarma bhasmani ratir bhūṣā bhujaṅgādhipaḥ | 
 janmālakṣyam asākṣikaṃ kulam avijñātā ca jātiḥ  
 kathaṃ sevyo’smābhir asau piśācapariṣadbhartā hatāḥ smo vayam  ||1649|| 
 
 
 dharmayogeśvarasya | 
 
 
 pāṇau brahmakapālam ashitbhir alaṅkāro’ṅgarāgaś citā 
 bhasmāvyāhatam uttarīyam uragaḥ krīḍā samaṃ mātṛbhiḥ | 
 yasyaitāny asamañjasāni tam anācāraiḥ piśācair vṛtaṃ 
 kaḥ sthāṇuḥ phalavāñchayā vada vṛṣād anyo janaḥ sevate  ||1650|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 3. gaṇāḥ 
 
 
 tulyaiveśvarasevā karma na vidmaḥ purākṛtaṃ kīdṛk | 
 bhṛṅgī yad asthiśeṣo bhṛśataram akṛśaś ca kūṣmāṇḍaḥ  ||1651|| 
 
 
 vākpateḥ | 
 
 
 eko giriśaḥ svāmī gaṇatā tulyaiva vallabhatvaṃ ca | 
 kiṃ kurmaḥ karmagatau śuṣyati bhṛṅgī vināyakaḥ pīnaḥ  ||1652|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 kapardī bhūtisaṃpanno jagatīpatir advayaḥ | 
 dhig daivam avyayaḥ so’pi bhṛṅgī śuṣyatyato bhṛśam  ||1653|| 
 
 
 amoghasya | 
 
 
 skande mandāvadhānaṃ carati gaṇapatau maulipātaṃ na dhatte 
 vṛnde vṛndārakāṇāṃ vinayavati bhṛśaṃ nādarān ātanoti | 
 kiṃ bhūmnā yaś ca devīṃ na namati girijāṃ tasya nirvyājavṛtteḥ 
 kṣīāsyāpy ekaniṣṭhā jayati bhagavatī bhṛṅgiṇas tasya bhaktiḥ  ||1654|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 kūṭasthaṃ śravaṇopakaṇṭhavilasatkrūradvijihvāśrayaṃ 
 dakṣadveṣiṇam aṅghralaṅghitavṛṣaṃ vaiṣamyabhīmekṣaṇam | 
 īśaṃ nirguṇavyayaprakṛtikaṃ saṃsevya bhṛṅgī cirād
