 ayi śākunika kṛto’ñjalir itare na katīha jīvanopāyāḥ | 
 hatvā śukān kim etad vipinam asārasvataṃ kuruṣe  ||1987|| 
 
 
 vaidyagadādharasya | 
 
 
 ekatra prākṛtaiḥ sāmyam anyatra paratantratā | 
 śukasya paritoṣāya na vanaṃ na ca pattanam  ||1988|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 ayi khalu badhirādhirāja kīraṃ  
 tudasi śalākanipātanena mohāt | 
 aniśam api sudhānidhānavāṇīṃ  
 racayatu maunamukho’stu vā samaste  ||1989|| 
 
 
 bhrātaḥ kīra kim atra nīrasataruskandhe madhusyandibhir 
 vyāhārais tava vastuvarṇitakathābandhair mudhāyaṃ śramaḥ | 
 naite dāḍimaśākhinaḥ pariṇatair yeṣāṃ phalair antaraṃ 
 nirbhidyāpi guṇānuraktam aśaṭhair āviṣkriyante mudaḥ  ||1990|| 
 
 
 laulikasya | 
 
 
 71. nānāpakṣiṇaḥ 
 
 
 svāmin khañjana muñca muñca phanabhṛdbhogādhirohagrahaṃ 
 tad viśrāmyatu naḥ phalaṃ kim api yad vandyena deyaṃ tvayā | 
 daivād eṣa yadi pradīptagaralas tvāṃ dandaśūko daśed 
 viśvālokakarī tadā śarad iyaṃ syād eva dṛgvañcitā  ||1991|| 
 
 
 vaidyagadādharasya | 
 
 
 ājanmaiva tamaḥ suhṛtkuṭilatā vaktre girāṃ nirgamo  
 grāmotsād akaraḥ śmaśānaviṭapī prāyeṇa yasyāśrayaḥ | 
 dhig dhātaḥ sasṛje sa eva malinaḥ krūraḥ kathaṃ kauśikaḥ  
 sṛṣṭo vā kim akalpyatāsya bhavatā kalpāntam āyuḥ sthiram  ||1992|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 ayi cakorakuṭumbini kātare  
 tiraya pakṣapuṭena kuṭumbakam | 
 bahu gataṃ kiyad apy avaśiṣyate  
 vyapagataṃ timirair uditaḥ śaśī  ||1993|| 
 
 
 pāpākasya | 
 
 
 kramagalitaiḥ śikhipucchair  
 maṇḍanam āstāṃ vadhena kiṃ śikhinaḥ | 
 kutukini punar na lābho 
 viṣadharaviṣame vane bhavitā  ||1994|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (sū.mu. 16.2) 
 
 
 bhrāmyadbhyo’pi gṛhe gṛhe kaṭutām apy ālapadbhyo giraṃ 
 gṛdhnubhyo’pi balād amedhyam athavāvajñāṃ vrajadbhyo’pi ca | 
 śayyotthāyam upāsate vasatim ity etāvatāyaṃ nṬṇāṃ 
 kākebhyo balir asti kokilabaliḥ kenāpi nākarṇitaḥ  ||1995|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 72. uccāvacam 
 
 
 bhrātaḥ paśya nikṛtya candanatarūcchākoṭako ropyate 
 sārāsāravicāriṇī matir iha grāme janānāṃ kutaḥ | 
 tad yāvad vayam asya sekasalilaṃ voḍhuṃ na mṛṣyāmahe  
 tāvat satvaram eva pāmarajana grāmād ito gamyatām  ||1996|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 dantair upatitaṃ sphuranti valayo niṣkālimānaḥ kacāḥ  
 śīrṇadeham apetam eva karaṇagrāmeṇa luptā matiḥ | 
 asminn apratikāradāruṇajarāvyādhau dayārdrātmanā  
 bhrātar vaidya vidhīyate tava kiyad yāvan mayā bheṣajam  ||1997|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 panthāḥ prajvalitaḥ sphuranti purataḥ krūrāḥ kṛśānutviṣaḥ 
 kāntāradrumagharmadīdhitir api vyomārdham ārohati | 
 asmābhiḥ śramavihvalair iha tarucchāyāsamālambibhir 
 na jñātāḥ paritaḥ kirātaśiviravyāptā vanaśreṇayaḥ  ||1998|| 
 
 
 tīrabhuktīyasarveśvarasya | 
 
 
 tadbrahmāṇḍam iha kvacit kvacid api kṣoṇī kvacin nīradās 
 te dvīpāntaraśālino jaladhayaḥ kvāpi kvacit parvatāḥ | 
 āścaryaṃ gaganasya ko’pi mahimā sarvair amībhiḥ sthitair 
 dūre pūraṇam asya śūnyam iti yannāmāpi nācchāditam  ||1999|| 
 
 
 keśarasya | (su.ra. 1193) 
 
 
 samālambyānyonyaṃ masṛṇacaraṇāḥ kampanajuṣo 
 na yātāḥ ke pāraṃ sati jaladhibandhe kapibhaṭāḥ | 
 taṭād eko’rvācaś cakitasurasiddhasthitisamut 
 samutplutya prāyāt paramaparapāraṃ sa hanumān  ||2000|| 
 
 
 chittipasya | 
 
 
 śrīdharadāsakṛte’smin saduktikarṇāmṛte caturtho’yam | 
 satkarmaṇy apadeśapravāha upadeśatāṃ bhajatu || 
 
 iti śrīmahāmāṇḍalikaśrīdharadāsakṛtau saduktikarṇāmṛte | 
 
 apadeśapravāho nāma caturthaḥ | vīcayaḥ 72 | ślokāḥ 360 || 
 
  o)0(o 
 
   
 saduktikarṇāmṛtam 
 
 
 
 
 (5) 
 uccāvacapravāhavīcayaḥ 
 
 
 manujas turaṅgagāvau paśavaḥ pārāvato balākā ca | 
 nānākhagāś ca girayo vanasravatyau viśeṣanadī  ||1|| 
 padmākaraḥ praśastaḥ sarasī cakraś ca cakravākī ca | 
 digdeśau vīradhanur bhaṅgau hanūmatprabhṛtiśauryam  ||2|| 
 rāvaṇa etasya śiraśchedo dūto’nuvādasaṃvādaḥ | 
 kavayo nānākavayaḥ pratyekakavir manasvikavayaś ca  ||3|| 
 kavidānaṃ guṇigarvo vāṇī kāvyaṃ ca kāvyamātsaryam | 
 kāvyamalimlucasajjanadurvṛttāḥ sujanadurjanau militau  ||4|| 
 dhanya udātto mānī kṛpaṇaḥ sevakamanasvibhajamānau | 
 duradhīśasevakaś ca kṣudrodayaduḥkhito’tha dāridryam  ||5|| 
 tat sacaṭu daridragṛhī tadgṛhiṇī tadgṛhaṃ jarāvṛddhaḥ | 
 anuśayanirvedāv atha vicāravicikitsite ca śamavighnaḥ  ||6|| 
 ardhaśamaḥ kāruṇikaḥ śāntyāśaṃsā kṛtārthaśāntaś ca | 
 śāntigato niṣkramaniḥspṛhavanagamanotsukās tapovipinam  ||7|| 
 tāpasabahuviṣayaśamau jñānī bhavitavyatā ca daivaṃ ca | 
 kālapitṛvanasamasyoccāvacapratirājasaṃstutayaḥ  ||8|| 
 iti ṣaṭkādhikasaptativīcibhir iha sarasakomalair ebhiḥ | 
 uccāvacapravāhaṃ śrīdharadāsaḥ kṛtī kṛtavān  ||9|| 
 1. manuṣyaḥ 
 
 
 aṅguṣṭhāgrimayantritāṅgulir asau pādārdhanīruddhabhūr 
 pārśvodvegakṛto nihatya kaphaṇidvandvena daṃśān muhuḥ | 
 nyagjānudvayamadhyayantritaghaṭīvaktrāntarālaskhalad 
 dhārādhvānamanoharaṃ sakhi payo gāṃ dogdhi dāmodaraḥ  ||2001|| 
 
 
 
 kasyacit | (padyā. 262; su.ra. 1157, upādhyāyadāmodarasya; sū.mu.
                            96.14) 
 
 
 tais tair jīvopahārair girikuharaśilāsaṃśrayām arcayitvā 
 devīṃ kāntāradurgāṃ rudhiram upatarukṣetrapālāya dattvā | 
 tumbīvīnāvinodavyavahitasarakām ahni jīrṇe purāṇīṃ 
 hālāṃ mālūrakoṣair yuvatisahacarā barbarāḥ śīlayanti  ||2002|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 1191, yogeśvarasya) 
 
 
 etāś candrodaye’sminn aviralamuśalotkṣepadolāyamāna 
 snigdhaśyāmāgrapīnastanakalasanamatkaṇṭhanālāgraramyāḥ | 
 udvelladbāhuvallīpracalitavalayaśreṇayaḥ pāmarāṇāṃ 
 gehinyo dīrghagītidhvanijanitasukhās taṇḍulān kaṇḍayanti  ||2003|| 
 
 
 śaraṇasya | 
 
 
 rajjukseparayonnamadbhujalatāvyaktaikapārśvastanī 
 sūtracchedavilolaśaṅkhavalayaśreṇījhaṇatkāriṇī | 
 tiryagvistṛtapīvaroruyugalā pṛṣṭhān ativyākṛtā 
 bhogaśroṇir udasyati pratimuhuḥ kūpād apaḥ pāmarī  ||2004|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (su.ra. 1152, kasyacit) 
 
 
 etās tā divasāntabhāskaradṛśo dhāvanti paurāṅganāḥ 
 skandhapraskhaladaṃśukāñcaladhṛtivyāsaṅgabaddhādarāḥ | 
 prātaryāta kṛṣīvalāgamabhiyā protplutya vartmacchido 
 haṭṭakrītapadārthamūlyakalanavyagrāṅguligranthayaḥ  ||2005|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 2. turaṅgaḥ 
 
 
 paścāt khuradvitayakhaṇḍitabhūmibhāga 
 mūrdhvīkṛtāgracaraṇadvayam ugraheṣam | 
 mūrdhāvagāhanavihastanijāśvavāra 
 bhārāj janaḥ parijahāra khalaṃ turaṅgam  ||2006|| 
 
 
 dhoyīkasya | 
 
 
 kṛtaśīkaravṛṣṭikeśarair 
 asakṛt skandham abandhuraṃ dhuvan | 
 apivac caraṇāgratāḍitaṃ 
 turagaḥ paṅkilam āpagatā payaḥ  ||2007|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 āghrātakṣoṇipīṭhaḥ khuraśikharasamākṛṣṭareṇus turaṅgaḥ  
 puñjīkṛtyākhilāṅghrīn kramavaśavinamajjānukaṃ muktakāyaḥ | 
 pṛṣṭhāntaḥ pārśvakaṇḍūvyapanayanavaśād dvistrirudvartitāṅgaḥ  
 protthāya drāṅ nirīhaḥ kṣaṇam atha vapur āsyānupūrvaṃ dhunoti  ||2008|| 
 
 
 vikramādityasya | (su.ra. 1167) 
 
 
 paścād aṅghrī prasārya trikanativitataṃ drāghayitvāṅgam uccair 
 āsajyābhugnakaṇṭhaṃ kṣaṇam uparisaṭāṃ ghūlidhūmrāṃ vidhūya | 
 ghāsagrāsābhilāṣād anavaratacalatprothatuṇḍas turaṅgo 
 mandaṃ śabdāyamāno vilikhati śayanād utthitaḥ kṣmāṃ khureṇa  ||2009|| 
 
 
 
 bhaṭṭabāṇasya || (Hc 3.5, Sv 2420, sū.mu. 102.4, su.ra. 1166) 
 
 
 kurvann ābhugnapṛṣṭho mukhanikaṭakaṭiḥ kandharāmātiraśvīṃ 
 lolenāhanyamānāṃ tuhinakaṇamucā cañcatā keśareṇa | 
 nidrākaṇḍūkaṣāyaṃ kaṣati nibiḍitaśrotraśuktis turaṅgas 
 tvaṅgat pakṣmāgralagnapratanubusakaṇaṃ koṇam akṣṇaḥ khureṇa  ||2010|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva || (Hc 3.6) 
 3. gauḥ  
 
 
 vyaktasnāyuvṛtāsthipañjarabharo romanthanidrālasaḥ 
 prātar gomayaliptapucchacaraṇo’py utthātukāmaḥ svayam | 
 pūrvavyūḍhivibhāvanaparivṛḍhair uttolitaḥ spandate 
 vṛddhokṣas trikabhaṅgalabdharudhirāt kākād bhiyā vidrutaḥ  ||2011|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 agre vitatya caraṇo vinamayya kaṇṭham 
 utthāpya vaktram abhihatya muhuś ca vatsāḥ | 
 mātrāvivartitamukhaṃ mukhalihyamāna 
 paścārdhasusthamanasaḥ stanam utpibanti  ||2012|| 
 
 
 cakrapāṇeḥ | (su.ra. 1168) 
 
 
 tiryaktīkṣṇaviṣāṇayugmacalanavyānamrakaṇṭhānanaḥ 
 kiṃcit kuñcitalocanaḥ khurapuṭair ācoṭayan bhūtalam | 
 niḥśvāsair atisantatair busakaṇājālaṃ khale vikṣipann 
 ukṣā goṣṭhataṭīṣu labdhavijayo govṛndam āskandati  ||2013|| 
 
 
 yogeśvarasya | (su.ra. 1186) 
 
 
 upanihitahalīṣāsārgaladvāram ārāt 
 paricakitapurandhrīsāritābhyarṇabhāṇḍam | 
 pavanarayatiraścīr vāridhārāḥ pratīcchan 
 viśati valitaśṛṅgaḥ pāmarāgāram ukṣā  ||2014|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 karṇābhyarṇāriśṛṅgakṣatirudhirarasāsvādanābaddhagargha 
 dhvāṅkṣacchāyāttabhītipratihatadhavalīvargasaṃvardhanecchaḥ | 
 śīlaty ākruddhagopīlaguḍahatinamatpṛṣṭhavaṃśaḥ kathañcit 
 prātaḥ kedāranīraṃ kalamadalabhiyā kṛṇitākṣo mahokṣaḥ  ||2015|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 4. nānāpaśavaḥ  
 
 
 paśyodañcadavāñcad añcitavapuḥ pūrvārdhapaścārdhabhāk 
 stabdhottānitapṛṣṭhaniṣṭhitamanāgbhugnārdhalāṅgulabhṛt | 
 daṃṣṭrākoṭiviśaṅkaṭāsyakuharaḥ kurvan saṭām utkarām 
 utkarṇaḥ kurute kramaṃ karipatau krūrākṛtiḥ keśarī  ||2016|| 
 
 
 subandhoḥ | (su.ra. 1655, V, p. 49) 
 
 
 ucchmaśrur vyāttavaktraḥ pravitatarasanāpallavālīḍhasṛkkā 
 pi go’grabhrāntanetraḥ pulakitataralottānalā gūlanālaḥ | 
 kutrāpy aklāntigāmī kvacid atipihitaḥ kvāpi tu gāgramātraś 
 citravyāghro’yam āptuṃ pramadavanamṛgītarṇakāṃs tūrṇam eti  ||2017|| 
 
 
 yogeśvarasya | 
 
 
 ākubjīkṛtapṛṣṭham unnatavaladvaktrāgrapucchaṃ bhayād  
 antarveśmaniveśitaikanayanaṃ niṣkampakarṇadvayam | 
 lālākīrṇavidīrṇasṛkkavikacaddaṃṣṭrākarālānanaḥ  
 śvā niḥśvāsanirodhapīvaragalo mārjāram āskandati  ||2018|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (su.ra. 1163) 
 
 
 durvārakelikalaimbhabhayād idānīṃ 
 vyālambilolakucakambalabhāramandā | 
 saṃdaśya viślatham udañcayatā mukhena  
 śāvaṃ śunī nayati śālipalālakūṭam  ||2019|| 
 
 
 śubhāṅkasya | 
 
 
 vilebhyo niṣkrāntaṃ pratinavaharidrārasanibhaṃ 
 piryāpṛṣṭhāśleṣapraṇayi kṛtasampannavajale | 
 svarān sānusvārān vividhatadavasthāvighaṭitaṃ 
 kulaṃ maṇḍūkānām udayagalagaṇḍaṃ vikurute  ||2020|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 5. pārāvataḥ 
 
 
 asau gireḥ śītalakandarasthaḥ  
 pārāvato manmathacāṭudakṣaḥ | 
 dharmālasāṅgīṃ madhurāṇi kūjan  
 saṃvījate pakṣapuṭena kāntām  ||2021|| 
 
 
 pāṇineḥ | 
 
 
 kiṃcit kuñcitacañcucumbanasukhasphārībhavallocanaṃ 
 svapremocitacārucāṭukaraṇaiś ceto’rpayantī muhuḥ | 
 kūjantī vinataikapakṣatipuṭenāliṅgya līlālasaṃ 
 dhanyaṃ kāntam upāntavartinam iyaṃ pārāvatī sevate  ||2022|| 
 
 
 matirājasya | 
 
 
 kalakvaṇitagarbheṇa kaṇṭhenāghūrṇitekṣaṇaḥ | 
 pārāvataḥ paribhramya riraṃsuś cumbati priyām  ||2023|| 
 
 
 daṇḍinaḥ | (śā.pa. 570) 
 
 
 prātar vāravilāsinījanaraṇan mañjīramañjusvanair 
 udbuddhaḥ paridhūya pakṣatipuṭaṃ pārāvataḥ saspṛham | 
 kiṃcit kuñcitalocanāṃ sahacarīṃ saṃcumbya cañcvā ciraṃ 
 manāndolitakaṇṭhakuṇṭhitagalaḥ sotkaṇṭham utkūjati  ||2024|| 
 
 
 vikramādityasya | (su.ra. 1154) 
 
 
 pakṣābhyāṃ sahitau prasārya caraṇāv ekaikaśaḥ pārśvayor 
 ekīkṛtya śirodharopari śanaiḥ pāṇḍūdare pakṣatī | 
 nidrāśeṣaviśeṣaraktanayano niryāya nīḍodarād 
 āsṛkkāntavidāritānanapuṭaḥu pārāvato jṛmbhate  ||2025|| 
 
 
 śṛṅgārasya | (su.ra. 1153, bhṛṅgārasya) 
 
 
 6. bakaḥ 
 
 
 gatvā puraḥ katicid eva padāni vegād 
 ākuñcitaikacaraṇo nibhṛtīkṛtākṣaḥ | 
 svairaṃ vidūravitatīkṛtakandharo’yaṃ 
 mīnaṃ saro’mbhasi nibhālayate balākaḥ  ||2026|| 
 
 
 kāmadevasya |  
 
 
 balākāḥ pānthānāṃ śiśirasarasīsīmni saratām  
 amī netrānandaṃ dadati caraṇācoṭitamukhāḥ | 
 dhunānā mūrdhānaṃ galabilaviśatsphāraśaphara 
 sphuratpucchānacchadyutiśavalabāṣpāruṇadṛśaḥ  ||2027|| 
 
 
 madhukaṇṭhasya | (su.ra. 1185) 
 
 
 harati purattaḥ pārśve paścād valantam anārataṃ 
 śapharam aparitrāṇaṃ gṛhṇan bakas taṭinītaṭe | 
 pravicalagarutpālir dattāparāparasatvara 
 tricaturakharatroṭīkoṭiprahāra itas tataḥ  ||2028|| 
 
 
 piyākasya | 
 
 
 udgrīvastimitekṣanas tata itaḥ paśyan nilīya sthitaṃ 
 pādodghṛṣṭiparasparapratibhayabhrāntaṃ calatpakṣatiḥ | 
 drāktroṭīpurakoṭikuṇṭhitarayaṃ prāktiryagūrdhvīkṛtaṃ 
 garbhāntaḥpraṇayīcakāra śapharaṃ kāsāracārī bakaḥ  ||2029|| 
 
 
 kasyacit |  
 
 
 payasi sarasaḥ svacche matsyāñjighṛkṣur itas tato 
 valitanayanaṃ mandaṃ mandaṃ padaṃ nidadhad bakaḥ | 
 viyati vidhṛtaikāṅghris tirag vivartitakandharo 
 dalam api calat sapratyāśaṃ muhur muhur īkṣate  ||2030|| 
 
 
 yogeśvarasya | (su.ra. 1164, kasyacit) 
 7. nānāpakṣiṇaḥ 
 
 
 utplutya dūraṃ paridhūya pakṣā 
 vadho nirīkṣya kṣaṇabaddhalakṣyaḥ | 
 madhyejalaṃ cañcati dattajhampaḥ 
 samatsya utsarpati matsyaraṅkaḥ  ||2031|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 1155) 
 
 
 nīḍād apakramya vidhūya pakṣau 
 vṛkṣāgram āruhya tataḥ krameṇa | 
 udgrīvam utpuccham udekapādam 
 uccūḍam ukūjati tāmracūḍaḥ  ||2032|| 
 
 
 madhoḥ | (su.ra. 1156) 
 
 
 iha sarasi salīlaṃ cārupatre vidhunvan 
 darataralitatiryakcañcukaṇḍūyitāṅgaḥ | 
 anusarati sarāgaḥ preyasīm agrayātām 
 anupadasam udañcatkaṇṭhanālo marālaḥ  ||2033|| 
 
 
 śiśokasya |  
 
 
 cañcac–cañcala cañcuvāñchitacalaccūḍāgram ugraṃ patac 
 cakrākārakarālakeśaraśaṭāsphārasphuratkandharam | 
 vāraṃ vāram udaṅghrilaṅghanapreṅkhannakhakṣuṇṇayoḥ 
 kāmaṃ kukkuṭayor dvayaṃ drutapadaṃ krūrakramaṃ yudhyate  ||2034|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (śā.pa. 572, su.ra. 1171) 
 
 
 utpucchaḥ pramadollasadvapur adhovisraṃsipakṣadvayaḥ 
 svairālokagatikrameṇa parito bhrāntvā salīlaṃ muhuḥ | 
 utkaṇṭhālasakūjitaḥ kalarutāṃ bhūyo riraṃsārasa 
 nyagbhūtāṃ caṭakaḥ priyām abhisaraty udvepamānaḥ svayam  ||2035|| 
 
 
 sohlokasya | (su.ra. 1183) 
 
 
 8. girayaḥ  
 
 
 mādyaddiggajagaṇḍabhittikaṣaṇair bhagnasravaccandanaḥ 
 pādālaktamauktikaśilaḥ siddhāṅganānāṃ gataiḥ | 
 krandatkandaragahvaro jalanidher āsphālito vīcibhiḥ  
 sevyo’yaṃ malayācalaḥ kim api me cetaḥ karoty utsukam  ||2036|| 
 
 
 śrīharṣasya | (Nn 1.9) 
 
 
 etāḥ sthānaparigraheṇa śivayor atyantakāntaśriyaḥ 
 prāleyācalamekhalāvanabhuvaḥ puṣṇanti netrotsavam | 
 vyāvalgadbalavairivāraṇavarapratyagradantāhati 
 śvabhraprasravadabhrasindhusavanaprasnigdhadevadrumāḥ  ||2037|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 1593) 
 
 
 channopāntā nikuñjais taruṇaśukakulaśyāmalaiḥ kīcakānāṃ 
 śaileyaprastarābhiḥ subhagaparisarāḥ pīvarībhiḥ śilābhiḥ | 
 ete te ruddharevārayamukharatayā yauvanoddāmakāma 
 vyāpārottālalīlā caturavanacarībandhavo vindhyapādāḥ  ||2038|| 
 
 
 yogeśvarasya | 
 
 
 imās tā vindhyādreḥ śukaharitavaṃśīvanaghanā 
 bhuvaḥ krīḍāloladviradaradanābhugnataravaḥ | 
 latākuñje yāsām upanadi rataklāntataruṇī 
 kapolasvedāmbhaḥparicayanudo vānti marutaḥ  ||2039|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (sa.ka.ā. 3.9, su.ra. 1588, dakṣasya) 
 
 
 karikavalitamṛṣṭaiḥ śākhiśākhāgrapatrair  
 aruṇasaraṇayo’mī sarvato bhīṣayante | 
 calitaśabarasenādattagośṛṅgacaṇḍa 
 dhvanicakitavarāhavyākulā vindhyapādāḥ  ||2040|| 
 
 
 kamalāyudhasya | (sa.ka.ā. 2.30, sū.mu. 103.14, su.ra. 1587) 
 
 
 9. aṭavī 
 
 
 pratyāsannasarāṃsi kokilavadhūlīlāsuhṛd icchada 
 cchāyāliptakakumbhi korakahasadvīrundhi vindhyāṭavī | 
 antardattamanojaruñji rucirakṣmāruṃhi bhṛṅgākulat 
 tvaṅnaddhāmpi latāgṛhāṇi dadhatī kāṃcin mucaṃ yacchati  ||2041|| 
 
 
 madhoḥ | 
 
 
 mithaḥ krīḍatkoḍāvalivilasitotkhātataṭinī 
 taṭī kṣubdhodgarjadgajagahanagarbheyam aṭavī | 
 guhābhir vyāghrāṇāṃ jaradajagaragrāsasaruṣāṃ 
 ghaṭatkāraṃ ghoraṃ pratiravavahābhir draḍhayati  ||2042|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 sarpaśvāsamaruttaraṅgataralāḥ kvāpi kvacic chvāpada 
 sphārodgīrṇagiro nirantaratamas tāruṇyamagnāḥ kvacit | 
 kvāpi krūrakṛśānudurmukhakathāśeṣīkṛtakṣmāruhaś 
 cetaḥ samprati kampayanti parito gambhīrabhīmā bhuvaḥ  ||2043|| 
 
 
 jalacandrasya | 
 
 
 kṣuṇṇakṣmāruhavīthayo vidalitagrāvopalagranthayaḥ 
 siṃhasvīkṛtamattavāraṇavadhūbaddhārtakolāhalāḥ | 
 etāḥ pallavayanti cetasi bhayaṃ bhallūkahikkāravair 
 ātaṅkāt patayālubālahariṇīgarbhābilā bhūmayaḥ  ||2044|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 iha mahiṣaviṣāṇavyastapāṣāṇapīṭha 
 skhalanasulabharohidgarbhiṇībhrūṇahatyāḥ | 
 kuharaviharamāṇaprauḍhabhallūkahikkā 
 cayacakitakirātasrastaśastrā vanāntāḥ  ||2045|| 
 
 
 murāreḥ | (Ar 5.20) 
 
 
 10. nadī 
 
 
 bhānty etāḥ śaivalinyo vanamahiṣakhurakṣuṇṇapāṭhīnapṛṣṭha 
 grāsavyagrodravṛndapraviralacaraṇanyāsamudrāṅkapaṅkāḥ | 
 niḥśaṅkodbhrāntakaṅkatrasaduragavadhūsambhramotphālamūrcchad 
 bhekārtasvānadīrghīkṛtaravavirasatkīcakagranthirandhrāḥ  ||2046|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 vyaktavyāghrapadāṅkapaṅktinicitonmudrārdrapaṅkodarās 
 toyottīrṇanivṛttanakrajaṭharakṣuṇṇasthalībālukāḥ | 
 sāndrasthūlanaloparodhaviṣamāḥ śaṅkyāvatārāḥ puraḥ 
 saṃtrāsaṃ janayanti kuñjasaritaḥ kācābhahnīlodakāḥ  ||2047|| 
 
 
 kasyacit (su.ra. 281) 
 
 
 antarmagnakareṇavaḥ kalabhakavyārugṇakandāṅkuraiḥ  
 sāmodāḥ paritaḥ pramattamahiṣaśvāsollasadvīcayaḥ | 
 saṃmodaṃ janayanti śailasaritaḥ succhāyakacchasthalī 
 sīmāno jalasekaśītalaśilānidrāṇarohidgaṇāḥ  ||2048|| 
 
 
 jalacandrasya |  
 
 
 jalarayadalatkūlotsaṅgāḥ pralambilatāgṛha 
 stimitagatibhir veṇībandhair viśṛṅkhalavīcayaḥ | 
 sthapuṭitaśilāsopāneṣu prakāmataraṅgitāḥ  
 śikharisarito netrānandaṃ kiranti samantataḥ  ||2049|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 vīcīsaṃkramadanturāḥ kalaravair vācālitāḥ sārasair 
 ānandaṃ janayanti pūragarimottānībhavadbālukāḥ | 
 bhrāntāgantukarājahaṃsapariṣatpādāṅkamudrābhṛtaḥ  
 prasthakṣmāruhatalpasuptakurarāḥ srotasvatībhūmayaḥ  ||2050|| 
 
 
 11. viśeṣanadī 
 
 
 kūjadbhir vanakukkubhir madakalaṃ vācālatīradrumā 
 bibhrāṇā vikacābjakeśararajaḥpiṅgās taraṅgāvalīḥ | 
 srotaḥkṣmāvipāṇḍusaikatasukhāsīnā rasatsārasā 
 dhanyeyaṃ tamasā nadī harati me dṛṣṭāpi mārgaśramam  ||2051|| 
 ete mekalakanyakāpraṇayinaḥ pātālamūlaspṛśaḥ 
 saṃtrāsaṃ janayanti vindhyabhidurā vārāṃ pravāhāḥ puraḥ | 
 līlonmūlitanartitapratihatavyāvartitaprerita 
 tyaktasvīkṛtanihnutapracalitaproddhūtatīradrumāḥ  ||2052|| 
 
 
 kasyāpi (su.ra. 1656) 
 
 
 majjanmātaṅgahastacyutamadamadirāmodamattālijālaṃ 
 snānaiḥ siddhāṅganānāṃ kucayugavilasatkuṅkumāsaṅgapiṅgam | 
 sāyaṃ prātar munīnāṃ kuśakusumacayacchannatīrasthalīkaṃ 
 pāyād vo narmadāmbhaḥ karikaramakarāklāntaraṃhas taraṅgam  ||2053|| 
 
 
 chittapasya | 
 
 
 iyaṃ sā kālindī kuvalayadalasnigdhamadhurā 
 madāndhavyākūjataralajalaraṅkupraṇayinī | 
 purā yasyās tīre sarabhasasatṛṣṇaṃ murabhido 
 gatāḥ prāyo gopīnidhuvanavinodena divasāḥ  ||2054|| 
 
 
 
 śaraṇasya | (padyā. 343, daśarathasya) 
 
 
 idaṃ tat kālindīpulinam iha kaṃsāsurabhido 
 yaśaḥ śṛṇvad vaktraskhalitakavalaṃ gokulam abhūt | 
 bhramadveṇukvāṇaśravaṇamasṛṇottāramadhura 
 svarābhir gopībhir diśi diśi samudghūrṇam aniśam  ||2055|| 
 
 
 
 keśaṭasya | (padyā. 345, moṭakasya) 
 
 
 12. taḍāgaḥ  
 
 
 aviratamadhupānāgāram indindirāṇām  
 abhisaraṇanikuñjaṃ rājahaṃsīkulasya | 
 pravitatabahuśālaṃ sadma padmālayāyā  
 vitarati ratim akṣṇor eṣa līlātaḍāgaḥ  ||2056|| 
 
 
 śrīmallakṣmaṇasenadevasya | 
 
 
 vīcīsamīradhutakāñcanapuṇḍarīka 
 paryastakeśaraparāgapiśaṅgitāmbhaḥ | 
 acchodam aikṣata sa devapurandhripāda 
 lākṣāruṇīkṛtaśilātalatīralekham  ||2057|| 
 
 
 ratnākarasya | 
 
 
 madataralamarālapreyasīcañcakoṭi 
 krakacavidalitāni vyaktam indīvarāṇi | 
 niviḍayati taḍāge yatra līlāvatīnāṃ 
 kuvalayadaladāmaśyāmalo dṛṣṭipātaḥ  ||2058|| 
 
 
 jalacandrasya | 
 
 
 luṭhadvīcīmauliḥ paripatati pūrvaṃ caraṇayor 
 athorū gṛhṇāti spṛśati jaghanābhogam abhitaḥ | 
 karau dhatte madhyaṃ kalayati samāśliṣyati kucā 
 kacān apy ādatte priya iva taḍāgo mṛgadṛśām  ||2059|| 
 
 
 govardhanasya | 
 
 
 etan mānini mānasaṃ surasaro nirlūnahemāmbujaṃ 
 pārvatyā priyapūjanārtham amuto gaṅgāsarinnirgatā | 
 asmāc citraśikhaṇḍibhiś ca parame parvaṇy upādīyate 
 snānottīrṇavṛṣāṅkabhasmarajasāṃ saṅgāt pavitraṃ payaḥ  ||2060|| 
 
 
 rājaśekharasya | (bā.rā. 10.35) 
 
 
 13. praśasta taḍāgaḥ  
 
 
 bhrāmyadbhṛṅgālidolāvidalitakumudāmodamedasvivātod 
 vellatkallolamālācalakamalakarākūtahūtādhvanīnāḥ | 
 pāthonāthopahāsollasitaradākāravisphāraphenās 
 tenākhyanyanta dantadyutiviśadayaśo haṃsanīḍās taḍāgāḥ  ||2061|| 
 
 
 bhaṭṭanārāyaṇasya | 
 
 
 tenākhāni jalāvagāhanarasavyāsaktapaurāṅganā 
 paryasyatkavarīvikīrṇakusumasmerormimālaṃ saraḥ | 
 yasminn acchatayā nidhāya nayane martyaiḥ sakautūhalaṃ 
 lakṣyante bhujagādhirājanagarī vāmabhruvāṃ vibhramāḥ  ||2062|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | (Sv 106.1) 
 
 
 unmīlallīlanīlotpaladaladalanāmodamedasvipūra 
 kroḍakrīḍadvijālīgarududitamarutsphālavācālavīciḥ | 
 etenākhāni śākhānivahanavaharitparṇapūrṇadrumālī 
 vyālīḍhopāntaśāntavyathapathikadṛśāṃ dattarāgas taḍāgaḥ  ||2063|| 
 
 
 kavipaṇḍitaśrīharṣasya | (Nc 12.101, sū.mu. 106.3) 
 
 
 taḍāgāste nānānilacapalapadmākaralasad 
 rasakṣodāmodākulamadhukarālīkavalitāḥ | 
 kṛtās toyakrīḍākulakuvalayākṣīkucataṭa 
 truṭadvīcīvellatkurarakulakolāhalajuṣaḥ  ||2064|| 
 
 
 viśveśvarasya | 
 
 
 athāyatanasaṃnidhau bhagavato bhavānīpater 
 manoharam acīkhanad bhuvanabhūṣaṇaṃ bhūpatiḥ | 
 vigāhanakutūhalottaralapaurasīmantinī 
 payodharabharatruṭadvikaṭavīcimudraṃ saraḥ  ||2065|| 
 
 
 vasukalpasya | 
 
 
 14. cakravākaḥ 
 
 
 tīrāt tīram upaiti rauti karuṇaṃ cintāṃ samālambate 
 kāntāṃ dhyāyati niścalena manasā yogīva yuktekṣaṇaḥ | 
 svaccāyām avalokya kūjati punaḥ kānteti hṛṣṭaḥ khago 
 dhanyās te khalu ye vimuktaviṣayāḥ kaṣṭaṃ paraṃ saṅginām  ||2066|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 līlāmbhoruhakānanena viśati dhvāntotkarāśaṅkayā 
 svakrīḍocchalitāś ca vārikaṇikās tārābhramāt paśyati | 
 satrāsaṃ muhur īkṣate ca cakito haṃsaṃ himāṃśubhramān 
 na svāsthyaṃ bhajate divāpi virahāśaṅkī rathāṅgāhvayaḥ  ||2067|| 
 
 
 dharmapālasya | 
 
 
 mitre kvāpi gate saroruhavane baddhānane klāmyati 
 krandatsu bhramareṣu vīkṣya dayitāśliṣṭān puraḥ sārasān | 
 cakrāhvāṇa viyoginā visalatā notkhaṇḍitā nojjhitā 
 vaktre kevalam argaleva nihitā jīvasya nirgacchataḥ  ||2068|| 
 
 
 yuvasenasya | 
 
 
 ehy āliṅga tvarayati mano durbalā vāsaraśrīr  
 āśliṣṭāsi kṣapaya rajanīm ekikā cakravāki | 
 nānyāsakto na khalu kupito nānurāgacyuto vā 
 daivādhīnaḥ sapadi bhavatīm asvatantras tyajāmi  ||2069|| 
 
 
 bhānoḥ | 
 
 
 bhaṅktvā bhīto na bhuṅkte kuṭilavisalatākoṭim indor vitarkāt 
 tārākārās tṛṣārto na pibati payasāṃ vipruṣaḥ patrasaṃsthāḥ | 
 chāyāmbhoruhāṇām alikulaśabalāṃ vetti sandhyām asandhyāṃ 
 kāntāvicchedabhīrur dinam api rajanīṃ manyate cakravākaḥ  ||2070|| 
 
 
 rajakasarasvatyāḥ | 
 
 
 15. cakravākī  
 
 
 āvepate bhramati sarpati moham eti 
 kāntaṃ vilokayati kūjati dīnadīnam | 
 astaṃ hi bhānumati gacchati cakravākī 
 hā jīvite’pi maraṇaṃ priyaviprayogaḥ  ||2071|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (Sv 1914) 
 
 
 na kuru kākurutair vikalaṃ śuco 
 jahihi pālaya bālakuṭumbakam | 
 sakhi rathāṅgakuṭumbini tadvidhe 
 vyatikare kim idaṃ paribhāvyate  ||2072|| 
 
 
 gosokasya | 
 
 
 pakṣāv utkṣipati kṣitau nipatati kroḍe nakhair ullikhaty 
 udbāṣpeṇa ca cakṣuṣā sahacaraṃ dhyātvā muhur vīkṣate | 
 cakrāhvā divasāvasānasamaye tattatkaroty ākulā  
 yenālohitamaṇḍalo’pi kṛpayā yāty eṣa nāstaṃ raviḥ  ||2073|| 
 
 
 sāhasāṅkasya || (Sv 1921) 
 
 
 ekenārkaṃ hutavahaśikhāpāṭalenāstasaṃsthaṃ 
 paśyaty akṣṇā sajalalulitenāpareṇa svakāntam | 
 ahnaś chede dayitavirahā śaṅkinī cakravākī 
 dvau saṃkīrṇau racayati rasau nartakīva pragalbhā  ||2074|| 
 
 
 
 madhoḥ | (sa.ka.ā. 5.495; da.rū. under 4.34)  
 
 
 sūrye cāstam upāgate kamalinīpaṇḍe ca nidrālase 
 cakrī kāntaviyogaduḥsahaśikhijvālāvalītāḍitā | 
 pratyutkūjati mūrcchati śvasiti ca vyāghūrṇane tāmyati 
 bhrāmyaty udvamati kṣamām iva nijaprāṇān muhur nindati  ||2075|| 
 
 
 16. diśaḥ 
 
 
 amarayuvatigītodgrīvasāraṅgaśṛṅgo 
 llikhitaśaśisudhāmbhaḥśādvalārāmaramyām | 
 surapatigajagaṇḍasraṃsidānāmbudhārā  
 prasavasurabhim āśāṃ vāsavīyāṃ namāmi  ||2076|| 
 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 seyaṃ mekalamekhalāniladaladvīcīnadannarmadā 
 keṣāṃ nāma na locanaśravaṇayor digdakṣiṇā prīṇanam | 
 kāñcīpattanakāminīnayanayor āvarjitā vibhramair 
 adhvanyāḥ ka ivāpare munir ato’gastyo’pi nāvartate  ||2077|| 
 
 
 ācāryagopīkasya | 
 
 
 velāśailaśayālumāṃsalaśilāśālūkamajjatpayo 
 vāhavyūhavarāhavibhramavatī prīṇāti digvāruṇī | 
 asyāṃ kuḍmalayan karān pariharan nāśās tyajan padminīr 
 vibhratkāñcanarāgam ambaramaṇiḥ sarvātmanā līyate  ||2078|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 astu svastyayanāya digdhanapate kailāsaśailāśraya 
 śrīkaṇṭhābharaṇenduvibhramadivānaktaṃbhramatkaumudī | 
 yatrālaṃ nalakūbarābhisaraṇārambhāya rambhāsphurat  
 pāṇḍimnaiva tanos tanoti virahavyagrāpi veśagraham  ||2079|| 
 
 
 
 jayadevasya | 
 
 
 prācīm abhrebhakumbhastanakalasalasanmaulikām indrapadmīṃ 
 śrīkhaṇḍakṣodalekhā darakhacitamukhīṃ kākakāntām avācīm | 
 sandhyāsindūramugdhām udakaparivṛḍhapreyasīṃ ca pratīcīṃ 
 vande yakṣendrajāyāṃ taralasurasarittārahārām udīcīm  ||2080|| 
 
 
 jalacandrasya | 
 
 
 17. deśaḥ 
 
 
 parṇaṃ nāgarakhaṇḍam ārdrasubhagaṃ pūgīphalaṃ phālayaḥ 
 karpūrasya ca yatra ko’pi caturas tāmbūlayogakramaḥ | 
 deśaḥ kerala eṣa kelisadanaṃ devasya śṛṅgāriṇas 
 taṃ dṛṣṭvā kuru komalāṅgi saphale drāghīyasī locane  ||2081|| 
 
 
 rājaśekharasya | (bā.rā. 10.67) 
 
 
 vāksattvāṅgasamudbhavair abhinayair nityaṃ rasollāsato 
 vāmāṅgyaḥ praṇayanti yatra madanakrīḍāmahānāṭakam | 
 atrāndhrās tava dakṣiṇena ta ime godāvarīsrotasāṃ 
 saptānām api vārnidhipraṇayināṃ dvīpāntarāṇi śritāḥ  ||2082|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (bā.rā. 10.70) 
 
 
 yat kṣemaṃ tridivāya vartma nigamasyāṅgaṃ ca yat saptamaṃ 
 svādiṣṭhaṃ ca yad aikṣavād api rasāc cakṣuś ca yad vāṅmayam | 
 tad yasmin madhuraṃ prasādi rasavat kāntaṃ ca kāvyāmṛtaṃ 
 so’yaṃ subhru purovidarbhaviṣayaḥ sārasvatījanmabhūḥ  ||2083|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (bā.rā. 10.74) 
 
 
 etanmālavamaṇḍalaṃ vijayate saujanyaratnāṅkuraiḥ 
 saṃpadvibhramadhāmabhiḥ kim aparaṃ śṛṅgārasārair janaiḥ | 
 yatrāruhya vicitracitravalabhīrlīlāśilāsadmanāṃ 
 nīyante jaladodayeṣu divasāḥ kāntāsakhaiḥ kāmibhiḥ  ||2084|| 
 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (bā.rā. 10.84) 
 
 
 krīḍatkinnarakāminīvihasitajyotsnāvalakṣīkṛtāḥ 
 kastūrīmadadurdinārdrasurabhīḥ prāgjyotiṣīyā bhuvaḥ | 
 nīhārasthalasaṃcariṣṇucamarīlāṅgūlasaṃmārjanī 
 helonmṛṣṭamerupuṣparajaso draṣṭuṃ samīhāmahe  ||2085|| 
 
 
 vasukalpasya | 
 
 
 18. vīraḥ 
 
 
 yāte kārmukavidyayā paribhavaṃ sārdhaṃ gaṇānāṃ gaṇaiḥ  
 ṣaḍvaktre samayaṃ vilaṅghya jayinīm uddiśya śaktiṃ sthite | 
 hastodastaparaśvadhaḥ svaśapathair yaḥ stambhitaḥ śambhunā 
 viśve paśyata kautukaṃ bhṛgupates tasyaiva rāmo’ṅkuśaḥ  ||2086|| 
 
 
 śihlaṇasya | 
 
 
 dhātrīm ekātapatrāṃ samiti kṛtavatā caṇḍadordaṇḍadarpād 
 āsthāne pādanamrapratibhaṭamukuṭādarśabimbodareṣu | 
 utkṣiptacchatracihnaṃ pratiphalitam api svaṃ vapur vīkṣya kiṃcit 
 sāsūyaṃ yena dṛṣṭāḥ kṣititalavilasan maulayo bhūmipālāḥ  ||2087|| 
 
 
 jayadevasya | 
 
 
 sādhu mlecchanarendra sādhu bhavato mātaiva vīraprasūr 
 nīcenāpi bhavadvidhena vasudhā sukṣatriyā vartate | 
 deve kupyati yasya vairipariṣanmārāṅkamalle puraḥ 
 śastraṃ śāstram iti sphuranti rasanāpatrāntarāle giraḥ  ||2088|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 ā laṅkānāthanārīstanataralapayovīcimudrāt samudrād 
 ā svargaṅgātaraṅgāvaliviralaśilādustarād uttarādreḥ | 
 ā prākśailāsurastrīsuratagativido magnabhāsvanmṛgāṅkād 
 ā ca prācetasābdher bhavatu mama puraḥ ko’pi yady asti vīraḥ  ||2089|| 
 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 iha vijayini vaṃśe kīrtidhārākalāpa 
 snapitasakalalokaḥ śrīyaśovigraho’bhūt | 
 jalaghaṭa iva yuddhottālabhūpāladarpa 
 jvalanaśamanalīlākovidaḥ ko’pi vīraḥ  ||2090|| 
 
 
 
 viśveśvarasya | 
 
 
 19. dhanurbhaṅgaḥ  
 
 
 rāme rudraśarāsanaṃ tulayati smitvā sthitaṃ pārthivaiḥ 
 śiñjāsañjanatatpare ca hasitaṃ dattvā mithas tālikāḥ | 
 āropya pracalāṅgulīkisalaye mlānaṃ guṇāsphālane  
 sphārākarṣaṇabhagnaparvaṇi punaḥ siṃhāsane mūrcchitam  ||2091|| 
 
 
 rājaśekharasya | (su.ra. 1550) 
 
 
 rundhann aṣṭavidheḥ śrutīr mukharayann aṣṭau krīḍayan 
 mūrtīr aṣṭa maheśvarasya dalayann aṣṭau kulakṣmābhṛtaḥ | 
 tāny akṣṇā vadhirāṇi pannagakulāny aṣṭau ca sampādayann 
 unmīlaty ayam āryadorbalacalatkodaṇḍakolāhalaḥ  ||2092|| 
 
 
 murāreḥ | (Ar 3.54) 
 
 
 dordaṇḍāñcitacandraśekharadhanurdaṇḍāvabhaṅgodyataṣ 
 ṭaṅkāradhvanir āryabālacaritaprastāvanāḍiṇḍimaḥ | 
 drākparyastakapālasaṃpuṭamiladbrahmāṇḍabhāṇḍodara 
 bhrāmyatpiṇḍitacaṇḍimā katham aho nādyāpi viśrāmyati  ||2093|| 
 
 
 bhavabhūteḥ | (Mc 1.54, da.rū.. 4.79, sā.da.. 3.227, sū.mu. 95.3) 
 
 
 yad vajrāntaḥkaṭhoraṃ tripuravighaṭanākhyātavīryaṃ 
 cchindaddarpaṃ bhujānāṃ daśamukhajayinaḥ kārtavīryārjunasya | 
 jīvākṛṣṭerivātair mṛḍamṛḍaninadair iṣṭadevaṃ smarat tad 
 rāmeṇodāradhāmnā dhanur amitabalaṃ bhagnam ardhendumauleḥ  ||2094|| 
 
 
 sarasīruhasya | 
 
 
 utkṣiptaṃ saha kauśikasya pulakaiḥ sākaṃ mukhairnāmitaṃ 
 bhūpānāṃ janakasya saṃśayadhiyā sārdhaṃ samāsphālitam | 
 vaidehīmanasā samaṃ ca sahasā kṛṣṭaṃ tato bhārgava 
 prauḍhāhaṃkṛtikandalena ca samaṃ bhagnaṃ tadaiśaṃ dhanuḥ  ||2095|| 
 
 
 
 gadādharanāthasya | 
 
 
 20. hanūmadādiśauryam  
 
 
 vaktīti vānarabalāni hasan hanūmān 
 madromavalliṣu dṛḍhaṃ kuru tavāvalambam | 
 yenaiva sāgaram ahaṃ laghu laṅghayāmi 
 kiṃ setunā samarakarmaṇi vo nayāmi  ||2096|| 
 
 
 rājaśekharasya | (bā.rā. 7.27) 
 
 
 nīlena sainyapatinā prabhutāḍanānte 
 muktas tathā kilakilādhvanir eṣa raudraḥ | 
 sraṣṭāpi vāñchati sarojabhavaḥ śravāṃsi 
 śaṅke yathā karayugena mudhā pidhātum  ||2097|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (bā.rā. 7.21) 
 
 
 kiyān eṣa kṣārāmbudhir ayam amuṣyāmbunivaho 
 na kumbhenāpy asyātmajakarapuṭenaiva tulitaḥ | 
 bhavadbhiḥ saptaite nanu kapicamūcakrapatayaḥ  
 sahelaṃ pīyantāṃ culukaculukair ambunidhayaḥ  ||2098|| 
 
 
 gosokasya | 
 
 
 bhujastambhair ebhiḥ parighagurubhir luṇṭhanahaṭhād 
 yaśāṃsi svacchandaṃ raṇavipaṇipaṇyāni kapayaḥ | 
 asādhyaṃ syād etad yadi ca tad amīṣām akṛpaṇāḥ  
 kraye santy evāmī likhitapaṭhitāmūlyam asavaḥ  ||2099|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 mūrdhnā jāmbavato’bhivādya caraṇāv āpṛcchya senāpatīn 
 āśvāsyāśrumukhān muhuḥ priyasakhān preṣyān samādiśya ca | 
 ārambhaṃ jagṛhe mahendraśikharād ambhonidher laṅghane 
 raṃhasvī raghunāthapādarajasām uccaiḥ smaran mārutiḥ  ||2100|| 
 
 
 abhinandasya | 
 
 
 21. rāvaṇaḥ  
 
 
 dordaṇḍās ta ime trilocanagirer uttambhasambhāvitās 
 tāny etāni daśānanāni daśabhir digbhir yadājñā kṛtā | 
 yasyādyāpi sa eva vīryamahimā tasmin naras tāpasaḥ  
 śocyaḥ so’pi ripuḥ sa caiva kupitas tasyāpi dūtaḥ kapiḥ  ||2101|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 dhanyaḥ śrīdaśakandharaḥ param ayaṃ rakṣogaṇagrāmaṇīr 
 ekā sā nikaṣā paraṃ tanayasūryasyāḥ suto rāvaṇaḥ | 
 dvāre nirjaraśekharārcitapadadvandvaś ciraṃ vṛtrahā 
 yasyāsthānavilambakāraṇakathātāmyanmanās tiṣṭhati  ||2102|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 rudrādes tulanaṃ svakaṇṭhavipinacchedo harer vāsanaṃ 
 kārāveśmani puṣkarasya cajayo yasyedṛśāḥ kelayaḥ | 
 so’haṃ durdamabāhudaṇḍasacivo laṅkeśvaras tasya me 
 kā ślāghā ghuṇajarjareṇa dhanuṣā kṛṣṭena bhagnena vā  ||2103|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 1548, bā.rā. 1.51) 
 
 
 bhagnaṃ bhagnam umāpater ajagavaṃ bālī kṣataś ca kṣatas 
 tālāḥ sapta hatā hatāś ca jaladhir baddhaś ca baddhaś ca saḥ | 
 āḥ kiṃ tena saśailasāgaradharādhāroragendrāspadaṃ 
 sādriṃ rudram udasyato nijabhujāñjānātyayaṃ rāvaṇaḥ  ||2104|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 nyakkāro hy ayam eva me yad arayas tatrāpy asau tāpasaḥ 
 so’py atraiva nihanti rākṣasabhaṭān jīvaty aho rāvaṇaḥ | 
 dhik dhik śakrajitaṃ prabodhitavatā kiṃ kumbhakarṇena vā 
 svargagrāmaṭikāviluṇṭhanavṛthocchūnaiḥ kim ebhir bhujaiḥ  ||2105|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (Dhvanyālokaḥ 3.16, sā.da. under 1.2, bā.rā.śeṣa 3.11) 
 
 
 22. rāvaṇaśiraśchedaḥ  
 
 
 kaṇṭhacchedaviśīryamāṇarudhiraprāgbhārabhagnadyuter  
 yena smeramukhena homaśikhinaḥ saṃdhukṣaṇākāṅkṣiṇā | 
 bhrūbhaṅgaḥ śitikaṇṭhakaṇṭhaphaṇine phūtkārahetoḥ kṛtaḥ 
 śauṭīryavratatuṣṭadhūrjaṭir asau kiṃ varṇyate rāvaṇaḥ  ||2106|| 
 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 svasattvasyodrekād api daśa śirāṃsi svayam ayaṃ 
 sakṛc chittvā chittvā bhujaparighamṛṣṭhāsṛg abhitaḥ | 
 mukhānāṃ smerākṣṇāṃ sarabhasavikāśād udayināṃ 
 kim adrākṣīl lakṣmīṃ patitapatitānāṃ nipatatām  ||2107|| 
 
 
 kasycacit | 
 
 
 nistriṃśapratibimbite’pi yaduraḥkampo na vīravrata 
 prauḍhiḥ seti na candrahāsamadhunotkaṇṭacchidā parvaṇi | 
 jūhuṣuḥ svaśirāṃsi śaṅkarapurohākāravaireṇa yaḥ  
 svāhākāram udāharan na sa daśagrīvo girāṃ gocaraḥ  ||2108|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 śrīkaṇṭhasya puraḥ parasparabalādhikṣepakakṣāvatāṃ 
 bāhūnāṃ daśakadvayaṃ daśaśiraśchede vivādākulam | 
 pratyekaṃ śamayaty asāv abhimatavyākṣepasāpatrapaś 
 chindhi tvaṃ juhudhi tvam ity upadiśann ekaḥ paraṃ rāvaṇaḥ  ||2109|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 lūne pañca tataś catuṣṭayam iti sraksaṃniveśaiḥ śiraḥ 
 padmair anyatamāvalokanamitair ucchoṇitair arcitaḥ | 
 hastasparśavaśena mūrdhni daśamaṃ mūrdhānam adhyāsayan 
 śambhor uddhatasāhasaikarasikaḥ kair na stuto rāvaṇaḥ  ||2110|| 
 
 
 23. dūtaḥ 
 
 
 ekasminn avapātite’pi śirasi krodhopaśāntiḥ kutaḥ 
 kiṃtu svānunayāya mūrdhanidhanaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ na yatrāriṇā | 
 tvatto mūrdhabahutvataḥ phalam idaṃ samyaṅ mayā labhyate 
 chinnaṃ chinnam avekṣya rākṣasapate svaṃ durnayaṃ jñāsyasi  ||2111|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 ajñānād yadi vādhipatyarabhasād asmatparokṣaṃ hṛtā  
 sīteyaṃ pravimucyatāṃ śaṭha marutputrasya haste’dhunā | 
 no cel lakṣmaṇamuktamārgaṇagaṇacchedocchalacchoṇita 
 cchatracchannadigantam antakapuraṃ putrair vṛto yāsyasi  ||2112|| 
 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 revāmbhogarbhamajjadvividhavaravadhūhastayantrotthitābhiḥ 
 krīḍan svacchandamadbhiḥ smarasi yad akarod arjunaḥ kārtavīryaḥ | 
 taddoṣṇāṃ yac ca rāmo raṇabhuvi vidadhe vegavalgatkuṭhāraḥ 
 prāyaḥ paulastya sā te śravaṇaparigatā kiṃ na vārteti vidmaḥ  ||2113|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (bā.rā. 2.38, rājaśekharasya) 
 
 
 kule paulastyānāṃ na nijam amalaṃ janma kalitaṃ 
 bahoḥ kālān nālocitam atulam uccaiḥ svam ayaśaḥ | 
 prasūnaṃ puṣpeṣoḥ śaram asahatā kiṃ ca bhavatā 
 sa patrī saumitrer aśanisahadharmā na gaṇitaḥ  ||2114|| 
 
 
 gosokasya | 
 
 
 śirobhir mā devīḥ śiva iva na te dāsyati punar 
 dṛśaṃ dadyāḥ setāvadhijaladhi kailāsasubhaṭaḥ | 
 hitaṃ tad brūmas tvāṃ mama janakadordaṇḍavijaya 
 sphuratkīrtistambha tyaja kamalabandhoḥ kulavadhūm  ||2115|| 
 
 
 gadādharanāthasya | 
 
 
 24. saṃvādānuvādaḥ 
 
 
 dyām ālokayatāṃ kalāḥ kalayatāṃ chāyāḥ samācinvatāṃ 
 kleśaḥ kevalam aṅgulīr dalayatāṃ mauhūrtikānām ayam | 
 dhanyā sā rajanī tad eva sudinaṃ dhanyaḥ sa eva kṣaṇo 
 yatrājhātacaraścirān nayanayoḥ sīmānam eti priyaḥ  ||2116|| 
 
 
 vasudharasya | (su.ra. 1649) 
 
 
 teṣāṃ tvaṃ nidhir āgasām asahanā mānonnatā sāpy ato 
 gantavyaṃ bhavatā na tadgṛham iti tvaṃ vāryase yāsi cet | 
 gāḍhaṃ mekhalayā balān niyamitaḥ karṇotpalenāhataḥ  
 kṣiptaḥ pādatale tadekaśaraṇo manye ciraṃ sthāsyasi  ||2117|| 
 
 
 chittipasya | (śā.pa. 1650) 
 
 
 jāne sāsahanā tathāham asakṛn mayy aṅgaṇasthe punas 
 tasyāḥ saṃbhavitā sa sādhvasarasaḥ ko’pi prakopāpahaḥ | 
 yenodyatpulakaprakampavikalair aṅgaiḥ kva karṇotpalaṃ 
 kutrātmā kva ca mekhaleti galitaḥ prāyaḥ sa mānagrahaḥ  ||2118|| 
 
 
 vasundharasya | (su.ra. 1651) 
 
 
 anyā sādhigatā tvayā kva yuvatī yasyāḥ sa mānagraho  
 yāte locanagocaraṃ priyatame saṃpraty apakrāmati | 
 asmākaṃ punar ugrapūruṣaśatāśleṣapragalbhātmanām  
 etādṛśy anabhijñapūruṣapariṣvaṅge kutaḥ sādhvasam  ||2119|| 
 
 
 chittipasya | 
 
 
 asmābhiḥ kalitaṃ purā na bhavatī bhuktā nṛbhiḥ kair api  
 prauḍhā mānavaśālinīti calitaṃ cetaḥ sakāmaṃ tvayi | 
 dhik tvāṃ saṃprati sadbhujaṅgajanatāsaṃśleṣam ātanvatī  
 gamyā sarvajanasya vāravanitevotkṣepaṇīyāsi naḥ  ||2120|| 
 
 
 
 vasundharasya | 
 
 
 25. kaviḥ 
 
 
 trailokyam udare viṣṇos tādṛg eva vyavasthitam | 
 tādṛg anyādṛg apy asti hṛdaye tu mahākaveḥ  ||2121|| 
 
 
 vasukalpasya | 
 
 
 yan netrais tribhir īkṣate na giriśo nāṣṭābhir apy abjabhūḥ 
 sakndo dvādaśabhis tathā na maghavā cakṣuḥsahasreṇa yat | 
 saṃbhūyāpi jagattrayasya nayanair draṣṭuṃ na yat pāryate  
 pratyāhṛtya dṛśau samāhitadhiyaḥ paśyanti tatpaṇḍitāḥ  ||2122|| 
 
 
 śālikanāthasya | (su.ra. 1249) 
 
 
 udanvacchinnā bhūḥ sa ca nidhirapāṃ yojanaśataṃ 
 sadā pānthaḥ pūṣā gaganaparimāṇaṃ kalayati | 
 iti prāyo bhāvāḥ sphuradavadhimudrāmukulitāḥ 
 satāṃ prajñonmeṣaḥ punar ayam asīmā vijayate  ||2123|| 
 
 
 
 rājaśekharasya | (bā.rā. 1.8, Sv 322, sā.da. under 7.4, su.ra. 1223) 
 
 
 nidhānaṃ vidyānāṃ kulagṛham apārasya yaśasaḥ 
 kalā sampadratnavratativiṭapānāṃ surataruḥ | 
 śuci kṣauṇīndrāṇāṃ sucaritakathādarpaṇatalaṃ 
 prakṛtyā gambhīraḥ kavir iti hi śabdo vijayate  ||2124|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 ||2125||  nāsty atra ślokaḥ | 
 
 
 26. nānākavayaḥ  
 
 
 bāṇaḥ sṛṣṭim apūrvavastuviṣayām eko’tra nirvyūḍhavān 
 niṣṇātaḥ kavikuñjarendracarite mārge girāṃ vā guruḥ | 
 vedhā vindhyapulindapāmaravadhūbhūgolajhañjhānila 
 prāye’rthe vacanāni pallavayituṃ jānāti yogeśvaraḥ  ||2126|| 
 
 
 bhavānandasya | (su.ra. 1699) 
 
 
 astaṃgatabhāraviravi kālavaśāt kālidāsavidhuvidhuram | 
 nirvāṇabāṇadīpaṃ jagad idam adyoti ratnena  ||2127|| 
 
 
 
 bhojadevasya | (su.ra. 1706) 
 
 
 bāṇaḥ prāṇiti keśaṭaḥ sphuṭam asau jāgarti yogeśvaraḥ  
 pratyujjīvati rājaśekharagirāṃ saurabhyam unmīlati | 
 yenāyaṃ kalikālapuṣpadhanuṣo devasya śikṣāvaśād 
 ākalpaṃ vasukalpa eva vacasi prāgalbhyam abhyasyati  ||2128|| 
 
 
 vasukalpasya | 
 
 
 unnīto bhavabhūtinā pratidinaṃ bāṇe gate yaḥ purā 
 yaś cīrṇaḥ kamalāyudhena suciraṃ yenāgamat keśaṭaḥ | 
 yaḥ śrīvākpatirājapādarajasāṃ saṃparkapūtaś ciraṃ 
 diṣṭyā ślāghyaguṇasya kasyacid asau mārgaḥ samunmīlati  ||2129|| 
 
 
 
 abhinandasya | (su.ra. 1733) 
 
 
 subandhau bhaktir naḥ ka iha raghukāre na ramate 
 dhṛtir dākṣīputre harati haricandro’pi hṛdayam | 
 viśuddhoktiḥ śūraḥ prakṛtimadhurā bhāvavigiras 
 tathāpy antar modaṃ kam api bhavabhūtir vitanute  ||2130|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 1698) 
 
 
 27. pratyekakaviḥ  
 
 
 vikacakumudakrīḍakrīḍan madhuvratajhāṅkṛteer 
 madakalakuhūkaṇṭhotkaṇṭhāvipañcitapañcamām | 
 abhinavavadhūpremālāpād api śrutisaṃmadaṃ 
 vidadhati kaver daṅkasyaitāḥ sudhāmadhurā giraḥ  ||2131|| 
 
 
 daṅkasya | 
 
 
 prayogavyutpattau pratipadaviśeṣārthakathane 
 prasattau gāmbhīrye rasavati ca kāvyārtharacane | 
 agamyāyām anyair diśi pariṇatair arthavacasor 
 mataṃ ced asmākaṃ kavir amarasiṃho vijayate  ||2132|| 
 
 
 śālikanāthasya | (su.ra. 1724) 
 
 
 pātu karṇarasāyanaṃ racayituṃ vācaḥ satāṃ saṃmatā 
 vyutpattiṃ paramām avāptum avadhiṃ labdhuṃ rasasrotasaḥ | 
 bhoktuṃ svādu phalaṃ ca jīvitataror yady asti te kautukaṃ 
 tad bhrātaḥ śṛṇu rājaśekharakaveḥ sūktīḥ sudhāsyandanīḥ  ||2133|| 
 
 
 śaṅkaravarmaṇaḥ | (bā.rā. 1.17, vi.śā.bha. 1.17, su.ra. 1700) 
 
 
 dhig dhik tān samayān pariśramarujo vaktuṃ giro nīrasā 
 yatrāmūr nipatanti vallaṇaguṇotkhātāmṛtaprītayaḥ | 
 romṇāṃ nṛtyabhuvo vilocanapayaḥpūrābdhicandrodayāḥ 
 sāhityapratigaṇḍagarvagalanaṃ glānikriyāhetavaḥ  ||2134|| 
 
 
 vallaṇasya | (su.ra. 1703) 
 
 
 devīṃ vācam upāsate hi bahavaḥ sāraṃ tu sārasvataṃ 
 jānīte nitarām asau gurukulakliṣṭo murāriḥ kaviḥ | 
 ābdhar laṅghita eva vānarabhaṭaiḥ kiṃ tv asya gambhīrtām 
 āpātālanimagnapīvaratanur jānāti manthācalaḥ  ||2135|| 
 
 
 murāreḥ | (Kuval, p. 58; su.ra. 1701) 
 
 
 28. manasvikaviḥ 
 
 
 vinyastā vikacaprasūnaghaṭanācāryeṇa kaṇṭhocitā 
 māleyaṃ bhujagabhrameṇa bhavatā janmāndha kiṃ dhūyate | 
 etasyāḥ kṣatir astu nāma kiyatī saṃvītahāsodgamās 
 tvām anyonyakarārpaṇapraṇayinaḥ paśyanti viśve janāḥ  ||2136|| 
 
 
 jalacandrasya | 
 
 
 avadhehi kṣaṇam ehi bhrātar bhāvajña bhāvaya giraṃ naḥ | 
 carame cakāsti cetasi mūkasvapnopamo bhāvaḥ  ||2137|| 
 
 
 
 gosokasya | 
 
 
 stambhāvadhehi nimiṣaṃ paṭhāmi sūktīḥ svacittanirvṛttaye | 
 mā budhyasva na tāvad vāg ulkābhiḥ kadarthayasi  ||2138|| 
 
 
 vallaṇasya | 
 
 
 śrīmadbhir draviṇavyayavyatikarakleśād avajñāyase 
 dveṣān bhaḥparipūrṇakarṇakuharair nākarṇyase sūribhiḥ | 
 itthaṃ vyarthitavāñchiteṣu hi mudhaivāsmāsu kiṃ khidyase 
 mātaḥ kāvyasudhe kathaṃ kva bhavatīm unmudrayāmo vayam  ||2139|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 arvācīnavacaḥ prapañcasukhināṃ duḥśikṣitānāṃ puro  
 gambhīraṃ kavipuṅgavasya kim aho sarvasvam uddhāṭyate | 
 vyarthaṃ kardamagandhagauravahṛtagrāmīṇagoṣṭhīmukhe  
 ko’yaṃ nāma sacetano’sti ya iha prastauti kastūrikām  ||2140|| 
 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 29. kavidānaṃ  
 
 
 niṣpanne sati candracūḍacarite tattannṛpaprakriyā 
 jātaiḥ sārdham arātirājakaśiroratnāñjalīnāṃ trayam | 
 saptasvarṇaśatāni viṃśatiśatīrūpyasya lakṣatrayaṃ 
 grāmāṇāṃ śatam antaraṅgakavaye cāṇakyacandro dadau  ||2141|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 dantivyūhaṃ kanakakalitaṃ cāmare hemadaṇḍaṃ 
 yo gauḍendrād alabhata kavikṣmābhṛtāṃ cakravartī | 
 khyāto yaś ca śrutidharatayā vikramādityagoṣṭhī 
 vidyābhartuḥ khalu vararucer āsasāda pratiṣṭhām  ||2142|| 
 
 
 dhoyīkasya | 
 kanakakunḍalamaṇḍitabhāṣiṇe 
 śakaripur viṣayān daśa vidviṣaḥ | 
 magadhakekayakeralakośalān 
 kariśataṃ ca madālasalocanam  ||2143|| 
 
 
 
 amaroḥ | 
 
 
 amuṣmai caurāya pratinihatamṛtyupratibhiye  
 prabhuḥ prītaḥ prādād uparitanapādadvayakṛte | 
 suvarṇānāṃ koṭīr daśa daśanakoṭikṣatagirīn  
 gajendrānapy aṣṭau madamuditakūjan madhulihaḥ  ||2144|| 
 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 śloko’yaṃ hariṣābhidhānakavinā devasya tasyāgrato 
 yāvad yāvad udīritaḥ śakavadhūvaidhavyadīkṣāguroḥ | 
 tāvat tāvad upoḍhasāndrapulakas tasmai sa devo dadau 
 lakṣaṃ lakṣam akhaṇḍitaṃ madhukaravyālolagaṇḍaṃ gajam  ||2145|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 30. guṇigarvaḥ  
 
 
 ṣaṭtarkān api śabdaśāsanam api sthānaiḥ sthitaṃ pañcabhir 
 mīmāṃsādvayam apy ananyasadṛśīṃ sāhityavidyām api | 
 vidmaḥ kiṃ ca mahāvikalpabahalajvālāvalītāpiteṣv 
 āsmākeṣu na jalpavahniṣu punaḥ kaiḥ kaiḥ pataṅgāyitam  ||2146|| 
 
 
 tapasvinaḥ | 
 
 
 tāvat tārkikacakravartipadavī tāvat kavīnāṃ giras 
 tāvac cāpratimallatāmadabharaḥ sāhityapāṇḍityayoḥ | 
 yāvan na pratiparvanirbharasudhānirvājabījaṃ kṣaṇād 
 vāgvallyo vilasanti karṇakuhare śrīdevabodheritāḥ  ||2147|| 
 
 
 devabodhasya | 
 
 
 bindudvandvaraṅgitāgrasaraṇiḥ kartā śirobindukaṃ 
 karmety anvayakalpanāṃ vidadhate ye ke’pi tebhyo namaḥ | 
 ye tu granthasahasraśāṇakaṣaṇatruṭyatkalaṅgair girām 
 ullāsaiḥ kavayanti vallaṇakavis teṣv eva saṃnahyate  ||2148|| 
 
 
 vallaṇasya | 
 
 
 yathā yūnas tadvat paramaramaṇīyāpi ramaṇī 
 kumārāṇām antaḥkaraṇaharaṇaṃ kaiva kurute | 
 maduktiś ced antar madayati sudhībhūya sudhiyaḥ 
 kim asyā nāma syād arasapuruṣānādarabharaiḥ  ||2149|| 
 
 
 kavipaṇḍitaśrīharṣasya | (Nc 22.152) 
 
 
 sarvasvaṃ gṛhavartikuntalapatir gṛhṇātu tan me punar 
 bhāṇḍāgāram akhaṇḍam eva hṛdaye jāgarti sārasvatam | 
 bhoḥ kṣudrās tyajata pramodam acirād eṣyanti manmandiraṃ 
 helāndolitakarṇatālakaraṭiskandhādhirūḍhāḥ śriyaḥ  ||2150|| 
 
 
 silhaṇasya | 
 31. vāṇī  
 
 
 suvarṇālaṅkārā prakaṭitarasāśleṣanipuṇā 
 sphuradvaidarbhoktir lalitapadabandhakramagatiḥ | 
 lasad bhūyo bhāvā mṛdur api vimardocitatanuḥ 
 kavīndra tvadvāṇī harati hariṇākṣīva hṛdayam  ||2151|| 
 
 
 sākokasya | (su.ra. 1716) 
 
 
 ghanarasamayī gabhīrā vakrimasubhagopajīvitā kavibhiḥ | 
 avagāḍhā ca punīte gaṅgā baṅgālavāṇī ca  ||2152|| 
 
 
 baṅgālasya | 
 
 
 vāṇi vraja suralokaṃ triśaraṇapālo’pi devi tatraiva | 
 saṃprati kāvyapariśramavadhirair avadhīraṇāṃ yāsi  ||2153|| 
 
 
 tripurāripālasya | 
 
 
 pipāsuḥ pīyūṣaṃ tvam asi sarasasvādumadhuraṃ 
 śrutibhyām aśrāntaḥ piba madhuramṛdvīḥ kavigiraḥ | 
 athaitāḥ santoṣaṃ vidadhati na cec cetasi tataḥ  
 sudhāpi syān manye pṛthuvamathulābhāya bhavataḥ  ||2154|| 
 
 
 dhañjokasya | 
 
 
 iyaṃ gaur uddāmā tava nibiḍabandhāpi hi kathaṃ 
 na vaidarbhād anyat spṛśati sulabhatve’pi hi katham | 
 avandhyā ca khyātā bhuvi katham agamyā kavivṛṣaiḥ 
 kathaṃ vā pīyūṣaṃ sravati bahu dugdhāpi bahubhiḥ  ||2155|| 
 
 
 
 śabdārṇavasya | (su.ra. 1725) 
 
 
 32. kāvyam 
 
 
 yad etadvāgarthavyatikaramayaṃ kiñcid amṛtaṃ 
 tad ānandasyandaiḥ sahṛdayamanāṃsi snapayati | 
 idaṃ kāvyaṃ tattvaṃ sphurati tu yad atrānuparamaṃ 
 tad antarbuddhīnāṃ sphuṭam atha ca vācām aviṣayaḥ  ||2156|| 
 
 
 hṛṣīkeśasya (su.ra. 1715, sū.mu. 4.34) 
 
 
 kavalayati na cetas tasya dāridryaduḥkhaṃ 
 na ca piśunajanoktiḥ karṇakaṇḍūṃ karoti | 
 varakavikṛtagoṣṭhībandhagandhopabhoge 
 ya iha madhu vamantīṃ kāvyacintāṃ karoti  ||2157|| 
 
 
 vyāḍeḥ | 
 
 
 etat kavīndramukhacandramasaḥ kadācit 
 kāvyābhidhānam amṛtaṃ yadi nāgāliṣyat | 
 saṃsāriṇāṃ vividhaduḥkhasahasrabhājāṃ 
 cetovinodasadanaṃ kim ihābhaviṣyat  ||2158|| 
 
 
 surabheḥ | 
 
 
 te varṇāḥ sapadakramās tad abhidhāvaidagdhyam avyāhṛtaṃ 
 gumphaḥ ko’pi sapaktrimaḥ sahṛdayāsvādyo rasaḥ ko’py asau | 
 he sabhyāḥ paribhāvya mādṛśakṛtīr brūta kvacin niṣkṛtaṃ 
 kiṃ tatrāsty aparaṃ purātanakaver yenaiṣa kolāhalaḥ  ||2159|| 
 
 
 gosokasya | 
 
 
 anudghuṣṭaḥ śabdair atha ca ghaṭanāt prasphuṭarasaḥ 
 padānām arthātmā ramayati natūttānitarasaḥ | 
 yathā kiṃcid dṛśyaḥ pavanacalacīnāṃśukatayā 
 stanābhogaḥ strīṇāṃ harati na tathonmudritavapuḥ  ||2160|| 
 
 
 dharmāśokasya | (su.ra. 1705) 
 
 
 33. kāvyamātsaryam 
 
 
 vāyūdgāragatis tataḥ pariṇatiḥ sṛṣṭer aho kauśalaṃ 
 vāyuḥ śloka ihaiva santi sakalāḥ kāvyasya te te guṇāḥ | 
 kasyāyaṃ mama huṃ tathaiva śṛṇumaḥ samyak punaḥ paṭhyatāṃ 
 jānāmi sphuṭatātra nāsti bhaṇitaṃ cānyaiḥ purāṇaṃ paṭha  ||2161|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 drākṣāpākaviḍambinīm api giraṃ mātsaryadāhajvarā 
 nnācāmanti manāg arocakaparādhīnāḥ kiyanto janāḥ | 
 ākaṇṭhaṃ paripīya satkavigavīpīyūṣam anye punar 
 no mādyanti yaśaḥśarīrapiśitatrāsāya baddhaspṛhāḥ  ||2162|| 
 
 
 jalacandrasya | 
 
 
 bhrāmyanti kutukāvalambitamanāḥ sārakhatānāśramān 
 asmai vāṇi vidhehi durjanamarusthānāya dūre namaḥ | 
 na prāṇanti yadarpaṇād iha guṇāḥ kāmaṃ yaśovallayaḥ 
 khidyante sarasāpi satkavirasasrotasvatī sīdati  ||2163|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 kva rasika rasadā rasālavallī 
 kva ca rasakaṇṭakasaṅkaṭoyamadhvā | 
 racayasi rucirāṇi vāṇi mohād 
 iha sukumārapadāni hā hatāsi  ||2164|| 
 
 
 rāmadāsasya | 
 
 
 īṣannāsānikocaḥ svaramukharasukhaprekṣaṇaṃ hāsaleśaḥ 
 svābodhād aprasādadhvananam asadavadyoktihelāvahelā | 
 maunavyāsaṅgavārtāntarapararuciraślokapāṭhādayas te 
 soḍhavyāḥ ke kiyantaḥ śiva śiva kavi te kucchalā matsarāṇām  ||2165|| 
 
 
 kavipaṇḍitaśrīharṣasya || 
 
 
 34. kāvyacauraḥ 
 
 
 dhanyās te bhuvanaṃ punanti kavayo yeṣām ajasraṃ gavām 
 uddāmadhvanipallavena paritaḥ pūtā diśāṃ bhittayaḥ | 
 dhik tān niḥsvavilāsinaḥ kavikhalāṃl lokadvayadrohiṇo 
 nityākampitacetasaḥ paragavīdohena jīvanti ye  ||2166|| 
 
 
 jalacandrasya | 
 
 
 baddho lambitacūḍam añjalir ayaṃ vāṇi kṣamasvāmṛtaṃ 
 na brūmas tvayi devabhāvasulabhaṃ na dyotate tanmahaḥ | 
 syāc ced īṣad api prasahya rasanāṭaṅkaiḥ kathaṃ khaṇḍaśaś 
 chindanto bhavatīṃ kavīndraghaṭitāṃ jīvanty amī dasyavaḥ  ||2167|| 
 
 
 vaidyagadādharasya | 
 
 
 niḥśaṅkaṃ hara kāñcanāny anibhṛtaṃ dārān guroḥ śīlaya 
 svacchandaṃ piba vāruṇīṃ jahi nirātaṅkaṃ dvijānāṃ kulam | 
 tais taiḥ pātakibhiḥ samaṃ vasa sukhaṃ mā satkavīnāṃ kṛthāḥ 
 steyaṃ sūktinidhānasadmani durucchedaṃ hi tatkilbiṣam  ||2168|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 iyaṃ gaur ekā naḥ kvacid api na saṃyojanavidhā 
 vamuṣyāḥ paśyāmo rasabharamucaḥ kāṃcid aparām | 
 gale baddhā dadhmo yadi na dhṛitir uddāmavidhṛtau 
 bhayaṃ gocorebhyas tad iha ka upāyaḥ prabhavatu  ||2169|| 
 
 
 selhūkasya | 
 
 
 hṛtkaṇṭhaśrutibhūṣaṇāni bahuśo bhrātaḥ suvarṇāny api  
 svāny asmābhir upāhṛtāni vipaṇisthāneṣu dainyān na kim | 
 dhik karmāṇi tulaiva nāsti na kaṣagrāvā na mānakramo 
 na kretā na parīkṣakaḥ param abhūd uccair bhayaṃ durjanān  ||2170|| 
 
 
 jitāreḥ | 
 35. sajjanaḥ 
 
 
 añjalisthāni puṣpāṇi vāsayanti karadvayam | 
 aho sumanasāṃ vṛttir vāmadakṣiṇayoḥ samā  ||2171|| 
 
 
 gobhaṭasya | (su.ra. 1232, śā.pa. 199) 
 
 
 ayaṃ nijaḥ paro veti gaṇanā laghucetasām | 
 udāracaritānāṃ tu vasudhaiva kuṭumbakam  ||2172|| 
 
 
 keśaṭasya | (su.ra. 1241) 
 
 
 sujano na yāti vairaṃ parahitabuddhir vināśakāle’pi | 
 chede’pi candanataruḥ surabhayati mukhaṃ kuṭhārasya  ||2173|| 
 
 
 śrīvyāsapādānām | (Sv 241, śā.pa. 237, sū.mu. 6.12) 
 
 
 asanto nābhyarthyāḥ suhṛd api na yācyas tanudhanaḥ  
 priyāvṛttir nyāyyā caritam asubhaṅge’py amalinam | 
 vipady uccaiḥ stheyaṃ padam anuvidheyaṃ ca mahatāṃ 
 satāṃ kenoddiṣṭaṃ viṣamamasidhārāvratam idam  ||2174|| 
 
 
 dharmakīrteḥ | (su.ra. 1213, Sv 280) 
 
 
 ye dīneṣu dayālavaḥ spṛśati yān alpo’pi na śrīmado 
 vyagrā ye ca paropakārakaraṇe hṛṣyanti ye yācitāḥ | 
 svasthāḥ saty api yauvanodayamahāvyādhiprakope’pi ye 
 te bhūmaṇḍanaikatilakāḥ santaḥ kiyanto janāḥ  ||2175|| 
 
 
 śabdārṇavasya || (su.ra. 1238, śā.pa. 228, sū.mu. 6.30) 
 36. durjanaḥ 
 
 
 ete snehamayā iti mā mā kṣudreṣu yāta viśvāsam | 
 siddhārthānām eṣāṃ sneho’py aśrūṇi pātayati  ||2176|| 
 
 
 gobhaṭasya | (su.ra. 1296) 
 
 
 ko’rthān prāpya na garvito bhuvi naraḥ kasyāpados taṃ gatāḥ  
 strībhiḥ kasya na khaṇḍitaṃ bhuvi manaḥ ko nāma rājñāṃ priyaḥ | 
 kaḥ kālasya na gocarāntaragataḥ ko’rtho gato gauravaṃ 
 ko vā durjanavāgurāsu patitaḥ kṣemeṇa yātaḥ pumān  ||2177|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (Sv 3470, śā.pa. 1534) 
 
 
 dūrād ucchritapāṇir ārdranayanaḥ protsāritārdhāsano 
 gāḍhāliṅganatatparaḥ priyakathāpraśneṣu dattottaraḥ | 
 antargūḍhaviṣo bahir madhumayaś cātīva māyāpaṭuḥ 
 ko nāmāyam apūrvanāṭakavidhir yaḥ śikṣito durjanaiḥ  ||2178|| 
 
 
 binduśarmaṇaḥ | (Sv 342) 
 
 
 guṇotkarṣadveṣāt prakṛtimahatām apy asadṛśaṃ 
 khalaḥ kiṃcid vākyaṃ racayati ca vistārayati ca | 
 na ced eṣāṃ tādṛk kamalakalikārdhapratinidhau 
 muner gaṇḍūṣe’bdhiḥ sthita iti kuto’yaṃ kalakalaḥ  ||2179|| 
 
 
 śaśī divasadhūsaro galitayauvanā kāminī 
 saro vigatavārijaṃ mukham anakṣaraṃ svākṛteḥ | 
 prabhur dhanaparāyaṇaḥ satatadurgataḥ sajjano 
 nṛpāṅgaṇagataḥ khalo manasi sapta śalyāni me  ||2180|| 
 
 
 śilhaṇasya | (Ns 10, Sv 3458, sā.da. 10.110, śā.pa. 1530) 
 
 
 37. sujanadurjanau 
 
 
 jīvantu sādhutaravaḥ sukṛtāmbusiktā 
 naśyantu paṅkapatitāḥ khalapāṃśavo’pi | 
 ye dhārayanty anugatopakṛtivratāni 
 yaiḥ sannidhau paraguṇā malinīkriyante  ||2181|| 
 
 
 saṅketasya | 
 
 
 satsaṅgād bhavati hi sādhutā khalānāṃ 
 sādhūnāṃ na tu khalasaṅgamāt khalatvam | 
 āmodaṃ kusumabhavaṃ mṛd eva dhatte 
 mṛdgandhaṃ na tu kusumāni dhārayanti  ||2182|| 
 
 
 prabhākaramitrasya | 
 
 
 ye kāruṇyaparigrahād agaṇitasvārthāḥ parārthaṃ prati 
 prāṇair apy apakurvate vyasaninas te sādhavo dūrataḥ | 
 vidveṣānugamād anūrjitakṛpo rūkṣo jano vartate  
 cakṣuḥ saṃhara bāṣpavegam adhunā kasyāgrato rudyate  ||2183|| 
 
 
 śrīharṣasya | (su.ra. 1499) 
 
 
 śiśutvavyāmohāt kalayasi na cet tattvam anayos 
 tadā stokaṃ brūmaḥ paricinu vacas tvaṃ sadasatoḥ | 
 satāṃ svāntaṃ yat tan madhumadhuram antaḥ kaṭu bahir 
 bahiḥ svādu svacchaṃ viṣaviṣamam antas tad asatām  ||2184|| 
 
 
 jiyokasya | 
 
 
 ārambhagurvī kṣayiṇī krameṇa  
 laghvī purā vṛddhimatī ca paścāt | 
 dinasya pūrvārdhaparārdhabhinnā  
 chāyeva maitrī khalu sajjanānām  ||2185|| 
 
 
 38. dhanyaḥ 
 
 
 bhrāmyadbāliśakīrapakṣaharitacchāyāṃ bahir bibhratīm 
 antar dantur apāribhadrakalikāgarbhaprabhātaskarīm | 
 śuktir mārakatīva kuṅkumalasajjambālapūrṇodarā 
 vāsālīsukṛtātmanāṃ praṇayinī celaṃ mukhaṃ cumbati  ||2186|| 
 
 
 sendūkasya | 
 
 
 viṣayapatir alubdho dhenubhir dhāma pūtaṃ 
 katicid abhimatāyāṃ sīmni sīrā vahanti | 
 śithilayati ca bhāryā nātitheyīṃ saparyām 
 iti sukṛtam anena vyañjitaṃ naḥ phalena  ||2187|| 
 
 
 śubhāṅkasya | 
 
 
 dhārānipātaravabodhitapañjarastha 
 dātyūhaḍambarakarambitakaṇṭhakūjāḥ | 
 aṭṭeṣu kāṇḍapaṭavāritaśīkareṣu 
 dhanyāḥ pibanti mukhatāmarasaṃ vadhūnām  ||2188|| 
 
 
 śrīhanūmataḥ | (su.ra. 224) 
 
 
 śilāpaṭṭodghṛṣṭā malayajarasālepasubhagāḥ 
 sphuraddhūmāmodā daradalitakarpūrasuhṛdaḥ | 
 itaḥ kambucchedacchavibhir ahivallīkisalayair 
 niṣevante ke’pi kramukaphalaphāṇīḥ sukṛtinaḥ  ||2189|| 
 
 
 rājaśekharasya |  
 
 
 śiśutvaṃ tāruṇyaṃ tad anu ca dadhānāḥ pariṇatiṃ 
 gatāḥ pāṃśukrīḍāviṣayaparipāṭīrūpaśatam | 
 luṭhanto’ṅke mātuḥ kuvalayadṛśāṃ puṇyasaritāṃ 
 pibanti svacchandaṃ stanam adharam ambhaḥ sukṛtinaḥ  ||2190|| 
 
 
 śrīhanūmataḥ | (su.ra. 1621) 
 
 
 39. udāttaḥ  
 
 
 vimalamatibhiḥ kair apy etaj jagajjanitaṃ purā 
 vidhṛtam aparair dattaṃ cānyair vijitya tṛṇaṃ yathā | 
 iha hi bhuvanāny anye dhīrāś caturdaśa bhuñjate  
 katipayapurasvānte puṃsāṃ ka eṣa madajvaraḥ  ||2191|| 
 
 
 bhartṛhareḥ | (Ss 2.14) 
 
 
 kenenduḥ kumudeṣu kena taraṇiḥ padmeṣu kenāmbudaḥ 
 sāraṅgeṣv atha kena śākhiṣu madhur dākṣiṇyam adhyāpitaḥ | 
 tat tuṅgānanubhūtasaurabhaparīvāropakāraṃ prati 
 śmaśrūdvejitakarṇajāham anujaḥ kaḥ prerayatv īśvarān  ||2192|| 
 
 
 śuṅgokasya | 
 
 
 bhavanti namrās taravaḥ phalāgamair 
 navāmbubhir dūravilambino ghanāḥ | 
 anuddhatāḥ satpuruṣāḥ samṛddhibhiḥ 
 svabhāva evaiṣa paropakāriṇām  ||2193|| 
 
 
 kālidāsasya | (Çak 5.12; Ns 63) 
 
 
 yadālokaṃ kurvan bhramati ravir aśrāntaturagaḥ 
 sadāloān dhatte yadagaṇitabādhā vasumatī | 
 na sambandhaḥ kiṃ tu prakṛtir iyam evaṃ hi mahatāṃ 
 yad ete lokānāṃ parahitasukhaikāntarasikāḥ  ||2194|| 
 
 
 meghārudrasya | 
 
 
 dhātrīṃ dhātuṃ vahati phaṇinām agraṇīḥ kasya śikṣāṃ 
 ko vā brūte timirapaṭalaploṣam ahnaḥ praṇetuḥ | 
 adriśreṇīm avati jaladhiḥ kena dattābhyanujñaḥ 
 karma prāyo bhavati mahatāṃ svānurūpaṃ mahimnaḥ  ||2195|| 
 40. manasvī 
 
 
 mā khedaṃ bhaja he vidhuntuda mudaṃ dhehi stuhi tvaṃ hares 
 tac cakraṃ vinikṛtya dagdham udaraṃ yenottamāṅgīkṛtaḥ | 
 paśyāsmān udarambharīn iha parābhūtān nirastān hatān 
 vidhvastānavavāritān adharitān etān dhanāhaṃyubhiḥ  ||2196|| 
 
 
 baṭeśvarasya | 
 
 
 yad ete sādhūnām upari mukharā eva dhanino 
 na sāvajñair eṣām api ca nijavittavyayabhayam | 
 na vā kleśo’muṣminn aparam anukampaiva bhavati 
 svamāṃsas trastebhyaḥ ka iha hariṇebhyaḥ paribhavaḥ  ||2197|| 
 
 
 bhartṛhareḥ | (su.ra. 1468, Ss 3.23) 
 
 
 śataṃ vā lakṣaṃ vā niyutam athavā koṭim athavā 
 tṛṇāyāhaṃ manye samayaviparītaṃ yadi bhavet | 
 śataṃ tal lakṣaṃ tan niyutam api tatkoṭir api tad 
 yad āptaṃ sammānād api tṛṇam anamraṇa śirasā  ||2198|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva |  
 
 
 mā gāḥ pratyupakārakātaratayā vaivarṇyam ākarṇaya 
 śrīkarṇāṭavasundharādhipa sudhāsiktāni sūktāni naḥ | 
 varṇyante kati nāma nārṇavanadībhūgolavindhyāṭavī 
 jhañjhāmārutacandramaḥprabhṛtayas tebhyaḥ kim āptaṃ mayā  ||2199|| 
 
 
 silhanasya |  
 
 
 rājā tvaṃ vayam apy upāsitaguruprajñābhimānonnatāḥ 
 khyātas tvaṃ vibhavair yaśāṃsi kavayo dikṣu pratanvanti naḥ | 
 itthaṃ mānada nātidūram ubhayor apy āvayor antaraṃ 
 yady asmāsu parāṅmukho’si vayam apy ekāntito niḥspṛhāḥ  ||2200|| 
 
 
 vallaṇasya | (su.ra. 1222) 
 
 
 41. kṛpaṇaḥ 
 
 
 varaṃ mṛto na tu kṣudras tathāpi mahad antaram | 
 ekasya bandhur nādatte nāmāny asyākhilo janaḥ  ||2201|| 
 
 
 śabdārṇavasya | (su.ra. 1323) 
 
 
 jīvatāpi śaveneva kṛpaṇana na dīyate | 
 māṃsaṃ vardhayatānena kākasyopakṛtiḥ kṛtā  ||2202|| 
 
 
 kavirājasya | (su.ra. 1325) 
 
 
 dṛḍhataranibaddhamuṣṭeḥ koṣaniṣaṇṇasya sahajamalinasya | 
 kṛpaṇasya kṛpāṇasya ca kevalam ākārato bhedaḥ  ||2203|| 
 
 
 gobhaṭasya | (sū.mu. 9.13, su.ra. 1327) 
 
 
 asambhogena sāmānyaṃ kṛpaṇasya dhanaṃ paraiḥ | 
 asyedam iti sambandho hānau duḥkhena gamyate  ||2204|| 
 
 
 śrīvyāsapādānām | (sū.mu. 9.1) 
 
 
 kṛpaṇasyāstu dāridryaṃ kārpaṇyāvṛtikārakam | 
 vibhavas tasya taddoṣaghoṣaṇāpaṭuḍiṇḍimaḥ  ||2205|| 
 
 
 teṣām eva | (su.ra. 1324) 
 
 
 42. sevakaḥ 
 
 
 maunān mūrkhaḥ pravacanapaṭur vātulo jalpako vā 
 dhṛṣṭaḥ pārśve vasati niyataṃ dūrataś cāpragalbhaḥ | 
 kṣāntyā bhīrur yadi na sahate prāyaśo nābhijātaḥ  
 sevādharmaḥ paramagahano yoginām apy agamyaḥ  ||2206|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (Ns 35) 
 
 
 gātrair girā ca vikalaś caṭum īśvarāṇāṃ 
 kurvann ayaṃ prahasanasya naṭaḥ kṛto’si | 
 na tvāṃ punaḥ pallitavarṇakabhājam etan 
 nāṭyena kena naṭayiṣyati dīrgham āyuḥ  ||2207|| 
 
 
 murāreḥ | (Ar 3.1, su.ra. 1526) 
 
 
 yad vaktraṃ muhur īkṣase na dhanināṃ brūṣe na cāṭuṃ mṛṣā 
 naiṣāṃ garvagiraḥ śṛṇoṣi na punaḥ pratyāśayā dhāvasi | 
 kāle bālatṛṇāni khādasi sukhaṃ nidrāsi nidrāgame 
 tan me brūhi kuraṅga kutra bhavatā kiṃ nāma taptaṃ tapaḥ  ||2208|| 
 
 
 silhaṇasya | (su.ra. 1602, Ss 1.14) 
 
 
 praṇamaty unnatihetor jīvanahetor vimuñcati prāṇān | 
 duḥkhīyati sukhahetoḥ ko mūḍhaḥ sevakād anyaḥ  ||2209|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (sā.da. under 10.93) 
 
 
 hasati hasati svāminy uccaiḥ rudaty api roditi 
 guṇasamuditaṃ preṣyākāraṃ pranindati nindati | 
 draviṇakaṇikākrītaṃ yantraṃ pranṛtyati nṛtyati  
 pracaladasibhṛddolrdaṇḍāriṃ pradhāvati dhāvati  ||2210|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (Sv 3232) 
 43. manasvisevakaḥ 
 
 
 soḍhaṃ dvāḥsthitaduḥsthitadurvacaḥ kaṭu tato dṛṣṭo durīśaś cirād 
 udgīrṇāḥ svaguṇāś ca yācitam atha śrotre kṛtā neti gīḥ | 
 asmin pātakapañcake sati mahaty ābrahmahatyādikaṃ 
 yat pāpaṃ mahad ūcire manumukhāḥ ko’nv eṣa teṣāṃ bhramaḥ  ||2211|| 
 
 
 dharmapālasya |  
 
 
 lajje lajje nimajja kvacid api nibhṛtaṃ tiṣṭha tiṣṭha pratiṣṭhe 
 gaccha droṇīṃ himādreḥ punar api tapase bhārati svasti tubhyam | 
 so’haṃ puṇyakṣayeṇa pracuraparibhavātaṅkini prauḍhatāpe 
 sevāpaṅke pratāmi draviṇakaṇadhiyā niṣkṛpāṇāṃ nṛpāṇām  ||2212|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 amīṣāṃ prāṇānāṃ tulinavisinīpatrapayasāṃ 
 kṛte kiṃ nāsmābhir vigalitavivekair vyavasitam | 
 yadīśānām agre draviṇamadamohāndhamanasāṃ 
 kṛtaṃ vītavrīḍair nijaguṇakathāpātakam api  ||2213|| 
 
 
 dharmakīrteḥ | (su.ra. 1467, Ss 1.9) 
 
 
 kāmaṃ vaneṣu hariṇās tṛṇena jīvanty ayatnasulabhena | 
 vidadhati dhaniṣu na dainyaṃ te kila paśavo vayaṃ sudhiyaḥ  ||2214|| 
 
 
 silhaṇasya | (Ss 1.15, śā.pa. 261, sū.mu. 26.1, su.ra. 1494) 
 
 
 vayam anipuṇāḥ karṇaprānte niveśayituṃ mukhaṃ 
 kṛtakamadhuraṃ bhartur bhāvaṃ na bhāvayituṃ kṣamāḥ | 
 priyam api vaco mithyā vaktuṃ janair na ca śikṣitāḥ 
 ka iha sa guṇo yena syāma kṣitīśvaravallabhāḥ  ||2215|| 
 
 
 bhartṛhareḥ | (su.ra. 1470) 
 44. durīśvarasevakaḥ 
 
 
 prāleyād api śītalo hutavahaḥ pīyūṣagarbhād api  
 svādīyo garalaṃ bhaved api mṛdur dambholir ambhojataḥ | 
 vyāhārād api subhruvāṃ khalavacaḥ karṇadvayīdohadaṃ 
 na tv etā duradhīśvarasya kuṭilakrūrāḥ kaṭākṣormayaḥ  ||2216|| 
 
 
 śaṅkhadharasya | 
 
 
 snātaṃ māravarocir ambhasi kṛtaḥ snehagrahaḥ saikate 
 pāṣāṇe jantoṅkuraḥ svakusumaiḥ sṛṣṭaḥ śiraḥśekharaḥ | 
 bandhyāyā vihitā sutena sakhitā kūrmāṅganāyāḥ payaḥ  
 pītaṃ yena niṣevya mugdhadhaninaḥ sampāditāḥ sampadaḥ  ||2217|| 
 
 
 paṇḍitaśaśinaḥ || 
 
 
 araṇyaruditaṃ kṛtaṃ śavaśarīram udvartitaṃ 
 sthale’bjam avaropitaṃ suicram ūṣare varṣitam | 
 śvapuccham avanāmitaṃ vadhirakarṇajāpaḥ kṛtaḥ 
 kṛtāndhamukurakriyā yad abudho janaḥ sevitaḥ  ||2218|| 
 
 
 silhaṇasya |  
 
 
 toyaṃ nirmathitaṃ ghṛtāya madhune nispīḍitaḥ prastaraḥ 
 pānārthaṃ mṛgatṛṣṇikormitaralā bhūmiḥ samālokitā | 
 dugdhā seyam acetanena jaratī dugdhāśayā śūkarī 
 kaṣṭaṃ yat khalu dīrghayā dhanatṛṣā nīco janaḥ sevitaḥ  ||2219|| 
 
 
 amarasiṃhasya | (su.ra. 1515) 
 
 
 stabdhas tiṣṭhasi paśyad andhapurataḥ kiṃ darśanākāṅkṣayā 
 jalpan mūkamukhāditaḥ prativacaḥ kiṃ śrotum ākāṅkṣasi | 
 yaḥ śṛṇvad vadhiraḥ śṛṇoti sa kathaṃ vijñaptikāṃ tāvakīṃ 
 prāṇapretam upāsamānanapaṭhanmūrkhas tvadanyo janaḥ  ||2220|| 
 
 
 vallaṇasya |  
 45. kṣudrodayaduḥkhitaḥ 
 
 
 sukhaṃ jīvanti jātāndhāḥ parvatāḥ sarito’pi ca | 
 kṣudrābhyudayasākṣibhyām akṣibhyāṃ hā hatā vayam  ||2221|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 dhanyāḥ khalu nīcānāṃ tṛṣṇātāpārtividhuramanasāpi | 
 bhrukuṭitaraṅgakuṭilāṃ na dṛṣṭisaritaṃ vigāhante  ||2222|| 
 
 
 śaṅkaradharasya | 
 
 
 alaṅghyaṃ sarveṣām iha khalu phalaṃ karmajanitaṃ  
 vipat karma praiṣyā vyathayati na jātāsi hṛdayam | 
 yadajñāḥ kurvanti prasabham upahāsaṃ dhanamadād  
 idaṃ tv antargāḍhaṃ paramaparitāpaṃ janayati  ||2223|| 
 
 
 
 dharmākarasya | 
 
 
 he locanadvaya calajjalabudbudābha 
 kiṃ na prayāsi kaṭakāmaṇivad vilīya | 
 yad daivalabdhavasumūrkhamukhāvalepa 
 mudrām udīkṣitum ayaṃ tava janmalābhaḥ  ||2224|| 
 
 
 vākkokasya | 
 
 
 vidyāvān api janmavān api tathā yukto’pi tais tair guṇair 
 yan nāpnoti manaḥ samīhitaphalaṃ daivasya sā vācyatā | 
 etāvat tu hṛdi vyathāṃ vitanute yatprāktanaiḥ karmabhir 
 lakṣmīṃ prāpya jaḍo’py asādhur api ca svāṃ yogyatāṃ manyate  ||2225|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 1482) 
 
 
 46. dāridryam 
 
 
 lagnaḥ śṛṅgayuge gṛhī satanayo vṛddhau gurū pārśvayoḥ 
 pucchāgre gṛhiṇī khureṣu śiśavo lagnā vadhūḥ kambale | 
 ekaḥ śīrṇajaradgavo vidhivaśāt sarvasvabhūto gṛhe 
 sarveṇaiva kuṭumbakena rudatā suptaḥ samutthāpyate  ||2226|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 1317) 
   
 prāyo daridraśiśavaḥ paramandirāṇāṃ 
 dvāreṣu dattakarapallavalīnadehāḥ | 
 lajjānigūḍhavacaso bahubhoktukāmā 
 bhoktāram ardhanayanena vilokayanti  ||2227|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 1320) 
 
 
 halam agu balasyaiko’naḍvān harasya na lāṅgalaṃ 
 padaparimitā bhūmir viṣṇor na gaur na ca lāṅgalam | 
 prabhavati kṛṣir naivādyāpi dvitīyagavaṃ vinā 
 jagati sakale nedṛg dṛṣṭaṃ daridrakuṭumbakam  ||2228|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 madgehe muṣalīva mūṣakavadhūr mūṣīva mārjārikā 
 mārjārīva śunī śunīva gṛhiṇī vācyaḥ kim anyo janaḥ | 
 kiṃ ca kṣutklamaghūrṇamānanayanair unnidram urvīṃ gataiḥ 
 kartuṃ vāgvyayam akṣamaiḥ svajananī bālaiḥ samālokyate  ||2229|| 
 
 
 durgatasya | (Sv 3197, kasyāpi)  
 
 
 jaradambarasaṃvaraṇagranthavidhau granthakāra eko’ham | 
 parimitakadannabaṇṭanavidyāpāraṃgatā gṛhiṇī  ||2230|| 
 
 
 bhānoḥ | (su.ra. 1313, vīrasya) 
 
 
 47. sacaṭudāridryam 
 
 
 ambā tuṣyati na mayā na snuṣayā sāpi nāmbayā na mayā | 
 aham api na tayā na tayā vada rājan kasya doṣo’yam  ||2231|| 
 
 
 
 kasyacit | (sa.ka.ā. 4.194, Sv 3185, śā.pa. 411) 
 
 
 ā janmanaḥ sahajatulyavivartamāna 
 daurgatyato’sti paramo na suhṛnmamānyaḥ | 
 yenātmano’parigaṇayya vināśam āśu  
 deva tvadāśrayaṇapuṇyadhanaḥ kṛto’smi  ||2232|| 
 
 
 
 daṅkasya | 
 
 
 durgatir ekā vanitā  
 mamāpi pitur iyaṃ pitāmahasyāpi | 
 tat kuru nātha yathāyaṃ  
 janaparivādaḥ praśāntim abhyeti  ||2233|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 dāridryagṛdhraparibhuktasamastamāṃsaṃ 
 snāyūparuddhasakalāsthicayāvaśeṣam | 
 pīyūṣavṛṣṭim iva nātha nidhehi dṛṣṭiṃ 
 kaṅkālajālam idam aṅkuram ātanoti  ||2234|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 dāridryaṃ nṛpatiḥ sa no nijapatir yasya prasādād abhūd 
 yācñā jīvitam aṃśukaṃ daśa diśaḥ sadmāni devālayāḥ | 
 madvidveṣiṇi labdhasaṃnidhir iti tvayy āśraye kupyatā 
 madvṛttyaiva puraskṛtās tvadarayas tenādhunā kā gatiḥ  ||2235|| 
 
 
 vittapālasya | 
 
 
 48. daridragṛhī  
 
 
 śīlaṃ śātayati śrutaṃ śamayati prajñāṃ nihanty ādarād 
 dainyaṃ dīpayati kṣamāṃ kṣapayati vrīḍām api vyasyati | 
 ceto jarjarayaty apāsyati dhṛtiṃ visātarayaty arthitāṃ 
 puṃsaḥ kṣīṇadhanasya kiṃ na kurute vairī kuṭumbagrahaḥ  ||2236|| 
 
 
 dāmodarasya | 
 
 
 uttiṣṭha kṣaṇam ekam udvaha sakhe dāridryabhāraṃ guruṃ 
 śrāntas tāvad ahaṃ cirān maraṇajaṃ seve tvadīyaṃ sukham | 
 ity ukto dhanavarjitena viduṣā gatvā śmaśānaṃ śavo 
 dāridryān maraṇaṃ varaṃ sukham iti jñātvā sa tūṣṇīṃ sthitaḥ  ||2237|| 
 
 
 
 vasukalpasya | (Sv 3195) 
 
 
 kṣutkṣāmāḥ śiśavaḥ śavā iva tanur mandādaro bāndhavo 
 liptā jarjarakarkarījalalavair no māṃ tathā bādhate | 
 gehinyāḥ sphuṭitāṃśukaṃ ghaṭayituṃ kṛtvā sakākusmitaṃ 
 kupyantī prativeśinī pratimuhuḥ sūcīṃ yathā yācitā  ||2238|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 1307) 
 
 
 tasminn eva gṛhodare rasavatī tatraiva sā kaṇḍanī 
 tatropaskaraṇāni tatra śiśavas tatraiva vāsaḥ svayam | 
 sarvaṃ soḍhavato’pi duḥsthagṛhiṇaḥ kiṃ brūmahe tāṃ daśām  
 adya śvo vijaniṣyamāṇagṛhiṇī tatraiva yat kunthati  ||2239|| 
 
 
 vainateyasya | (su.ra. 1310) 
 
 
 āstāṃ kiṃ bahubhiḥ paropakṛtayaḥ saṃsārasāraṃ phalaṃ 
 siddhaṃ tat pratikūlavartini vidhau na stokam apy atra naḥ | 
 ete smaḥ kila mānuṣā vayam api vyarthaṃ vyapetāyuṣo 
 yeṣāṃ svodarapūrtir eva hi kim apy aṣṭau mahāsiddhayaḥ  ||2240|| 
 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 49. tadgṛhiṇī  
 
 
 adyāśanaṃ śiśujanasya balena jātaṃ  
 śvo vā kathaṃ nu bhaviteti vicintayantī | 
 ity aśrupātamalinīkṛtagaṇḍadeśā  
 necched daridragṛhiṇī rajanīvirāmam  ||2241|| 
 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 1311) 
 
 
 yāvad duḥkhakuṭumbinīkaratalasparśāt samālokate 
 tattatkṣudrakaṇādirakṣaṇadhiyā ghoraṃ ghane varṣati | 
 tāvaj jīrṇakuṭīrakoṭaraviśatsaudāminīdīpitaṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā tūlakajālam ābilajalākīrṇaṃ muhur mūrcchati  ||2242|| 
 
 
 yogeśvarasya | 
 
 
 kumbhīsaṃcitataṇḍulāḥ pratidinaṃ nītāḥ kṣayaṃ mūṣikair 
 vāstuṣv eva piśaṅgitodaratalāḥ śīryanti vārtākavaḥ | 
 jīrṇaṃ jālakamāranālapiṭharīgarbhe ca kākāravaṃ 
 dīnāyāḥ pathikastriyāḥ priyatamapratyāgamākāṅkṣayā  ||2243|| 
 
 
 nīlasya | 
 
 
 vairāgyaikasamunnatā tanutanuḥ śīrṇāmbaraṃ bibhratī 
 kṣutkṣāmekṣaṇakukṣibhiś ca śiśubhir bhoktuṃ samabhyarthitā | 
 dīnā duḥsthakuṭumbinī pravigaladbāṣpāmbudhautānanāpy 
 ekaṃ taṇḍulamānakaṃ dinaśataṃ netuṃ samākāṅkṣati  ||2244|| 
 
 
 vīrasya | 
 
 
 saktūñ śocati saṃplutān pratikaroty ākrandato bālakān 
 pratyutsiñcati karpareṇa salilaṃ śayyātṛṇaṃ rakṣati | 
 dattvā mūrdhni viśīrṇaśūrpaśakalaṃ jīrṇe gṛhe vyākulā 
 kiṃ tad yan na karoti duḥsthagṛhiṇī deve bhṛśaṃ varṣati  ||2245|| 
 
 
 laṅgadattasya | (su.ra. 1312, yogeśvarasya; Sv 3201) 
 
 
 50. tadgṛhaṃ  
 
 
 calatkāṣṭhaṃ galatkuḍyam uttānatṛṇasaṃcayam | 
 gaṇḍūpadārthimaṇḍūkakīrṇaṃ jīrṇaṃ gṛhaṃ mama  ||2246|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 hastaprāpyatṛṇojjhitāḥ pratipayovṛttiskhaladbhittayo 
 dūrālambitadārudanturamukhāḥ paryantavallīvṛttāḥ | 
 vastrābhāvavilīnasatrapavadhūrdattārgalā nirgiras 
 tyajante ciraśūnyavibhramabhṛto bhikṣācarair mṛdgṛhāḥ  ||2247|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 pṛthukārtasvarapātraṃ bhūṣitaniḥśeṣaparijanaṃ nātha | 
 vilasatkareṇugahanaṃ saṃprati samam āvayoḥ sadanam  ||2248|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 1644, Sāh.D. 7.20, 10.13) 
 
 
 dhūmena riktam api nirbharabāṣpakāri 
 dūrīkṛtānalam api pratipannatāpam | 
 dainyātiśūnyam api bhūṣitabandhuvargam  
 āścaryam eva khalu khedakaraṃ gṛhaṃ naḥ  ||2249|| 
 
 
 jalacandrasya | 
 
 
 utsannacchadir ucchvasadvṛti galadbhitti skhalanmaṇḍali 
 bhrāmyatkuṇḍali hiṇḍadākhu khuraliprakrīḍibhekāvali | 
 pañcaccarmacaṭaughapakṣatipuṭaprārabdhabhāṃbhāṃkṛti 
 śrīmatsenakulāvataṃsa bhavataḥ śatror ivāsmadgṛham  ||2250|| 
 
 
 
 sohnokasya | 
 
 
 51. jarā 
 
 
 ekagarbhoṣitāḥ snigdhā mūrdhnā satkṛtya dhāritāḥ | 
 keśā api virajyante jarayā kim utāṅganāḥ  ||2251|| 
 
 
 
 śrīvyāsapādānām | (su.ra. 1525) 
 
 
 keśāḥ pākam upāgatâḥ śithilatām aṅge’py anaṅgo gataḥ  
 sarvāṅgaṃ baliveṣṭitaṃ priyatamā sabhyaṃ janatvaṃ gatā | 
 ye vānye guṇaśālino’pi suhṛdas te cāpi yātā divaṃ 
 tan māṃ muñca ghanāgamaṃ vraja vanaṃ cetaḥ kutaḥ sthīyate || 
 
 
 taraṇikasya | 
 
 
 keśāḥ kāśanibhāḥ kapālaphalake tvagbhis taraṅgāyitaṃ 
 kācenocitatārakeṇa khacite paryaśruṇī locane | 
 aṅgānām avasāditāpi ca girāṃ kampas tathāpy eṣa me 
 mohaḥ snehamayo na muñcati manaḥ kasmai samāvedyatām  ||2253|| 
 
 
 suvratasya | 
 
 
 śauryābhimānavanadāvaśikhe subaddha 
 prasthānavṛttimativibhramamūlabandho | 
 mṛtyoḥ puraḥsarabaladhvajavaijayanti 
 mātar jare satatam astu nama bhavatyai  ||2254|| 
 
 
 dharmapālasya | 
 
 
 digvibhramaṃ daśanakhaṇḍanam aṅgabhaṅgaṃ 
 keśagrahaṃ ratividhau madanādaraṃ ca | 
 śvāsaprakampajaḍabhāvasughūrṇitāni  
 dhatte jarā praṇayinīva mayopagūḍhā  ||2255|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 52. vṛddhaḥ 
 
 
 svasti sukhebhyaḥ saṃprati salilāñjalir eṣa manmathakathāyāḥ | 
 tā api mām ativayasaṃ taraladṛśaḥ saralam īkṣante  ||2256|| 
 
 
 śatānandasya | (Sv 3395, su.ra. 1522) 
 
 
 ākrāntaṃ valibhiḥ prasahya palitair atyantam āskanditaṃ  
 vārdhakyaṃ ślathasaṃdhibandhanatayā niḥsthāma nirdhāma ca | 
 etan me vapur asthikevalajaratkaṅkālam ālokaya  
 sthūlaśirākarālaparuṣatvaṅmātrapātrīkṛtam  ||2257|| 
 
 
 
 daṅkasya | 
 
 
 galitaṃ yauvanam adhunā vanamadhunā sevanīyam asmākam | 
 sphuraduruhāramaṇīnāṃ hāramaṇīnāṃ gataḥ kālaḥ  ||2258|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 sthūlaprāvaraṇo’tivṛttakathanaḥ kāsāśrulālāvilo 
 bhugnāṅghritrikapṛṣṭhajānujaghano mugdho’tithīn vārayan | 
 śṛṇvan dhṛṣṭavadhūvacāṃsi dhanuṣā saṃtrāsayan vāyasān 
 āśāpāśanibaddhajīvavihago vṛddho gṛhe glāyati  ||2259|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (Ss 2.29) 
 
 
 vikāsayati locane spṛśati pāṇinā kuñcite 
 vidūram avalokayaty atisamīpasaṃsthaṃ punaḥ | 
 bahir vrajati sātape smarati netravṛtteḥ purā  
 jarāpramukhasaṃsthitaḥ samavalokayan pustakam  ||2260|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 1179) 
 
 
 53. anuśayaḥ 
 
 
 kṣāntaṃ na kṣamayā gṛhocitasukhaṃ tyaktaṃ na saṃtoṣataḥ 
 soḍhā duḥsahaśītavātatapanakleśā na taptaṃ tapaḥ | 
 dhyātaṃ vittam aharniśaṃ na ca punar viṣṇoḥ padaṃ śāśvataṃ 
 tat tat karma kṛtaṃ yad eva munibhis tais taiḥ phalair vañcitam  ||2261|| 
 
 
 bhartṛhareḥ | (Ss 1.9: Sv 3178, śā.pa. 4153, su.ra. 1632) 
 
 
 nāthe śrīpuruṣottame trijagatām ekādhipe cetasā 
 sevye svasya padasya dātari sure nārāyaṇe tiṣṭhati | 
 yaṃ kaṃcit puruṣādhamaṃ katipayagrāmeśam alpārthadaṃ 
 sevāyai mṛgayāmahe naram aho mūḍhā varākā vayam  ||2262|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (Ss 1.11) 
 
 
 uṣasy eva bhrāntaṃ hatajaṭharahetos tata itaḥ 
 svayaṃ ca svaṃ bibhrad vicarati kuṭumbaṃ diśi diśi | 
 batāsmābhiḥ kākair iva kavalamātraikamuditair  
 na cāyurdurgatyor avadhir iha labdhaḥ katham api  ||2263|| 
 
 
 veśokasya | 
 
 
 kauśalyā nanu rodhanā janakabhūr dūrīkṛtā kiṃ tu na 
 prāptā pañcavaṭī na vānarapater āsāditaṃ sauhṛdam | 
 sāmarṣeṇa na vārirāśir acirād ullaṅghitaḥ kevalaṃ 
 kākutsthena mayā daśānanatiraskārāspadībhūyate  ||2264|| 
 
 
 hareḥ | 
 
 
 janasthāne bhrāntaṃ kanakamṛgatṛṣṇāndhitadhiyā 
 vaco vaidehīti pratipadam udaśru pralapitam | 
 kṛtā laṅkābhartur vadanaparipāṭīṣu ghaṭanā 
 mayāptaṃ rāmatvaṃ kuśalavasutā na tv adhigatā  ||2265|| 
 
 
 śūlapāṇeḥ | (Sv 3264, sā.da. under 4.17, sū.mu. 127.5, su.ra. 1472) 
 
 
 54. nirvedaḥ 
 
 
 pitror nopakṛtaṃ himāṃśudhavalaṃ nopārjitaṃ vā yaśo 
 mitrāṇām upakāritā na vihitā dattaṃ na ca svecchayā | 
 gāḍhāliṅganalālasāpi dayitā nāliṅgitā kevalaṃ 
 kālo’bhyeti calaṃ ca jīvitam iti kṣuṇṇaṃ manaś cintayā  ||2266|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 no khaḍgapravidāritā karighaṭā nodvejitā vairiṇas 
 tanvaṅgyā vipule nitambaphalake na krīḍitaṃ līlayā | 
 no juṣṭaṃ girirājanirjharacalajjhaṅkāri gāṅgaṃ payaḥ 
 kālo’yaṃ paripiṇḍalolupatayā kākair iva preritaḥ  ||2267|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 na prāptā bhuvi vārivṛndadamanī vidyā vinodocitā  
 khaḍgāgraiḥ karikumbhapīṭhadalanair naivānunītaṃ yaśaḥ | 
 kāntākomalapallavādhararasaḥ pīto na candrodaye  
 tāruṇyaṃ gatam eva niṣphalam aho śūnyālaye dīpavat  ||2268|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (sū.mu. 3400) 
 
 
 no meghāyitam arthavārivirahakliṣṭe’rthiśasye mayā 
 noddhṛttapratipakṣaparvatakule nirghātavātāyitam | 
 no vā vāmavilocanāmalamukhāmbhojeṣu bhṛṅgāyitaṃ 
 mātuḥ kevalam eva yauvanavanacchede kuṭhārāyitam  ||2269|| 
 
 
 bhartṛhareḥ | (su.ra. 1498) 
 
 
 nākrāntāmbudhimekhalā vasumatī lakṣmīḥ samāveśitā 
 no vidvadbhavaneṣu pakṣmaladṛśāṃ nāśrāvi sūktāmṛtam | 
 janma vyarthaphalodayaṃ bata paraṃ gṛhṇadbhir asmādṛśair 
 vyāptaṃ vyoma kiyadbhujaṅgamapater bhāraḥ kiyān arpitaḥ  ||2270|| 
 
 
 sāñcādharasya | 
 
 
 55. vicāraḥ 
 
 
 dadāti tāvad amī viṣayāḥ sukhaṃ 
 sphurati yāvad iyaṃ hṛdi vāsanā | 
 manasi tattvavidāṃ ca vivecake 
 kva viṣayāḥ kva sukhaṃ kva parigrahaḥ  ||2271|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 1607) 
 
 
 āyur vāsaramāsavatsaragaṇe gacchaty adūraṃ pathair  
 ākrāmanti kṛtāntakāsarakhurakṣuṇṇā rajorājayaḥ | 
 īṣallaṅghitaśaiśavā iti vayaḥsaṃdhiṃ dadhānā iti 
 vyaktā varjitayauvanā iti tathā nandanti tandrālavaḥ  ||2272|| 
 
 
 
 jalacandrasya | 
 
 
 tan mitraṃ yad ayantraṇaṃ sa vibhavo yaḥ sādhusādhāraṇas 
 tasyāṃ yoṣiti bhāvayed abhiratiṃ bhāvānuraktaiva yā | 
 tāṃ cintāṃ manasodvaheta satataṃ yasyāḥ phalaṃ bhujyate 
 tānīheta phalāni yāny avidhurāṇy āśā mahījanmanaḥ  ||2273|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 tat pāṇḍityaṃ na patati punar yena saṃsārabandhe 
 tat sauhārdaṃ na calati punar yat sukhe vāsukhe vā | 
 sambhogās te ratiṣu viduṣāṃ ye na vācyāḥ pareṣāṃ 
 tac caiśvaryaṃ jagati mahatāṃ yat pareṣāṃ sukhāya  ||2274|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 sadvidyā yadi kalpaśākhibhir alaṃ yady arthinaḥ kiṃ tṛṇaiḥ 
 santaś ced amṛtena kiṃ yadi khalās tatkālakūṭena kim | 
 kiṃ karpūraśalākayā yadi dṛśaḥ panthānam eti priyā 
 saṃsāre’pi satīndrajālaghaṭanaṃ yady asti tenāpi kim  ||2275|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (sa.ka.ā. 4.71) 
 
 
 56. vicikitsititam 
 
 
 bībhatsā viṣayā jugupsitatamaḥ kāyo vayo gatvaraṃ 
 prāyo bandhubhir adhvanīva pathikair yogo viyogāvahaḥ | 
 hātavyo’yam asāra eva virasaḥ saṃsāra ity ādikaṃ 
 sarvasyaiva hi vāci cetasi punaḥ kasyāpi puṇyātmanaḥ  ||2276|| 
 
 
 silhaṇasya | (Ss 1.20, su.ra. 1610) 
 
 
 taḍinmālāloklaṃ prativiratidattāndhatamasaṃ 
 bhave saukhyaṃ hitvā śamasukham upādeyam anagham | 
 iti vyaktodgāraṃ caṭulavacasaḥ śūnyamanaso 
 vayaṃ vītavrīḍāḥ śuka iva paṭhāmaḥ param amī  ||2277|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (Ss 1.21, su.ra. 1614) 
 retaḥśoṇitayor iyaṃ pariṇatir yad varṣma tac cābhavan 
 mṛtyor āspadam āśrayo guruśucāṃ rogasya viśrāmabhūḥ | 
 jānann apy avaśo vivekavirahān majjann avidyāmbudhau 
 śṛṅgārīyati putrakāmyati bata kṣetrīyati strīyati  ||2278|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (Ss 1.26, su.ra. 1634) 
 
 
 bībhatsāḥ pratibhānti kiṃ nu viṣayāḥ kiṃ nu spṛhāyuṣmatī 
 dehasyāpacayo matau niviśate gāḍho gṛheṣu grahaḥ | 
 brahmopāsyam iti sphuraty api hṛdi vyāvartikā vāsanā  
 kā nāmeyam atarkyahetugahanā daivī satāṃ yātanā  ||2279|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (Ss 1.7) 
 
 
 sthirāpāyaḥ kāyaḥ praṇayiṣu sukhaṃ sthairyavimukhaṃ 
 mahārogo bhogaḥ kuvalayadṛśaḥ śaṣpasadṛśaḥ | 
 gṛhāveśaḥ kleśaḥ prakṛticapalā śrīr api khalā  
 yamaḥ svairī vairī tad api na hitaṃ karma vihitam  ||2280|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (sa.ka.ā. 2.209, Ss 2.12) 
 
 
 57. śamavighnaḥ  
 
 
 premṇā purā praṇihitaṃ mayi cakṣur īṣad 
 ullāsitārdhakucayā mitamadhyayā yat | 
 sampraty atistimitavaktram ivāṅgalagnam 
 etaj jihāsur api hātum anīśvareṇa  ||2281|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 1631) 
 
 
 bhikṣāśanaṃ bhavanam āyatanaikadeśaḥ 
 śayyā mahī parijano nijadehabhāraḥ | 
 vāsaḥ sujīrṇapaṭakhaṇḍanibaddhakanthā 
 hā hā tathāpi viṣayān na jahāti cetaḥ  ||2282|| 
 
 
 silhaṇasya | (su.ra. 1633) 
 
 
 madhuram aśanaṃ sūkṣmaṃ vāso vibhūṣaṇam ujjvalaṃ 
 taruṇataravaḥ krīḍārāmāḥ sudhāśucayo gṛhāḥ | 
 tad idam akhilaṃ tyaktuṃ śakyaṃ bhavaty api dehināṃ 
 praṇayasarasā ye’mī dārās ta eva hi dustyajāḥ  ||2283|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 gaṅgādhautaśilātale phalabharacchinnārdhakūladrume 
 siddhādhyāsitakandare himavati sthāne sthite śreyasi | 
 kaḥ kurvīta śiraḥ praṇāmamalinaṃ mānyaṃ manasvī jano 
 yad vitrastakuraṅgaśāvanayanā na syuḥ smarāstraṃ striyaḥ  ||2284|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (Sv. 2244) 
 
 
 saṃsāre’sminn asāre kunṛpatibhavanadvārasevākalaṅka 
 vyāsaṅgavyastadhairyaṃ katham amaladhiyo mānasaṃ saṃvidadhyuḥ | 
 yady etāḥ prodyadindudyutinicayabhṛto na syur ambhojanetrāḥ  
 preṅkhatkāñcīkalāpāḥ stanabharavinamanmadhyabhājas taruṇyaḥ  ||2285|| 
 
 
 kasyacit (ÇṛÇ 31 (97); Sv. 2245) 
 
 
 58. ardhaśamaḥ  
 
 
 ekaṃ sāgaratīranīranikarasphārāñjalikṣālitaiḥ 
 puṣpair acyutapūjanaṃ nijakaravyāpārasaṃpāditaiḥ | 
 no cen mañjulamālatīdalalasatkhaṭvārcite mandire 
 kāntātuṅganitambabimbasuratakrīḍārasaiḥ sthīyate  ||2286|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 praśānte dhīrāṇāṃ manasi paramabrahmarasike 
 rajo vā rājyaṃ vā dvayam idam abhedaṃ sukṛtinām | 
 dhig asmākaṃ citte vigalitaviveke punar iha 
 priyā vā prāṇā vā sadṛśam athavā pūrvam adhikam  ||2287|| 
 
 
 purokasya | 
 
 
 dhanyānāṃ girikandarodarabhuvi jyotiḥ paraṃ dhyāyatām 
 ānandāśrujalaṃ pibanti śakunā niḥśaṅkam aṅkasthitāḥ | 
 asmākaṃ tu manorathoparacitaprāsādavāpītaṭa 
 krīḍākānanakelimandirajuṣāṃ cetaḥ paraṃ sīdati  ||2288|| 
 
 
 satyabodhasya | (VaiS 196, Ss 1.5, śā.pa. 4155, sū.mu. 126.9, su.ra.
                            1461) 
 
 
 sadyaḥ kāśmīramṛṣṭastanakalasaluṭhattārahārāvalībhiḥ 
 karpūrodgāriṇībhiḥ samam asamasukhāḥ kelayaḥ keralībhiḥ | 
 no ced bhikṣāprasanne manasi manasijakleśanāśe vilāso 
 vārāṇasyāṃ nivāsaḥ smaraharacaraṇopāsanāvāsanābhiḥ  ||2289|| 
 
 
 vāsudevasya | 
 
 
 agre gītaṃ sarasakavayaḥ pārśvato dākṣiṇātyāḥ  
 pṛṣṭhe līlāvalayaraṇitaṃ cāmaragrāhiṇīnām | 
 yady asty evaṃ kuru bhavarasāsvādane lampaṭatvaṃ  
 no cec cetaḥ praviśa sahasā nirvikalpe samādhau  ||2290|| 
 
 
 
 utpalarājasya | (su.ra. 1605, Sv 3467, śā.pa. 4167, VaiS 183) 
 
 
 59. kāruṇikaḥ  
 
 
 niṣkaṃcanatvād vidhurasya sādhor 
 abhyarthitasyārthijanasya kiṃcit | 
 nāstīti varṇā manasi bhramanto 
 nirgantum icchanty asubhiḥ sahaiva  ||2291|| 
 
 
 maṅgalasya | 
 
 
 tāṃ sampado vipada eva na yāḥ samagram 
 uttārayanti jagad āvilam ārtipaṅkāt | 
 tallauham eva hṛdayaṃ yad aśaktam ārte 
 svīyārtibhāvayati na sphuṭitena śuddhim  ||2292|| 
 
 
 mālokasya | 
 
 
 ete vayaṃ tanudhanāḥ kṛpaṇeyam urvī 
 dīnāḥ śataṃ mṛdu ca vistarayanti vācaḥ | 
 tad bhrātaraḥ śakunipheravasārameyā 
 ḍhaukadhvam etad ahaha sphuṭatu kṣaṇena  ||2293|| 
 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 yatra prāṇabalena yatra piśitair yatra tvacā kevalaṃ 
 yātrām arthijanocitām upagataḥ ślāghyaḥ sa kālo gataḥ | 
 kurmaḥ kiṃ dhanam anyad asti na kim apy asmākam asmāt paraṃ 
 vādhiryaṃ kṛtam atra karṇakuhare dūre’stu vāgarthinaḥ  ||2294|| 
 
 
 paraśurāmasya | 
 
 
 mudā yatra prāṇās tṛṇam iva parārthavyasaninas 
 tyajanto lajjante kiyad iti dhiyā tad yugam agān | 
 tṛṇaṃ prāṇaprāyaṃ tyajati na jano yatra samaye 
 vayaṃ jātās tatrety ahaha kṛpaṇaṃ jīvitam idam  ||2295|| 
 
 
 devabodhasya | 
 
 
 60. śāntyāśaṃsā  
 
 
 kadā bhikṣābhakṣyaiḥ karagalitagaṅgāmbutaralaiḥ 
 śarīraṃ me sthāsyaty uparatasamastendriyasukham | 
 kadā brahmābhyāsasthiratanutayāraṇyavihagāḥ 
 patiṣyanti sthāṇubhramahatadhiyaḥ skandhaśirasi  ||2296|| 
 
 
 
 bhartṛhareḥ | (Ss 4.18) 
 
 
 gaṅgātīre himagiriśilābaddhapadmāsanasya  
 brahmadhyānābhyasanavidhinā yoganidrāṃ gatasya | 
 kiṃ tair bhāvyaṃ mama sudivasair yatra te nirviśaṅkāḥ 
 saṃprāpsyante jaraṭhahariṇā gātrakaṇḍūvinodam  ||2297|| 
 
 
 kṛṣṇasya | (Ss 4.17) 
 
 
 rathyātaścaratas tathā dhṛtajaratkanthālavasyādhvagaiḥ 
 satrāsaṃ ca sakautukaṃ ca sakṛpaṃ dṛṣṭasya tair nāgaraiḥ | 
 nirvyājīkṛtacitsudhārasamudā nidrāyamāṇasya me 
 niḥśaṅkaṃ karaṭaḥ kadā karapuṭībhikṣāṃ viluṇṭhiṣyati  ||2298|| 
 
 
 vallaṇasya | (Ss 4.19, sā.da. under 3.228) 
 
 
 kadā vārāṇasyām amarataṭinīrodhasi vasan 
 vasānaḥ kaupīnaṃ śirasi nidadhāno’ñjalipuṭam | 
 aye gaurīnātha tripurahara śambho trinayana 
 prasīdeti krośan nimiṣam iva neṣyāmi divasān  ||2299|| 
 
 
 
 viśveśvarasya | (Kuval. 183) 
 
 
 ahau vā hāre vā balavati ripau vā suhṛdi vā  
 maṇau vā loṣṭe vā kusumaśayane vā dṛṣadi vā | 
 tṛṇe vā straiṇe vā mama samadṛśo yāntu divasāḥ  
 kvacit puṇye’raṇye śiva śiva śiveti pralapataḥ  ||2300|| 
 
 
 
 muñjasya | (Sv 3413, śā.pa. 4102) 
 
 
 61. kṛtārthaśāntaḥ 
 
 
 kāntāyāḥ karajaiḥ kapolaphalake patrāvalī kalpitā 
 kelidyūtapaṇīkṛto viharatā pītaḥ sa bimbādharaḥ | 
 svedārdrīkṛtacandanastanataṭī sānandam āliṅgitā 
 nirviṣṭā viṣayāḥ śivātmamahasi nyastaṃ manaḥ saṃprati  ||2301|| 
 
 
 
 muñjasya | 
 
 
 yal līlākamalāhatau pramuditaṃ yan manmathasyāspadaṃ 
 yat kāntāpraṇayāparādhakalahe paryāptakautūhalam | 
 yat premārdavadhūvilāsatulitabhrūlāsyabaddhaspṛhaṃ 
 tac cetaḥ smaravairibhagnasadanaprānte sthitīr vāñchati  ||2302|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 jiteyaṃ dordarpāj jaladhipariveśā vasumatī 
 śiraḥ kṣauṇīndrāṇāṃ nijacaraṇapīṭhe viluṭhitam | 
 kṛtaṃ dattaṃ bhuktaṃ kṛtam api kule yat samucitaṃ 
 kṛtārthaṃ tīrtheṣu bhramaṇam adhunā vāñchati manaḥ  ||2303|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 abhyastāḥ sphuṭam eva śāstragatayaḥ samyakkavitvodadheḥ  
 pāraṃ cādhigataṃ satāṃ pariṣadi prāptaḥ pratiṣṭhodayaḥ | 
 nirviṇṇasya mamādhunā nanu paraḥ panthā na dainyaṃ vinā  
 netuṃ vāñchati vāsanā suradhunītīre’nurūpaṃ vayaḥ  ||2304|| 
 
 
 
 vāsudevasya | 
 
 
 kīrtir labdhā sadasi viduṣāṃ śīlitāḥ kṣoṇipālā 
 vāksandarbhāḥ katicid amṛtasyandino nirmitāś ca | 
 tīre sampraty amarasaritaḥ kvāpi śailopakaṇṭhe 
 brahmābhyāsapravaṇamanasā netum īhe dināni  ||2305|| 
 
 
 dhoyīkasya | (Pavanadūta 104) 
 
 
 62. śāntaḥ  
 
 
 sūktiṃ karṇasudhāṃ vyanaktu sujanas tasmai na modāmahe 
 brūtāṃ vācam asūyako viṣamucaṃ tasmai na khidyāmahe | 
 yā yasya prakṛtiḥ sa tāṃ vitanutāṃ kiṃ nas tayā cintayā  
 kurmas tat khalu karma janmanigaḍacchedāya yaj jāyate  ||2306|| 
 
 
 bhartṛhareḥ | (Ss 1.22) 
 
 
 yadāsau durvāraḥ prasarati madaś cittakariṇas 
 tadā tasyoddāmaprasararasarūḍhair vyavasitaiḥ | 
 kva taddhairyālānaṃ kva ca nijakulācāranigaḍaḥ 
 kva sā lajjārajjuḥ kva vinayakaṭhorāṅkuśam api  ||2307|| 
 
 
 bhartṛhareḥ | (Ss 1.22) 
 
 
 sajjanmāpi hi niṣphalaṃ śrutam api vyarthaṃ guṇāḥ kiṃ kṛte 
 hā dhik kaṣṭam anarthakaṃ gatam idaṃ niḥśeṣam asmadvayaḥ | 
 mārgaḥ ko’pi niratyayaṃ na vahati vyāghātabaddhagraho 
 dharmārthādicatuṣpathe nivasati krūro vidhir gaulmikaḥ  ||2308|| 
 
 
 mahāvratasya | 
 
 
 mahāśayyā bhūmir masṛṇam upadhānaṃ bhujalatā 
 vitānaṃ cākāśaṃ vyajanam anukūlo’yam anilaḥ | 
 sphuraddīpaś candraḥ surabhivanitāsaṅgamuditaḥ 
 sukhaṃ śāntaḥ śete nanu ca bhavabhīto nṛpa iva  ||2309|| 
 
 
 bhavabhītasya | (Ss 4.8) 
 
 
 avaśyaṃ yātāraś cirataram uṣitvāpi viṣayā  
 viyoge ko bhedas tyajati na jano yat svam amūn | 
 vrajantaḥ svātantryād atulaparitāpāya manasaḥ  
 svayaṃ tyaktā hy ete śamasukham anantaṃ vidadhati  ||2310|| 
 
 
 
 hareḥ | (Ss 3.3, Sv 3386, su.ra. 1617, VaiS 157) 
 
 
 63. niṣkramaḥ 
 
 
 pūrvaṃ tāvat kuvalayadṛśāṃ lolalolair apāṅgair 
 ākarṣadbhiḥ kim api hṛdayaṃ pūjitā yauvanaśrīḥ | 
 saṃpratyantarnihitasadasadbhāvalabdhaprabodha 
 pratyāhārāpahṛtahṛdayo vartate ko’pi bhāvaḥ  ||2311|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (Ss 4.16) 
 
 
 iyaṃ bālā māṃ praty anavaratam indīvaradala 
 prabhācauraṃ cakṣuḥ kṣipati kim abhipretam anayā | 
 gato moho’smākaṃ smarasamarabāṇavyatikara 
 jvarajvālā śāntā tad api na varākī viramati  ||2312|| 
 
 
 
 jñānaśivasya | (su.ra. 1620) 
 
 
 yad āsīd ajñānaṃ smaratimirasaṃskārajanitaṃ 
 tadā dṛṣṭaṃ nārīmayam idam aśeṣaṃ jagad api | 
 idānīm asmākaṃ paṭutaravivekāñjanajuṣāṃ 
 samībhūtā dṛṣṭis tribhuvanam api brahma manute  ||2313|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (Ss 4.14, sa.ka.ā. 5.115; su.ra. 1611) 
 
 
 kim asmān vāmākṣi smaravijayayātrābhyudayikair 
 vṛthā śāntān lājjair iva hasitaleśaiḥ snapayasi | 
 idānīṃ golomnā śucini tanukālāvujaṭhare 
 patadbhaikṣyāhāre valati hi paraṃ lāñchini manaḥ  ||2314|| 
 
 
 jalokasya | 
 
 
 gataḥ kālo yatra praṇayini mayi premakuṭilaḥ 
 kaṭākṣaḥ kālindīlaghulaharivṛttiḥ prabhavati |
