 idānīm asmākaṃ jaraṭhakamaṭhīpṛṣṭhakaṭhinā 
 monovṛttis tat kiṃ vyasanini mudhaiva kṣapayasi  ||2315|| 
 
 
 vallaṇasya | (Ss 4.13, sū.mu. 131.33, su.ra. 1599) 
 
 
 64. niḥspṛhaḥ 
 
 
 vāso valkalamāstaraḥ kisalayānyokas tarūṇāṃ talaṃ 
 mūlāni kṣataye kṣudhāṃ girinadītoyaṃ tṛṣāśāntaye | 
 krīḍā mugdhamṛgair vayāṃsi suhṛdo naktaṃ pradīpaḥ śaśī 
 svādhīne’pi dhane tathāpi kṛpaṇā yācanta ity adbhutam  ||2316|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 1598, Ss 2.20) 
 
 
 nītāḥ puṇyāgnigehe śiśirarajanayaḥ stomasatre nidāghaṃ 
 śīrṇe kugrāmadevīparisarasadane vāsarāḥ prāvṛṣeṇyāḥ | 
 dṛṣṭaṃ vyābhugnabhīmabhrukuṭi ca vadanaṃ sampadā garvitānāṃ 
 tattvaṃ tṛṣṇe kṛtārthībhava kuru viratiṃ muñca naḥ sādhu yāmaḥ  ||2317|| 
 
 
 yogeśvarasya | 
 
 
 nijaṃ karma kṣīṇaṃ sa khalu viparīto hatavidhiḥ 
 sukṛtye vā tattve bhṛśam upagatā yatnanicayāḥ | 
 idānīm asmākaṃ sphuradurujarājarjaram idaṃ 
 vapur jātaṃ tṛṣṇe virama viramety añjaliśatam  ||2318|| 
 
 
 gosokasya | 
 
 
 vayam iha parituṣṭā valkalais tvaṃ ca lakṣmyā 
 sama iha paritoṣo nirviśeṣo viśeṣaḥ | 
 sa tu bhavatu daridro yasya tṛṣṇā viśālā 
 manasi ca parituṣṭe ko’rthavān ko daridraḥ  ||2319|| 
 
 
 kṛṣṇamiśrasya | (Sv 3475, śā.pa. 308, da.rū.. under 4.2, VaiS 177) 
 
 
 mātar lakṣmi bhajasva kaṃcid aparaṃ matkāṅkṣiṇāṃ mā sma bhūr 
 bhogebhyaḥ spṛhayālavas tava vaśāḥ kā niḥspṛhāṇām asi | 
 sadyaḥsyūtapalāśapatrapuṭikāpātre pavitrīkṛtair 
 bhikṣāsaktubhir eva samprati vayaṃ kāśyāṃ samīhāmahe  ||2320|| 
 
 
 lakṣmīdharasya | (Ss 4.11, su.ra. 1612) 
 65. vanagamanotsukaḥ 
 
 
 aye diṣṭyā naṣṭo mama gṛhapiśācīparicayaḥ 
 parāvṛttaṃ mohāt sphurati ca manāg brahmaṇi manaḥ | 
 vikāro’py akṣāṇāṃ galita iva nirbhāti viṣayāt 
 tathāpi kṣetrajñaḥ spṛhayati vanāya pratimuhuḥ  ||2321|| 
 
 
 bhartṛhareḥ | 
 
 
 ramyaṃ harmyatalaṃ vasataye śravyaṃ na gītādi kiṃ 
 kiṃ vā prāṇasamāsam āgamasukhaṃ naivādhikaprītaye | 
 kiṃ tu prāntapatatpataṅgapavanam āloladīpāṅkura 
 cchāyācañcalam ākalayya sakalaṃ santo vanāntaṃ gatāḥ  ||2322|| 
 
 
 vijñātātmanaḥ | (Ss 2.15, Sv 3326, śā.pa. 4114, sū.mu. 131.51) 
 
 
 āstām akaṇṭhakam idaṃ vasudhādhipatyaṃ 
 trailokyarājyam api deva tṛṇāya manye | 
 niḥśaṅkasuptahariṇīkulasaṅkulāsu 
 cetaḥ paraṃ luṭhati śailavanasthalīṣu  ||2323|| 
 
 
 śālavāhasya | (su.ra. 1606, Ss 2.16) 
 
 
 hariṇacaraṇakṣuṇṇopāntāḥ saśādvalanirjharāḥ 
 kusumaśavalair viṣvagvātais taraṅgitapādapāḥ | 
 muditavihagaśreṇīcitradhvanipratināditā 
 manasi na mudaṃ kasyādadhyuḥ śivā vanabhūtayaḥ  ||2324|| 
 
 
 guṇākarabhadrasya | (su.ra. 1595, Ss 2.17) 
 
 
 kuraṅgāḥ kalyāṇaṃ prativiṭapam ārogyam aṭavi 
 sravanti kṣemaṃ te pulinakuśalaṃ bhadram upalāḥ | 
 niśāntād asvantāt katham api ca niṣkāntam adhunā 
 mano’smākaṃ dīrghām abhilaṣati yuṣmatparicitim  ||2325|| 
 
 
 lakṣmīdharasya | (su.ra. 1626, Ss 2.19) 
 66. tapovanam 
 
 
 pratyagragomayaviliptavitardikāni 
 pūrṇāhutiprabalavahniśikhāśatāni | 
 śuśrūṣamāṇamṛgalocanakanyakāni  
 tāny adya tāpasavanāni mano haranti  ||2326|| 
 
 
 narasiṃhasya | 
 
 
 ete nīvāravaprāḥ pṛthukusumasamitpārvataḥ  
 devīyaṃ jahnuputrī sikatilaśayitaḥ śāntaniḥśaṅkaraṅkaḥ | 
 kāntāre darbhadūrvācayaśucini vacaḥ smārtam āvartayanti 
 brahmāṇo durvipākagrahagahanatayā yāminījāgarūkāḥ  ||2327|| 
 
 
 maghoḥ | 
 
 
 etāni kratupṛṣṭhavediviluṭhadviprāṇi vātapramī 
 cchannopāntatarūṇi paśya dadhate puṇyāśramāṇi śriyam | 
 yāny utkṣipya manaḥ parāñcati paraṃ nārāyaṇārādhana 
 śraddhāmoditam ekadaiva dhanikadvāre ca dāreṣu ca  ||2328|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 ete puraḥ surabhikomalahomadhūma 
 lekhānipītanavapallavaśoṇimānaḥ | 
 puṇyāśramāḥ śrutisamohitasāmagīti 
 sākūtaniścalakuraṅgakulāḥ sphuranti  ||2329|| 
 
 
 śrīmallakṣmaṇasenasya | 
 
 
 śārdūlī snehagarbhaṃ mukulitanayanaṃ leḍhi śāvaṃ hariṇyā 
 bandhuprītyā śikhaṇḍī tirayati phaṇinām ātapaṃ kīrṇabarhaḥ | 
 siṃhī rakṣaty apatyaṃ svam iva kalabhakaṃ nirgatāyāṃ kariṇyāṃ 
 maitryā yeṣāṃ nivāse gahanagiridarīśāyinas te jayanti  ||2330|| 
 
 
 candrayoginaḥ | (sū.mu. 109.42) 
 
 
 67. tāpasvī 
 
 
 pāṇiḥ pātraṃ pavitraṃ bhramaṇaparigataṃ bhaikṣyam akṣayyam annaṃ 
 vastraṃ vistīrṇam āśādaśakam apamalaṃ talpam asvalpam urvī | 
 yeṣāṃ niḥsaṅgatāṅgīkaraṇapariṇatisvastisantoṣiṇas te  
 dhanyāḥ saṃnyastadainyavyatikaranikarāḥ karma nirmūlayanti  ||2331|| 
 
 
 nagnācāryasya | (Ss 4.7) 
 
 
 dhig dhik tān kṛminirviśeṣavapuṣaḥ sphūrjanmahāsiddhayo 
 niṣpandīkṛtaśāntayo’pi ca tapaḥkārā gṛheṣv āsane | 
 taṃ vidvāṃsam iha stumaḥ karapuṭībhikṣālpaśāke’pi vā  
 bālāvaktrasarojinīmadhuni vā yasyāviśeṣo rasaḥ  ||2332|| 
 
 
 vallaṇasya | (Ss 4.10, su.ra. 1609) 
 
 
 vārāṃs trīn abhiṣuṇvate vidadhate vanyaiḥ śarīrasthitīr 
 aiṇeyyāṃ tvaci saṃviśanti vasate cāpi tvacaṃ tāravīm | 
 tat paśyanti ca dhāma nābhipatato yac cārmaṇe cakṣuṣī  
 dhanyānāṃ virajas tamā bhagavatī caryeyam āhlādate  ||2333|| 
 
 
 murāreḥ | (Ar 2.29) 
 
 
 valmīkārdhanimagnamūrtir uragatvagbrahmasūtrāntaraḥ 
 kaṇṭhe jīrṇalatāpratānavalayenātyarthasaṃpīḍitaḥ | 
 aṃsavyāpiśakuntanīḍanicitaṃ bibhrajjaṭāmaṇḍalaṃ 
 yatra sthāṇur ivācalo munir asāv abhyarkabimbaṃ sthitaḥ  ||2334|| 
 
 
 kālidāsasya | (Çak 7.11) 
 
 
 prāṇānām anilena vṛttir ucitā satkalpavṛkṣe vane 
 toye kāścana padmareṇukapiśe puṇyābhiṣekakriyā | 
 dhyānaṃ ratnaśilāguhāsu vibudhastrīsannidhau saṃyamo 
 yad vāñchanti taopbhir anyamunayas tasmiṃs tapasyanty amī  ||2335|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (Çak 7.12, sa.ka.ā. 1.106) 
 
 
 68. bahuviṣayaśāntiḥ 
 
 
 naikaṃ janma tavaiva vatsa na paraṃ tulyā ca karmasthitir 
 bhoktavyeṣu sukheṣu hṛṣyasi mudhā duḥkheṣu kiṃ tāmyasi | 
 bhrātaḥ sthairyam upehi nanv iha bhavān saṃsāradīrghādhvagaḥ  
 succhāyās taravaḥ kvacin marubhuvaḥ kvāpi pracaṇḍātapāḥ  ||2336|| 
 
 
 daśarathasya | 
 
 
 nanv ātmany avadhīyatāṃ gṛharasād vairāgyam ādhīyatāṃ 
 cetaḥ samprati damyatāṃ surasarittīre sadā sthīyatām | 
 bhikṣārthaṃ vyavasīyatāṃ samucitaṃ sat karma saṃciyatāṃ 
 kṛṣṇaś cetasi dhīyatāṃ parataraṃ brahmānusandhīyatām  ||2337|| 
 
 
 bhartṛhareḥ | (Ss 3.11) 
 
 
 te tāvat kṛtinaḥ parārthaghaṭakāḥ svārthasya bādhena ye 
 sāmānyās tu parārtham udyamakṛtaḥ svārthāvirodhena ye | 
 te’mī mānuṣarākṣasāḥ parahitaṃ yaiḥ svārthato hanyate 
 ye tu ghnanti nirarthakaṃ parahitaṃ te ke na jānīmahe  ||2338|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | 
 
 
 vivekaḥ kiṃ so’pi svarasavalitā yatra na kṛpā 
 sa kiṃ yogo yasmin bhavati na parānugraharasaḥ | 
 sa kiṃ dharmo yatra sphurati na paradrohaviratiḥ 
 śrutaṃ tat kiṃ sākṣād upaśamapadaṃ yan na nayati  ||2339|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 1629, Ss 2.25) 
 
 
 kṛmikulacittaṃ lālāklinnaṃ vigandhijugupsitaṃ 
 nirupamarasaṃ prītyā khādan narāsthi nirāmiṣam | 
 surapatim api śvā pārśvasthaṃ vilokya na śaṅkate 
 na hi gaṇayati kṣudro jantuḥ parigrahaphalgutām  ||2340|| 
 
 
 śūrasya (nī.śa. 9 (30); su.ra. 1628, Ss 2.9) 
 
 
 69. athādhyātmavit 
 
 
 bhavāraṇyaṃ bhīmaṃ tanugṛham idaṃ chidrabahulaṃ 
 balī kālaś cauro niyatam asitā moharajanī | 
 gṛhītvā jñānāsiṃ viratiphalakaṃ śīlakavacaṃ 
 samādhānaṃ kṛtvā sthirataradṛśo jāgṛta janāḥ  ||2341|| 
 
 
 silhaṇasya | 
 
 
 aye dūrabhrāntaṃ viṣayaviṣamāraṇyavipathe  
 paribhrāntaṃ ceto mama vidhuritaṃ svairamadhunā | 
 nirāvarte nitye sthiraniravadhānabhramamaye  
 vivekaprabhraśyadvikṛtiparamānandajaladhau  ||2342|| 
 
 
 bhavānandasya | 
 
 
 dhyāyann eṣa tam ādidevam amarasrotasvatīrodhasi 
 kvāpi kleśakaṣāyitābhir upariglāno manovṛttibhiḥ | 
 abhyāsopahatāṅgulikramamilannirvedavīṇākala 
 dhvānāvarjitanirjitendriyagatir līnaḥ pare brahmaṇi  ||2343|| 
 
 
 śaṅkaradevasya | 
 
 
 mṛtpiṇḍena bhuvaiva kiṃ tad anu tad bhedena kiṃ meruṇā 
 kiṃ brahmāṇḍajarāyukoṭarakuṭīkīṭaiḥ surākhyair api | 
 trailokye’pi dayālusaukhyalalitāny āścaryam etat punaś  
 cetodvaitasamādhinīradhisudhāpūraplavaṃ gāhate  ||2344|| 
 
 
 ballaṇasya | 
 
 
 nānāpy ekaṃ yad iha daharaṃ puṇḍarīkaṃ yad oka 
 stoke yasyāpy anubhavavidhau na svadante madhūni | 
 yasyonmeṣād dinamaṇiruco’py andhakāraprakārāḥ  
 śaśvat tasmai praṇama hṛdaya brahmaṇe śāśvatāya  ||2345|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 70. bhavitavyatā  
 
 
 sṛjati tāvad aśeṣaguṇākaraṃ 
 puruṣaratnam alaṅkaraṇaṃ bhuvaḥ | 
 tad anu tatkṣaṇabhaṅgi karoti ced 
 ahaha kaṣṭam apaṇḍitatā vidheḥ  ||2346|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (Sv 3126, śā.pa. 4000, sū.mu. 131.39, su.ra. 1473) 
 
 
 adhvaśramāya caraṇau virahāya dārā 
 abhyarthanāya vacanaṃ na vapur jarāyai | 
 etāni me vidadhatas tasya sarvadaiva 
 dhātas trapā na yadi kiṃ na pariśramo’pi  ||2347|| 
 
 
 rājaśekharasya | (su.ra. 1321) 
 
 
 ālambanāya dharaṇī na ca nāgabhūmīḥ 
 svarvāsināṃ ca vasatir bhaved amuṣya | 
 pūrvārjitāśubhavaśīkṛtapauruṣasya 
 kalpadrumo’pi na samīhitam ātanoti  ||2348|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 1097) 
 
 
 guṇavat pakṣaparāṅmukhi svajanakulocchedabaddhanirbandhe | 
 api vīravaṃśavairiṇi bhagavati bhavitavyate jayasi  ||2349|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 vidvattā dhanasaṅgatā cirataraṃ nākāri nākāri cej 
 jyotsnāsundaravigrahaḥ pratidiśaṃ sampūrṇabimbaḥ śaśī | 
 āmṛtyu stanajanmayauvanamado nākāri vāmabhruvāṃ 
 dhik dhātāram akāri yena jagati vyaṅgaḥ sa gaṅgādharaḥ  ||2350|| 
 
 
 kasyacit |  
 71. daivaṃ  
 
 
 karotu nāma nītijño vyavasayam itas tataḥ | 
 phalaṃ punas tad evāsya yad vidher manasi sthitam  ||2351|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (sū.mu. 112.10) 
 
 
 bhugnāśasya karaṇḍapiṇḍitatanor glānendriyasya kṣudhā 
 kṛtvākhur vivaraṃ svayaṃ nipatito naktaṃ mukhe bhoginaḥ | 
 tṛptas tatpiśitena satvaram asau tenaiva yātaḥ pathā 
 susthās tiṣṭhata daivam eva jagataḥ kṣāntau kṣaye cākulam  ||2352|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (Sv 3143, su.ra. 1334, Ns. 26) 
 
 
 vandyo’sau vidhir eva yasya jagato nirmāṇam atyujjvalaṃ 
 pratyākāram apūrvavasturacanāvaicitryam atyadbhutam | 
 kiṃ cātyantam ito vicitram aparaṃ śakrasya yad vajriṇas 
 trailokyodaravartikarmaphalayor dṛggocare kuñjikā  ||2353|| 
 
 
 daśarathasya |  
 
 
 ya eko lokānāṃ paramasuhṛdānandajanakaḥ 
 kalāśālī śrīmān nidhuvanavidhau maṅgalaghaṭaḥ | 
 sudhāsūtiḥ so’yaṃ tripuraharacūḍāmaṇir aho 
 prayātyas taṃ hanta prakṛtiviṣamā daivagatayaḥ  ||2354|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (su.ra. 1370) 
 
 
 yad bhagnaṃ dhanur īśvarasya śiśunā yaj jāmadagnyo jitas 
 tyaktā yac ca guror girā vasumatībaddho yad ambhonidhiḥ | 
 ekaikaṃ daśakandharakṣayakṛto rāmasya kiṃ varṇyatāṃ 
 daivaṃ varṇaya so’pi yena sahasā nītaḥ kathāśeṣatām  ||2355|| 
 
 
 śrīhanūmataḥ | (su.ra. 1359) 
 
 
 72. kālaḥ 
 
 
 ghātayati mahāpuruṣān samam eva bahūn anādareṇaiva | 
 parivartamāna ekaḥ kālaḥ śailānivānantaḥ  ||2356|| 
 
 
 bāṇasya | (Hc 5.2) 
 
 
 vyomaikāntavihāriṇo’pi vihagāḥ samprāpnuvanty āpadaṃ 
 badhyante nipuṇair agādhasalilān mīnāḥ samudrād api | 
 durṇītaṃ kim ihāsti kiṃ sucaritaṃ kaḥ sthānalābhe guṇaḥ 
 kālo hi vyasanaprasāritakaro gṛhṇāti dūrād api  ||2357|| 
 
 
 vasubhāgasya |  
 
 
 bhīmenātra vijṛmbhitaṃ dhanur iha droṇena muktaṃ śucā  
 karṇasyātra hayā hatā rathapatir bhīṣmo’tra yoddhuṃ sthitaḥ | 
 viśvaṃ rūpam ihārjunasya hariṇā saṃdarśitaṃ kautukād 
 uddeśās ta ime na te sukṛtinaḥ kālo hi sarvaṃkaṣaḥ  ||2358|| 
 
 
 halāyudhasya | 
 
 
 divasarajanīkūlacchedaiḥ patadbhir anārataṃ 
 vahati nikaṭe kālasrotaḥ samastabhayāvaham | 
 iha hi patato nāsty ālambo na cāpi nivartanaṃ 
 tad api bhavatāṃ mohaḥ ko’yaṃ yad evam anākulaḥ  ||2359|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (Ss 3.2) 
 
 
 dayālur no bāle na ca sujanagoṣṭhīṣu ramate 
 vilāsair nārīṇāṃ na hi bhavati sambhāvitarasaḥ | 
 anudvignaḥ kālaḥ kavalayati kṛtsnaṃ jagad aho 
 nisargakrūrāṇāṃ na khalu karuṇārdraḥ paricayaḥ  ||2360|| 
 
 
 yogeśvarasya | 
 
 
 73. śmaśānam 
 
 
 ardhapluṣṭaṃ bahubhyaḥ śavapiśitam upāhṛtya hṛṣṭaś citābhyo  
 jātagrāsātirekaḥ sphuṭataradhamanīnaddhaśuṣkārdrakāyaḥ | 
 pretaḥ saṃtarjya dṛṣṭyā kuṭilaparuṣayā majjaniṣkarṣaśuṣkair  
 āhantyāhāralubdhān muhur abhipatato jambukān asthikhaṇḍaiḥ  ||2361|| 
 
 
 jayādityasya | 
 
 
 śirāṃ pretaḥ kaścid daśati daśanāgreṇa sarasāṃ 
 lilikṣur mastiṣkaṃ kalayati ca mūrdhānam itaraḥ | 
 karaṃ dhūtvā dhūtvā jvaladanaladīptāṅguliśikhaṃ 
 citāsthālīpakvaṃ harati kuṇapakravyam aparaḥ  ||2362|| 
 
 
 nīlāmbarasya | 
 
 
 nṛtyadvetālamālāvalayitavikaṭaprāntam uḍḍāmarogra 
 prakrīḍaḍḍākinīkaṃ pratipadam udayatpūtanotphālalīlam | 
 utkhelatkolakelīkavalitavighasagrāsasaṃsaktagṛdhrā 
 kṛṣṭann asthipramodaṃ na janayati kathaṃ dṛśyamānaṃ śmaśānam  ||2363|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 udbuddhebhyaḥ sudūraṃ ghanarajanitamaḥpūriteṣu drumeṣu 
 prodgrīvaṃ paśya pādadvayanamitabhuvaḥ śreṇayaḥ pheravāṇām | 
 ulkālokaiḥ sphuradbhirnijavadanadarīsarpibhir vīkṣitebhyaś 
 cyotatsāndraṃ vasāmbhaḥ kvathitaśavavapurmaṇḍalebhyaḥ pibanti  ||2364|| 
 
 
 pāṇineḥ | (su.ra. 1529) 
 
 
 cañcatpakṣābhidhātajvalitahutavahaprauḍhadhāmnaś citāyāḥ  
 kroḍād vyākṛṣṭamūrter aham ahamikayā caṇḍacañcugraheṇa | 
 sadyas taptaṃ śavasya jvalad iva piśitaṃ bhūri jagdhvārdhadagdhaṃ 
 paśyāntaḥ pluṣyamāṇaḥ praviśati salilaṃ satvaraṃ gṛdhravṛddhaḥ  ||2365|| 
 
 
 tasyaiva | (sū.mu. 94.6, su.ra. 1528) 
 
 
 74. samasyā 
 
 
 thūthūkṛtya vamadbhir adhvagajanair aprāptakaṇṭhaṃ payaḥ 
 śuṣyattālugalair viruttya lavaṇodanvānupālabhyate | 
 kena kṣārakhane vṛthaiva bhavato nāmānṛtaṃ nirmitaṃ 
 pāthodhir jaladhiḥ payodhir udadhir vārāṃ nidhir vāridhiḥ  ||2366|| 
 
 
 vidyāyāḥ | 
 
 
 aye keyaṃ dhanyā dhavalagṛhavātāyanagatā  
 tulākoṭikvāṇair viṣamaviśikhaṃ jāgarayati | 
 purā yā prāṇeśe gatavati kṛtā puṣpadhanuṣā  
 śarāsārai rātriṃdivam akṛpam ujjāgarakṛśā  ||2367|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | (sū.mu. 49.11) 
 
 
 haraśirasi śirāṃsi yāni rejuḥ 
 śiva śiva tāni luṭhanti gṛdhrapādāḥ | 
 ayi khalu viṣamaḥ purā kṛtānāṃ 
 vilasasi jantuṣu karmaṇāṃ vipākaḥ  ||2368|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 upari vidhṛtaśāriprauḍhadhanviprasārād 
 iha payasi nadīnāṃ gāhituṃ naiva śaktāḥ | 
 taṭanikaṭanirūḍhāḥ prasthitau yasya caṇḍāḥ 
 saralitakaradaṇḍāḥ kumbhino’mbhaḥ pibanti  ||2369|| 
 
 
 gaṅgādharanāthasya | 
 
 
 sītāyā hṛdaye śirīṣakusumaprāye paphāloccakaiḥ 
 paulastyasya sadaiva kuṇṭhakuliśe vajrādhike vakṣasi | 
 āpuṅkhaṃ nimamajja tat katham aho naitad vijānīmahe 
 kaḥ śākhī sakhi yasya puṣpam abhavat puṣpāyudhasyāyudham  ||2370|| 
 75. uccāvacam 
 
 
 dhenuḥ kāmadughā kim icchati tadā sthātuṃ na madhyegṛhaṃ 
 kiṃ na prārthayati sthitiṃ karatale cintāmaṇiḥ sādaram | 
 utkaḥ kiṃ bhavanāṅgaṇāntikam alaṃ kartuṃ na kalpadrumaḥ 
 puṃsaḥ puṇyavato yadā kila bhaved ājñāvidheyo vidhiḥ  ||2371|| 
 
 
 kasyacit | 
 
 
 kim asmān vidvekṣi kṣapitabahudoṣavyatikarān 
 guṇān vaidheyānāṃ śriyam udayinīṃ vīkṣya dhaninām | 
 paricchedaḥ śaucaṃ vinayaparatā cendriyajayo 
 vivekotaḥ kṛtaṃ na khalu vayam arthapratimukhaḥ  ||2372|| 
 
 
 chittapasya | 
 
 
 utthāyotthāya pāpeṣv abhiramati matir mandabuddher yadā te 
 naivodvego na śāntir na ca bhavati ghṛṇā kurvataḥ karma nindyam | 
 tat kiṃ naiva prabhāte jvaladanalasamā rauravī nāma raudrī 
 tīkṣṇāyaḥkīlacakrakrakacapaṭuravā rājadhānī yamasya  ||2373|| 
 
 
 śrīmatpuruṣottamadevasya | 
 
 
 śailair bandhayati sma vānarahṛtair vālmīkir ambhonidhiṃ 
 vyāsaḥ pārthaśarais tathāpi na tayor atyuktir udbhāvyate | 
 vāg arthau ca tulādhṛtāv iva tathāpy asmatprabandhānayaṃ  
 loko dūṣayituṃ prasāritamukhas tubhyaṃ pratiṣṭhe namaḥ  ||2374|| 
 
 
 dharmakīrteḥ | (su.ra. 1726) 
 
 
 prāsādāḥ śikharaskhalajjaladharāḥ khātāni vārāṃ nidhi 
 spardhāvanty upayānti bhūmisamatāṃ kālena rājñām api | 
 kṣudrasyāpi kaveḥ sadartharacanākīrtis tu yā vāṅmayī 
 nādṛṣṭvā yugaviplavaṃ punar asau prāyaḥ parikṣīyate  ||2375|| 
 
 
 puruṣottamapādānām |  
 76. pratirājastutiḥ 
 
 
 ānandaṃ viduṣāṃ tanoti tanute karṇajvaraṃ vidviṣāṃ  
 śrīmān ādivarāhapādasarasījanma praṇāmaṃ muhuḥ | 
 sadbandhur guṇasindhur andhalaguḍo dharmasya vartmāvaneḥ  
 śrīmallakṣmaṇasenadakṣiṇabhujādaṇḍo’pi daṇḍe kaṭuḥ  ||2376|| 
 
 
 dharmādhikaraṇamadhoḥ | 
 
 
 yo heloktibhir āhito dhanavatām udvignakāntāvaco 
 gumphair labdhagatiḥ kṣudhākulaśiśukreṅkārasaṃvardhitaḥ | 
 pītvā jaṅgamakalpabhūruhavara tvadvācam etāṃ sudhā 
 sadhrīcīṃ baṭudāsa śāmyatu sa me proddāmakarṇajvaraḥ  ||2377|| 
 
 
 sāñcādharasya | 
 
 
 payodhirparimāṇeṣu dhaneṣu ca raṇeṣu ca | 
 vandīndrāṇāṃ narendrāṇāṃ baṭudāsas taraṇḍakaḥ  ||2378|| 
 
 
 rājavetālasya | 
 
 
 alam ādivarāheṇa baṭudāsaṃ paraṃ stumaḥ | 
 jagaduddharatā yena na vakrīkṛtam ānanam  ||2379|| 
 
 
 umāpatidharasya | 
 
 
 tatprāṅgaṇāntam adhirohati kalpavallī 
 cintāmaṇir luṭhati padatale ca tasya | 
 yenekṣitaḥ sukṛtasāgarapāradṛśvā 
 viśvānurañjanapaṭur baṭudāsadevaḥ  ||2380|| 
 
 
 kavirājavyāsasya | 
 
 
 śrīdharadāsavinirmite saduktikarṇāmṛte pravāho’yam | 
 pañcama uccāvaca iti vividhapramodaṃ tanotu rasikānām || 
 
 iti mahāmāṇḍalikaśrīśrīdharadāsakṛtau saduktikarṇāmṛte  
 uccāvacapravāho nāma pañcamaḥ pravāhaḥ |  
 
 vīcayaḥ 76 | ślokāḥ 380 | 
 
 śrīdharadāsavinirmitasaduktikarṇāmṛte pravāhāṇām | 
 pañcakam iha ṣaṭsaptatyadhikaśatacatuṣṭayī vīciḥ || 
 ślokānāṃ ca śatatrayam aśītyupetaṃ sahasrayor dvitayam | 
 granthaś ca ṣaṣṭhisamadhikasaptaśatādhikasahasrapañcatayam || 
 śāke’tra saptaviṃśatyadhikaśatopetadaśaśate śaradām | 
 śrīmallakṣmaṇasenakṣitipasya rasakaviṃśe’bde || 
 savitur gatyā phālgunaviṃśeṣu parārthahetave kutukāt | 
 śrīdharadāsenedaṃ saduktikarṇāmṛtaṃ cakre || 
 bhavatu nṛpo dharmaparaḥ paramasamṛddhā ca bhavatu vasudheyam | 
 dheyāt sukhāni loke keśavacaraṇāmbujadvitayam || 
 
 
 
 iti mahāmāṇḍalikaśrīśrīdharadāsavinirmitasaduktikarṇāmṛtākhyaḥ  
 ślokasamuccayaḥ samāptaḥ |  
 
 
 vīcayaḥ 476 | prativīcipañcaślokaniyamena ślokāḥ 2380 |
